na rta mchog rgyug lta'i chu/ /nub ri mtshan ma rma bya'i mdongs ldan byang gi lhun po 'dab bzang ri/ /ri dwags rgyal po bzhad pa'i gdong can dbus kyi sa 'dzin dpal kun
'dzin/ /de phyir rgyal ba'i gdan sa mchog 'di byang chub snying po ma lags grang / /zhes gsungs pa ltar/ shar ri brag chung glang po che'i spyi gtsug ltar mtho ba/ lhor grum
chu rta mchog rin po che ltar rgyug pa/ nub chu mig rdzing kha rma bya'i mdongs dang ldan pa/ byang dpon po ri mkha' lding gi gshog pa ltar rgyangs pa/ dbus kyi sa dkar
logs 'di ri dwags kyi rgyal po mngon par 'gying ba dang 'dra ba/ tsha zer dbang po 'char snga zhing nub bul ba/ lho phyogs kyi ri rin po che'i phung po brdal ba lta bu/
jo mo stag 'tsher gdugs kyi dbyibs su yod pa sogs bkra shis rtags brgyad/ gnam 'khor lo rtsibs brgyad/ sa padma 'dab brgyad sogs

dge mtshan thams cad dang ldan pa'i gnas so/ /de dag gi don bsdu na/ dbang phyogs sa 'dzin lag ldan myos bum rtser/ /'gro 'dren dpa' bo mi bskyod rdo rje'i zhabs/ /lho phyogs
bzang po'i rta mchog kha 'bab rgyun/ /rin chen 'byung ldan phrin las dpal du che/ /yid 'phrog chu lha'i phang par 'jug sgra can/ /ne'u gseng g.yu ngogs bkra shis ke sgras
'phyo/ /'od mtshan 'gro ba dpag med 'dren pa'i mgon/ /ma chags padmar ngal 'tsho gnod sbyin phyogs/ /mkha' 'gro'i dbang phyug lus skyes rdzogs pa'i khrod/ /sa skyob spo
la don yod grub pa'i sku/ /'jigs med ri dwags dbang po 'gying ba'i sa/ /dpal ldan rdo rje 'chang gi bsti gnas lags/ /zhes kyang smras so// // ! gnyis pa rigs rus cho 'brang
phun sum tshogs pa dang ldan pa'i gdung rabs byon tshul bshad pa ni/ khri brgyad stong pa las/ de la byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i rigs phun sum tshogs pa
gang zhe na/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i rigs chen po dag tu skye ba ste/ de ni byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i rigs phun sum tshogs pa yin no/ /de
la byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i cho rigs phun sum tshogs pa gang zhe na/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rgyal rigs shing sA la chen po dag dang / bram
ze'i rigs shing sA la chen po dag tu skye ba ste/ de ni byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i cho rigs phun sum tshogs pa yin no/ /de la byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa'
chen po'i rus phun sum tshogs pa gang zhe na/ rigs gang las sngon gyi byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po dag byung bar gyur pa ste/ de ni byang chub sems dpa' sems
dpa' chen po'i rus phun sum tshogs pa yin no/

/zhes gsungs shing / des na sngon gyi mkhas pa rnams/ bod 'dir bram ze'i rigs su gsal ba ma byung bas/ rgyal rigs/ rje rigs/ dmangs rigs gsum du 'du bar bshad pas/ dkon pa
rje gung stag gam dpal bo che zhes/ chos kyi rgyal po khri srong lde'u btsan gyi nang blon de nyid kyis ni/ zhang blon rje'u rigs su bshad pa'ang yod mod/ gzugs khams lha
gnas gsum pa 'od gsal nas gnam gyi lha mched gsum byon pa'i bar pa las mched pas lha rigs gtsang ma 'gran bral nyid du 'khums shing rus ni rigs ma nyams pa'i pha de'i brgyud
pa las byung ba ste/ des na gang gi lha rigs gtsang ma gang las byung bar gyur pa'o/ /cho 'brang ni zhang po khungs dang ldan pa la 'jug ste 'og tu 'chad lags/ don de
dag la dgongs nas ngor chen thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub kyi gsungs las/ mi shes gdol pa'i phrug gu phongs pa yi/ /'khor gyis bteg la 'jig rten 'dren pa zhes/
/smig rgyu 'bab chur sgrogs pa'i grag stong sgras/ /'jig rten yangs por byed dang 'di mi mtshungs/ /zhes kyang bsngags par mdzad do/ /de yang gnam lha mched gsum 'byon
nas kyang yul mtho zhing gtsang ba mnga' ris stod kyi sa'am lo rgyus 'ga' zhig na byang gi shel tsha rgyal mo'i gangs 'gram du byon par yang bshad pas/ gcung po g.yu ser
sras bzhi byon pa yab bcas lha yul du gshegs/ bar pa g.yu ring dang dmu bza' ldem bu las/ sras ma sangs spun bdun byon pa'i gcen drug yab dang bcas kyang lha yul gshegs/
bdun pa ma sangs spyi rje dang thog lcam 'ur mo'i sras dpa' bo stag /de dang klu lcam dra ma'i sras stag po 'od can te 'di rnams bar snang la bzhugs par bzhed/ /de dang
mon bza' 'tsho morgyal gyi sras g.ya' spang skyes rnams ni lha'i gdung rabs so/ /des srin po

skya rengs khrag med bsad/ chung ma g.ya' 'brum si li ma phrogs te khab tu bzhes pas/ lha dang srin po 'khon pa'i bar du 'khrungs pa'i sras 'khon bar skyes/ de dang btsan bza'
lcam bu sgron gyi sras dkon pa rje gung stag gam 'khon dpal po che/ de dang rlangs bza' ne chung ma'i sras gcen klu dbang dang / gcung rdo rje rin chen/ phyi ma'i lcam
'gro bza' g.yang lon skyid la/ sras bdun byon pa'i gcen drug las/ che ba mang yul/ de 'og gung thang / de 'og srad dang / de 'og gnyal lo ro/ de 'og myang shab rnams las
sku brgyud 'phel yang ngos 'dzin dang bral zhing bdun pa'i sku brgyud ma 'khrigs sde gsum du grags/ drug pa shes rab yon tan g.ya' lung du bzhugs/ sras gnyis kyi chung
ba khab so stag tu byon pa las/ la stod byang gi 'khon tsho rnams 'phel bar bshad/ che ba yon tan 'byung gnas la sras gsum byon pa'i gras tshul khrims rgyal po ste/ de la
yang sras gsum gyi bar pa brdal gyi chang tshang du byon/ thog mtha' gnyis g.ya' lung du bzhugs pa'i che ba gtsug tor shes rab la sras bdun gcung dang bcas la 'khon tsho
brgyad du grags pa'i lnga pa dge skyabs shab tu byon pa'i sras gnyis kyi gcung las shab stod kyi 'khon tsho gyes/ gcen po dge mthong sras bal po/ /de sras shAkya blo gros/
de sras shes rab tshul khrims dang / dkon mchog rgyal po gnyis las/ shes rab tshul khrims yan 'khon gyi gdung rabs gsang sngags snga 'gyur gyi bdag po/ grub pa'i sa la
zhugs te brag la phur pa 'debs pa dang / rnga la chibs nas nam mkhar thogs med phebs pa sogs rdzu 'phrul bsam gyis mi khyab par ston par mdzad pa sha dag go /'khon ston
dpal po che nas shes rab tshul khrims bar dbu bla ma nges shing / 'on kyang klu dbang sku mched ni/

mkhan chen zhi ba 'tsho dang / slob dpon rin po che padma'i zhal slob yin cing / phyi ma 'khon dkon mchog rgyal po shing khyir 'khrungs nas re dgu chu rtar gshegs pa des/ bzhi
bcu chu glang lor dpal ldan sa skya btab/ yab dang / gcen po/ khyin lo/ 'brog mi/ se kun rig /'gos lo/ shes rab gsang ba/ rma lotstsha/ mal lo/ ba ri ba/ kha'u pa sku
mched/ 'khon sgyi chu ba/ skyu ra a seng sogs las gsan pa rgya mtsho'i pha mthar son cing / gur zhang mor chu spre'u lo yab nga dgu'i thog sa chen kun dga' snying po 'khrungs
nas re bdun sa stag gshegs/ de'i dbu bla ni/ 'jam dbyangs/ sgrol ma/ mi g.yo ba/ birWa pa/ nag po pa/ ga ya dha ra/ nags khrod pa/ ko tra li/ yab dkon mchog rgyal po/
ba ri ba/ brang ti dar ma snying po/ dge bshes khyung / khyung rin chen grags pa/ dpal me dig pa/ mes lhang 'tsher/ kha'u pa/ sgyi chu ba/ mal lo/ spu hrang lo chung /
skyu ra a skyabs/ padma shrIH /dznyA na badzra/ bha dra rA hu la/ dge bshes rngog /zhang ston chos 'bar/ dpal sga lo sogs lha mi'i dam pa du ma las/ yongs rdzogs bstan pa
rin po che'i mnga' bdag tu bzhugs pa de'i btsun mo dang po tsha rong jo lcam phur mor/ kun dga' 'bar dang gnyis pa tsha rong 'od sgron ma'i sras/ slob dpon rin po che bsod
nams rtse mo/ rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ dpal chen 'od po ste gsum byon zhing / zhal slob kyang phyag chen thob pa gsum/ bzod pa thob pa bdun/ gzhon
nu'i sar gnas gcig /gzhan yang dpal chen sga lo/ byang sems zla ba rgyal mtshan/ dpal phag mo gru pa/ sgom pa rta rgan phag ston/ rgyal tsha tal phug pa/ dbyar ston sbum
pa/ gshen rdor seng / gshen dgon dkar ba/ zhang ston gsum thog pa/ zhang ston spe dmar ba/ brag dmar gzhu/ skyur

a skyabs/ a seng / ne co sbal ston/ lho brag dkar ston/ mdzangs ston mdza' ne/ bsod nams rdo rje/ gnyag ston dbang rgyal/ rgya sgom tshul khrims grags/ mi nyag ston pa/ khams
pa sga theng / 'a 'u ma sogs te shar phyogs rgya mtsho'i mtha' klas pa'i dam pa rnams thugs rje che ldan de yi slob brgyud du grags pa lags/ de sras dpal chen 'od po yab
nga dgu lcags rtar 'khrungs shing / nga bzhi chu phag la gshegs pa de'i lcam gar phu nyi khri la 'jam mgon sa skya paNDi chen po dang / bzang tsha bsod nams rgyal mtshan
gnyis byon pa las/ phyi ma yab so lnga shing 'brug la 'khrungs shing / nga drug sa phag la gshegs pa de nyid la btsun mo lnga las/ dang po tsha sna kun skyid kyi sras
su 'gro ba'i mgon po chos rgyal 'phags pa dang / 'gro mgon phyag na rdo rje gnyis bltams/ phyi ma'i btsun mo mam gal/ chos 'bum/ zha lu mkha' 'gro 'bum gsum las phyi ma'i
sras dharma pha la/ de'i lcam dpal stag gnyis kyi phyi mar ratna bha dra bltams/ bzang tsha'i btsun mo gnyis pa chu mdo mar rin chen rgyal mtshan lcam bcas byung / gsum
pa gung thang lha gcig mdzes mar bsod 'bum dang nyi 'bum zhes lcam gnyis dang / bzhi pa g.ya' lung hor lcam la'ang sras mo gcig /lnga pa mdzes ma'i nye gnas rdo rje ldan
la yab nga lnga sa khyir ye shes 'byung gnas 'khrungs shing / so bdun shing khyir gshegs pa de'i btsun mo khab smad 'bum mer yab nyer lnga chu khyi la/ bdag nyid chen po
bzang po dpal bltams shing re gsum shing byir gshegs pa der sman rtse ma dang / lung phud btsun mo drug ste bdun gyi sman rtse'i sras chung ngur gshegs/ lung phud dang po
rgyal po'i lcam mu dgan gyi sras su bsod nams bzang po lcam sring gnyis/ bsod nams bzang po'i btsun mo buddha gan gyi sras su ratna bha dra bcas/ lung phud gnyis pa mang

mkhar sogs sbe ngang mor/ ti shri kun dga' blo gros byon pa ste spyi la dbang bsgyur gyi gdung rabs sras su grags pa rnams so// // ! de las gyes pa gzhi thog bla brang gi gdung
rabs ni/ lung phud gsum pa glang mtshon spe ma nam mkha' rgyal mor/ yab zhe bzhi pa shing sbrul lor mkhas btsun nam mkha' legs pa 'khrungs shing / so dgu chu lug la
gshegs pa des/ yab dang mkhas pa nor bzang dpal sogs bsten cing / zhal slob chos rje bla ma dam pa sogs so/ /nam mkha' bshes gnyen dang nam mkha' rgyal mtshan rnam gnyis
ni de'i gcung ngo / /mkhas btsun chen po'i btsun mo ngam ring khang gsar ma dge 'dun 'bum la/ yab so lnga sa yos lor kun dga' rin chen 'khrungs shing / re gcig sa yos la
gshegs pa de'i dbu bla ni/ chos rje bla ma/ mnyam med grags rgyal/ zhang ston dbang phyug rgyal/ mgon rgyal/ 'jam sngon/ gung ru sogs bsten cing zhal slob kyang mang du byung
'dra/ btsun mo gnyis kyi dang po nyi thog nam par blo gros rgyal mtshan 'khrungs shing / de'i btsun mo sa skya rgyal mo skyid la kun dga' dbang phyug bltams/ btsun mo
gnyis pa mnyam med dpon mo ma gcig dge ma la grags pa blo gros/ kun dga' blo gros/ gzhan yang lcam gcig bcas 'khrungs shing / grags blo'i btsun mo brag dkar mar blo gros
dbang phyug 'khrungs pa rnams ni/ gzhi thog bla brang ba'i gdung rabs su grags pa'o// // ! de nas bla brang rin chen sgang pa'i gdung rabs ni/ lung phud btsun mo drug pa
zha lu gzhon 'bum gyi sras su kun dga' nyi ma/ don yod rgyal mtshan/ bsod nams rgyal mtshan te sku mched gsum las/ don yod rgyal mtshan yab nyer dgu lcags khyir 'khrungs
shing / /so lnga shing sprer gshegs pa des yab dang / bsod nams grags pa/ dpal ldan seng ge /grags pa seng ge /spang lotstsha ba/ bsod

nams dpal/ rgyal sras thogs med/ chos dpal bzang sogs bsten nas tshogs chos gsungs pas/ zhal slob kyang shin tu mang ba de'i btsun mo zha lu ma yon tan dpal 'bum gyi sras su
nyi ma rgyal mtshan dang / zla ba rgyal mtshan gnyis bltams pa'i phyi ma la bla chen kun dga' rgyal mtshan zhes grags pa de yab so lnga shing sprer 'khrungs nas/ sa khyi
don lngar gshegs pa de'i dbu bla ni/ chos rje bla ma/ mnyam med grags rgyal sogs bsten cing zhal slob sa bzang 'phags pa dang / theg chen kun dga' bkra shis sogs so/ /btsun
mo zha lu ma nam mkha' rgyal mor yab nga lnga sa stag lor 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan 'khrungs shing / don lnga pa chu 'brug lor gshegs pa des yab dang / theg
chen rje/ bsod nams rgyal mchog /rdo rje rgyal mtshan sogs dbu blar bsnyen cing / de'i gcung bdag chen zhwa lu ba bsod nams rgyal mtshan lcam mo gnyis dang bcas par sras
lcam sring bzhir grags shing / 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan gyi btsun mo khro mda' ma dpal 'byung rgyal mor sras mo bzhi dang / sras gnyis kyi che ba rgya gar shes
rab rgyal mtshan dang chung ba bdag chen rdo rje 'chang blo gros rgyal mtshan/ bdag chen zhwa lu pa'i btsun mo ldan yul ma kun dga' 'bum la grags pa rgyal mtshan 'khrungs
pa ste de rnams ni/ bla brang rin chen sgang pa'i gdung rabs su grags pa'o// // ! de nas lha khang bla brang pa'i gdung rabs ni/ lung phud btsun mo bzhi pa sha zug ma
kun dga' nam mkha'i rgyal mtshan zhes bya ba'i sras su dbang kun dga' legs pa'i 'byung gnas dang / kun dga' rgyal mtshan gnyis 'khrungs pa'i phyi ma yab zhe dgu pa lcags
khyir 'khrungs nas/ zhe dgu sa khyir gshegs pa de'i btsun mo gnyis

kyi dang po kha phyar mar yab nyer gsum chu sprer chos kyi rgyal mtshan 'khrungs shing nyer brgyad sa phag la gshegs/ btsun mo gnyis par lung bsod dpal ma'i sras su gcung po
blo rgyal ba 'khrungs pa dang / chos rgyal mtshan gyi btsun mo dang po chu mdo rgyal mo mtshor theg chen chos kyi rgyal po dang / gnyis pa nyang stod sras skyabs la dharma
dhwa dza dang rdo rje rin chen gnyis bltams/ gsum pa lho ba dpal ldan 'bum la bsod nams bkra shis yab nyer gcig chu 'brug lor 'khrungs shing nga drug me phag la gshegs
pa de'i dbu bla ni/ gzhi thog bdag po kun dga' rin chen/ sa bzang ma ti/ chos rje bla ma sogs bsten cing zhal slob kyang mang du byung ba de'i btsun mo byang mo ma gcig
nam par yab gshegs pa'i phyi lo sa byir bde legs bkra shis bltams pa'i dgung grangs dbu bla zhal slob rnams mi gsal/ de'i btsun mo byang bdag sras mor bsod nams rgyal mtshan/
shAkya seng ge /don grub rgyal mtshan/ bsam 'grub rgyal mtshan te sras bzhi byon pa las/ shAka seng btsun mo dang po gcung dpon mor kun bkras/ kun rgyal/ kun dga' snying
po ste gsum dang / gnyis pa ma gcig yum par rin chen rgyal mtshan zhes sku mched mtshan 'dra ba rnam gnyis 'khrungs/ kun dga' rgyal mtshan btsun mo gling kha dpon dkar
mor chos kyi rgyal mtshan dang / kun dga' legs pa 'khrungs pa rnams ni/ lha khang bla brang pa'i gdung rabs su grags pa rnams so// // ! de nas dus mchod bla brang pa'i
gdung rabs ni/ lung phud lnga pa re mda' ma nyi ma rin chen ma'i sras su nyi ma dpal/ lcam gcig /kun dga' legs 'byung dang gsum 'khrungs pa'i phyi ma yab zhe bdun sa sprer
bltams shing nyer dgu me byir gshegs pa de'i btsun mo dang po gung thang kun skyong mar lcam gcig 'khrungs/ gnyis pa ngam ring dge 'bum gyi

sras bsod nams blo gros dang / sku 'bring ni chung ngur gshegs/ grags pa rgyal mtshan te rnam pa gsum gyi phyi ma yab gshegs pa'i me byir bltams nas zhe gnyis sa sbrul gshegs
pa des chos rje/ gcen brag phug pa/ mnyam med pa sogs bsten nas zhal slob mi gsal ba de'i btsun mo dang po lha rin mar kun dga' legs pa'i blo gros dang / rnam sras rgyal
mtshan mched gnyis byon/ gnyis pa stag tshang sras 'dren mar 'jam dbyangs chos rgyal bltams pa las rnam sras rgyal mtshan yab nyer lnga pa lcags byir 'khrungs shing zhe
dgu sa byir gshegs pa des chos rje bla ma/ bsod nams blo gros sogs bsten cing zhal slob mi gsal ba de'i btsun mo dang po rta nag gru gur dbang kun dga' legs pa'i blo gros
dang / gnyis pa yar 'brog bsod nams 'bum la yab bzhi bcu sa yos lor nam mkha' legs pa 'khrungs shing zhe drug shing byir gshegs pa des 'brom ston seng ge sogs bsten cing
zhal slob kyang mang du yod snyam zhing sku mched du gtogs pa'i lcam lnga'ang 'khrungs/ btsun mo dang po yar 'brog dpal chen la lcam gnyis dang / gnyis pa mi nyag btsun
ma skyid la nam mkha' rgyal mtshan yab so bdun shing yos lor 'khrungs nas nyer dgu chu lug lor gshegs pa de'i bla slob mi gsal zhing lcam lnga'ang 'khrungs/ btsun mo dang
po shangs mthong smon rgan par lcam gcig gzhon par slob dpon chen po rin rgyal ba 'khrungs/ gsum pa gnam gling dpal 'byor bzang mor yab nyer bzhi sa stag la nam mkha'
bkra shis 'khrungs shing zhe drug chu phag la gshegs pa des stag tshang lotstsha ba/ mi nyag grags rdor sogs bsten cing zhal slob kyang du ma byon/ btsun mo dma' ze hor mo
tshe brtan gyi sras su sa lo kun dga' bsod

nams/ ngag gi dbang phyug /'jam dpal grags pa/ sangs rgyas tshe brtan bkra shis te sku mched rnam bzhi las phyi ma yab so lnga chu byir bltams nas lnga bcu lcags glang la gshegs/
des mus chen sangs rgyas rin chen/ sa lo sku mched sogs bsten cing zhal slob kyang mang du byon snyam/ yar 'brog bu 'dren skyid khab tu bzhes pa'i sras sku mched gnyis
byon pa'i dang po nas phyis byon rtse gdong bla brang pa'i gdung rabs rnams mched pa ste/ de yang / bdag chen kun dga' bsam 'grub yab nyer bzhi shing phag lor 'khrungs
nas nga brgyad chu sprer gshegs pa des sa lo/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun 'grub/ kun dga' legs grub/ sman sdings lo chen sogs bsten nas zhal slob kyang mang du byung / btsun
mo bde skyid gling pa ma gcig la yab so lnga sa byir kun dga' bde legs bltams shing bzhi bcu sa byir gshegs pa des kun dga' legs grub/ kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ yab/ dkon
mchog dpal ldan/ thar rtse paN chen/ byams pa rab brtan sogs bsnyen cing zhal slob kyang mang du byon/ btsun mor rta nag bya bzang dpal bu 'khrid la rtse gdong khri chen
bsod nams lhun grub/ tshe dbang hor sogs bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ 'jig rten rgya hor rnam gsum las/ phyi ma yab sum cu sa stag la bltams nas zhe brgyad shing glang la gshegs
pa de'i dbu blar gcen bgres pa dang / thar rtse paN chen/ byams pa rab brtan thub bstan mkhan chen chos 'od zer sogs bsten cing zhal slob kha shas dang / btsun mo stag
lung ma nor 'dzom bu 'khrid la bsod nams blo gros/ byams pa bsod nams lhun grub/ ngag dbang bsod nams lhun grub gsum byon pa'i phyi ma yab so drug chu glang lor 'khrungs
nas re bzhi me 'brug la gshegs pa des gcen mched dang / 'jam mgon a mes zhabs sogs

dam pa mang du bsten cing zhal slob kyang kha shas byung / btsun mo yol gdong ma nor bu buu khrid la bstan 'dzin dbang / bsod nams 'phags pa/ bsod nams dbang rgyal gsum las
phyi ma yab so gsum shing byar bltams nas re drug lcags stag la gshegs pa des gcen bgres pa dang / ngag dbang bstan pa'i rdo rje sogs bsten nas zhal slob kyang kha shas
byung / btsun mo stag lung ma bkra shis tshe ring la kun dga' tshe dbang rig 'dzin dang / ngag dbang nor bu rgyal mtshan gnyis/ yang phal mo zhig las sras gcig ste gsum byon
pa'i nor bu rgyal mtshan gyi btsun mor bya sgo ma tshe ring bu khrid bzhes mod/ yab sras lcam bcas de dag gi sku thog la bstan gegs kyis gdan sa 'thor ba nas bzung yun
ring 'das shing / phyis su drin can rtsa ba'i bla ma dam pa dpal sa skya pa chen po sngags 'chang bla ma thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang kun dga' blo gros sangs rgyas bstan
pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po zhes sku drin mtshungs pa ma mchis pa'i zhal snga nas de nyid dgung grangs bcu drug tu byon pa shing byi lor gdan sa chen po rtse gdong
phyag 'byor byung ba ste/ phyis byon rtse gdong bla brang ba'i gdung rabs su grags pa rnams so/ /gong gi kun dga' bsam grub kyi gcung po sngags 'chang bdud kyi stobs 'phrog
ngag dbang kun dga' rin chen bkra shis grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po nyid yab nyer drug pa me glang lor 'khrungs shing re brgyad pa shing sprer gshegs pa de'i
dbu bla ni/ sa lo chen po ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/ 'phags chen dpal ldan bkra shis/ spyan snga ngag dbang chos grags/ ngor chen sangs rgyas seng ge /mkhan chen legs
pa'i blo gros sogs bsnyen nas zhal slob ris med nor 'dzin gyi rdul dang mnyam pa bskrun par mdzad de/

btsun mo gsum gyi dang po shar gling mar sras mo gnyis dang / gnyis pa gdong dga' ma bgres pa bsod nams legs mdzom dkar mo las 'jam dbyangs bsod nams dbang po dang sras mo
gsum bcas bltams/ gsum pa gzhon pa bkra shis dpal gyi bu 'khrid las yab zhe bdun chu phag lor sngags 'chang grags pa blo gros zhes bya ba'am mtshan gzhan bsod nams rgyal
mtshan 'khrungs shing nga lnga me sbrul la gshegs pa des yab dang gcen/ spyan snga dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ thar rtse paN chen sogs bsnyen nas zhal slob kyang mang du bskrun
par mdzad cing / byang bdag lha sras bsod nams rgyal mo khab tu bzhes par sras drug byon pa'i dang po gnyis dang bzhi pa chung ngur gshegs /gsum pa sgar chen mthu stobs
dbang phyug /lnga pa sngags 'chang kun dga' dbang rgyal/ drug pa ni sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po'i bstan pa rin po che spel bar bsams bzhin byon pa'i ngag dbang kun dga'
bsod nams grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po zhes grags pa de nyid yab so lnga me bya lor bltams nas re gsum sa phag la gshegs pa de'i dbu bla ni/ khu bo sku mched/
rtse gdong khri chen bsod nams lhun grub/ gcen po gnyis/ gcig chog mus pa chen po/ sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ thar rtse paN chen/ spyan snga kun dga' don grub/ nags dgon pa
sbyin pa grags/ 'bum chen kun dga' dpal/ dbang phyug rab brtan/ ngag dbang chos grags sogs bsnyen cing / zhal slob ni nyi zer rdul ltar bskrun par mdzad/ sku mched gsum
la sde srid lhun rtse ma'i nye gnas cha shod mthong smon bu sring ma bkra shis dpal gyi bu bskyed ces bya ba khab tu bzhes par lcam gcig dang gdung gcig phebs pa chung ngur
gshegs/ de nas ko cag 'gro mgon 'jigs bral gyi sras mo auDyin skyabs ma bzhes par yab zhe gnyis sa stag la 'jam dbyangs bsod nams dbang phyug

bltams nas zhe brgyad shing glang la gshegs pa des yab dang / ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ ka spe ba bstan pa rab rgyas/ mkhan chen lhun grub dpal
ldan/ byang bdag bsod nams grags pa/ la ru ba ngag dbang dpal bzang sogs bsnyen nas nyid kyi rigs sras sogs zhal slob kyang mang du bskrun/ mgon de'i btsun mor bdag chen
shar pa pad dkar bu 'khrid bzhes par yab bcu dgu me sprer ngag dbang kun dga' bkra shis 'khrungs shing nga drug lcags yos la gshegs pa des 'jam mgon a mes zhabs/ nyid kyi
yab rje/ ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ bstan pa rab rgyas/ lhun grub dpal ldan/ bzang po rgyal mtshan/ sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ smin gling lo chen/ dza lung pa/ bco brgyad chen
mo sogs las gsan pa rgya mtsho'i mthar son cing rigs sras mchog sogs zhal slob kyang mang du byon/ de'i gcung gzhon nur gshegs/ btsun mo dang po sngon dus rlangs bza' ne
chung ma sogs sku gnyen dang / dus phyis si tu byang rgyal sogs bstan dgra'i brgyud sne'u gdong ma bkra shis dbang mor sras mi mnga'/ phyi ma sku zhang rnga sgra'i sras
mo mkha' 'gro 'bum nas bzung sa skya pa'i sku zhang rang bzhi tsam mdzad pa'i brgyud pa 'phan yul bco brgyad pa'i sras mo bstan 'dzin bsod nams bzang mor thog mar gdung gnyis
bltams kyang bstan gegs kyis chung ngur gshegs/ de nas rje btsun drung / de nas 'jam dbyangs bsod nams rin chen yab lnga bcu shing byar 'khrungs shing so bdun lcags
byar gshegs/ des yab rje dang / bstan 'dzin phun tshogs/ lha btsun kun bzang pa bco brgyad mkhyen brtse rab brtan/ stag rtse byams pa lha dbang rig 'dzin/ mchod dpon dkon
mchog rgyal po/ sgro lung pa mang thos bsod nams

chos 'phel/ gong dkar ba blo gros dbang phyug /ngor chen bsod nams bzang po/ thar rtse rdo rje 'chang / thub bstan mkhan chen tshul khrims bzang po/ lha chen mkhan po dbang
phyug phun tshogs/ dza lung ba phrin las rdo rje gsang sngags bstan 'phel sogs bsnyen cing zhal slob kyang thar rtse rje/ gnas gsar rje/ brag rtsa rje/ rje rdo rje 'chang
sku mched sogs bstan 'dzin mang du bskrun par mdzad/ mgon de'i btsun mo dang po bzhad chos ma'i sras gnyis chung ngur gshegs shing / phyi ma 'gro mgon ma bsod nams dpal
gyi dbang mo de nyid ni gong gi 'og tu 'chad rgyu'i cho 'brang phun sum tshogs pa ste/ de yang sngon mkhan slob chos gsum skabs kyi rje 'bangs nyer lnga'i gras/ dkon mchog
'byung gnas thog chen mda' ltar 'phen/ zhes lang 'gro dkon mchog 'byung gnas kyi sku brgyud las 'phel zhing / auDyin gyi slob dpon chen po padma 'byung gnas kyi ring lugs
pa mthu stobs dang / nus pa'i bdag nyid can sha dag tu byon pa ko cag sngags pa'am 'gro mgon par grags pa'i sras mo mkha' 'gro'i mtshan can de nyid la/ sras mo bzhi dang
gdung brgyud gsum ste bdun byon pa las/ drug pa'i btsun mor sger pa bkra shis dbyangs can las da lta'i rje btsun drung 'di nyid dang / gsum pa ni/ rigs dang dkyil 'khor
thams cad kyi bdag po/ 'jig rten gsum gyi ma rig pa'i mun pa 'phrog pa'i phan bde'i sgron me/ yongs rdzogs bstan pa rin po che'i mnga' bdag tu gyur pa snyigs ma'i dus
kyi rgyal ba gnyis pa/ mkhas grub rgyu skar gyi dbyings na mtshan dpe'i snang ba 'phro ba'i bsil sbyin mkhan po/ mkhas dang bstan pa'i bgyi bar gzhan dring mi 'jog pa'i spobs
pa gzengs mtho ba/ mdor na 'brel tshad don ldan gyi bdag nyid du

gyur pa'i dpal sa skya pa chen po sngags 'chang bla ma thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang kun dga' blo gros sangs rgyas bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po zhes snyan pa'i ba
dan khor yug ri bo'i khongs su'ang rgyu ba de nyid ni/ yab rje nyer lnga sa byar 'khrungs tshul rgyas pa dang dbu bla sogs 'og tu rim gyis 'byung zhing / nga lnga chu yos
la bde ba nas bde ba'i dbyings su phebs pa de nyid kyi btsun mo dang po ru thog chos lung rgyal po'i sras mo phun tshogs tshe ring mar lcam gcig 'khrungs/ gnyis pa ni/
sku drin nam yang 'khor med bskal bzang bde skyid bu khrid ces sems ma'i ngo bo yab rje chos kyi rgyal po chen po de nyid dgung grangs so lngar phebs pa/ nyi ma zhes pa chu
mo lug gi lor skyabs mgon khams gsum dbang sdud ngag dbang kun dga' dpal ldan chos skyong bkra shis grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po 'di nyid dang / dgung grangs so
brgyad du phebs pa mi zad ces pa mi khyi lor skyabs mgon srid zhi'i phan bde'i mdzad po ngag dbang kun dga' phan bde rgya mtsho theg mchog bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang
po 'di nyid bcas ngo mtshar bkra shis kyi mtshan mas tha grur dkrigs te bstan 'gro'i dpal mgon chen por bltams shing / ji srid 'khor ba ma stongs kyi bar du gdung rabs
rin po che chu bo'i rgyun ltar 'bad med lhun grub tu 'byung zhing sku tshe mdzad phrin bzhed dgongs mthar phyin par 'gyur ro/ /de dag gi don bsdu na/ phyag na padmas gdul
zhing kha ba'i ljongs/ /bde skyid chu klung 'dren pa'i dam pa'i khyu/ /zo chun 'khyud mo'i rnam par grub mod kyi/ /gcig tu zas gtsang sras de'i thugs bskyed grogs/ /mnga'
ris sa 'dzin gtos su gangs can 'di'i/ /bsod nams mgron du gnam lha dkon mchog gsum/ /gtsang ma chos kyi 'bab rgyun spyi rje las/ /stag mtshan nyi zla gnyis rnams bar

snang bsti/ /'od kyi g.ya' spang mtshams bskyangs lha'i gdung rabs/ /ma rungs srin por 'khon bar btsas de'i dpal/ /'jam dbyangs chos rgyal bka' yi kha lo bsgyur/ /dang po'i
rab byung gras su nA gendraH gcung las g.ya' lung kha bso stag rtsen las/ /byang gi 'khon tsho brdal gyi chang tshang dang / /'khon tsho brgyad dang shab stod 'khon yang
gyes/ /dge bar mthong nas shes rab tshul khrims bar/ /snga 'gyur grub mtshan thogs med sha dag dang / /lha rigs 'khon dang sa skya par sgrogs pa'i/ /mtshan gsum lto 'gro'i
kha gnon ratna che/ /khor yug phyogs kyi rna bar bstan pa'i bdag /rnam lngar grags pa'i khu dbon mtshan snyan ni/ /shar phyogs gnam bskos zur phud thod bcings su/ /lhur
bzhes rim rgyud ti shrI kun dga'i mtshan/ /bar du byon rnams spyi la dbang bsgyur ro// ! lung phud gsum par mkhas btsun legs lam nas/ /rnyog bral dag pa'i chu klung 'phel
ba'i rgyun/ /ma rig 'gogs pa'i blo gros dbang phyug pa/ /bar du gzhi thog bla brang gdung rabs 'khrungs// ! lung phud drug par don yod dge mtshan che/ /rin chen bstan
pa'i sgang du nyer 'phos nas/ /snyan grags rgyal mtshan 'dzin pa'i bar dag tu/ /bla brang rin chen sgang pa'i gdung zhes grags// ! lung phud bzhi pa kun dga' sa'i thig ler/
/bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan srid rtser sgreng ba'i gnas/ /kun la dga' ba legs pa'i lam ston par/ /lha khang bla brang gdung rabs nyid du mngon/ /!lung phud lnga par kun mkhyen
dga' ba'i zhing / /legs pa'i 'byung gnas byang phyogs dbyig 'dzin mar/ /srid zhi'i bsod nams dpal du byams bstan bar/ /dpe zlas dben pa'i gdungs rabs rin chen phreng
/ /mtshan mchog gsum ldan rtsod bral mkhas grub

rgyun/ /dus gsum mchod pa'i rten gyi bla brang gdung / /rgyal bstan bdag por lhun grub rgyun mi chad/ /dge legs dpal gyi phrin las bla na mtho/ /zhes kyang smras so/ /!gsum
pa gdung rabs de rnams kyi nang nas skabs su babs pa/ gang nyid yum gyi lhums su zhugs pa dang sku ji ltar bltams pa'i tshul ni/ rgyud bla ma las/ ji bzhin yang dag mthong
ba'i phyir/ /skye sogs rnams las 'das gyur kyang / /snying rje'i bdag nyid skye ba dang / /'chi dang na dang rga ba ston/ /zhes gsungs pa bzhin rten rgyal ba bskyed pa'i
yum mchog dam pa bsod nams dpal gyi dbang mo de nyid la/ brten pa 'jam mgon srid zhi'i dpa' bo gang 'dul sgyu ma'i rol rtsed mkhan de lhums zhugs snga rol dang bcas pa'i
ltas bzang ngo mtshar can mang po 'khrungs pa dang / dge mtshan mngon par gsal ba'i ngang nas gzugs sku 'dod 'byung dbang gi rgyal po 'dzam gling bstan 'gro'i dpal mgon
du bzhengs pa'i tshul ni 'di lta lags/ chu yos chu stod tshes lnga'i tho rengs yum gyi mnal ltas su sa skya nas mgron gnyer kun bzang dbang po yin zer ba'i rgya lu chas
la dar dmar thod can zhig nas khyed gdan sar yong dgos zer bar ci yin gsungs pas/ rigs gsum lha khang gi sku gnyer byed dgos yin 'dug zer/ kho mos mchod bshams yang mi shes
pas dgongs zhu mdzod gsung bar de 'dra ma zer sngon nas bskos pa yin pas/ dgongs pa zhu re med zer nas phyag mdud dmar ljang dkar gsum phul zhing / gtsug lag khang de
gang na yod gsungs pas sgrol ma'i gtsug lag khang gi steng na yod zer ba 'khrungs pa'i sang de gnyer tshang ba rnam sras nas 'gro mgon yab yum la sras mo sa skyar 'byon
dgos tshul zhus/ de nas 'byon grabs skabs mnal lam du/ jo bo sku rgyab zer ba'i ri 'gram sher gling zam pa'i thad

nas nor bu yin zer ba'i rdo ba kha dog mi 'dra ba gsum rnyed pas kho mo 'gro ba'i gtsug lag khang der 'bul rgyu yod 'dra dgongs sku hrag tu bsnams pa shar zhing / de dus rigs
gsum lha khang gi sku gnyer mdzad dgos zer ba ni/ rje btsun sa skya pa'i gdung rabs la rigs gsum mgon po'i sprul pa 'byon par sngon gyi mkhas grub du mas bshad cing don
la'ang gnas pa bzhin gdung sras gsum 'byon 'gyur dang / nor bu kha dog mi 'dra ba gsum rnyed pa yang yid bzhin nor bu lta bu'i gdung rabs gsum la'ang sku tshe ring thung
mi 'dra ba gsum 'byung ba'i brda dang / de nas gdan sa'i gzim chung du phebs dgongs mnal lam du/ yab rje ratna'i mtshan can nyid bzhugs khri shin tu mtho bar slob dpon
za hor ma'i chas can sku mdun na nyi zla yod pa shin tu gzi brjid can dang mjal bas maNDal gyi steng du nor bu gsum bcas 'bul gnang dang / sku lus las rnag khrag sogs byung
ba'i mod nas brtse chen lha khang gi sgo 'gag na grwa pa gzugs thams cad mig gis gang ba zhig nas gzhan ma yag po yod ste dga' ldan pa'i dam sri la bcos ka gyis zer ba
zhig 'khrungs shing / bsam yas chos skyong dang ra ba smad chos skyong gnyis kyi lung las/ yul dbus su/ mchod rten khang bu brtsegs pa dang jo dar 'dzugs dgos kyi bka' lung
bzhin gong dkar grub dbang blo gros dbang phyug gis sa dpyad gzigs pas/ sgrol ma lha khang dang jo mo thags ra gnyis yul dbus su ngos 'dzin gyis mchod rten sgrol ma g.yu
mkhar mo'i gtsug lag khang gi rgyab dang / jo dar jo mo thags rar btsugs dus dar shing las yal ga khru gang tsam gsum skyes skad dang / yang sa spre'u dbo zla'i nang
mnal lam du skyed lhas mgon khang yin snyam pa zhig na shing leb la bram gzugs bla brgyud kyi mtshan zhal gyi sngags bcas 'dug pa de sku srung du bcangs

pa dang / yang lo de'i sa ga zla nang gzungs gra lnga thugs las bton pa tshar gnyis 'khrungs pa ni/ rje rdo rje 'chang nyid kyis 'di'i rig gtad gsan pa nas bzung rje btsun
sa skya pa'i gdung rabs rin po che'i srid mtha'i bar du chad med myur byon sku rim la ched du dgongs nas/ gra lnga'i sgrub mchod phye nyis brgya brgal tsam bka' drin bskyangs
te gtso mo lnga'i sgom bzlas chag med rgyun ring mdzad pa dang / 'di rnams kyi lugs sku khri rgyab can gtsug lag khang dang bcas pa dang par sku grangs mang rnams gegs
med mthar phyin bskrun par mdzad rgyu'i mnal ltas shin tu gsal ba so skye'i spyod yul las 'das pa 'di lta bu ni rjes su yi rang gi thal mo spyi bor bca' ba'i 'os so/ /yang
skabs shig yab rje ratna'i mtshan can gyis phun tshogs gling du lha bsangs gnang ba'i mchod dpon yum nyid kyis mdzad nas chos dung rin po che dkar po rgyang grags gsung
bskul dang chabs gcig chos dung nang nas 'phel gdung mang du byon pa yum rang gis bzhes shing lhag ma tshags mdzad pa sogs 'khrungs/ yang gong dkar grub dbang de nyid
la so 'brang gi rjes gnang gsan nas zhag bdun ring bcad brgya'i thog nas de'i sgom bzlas mdzad pa'i mnal lam du/ bud med pad ma chos dpal gyis 'bras snye gsum dang a ru
ra rnam rgyal yin zer ba'i a ru lag mgo tsam zhig phul nas 'bras snye'i 'phros mang mkhar mu gu lung nas yod zer/ de dang dus mtshungs gzim dpon bsod nams mang mkhar chu
zhor la mu gu lung mjal bas de nas gro snye rtsa ba gcig la snye bon gsum re yod pa spar lcag gang tsam phul ba 'di dag la/ phyis su rje rdo rje 'chang gi gsung las/ gnas
gsar rdo rje 'chang las gsung ngag zab mo slob bshad yongs rdzogs thob pa dang myong 'gyur gyi ltas shig yin 'dra gsungs/ yang chu stod tshes bcu'i mnal ltas su yum mchog
nyid phyi skor la phebs pas kun mkhyen sgrub chu'i grog nang na chu

dkar zhing dwangs pa'i khrod nas smyug ma lag ngar tsam zhig rnyed pa'i nang thams cad hUM dkar pos khengs pa dang / yang zla ba de nang ko lcag yin snyam pa'i brag ri mtho
zhing skya chod de ba zhig gi dkyil nas 'khor lo bde mchog zhal sbyor rdo la rang byon 'khrungs pa zhig dang / brag seng nas g.yu'i rdo rje rgya gram dar tshon la gril ba
zhig rnyed pa dang / yang gro bzhin tshes gsum la nam mkha' nas yi ge AHkha ba babs pa ltar byung nas sum mchog nyid kyi phyag gis bzung zhal du gsol ba sogs dang / de
lo lha khang chen mo'i 'obs nang rnams dang lhag par rig 'dzin pho brang gi mdun du 'jam dbyangs me tog thon che ba kun gyi mig lam du snang ba dang / mi rnams kyi'ang da
lo sku gdung zhig byon yod 'dra gleng ba sogs byung zhing / yang skabs shig lha khang rtse'i ga ya dha ra'i bum chu'i drung na byon mur bla ma mchod dpon yin snyam pa zhig
nas bum chu 'di'i bdag po lha mo rig byed ma yin gsung mur bud med dmar mo zhig gis chu zhig zhus pa dang / yang bud med cig gis a ma dgra lha ma'i yin zer ba'i ril dkar
thum dang shel gyi mchod rten rgya phibs can gyi nang shel gyi bum par rigs lnga'i bum chu yin zer nas phul bar shar ba la yang / rje rdo rje 'chang gi gsung las kho bo
rig byed ma'i chos skor la byang chub pa dang dze tA ri'i lugs kyi tshe chog grangs mang byed cing gdung sku mched sogs la 'di'i dbang mang po 'bul thub pa 'dir rtags pa
'dra zhes gsungs/ skabs shig stag mtsher ma'i gangs rtser phebs nas gur dkar nang khri mthon po zhig gi 'gram bud med mang po mchis par/ khri 'dir su bzhugs gsungs pas
'dir bzhugs mkhan phyi lo yong zer nas bza' btung mang po zhus pa dang / gangs rtser dar cog btsugs pa'i mnal ltas shar zhing 'di dang tshul mtshungs par sa yos lo rje rdo
rje 'chang de nyid kyi 'od gsal du stag 'tsher gangs rtser phebs 'dug pa la spang gshongs lha sar 'dra mo zhig na skyes bud med mang po

glu gzhas byed pa zhig 'khrungs pa mthun zhing de dus gangs mchod ljags bsgrigs 'di yang mdzad/ yang lo de'i khrums zla'i nang yab rje bsod nams rin chen kha'ur sman chab la
phebs pa dang chabs gcig skyed lhas mgon khang du sku mtshams zhag bdun dang thug 'dzugs sogs gnang skabs kyi mtshan lam du mchod rten zhig gi logs nas raksha gdong gcig
mang po dang / dung chung rtse gsum rdo rje rnams phyag tu babs pa 'khrungs pa ni gong gi yum mchog dam pa'i mnal ltas dang mthun pa mgon po 'di'i chos skor tshang ma sngon
gyi phyag len dang mthun par rje rdo rje 'chang de nyid kyis gsan bzhes mdzad pa'i mtshan mar gdon mi za'o/ /yang lo de'i nang gong dkar dam pa de nyid kyis bu rdzi
ma'i mdos 'dzugs gnang skabs kyi mnal ltas su de bzhin gshegs pa 'od zhi spos snang dpal dang / bskal bzang sangs rgyas stong / rigs gsum mgon po'i sku rnams gser thang du
bzhengs pas gdung brgyud 'byung gsungs ba bzhin 'phral bzhengs thang ka rnams da lta mkha' spyod lha khang nang bzhugs shing / de dus mdos kyi zas sna'i dkyil du nas ljang
mtho gang tsam skyes pa dang / yang dbyug zla'i nang brdal chu'i bsam 'grub sman skyong gi thad tsam gyi rdo dkyil nas rdo la kye rdor yab yum zhal sbyor yod pa zhig
dang / sgrol mar phebs mur sgrol ma'i phyag mthil nas a ra pa tsa na dhIHzhes pa'i yi ge nas 'bru tsam mang du gzigs pa dang / skyed lhas mgon khang steng gi phyag rdor phug
gi brag khrod nas lcags phur dang rdo la badzra gu ru rang byon 'bur du yod pa zhig dang / yang rje btsun rin po che mjal du phebs 'dun gyi sgo rum ltag nas rdo'i par
bu zhig gi nang na dam rdzas las grub pa'i 'jam dbyangs dmar ser gyi sku tshon gang ba zhig dang / yang chu chen po zhig la mi mang po sgrol 'don mdzad cing chu dkyil nas
dung dkar shin tu che ba cha gcig rnams rnyed pa'i thugs snang dang /

yang yab rje grub dbang nas rgyal zla'i nang btsun mo'i steng du ru mtshon 'dzugs chog skabs 'bras chang dgos phebs par sngar bzo myong med kyang khrung dpon phur pas the tshom
gyi khyogs la 'chang bzhin du btsos pa gnang dus der nas chang shin tu legs pa bas bldabs 'gyur gyi ro dro ba byung ba dang / yang yum mchog nyid la bud med padma chos
dbang yin snyam pa'i btsun ma ral can ras sngon gyon pa zhig nas/ gnam kha'u pa'i bum chur yin zer bum pa legs pa zhig nas chu ser po shin tu dwangs pa dam rdzas kyi ro
bro ba zhig nas mchod cing sku lus bkrus pa dang / yang zla ba de nang zhu lu rgyan gong mgon khang na byon 'dug par bud med cig gis gro sder gang gi nang dung chung gcig
/ba so'i phreng ba dril bu g.yer khas brgyan pa/ rus pa'i rgyan drug cha tshang bcas phul nas lte bsgyur yong bas gnyer gyis zer ba 'khrungs pas rten 'brel khyad zha lu
sku zhang la lte bsgyur 'khor lo zhu gnang dang / sa bya dbo zla'i nang yab rje rdo rje 'chang bsod nams rin chen gyis gzhi thog gzim shar mgon khang du chos skyong gtso
bsdus la yum gyi sku 'khril sku gdung gegs med phebs thub pa'i phrin 'chol bka' drin che skabs/ rdo rje rab brtan ma'i thang sku'i nu ma g.yas nas 'o ma byon 'dug pas mnal
lam dang rtags de rnams la rje rdo rje 'chang chen po'i gsung las/ kho bo la zha lu'i bag chags sad rgyu 'dug pa bzhin der bzhugs/ sgrub dkyil 'gran med dpe hrul sus
kyang nyams gso ma thub pa rnams sde dger par gyi mgo 'dren zhus pa bzhin ring mo zhig nas tshang 'grig tu zha lur phul ba dang / dgon gnas khyad par can de na gso sbyong
sogs 'dul ba'i nam gzhag la 'du skabs chos kyi gaNDi tshad ldan mi 'dug pas na gaNDi tshad ldan yang phul zhing / phan 'gyur snyan sgron yang yang zhu ba sogs phul byung
gi byed pa 'di la brtags pa 'dra/ zhes bka' stsal skabs shig yum mchog nas grub rgyal tshe sgrub zhag bdun mdzad dus spyan ltas su/ 'ja' 'od kyi dkyil nas shel gyi mchod
rten khru

gang ba zhig gi bum dkyil na 'jam dbyangs dmar ser shin tu 'od zer 'phro ba zhig gzigs pa'i mod bud med cig nas sgrol ma la gsol ba btab na 'di yod zer ba bzhin du sgrol ma
'bum ther stsal ba dang / sgrol ma lha khang dang dbu rtser sgrol 'don dang tshe chog 'dzugs gnang skabs tshe gtor gyi dkyil du ljang pa mtho gang tsam skyes shing / mchod
me yang nyin zhag du ma thub pa sogs ngo mtshar bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang / sgrub chen jo mo ba rnams la tshes bcu brgya tshar gnang bas bstan 'dzin klong yangs zer ba'i
mnal ltas su/ bud med mang po zhig gis dngul gyi mchod rten 'od zer shin tu che ba zhig 'ja' sprin gyi dkyil du khyer song ba gang du phyin 'gro snyam pa'i mur btsun
mo'i thog khar babs pa rmis pa dang / gzhan yang btsun mo'i rtsa bar khyi rnams kyi phrug gu skye tshang 'cha' ba dang / byi bla 'khyams po zhig gi phrug tu sgam khri'i 'og
tu skyes pa gnyis nag po gcig /dkar po stag ris can du byung ba dang / bu rdzi ma'i rten rdzas ma mo nag mo zhig smon bder mchis par pho lug dkar po skyi dkar can sogs
btsas pa dang / rdzong skor ba'i bus pa rnams btsun mo'i gdong du nyin re bzhin tshogs te gzhas byed pa sogs nang gi ngo mtshar phyi rol du gsal ba'i rten 'brel phun sum
tshogs pa ma bcos lhun grub tu byung ba dang / sa bya nag zla sngon ma'i tshes bcu mchod pa mdzad dus tshogs chang lud/ dpal gtor dngos grub tshul du de skor nas myangs
bas bu ram gyi ro 'dra ba byung gsungs pa ni de dus ma zad phyis su'ang rgyal yum de nyid nas tshes bcu gnang ba'i gtor ma kha shas la ro de bzhin dang / tshogs chang lud
pa lan cig tsam byung zhes rje rdo rje 'chang nyid kyis bka' stsal zhing / de'i nam phyed tsam nas 'khrungs ran grabs kyi mnal ltas su/ mi pho mo sna tshogs gzabs 'chor
gyis sa skya'i phyi skor la 'gro zhing badzra gu ru/ rigs gsum mgon po'i gzungs rnams gdangs dang bcas byed mur rgyal yum nyid gzim yod snyam pa las padma chos dpal gyis
phyag nas

'then te yar bzhengs bcug nas da lam gyi bu chung 'di la bzang po mchog tu thogs shig zer ba 'khrungs pa sogs te/ stod 'grel skad du zhi bar 'bod cing / drug cu'i lo khams
dang sbyar ba'i sa mo bya lo/ skar rtsis dpyid 'bring gi zla ba'am lugs gcig na dpyid thar 'dod pa/ hor lugs mA yol du 'bod cing / rgyu skar nag pas nya ba/ ston pas dus
'khor shrI dhA nya ka Ta kar gsungs pa'i dus chen gyi zla ba nyis brtsegs kyi dang po'i tshes bcu gcig /dga' ba gsum pa/ dbyangs ha yig /khams nam mkha'/ 'dod yon sgra/ na
tshod byis pa/ gsal byed nThAM/ nyi ma byi ba/ rten 'brel reg pa spar kha dwa/ sme ba lnga ser/ res gza' nyi bu/ res skar skag ste gza' skar khams 'phrad lang tsho sbyor
ba/ 'phrod chen yid dang ldan pa'i nyi shar tatkAl e Da ka'i dus su nam mkha' 'ja' 'od kyis gang ste btsun mor zug pa dang / me tog gi char nyil ba sogs bkra shis pa'i
dge mtshan dpag tu med pa dang ldan pa'i ngang nas yum la gnod pa med par gzugs sku'i dkyil 'khor bde ba nyid du bltam par gyur to/ /de dag gi don bsdu na/ sngon tshe skabs
gsum 'chi med bkangs nas/ /tshe dus lta nyon sems can lnga bdo'i mgon/ /mche ba drug ldan thal dkar gnyis 'thung ni/ /rnam lnga'i gzigs pas sgyu 'phrul lhums zhugs su/
/dge mtshan don kun 'grub pa'i ltas mtshar po/ /snang srid khyon la rdzogs pa'i go skabs bral/ /de lta'i rmad byung dpal la co 'dri ba'i/ /ngo mtshar khong nas 'dzum pa'i
ku su maH /dbus 'gyur 'chang nas brgya phrag dpag tshad kyis/ /bskal pa'i rnam snang pho brang gnyis pa'i ljongs/ /dbyig 'dzin dga' tshal skyed byed ma ma'i ltor/ /'phos
'phral ya mtshan gsar ba'i phyi nang gi /rten cing 'brel 'byung ra yig gnyis pa'i glu/ /ltar snang gcam bu'i 'gyur khugs dang bral nas/ /yang dag don gyi gtam snyan kha
lo ba/ /gnas skabs de las gzhan du ma 'gyur

bar/ /gcig min yang yang rtse ba'i 'byung 'gyur gyi/ /phan bde'i nyi ma 'jig rten kun gsal ba'i/ /dkyil 'khor dbang phyogs sa 'dzin do ker rtser/ /nyes bral bstan 'gro'i dpal
du e ma ho/ /zhes kyang smras so// // ! gsum pa 'khrungs ma thag nas dgung grangs bcu gcig yan sku gzhon nu'i dus kyi ngo mtshar mdzad pa'i cha rnams lo khams ma 'khrul
bar go rim bzhin du ston pa la/ thog mar lo mgo 'dzin tshul yang lugs mang du 'byung ste/ rags tsam brjod na/ dpal dus kyi 'khor lo dang mdo sde gser 'od dam pa sogs nas
yar ngo sngon 'gro'i nag zla lug khyim dang / mchims sogs 'dul 'dzin sngon ma rnams khrums zla'i tshes bcu drug nas dang / shAkya shrI sogs 'dul 'dzin kha cig tha skar
zla ba'i tshes bcu drug nas dang / 'dul 'dzin phyi ma rnams smin drug zla ba'i tshes bcu drug nas dang / khyung dang phug lugs sogs nag rtsis pa dang 'jig rten yongs grags
rnams mgo zla'i tshes gcig nas dang / bod rgyal po'i rjes su 'brangs pa rnams bde mchog rdo rje mkha' 'gro'i rgyud las/ dgun zla 'bring po nas brtsams te/ /nyi ma byang
du bgrod pa'i dus/ /zla ba rnam pa bcu gnyis ni/ /rim ni rim pa bzhin du bzhag /ces gsungs pa dang bstun dgun zla 'bring po rgyal zla ba nas dang nag rtsis pa kha cig kyang
de bzhin/ hor lugs dang nag rtsis pa kha cig gso dpyad pa rnams rta zla nas dang / mdo lugs pa kha cig dbo zla nas lo mgo 'dzin pa sogs rnam grangs mang yang / rang lugs
bod rgyal po'i rjes su 'brangs te rgyal zla nas 'dzin pa'i dbang du zhus nas/ de ltar skye dgu'i bsod nams kyi bgo skal du rnyed pa'i dgos 'dod ma lus pa 'bad med du
'byung ba'i gzugs sku 'dod 'byung dbang gi rgyal po de nyid ni/ 'khrungs ma thag nas sku lta bas chog mi shes pa gzi brjid dang dpal mngon par 'bar zhing sku bskyed che ba/
rang bzhin bzang bas byis skad 'byin pa sogs

ye mi mnga' ba khong yangs shing dkyil che ba zhig ste/ 'khrungs 'phral ljags steng du dri bzang gi phye mas dhIHpar rje btsun rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i sin dkyil ltar 'debs
par mdzad de mi 'bral ba'i sku bsrung dang sku khrus gtang rag 'bul ba sogs gang ci'i mtshams yab rje ratna'i mtshan can nyid kyis bka' drin bskyangs/ gzhon nur gyur pa de
nyid nyin mtshan phal cher 'od gsal gyi ngang du mnyam gzhag kho nas dus 'da' bar mdzad cing phyag zhabs brkyang bskum tsam yang cher mi gnang bas/ sku sha'i hrag rnams
la rul g.ya' zug pa sogs kyi skabs yum mchog sku 'khor sogs tshang ma 'di 'dra ni rdo rje 'chang gi bzhugs stangs rang yin 'dug /ces gleng bar mdzad/ skabs 'ga' chab zho
bzhes mur zhal gyi sgor skya nyog ge 'khyil ba'ang thugs dran gsal ba dang / sku de ni shin tu zhal lor 'du ba zhig snang bas sras rdzi rgan mo bkra shis rab mdzes zer ba
des/ bla ma 'dis bdag skyid du bcug ces yang yang bsngags brjod kyi me tog 'thor/ mdzod pa bka' bzhi pas/ zhabs brtan bden tshig la snga ba ngag la dbang bsgyur ma stsal
ba'ang spyir tshig sgra legs shing khyad par thugs kyi bzhed don 'gyur med zhabs brtan shog gsung ba 'di/ phyis su'ang rje rdo rje 'chang chen po'i gsung las/ 'di nged
rang la gzhan las rten 'brel dge ba yin 'dug ces gsung bar mdzad/ yab rje rdo rje 'chang bsod nams rin chen gyi zhal snga nas tshe dbang byabs khrus sogs yang yang stsal
ba dang / mtshan yang ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams grags pa blo gros zhes mnga' gsol stsal bas/ mi rnams mtshan 'di la dpags nas sngags 'chang grags pa blo gros kyi rnam
sprul du gleng yab rje rdo rje 'chang gis zhal bzhes rang ni ma mdzad 'dra/ 'on kyang min pa'ang ma grub la/ yab rje mchog nas smin byed kyi dbang gi thog ma dpal gsang
ba 'dus pa 'phags lugs ras dkyil gyi steng nas bka' drin che ba dang / gur lha brgyad kyi rjes gnang dus

btsun mo'i rab gsal gyi bya gdang khar bya rog cig babs nas skad snyan sgrogs shing rjes gnang zhu mi rnams la lta ba'ang thugs la shin tu gsal ba dang / brdal chur yab rje
nyid chab zhugs shig gi skabs pu tras bskur byung gsung ba'i rdo gri ka to'i dbyibs can logs la las mkhan gyi bla rdo pha wang long bu kha shas 'byar ba zhig rje rdo rje
'chang nyid la stsal ba phyis su nang so nyams gso'i dus pu tra'i gzungs la phul bar grags/ gzhan yang 'khrungs lo der thugs dran gsal ba'i rnam thar ngo mtshar can 'di
lta byung ste/ skabs shig btsun mo'i thab tshang sgo 'gag byang de nas shar gzigs la bla ma rab byung ba bgres po zhig gis dbang gnang ba'i dril lce la phyag gis 'tham pa
zhig thugs dran gsal ba/ phyis su gzhan dag la bka' 'dri gnang bas gong dkar grub dbang de nyid yin par gleng ba dang / yang btsun mo'i steng gi g.yab gog nyams can de'i
logs bris la lha sku mdog khro bo zhig gzigs pa'ang phyis su khyung khra yin pa dang / de dus nub phyogs la khebs shig yod pa de'i srubs nas gzigs pas mi gzugs phra rid
khyom me ba lnga tsam gar byed pa gzigs pa/ de skabs g.yul thang na gu ge chos rgyal bzhugs dus te 'khrungs lo sa bya'i lo rgyus rags tsam dang// // ! dgung grangs gnyis
pa lcags khyi lor dga' ston gyi mdos chen gzabs spras gnang ba'i skor zhib gsal ma mchis shing / 'on kyang / chos khri thang mo che'i mtha' skor lcags ri shar nub sgor nyis
hral gnyis sogs 'phral phug brling mdzes kyi nyams gso bgyis pa dang / dus mdos gzabs ma'i 'chams chas sgros gtsang 'di rnams thog mar gyon nas mdzad dus de nyid yin 'dug
cing / phur sgrub skabs shig rje rdo rje 'chang nyid sras rdzi'i rgyab la gdan drangs te btsun mo'i thog steng byang de na mchis dus/ thugs snang la lha sar 'dra mo zhig
na keng rus 'chams byed pa

gzigs pa ni dur khrod bdag po'i 'chams mdzad pa de dang / yang 'chams sku yin dgongs pa de 'dra lho gzigs la 'byon pa'i gyon mi rnams kyis stag lhwam bsam yas chos skyong gi
zhabs 'chags 'dra ba gyon pa dang / yang gzim chung lho'i glo skar de nas gzigs pas 'khris kyi grong ba dpon to pa'i mthongs khung lho der gra ba mgo med cig 'gul 'gul
byed pa'i gzigs snang rnams kyang thugs dran gsal ba ste dgung grangs gnyis pa'i lo rgyus dang // // ! dgung grangs gsum pa lcags phag lor zhabs kyis bcags pa las gog po
'gog pa sogs mi mdzad cing / gsung 'byon pa'i thog ma yang rje btsun 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi gzungs a ra pa tsa na dhIHzhes bod skad du 'gro ba smin par byed pa'i blor 'gyur
ba de nyid gsungs shing / tshul 'di ni sngon dus mi thub zla ba'i rnam sprul slob dpon rin po che bsod nams rtse mo 'khrungs ma thag /kho bo ni byis pa'i spyod pa las 'das
pa'o/ /zhes lan gnyis gsum bstud mar gsungs pa dang mtshungs pas/ gzur gnas dam pa rnams rnam thar 'di kho nas kyang thugs dad dbang med du 'khrungs par 'gyur lags/ de
skabs yum mchog la snyun gzhi thu mo zhig bzhes dus de'i sku rim mdzad nyams kyis/ btsun mo'i thab tshang de them pa shin tu mtho yang de la brten bcas nas sku stod phyir
rmyang mdzad de them phyir ja shog ser po ling ga'i tshul bgyis/ hU~M mdzad phyag rgya bca' ba'i stangs ka byang chub mchog rgya 'dra ba gnang ste/ sangs rgyas kyi bka'
bden pa dang zhes sogs gsung mur dgug gzhug gi rnam pas shog bu bzhes te thab sgor sreg par mdzad pas yum mchog kyang myur du snyun las grol ba sogs ngo mtshar grub pa'i
mtshan mar gzhan dring mi 'jog pa ni de dus nas ka mnga' zhing / sku'i na bza' yang dkar dmar gnyis las gzhan mi bzhes pa ni/ slad nas rab byung dang sngags 'chang gnyis
char rim pas mdzad dgos pa'i lkog

gyur rjen gzigs kyi brdar mngon zhing / re zhig gzi khra'i bgo ba legs pa zhig phul bas shin tu ma dgyes pa'i rnam pas gtan nas ma bzhes/ de skabs tsam nas bzung mi 'di dang
'di zhes bya bas bya ba 'di dang 'di byed kyi gnad thams cad mkhyen cing / so so'i lad mo rnams kyang dbyibs dang rnam 'gyur gyis mtshon chos 'jig rten gyi bya ba phal
cher thugs kyi bang mdzod du bzhugs pa'i sgo dang po'ang 'di tsam nas dod de/ 'di 'dra'i mi dran dgu dran gyi mkhyen rab mnga' ba'i bla ma zhig ang / zhes gleng mi'ang mang
po byung skad dang / de nas brtse chen lha khang nyams gso byang bskyed skabs yab sras nas grub mtshan ston bzhed kyis kun rdzob tu klu zhig gnod pa'i zol gyis sku dkyil
phar cher shu 'thor gyis lums pas/ yab rje'i gsung las/ ar po byed bzhin pa 'di'i rtsig sked tsam na rdo sgam 'dra ba zhig la gnas pa'i sa bdag gnod pas de phab la dkyil
khang du klu mkhar bcos te de'i nang du chug gsungs pa bzhin bgyis pas sku'i shuu ba'ang rim gsos su gyur/ phyis rje rdo rje 'chang chen po'i gsung las/ de skabs phun
tshogs gling gi bzhugs g.yab tu byug sman spyi dang dres thag mer sbyangs kyi thal sman byugs pas bzod glags med pa'i tsha zug 'khrungs kyang phyag zhabs gzing gzing tsam
las gsung ye mi shor ba'i dam bca' mdzad/ ces gsungs/ lo de'i ril sgrub 'dam la yab rje'i phyag bzo phag gzugs chung ngu zhig sku srung du stsal ba nas phyis su 'og gdon
gyi gnod pa phal cher des bsrungs thub byung zhes gsungs/ de'i tshe brtse chen lha khang du thar rtse rjes gsung bskang gnang ba dang / bka' dbang zhig la rdor le mda' gzhu'i
'khor lo bskor ba bya gsungs ba zhig thugs mtshor 'jags pas 'jigs byed dug dbang bskur tshig cig la rdo rje mda' gzhu'i zer ba 'dra ni med dam gang ltar de 'dra zhig
thugs la gsal po 'dug gsungs/ yang skabs shig

tshogs khang gral gdan mang po can zhig na khro 'bag ka bar sbrags pa gcig dang / yang nam zir yin dgongs pa zhig la sras rdzi'i rgyab tu phebs te yum mchog dang a lce drung
zung bcas gtsug lag khang sgo shar bstan steng na seng ge dang / mda' na rdo bcal dbus su shing sdong can khyi skad lhang lhang 'byin pa zhig tu phebs pa'ang thugs dran
gsal zhing / slad nas brtags tshe ci yin ni ngo ma gsal/ de tsam la gong dkar rnam grangs dpon slob bcu phrag nas mdos sogs sku rim mdzad skabs yin pas lha chen lcags sgo'i
shar tsam na king ki Ni'i 'chams pas ling gar me mda' rub rgyag gi skad 'dra ba gsan pa dang / de nas gzhi thog gsang sngags pho brang gzim chung mda' phug can du bya
khra ma'i shar brgyud de phebs shing / ring min nas yab rje ratna'i mtshan can gyis tshoms dmar du zho 'bras stsal ba/ dung mkhan ye shes rgyal mtshan gyis chos dung rin
po che gsung bskul bgyis pa dang / de dus gling dpon mo dang dpon slob 'byung gnas kyi dngos 'bul rnams thugs dran shin tu gsal bar 'khrungs pa dang / yang zhabs phyi zhig
gi rgyab tu sku rin po che gdan 'dren gyis nang so'i mgon khang mjal bar mdzad pas/ zangs chen bkra shis 'od 'bar gyi mtsho la mthongs khung nas nyi ma shar ba lta bu'i
'od chen po zhig gzigs pa'ang phyis su zhib 'jug mdzad pas de 'dra yong don ye mi mnga' bas zangs chen gyis mtshon nang so rten brten par zhabs tog mthar phyin du 'grub
pa'i rten 'brel bla na med pa'ang de dus nas rang 'grig dang / de nas gsang sngags pho brang du bzhugs skabs 'di yin med pa'i snyun gzhi bying nge ba zhig bzhes pas sman
bcos rim gro spyi dang / yab rje mchog nas tshe dbang ljags chu sogs gang 'tshams bka' drin che yang bskyed ma bzhes pa'i tshul gyis gzim mal du bzhugs skabs gzim chung
phug mar

dbu sngas byang bstan steng bla bre padma 'dab brgyad bkra shis rdzas rtags kyi ri mo can zhig dang / nyin cig gzim mal drung yab yum zhabs phyi 'ga' dang bcas bzhugs mur dar
cig ljags dbugs kyi rgyu ba chad cing spyan yang btsum ste dgongs pa chos dbyings su mnyam par bzhag mur snyan khung g.yon na mar i ri ri zer ba'i sgra zhig yun ring gsan

/ skyes bu dam pa'i khyad par gyi chos tshe sems yo byad las skye ba rdzu 'phrul sogs la mnga' brnyes pa'i brda ni 'di lta bu'o zhes ston par mdzad pa yin grang / de skabs
kyi i ri ri zer ba'i sgra de yab rje mchog nas tshe gzungs ljags bzlas kyi cha bsnyan khung du blugs pa dang / khra gsal gyis gzigs dus thugs dran gsos pa yin 'dug /ces
phyis su yang yang bka' stsal/ rim gyis snyun las grol tshul bzhes te yab rje mchog nas yongs rdzogs bstan pa rin po che'i nyams len 'jigs bral stobs kyi mgon po dpal ldan

can gyi steng nas stsal ba'i zhal slob kyi dbus su rje rdo rje 'chang nyid kyang yum gyi sku pang du phebs te gsan bzhes mdzad do// // ! dgung grangs bzhi pa chu byir sngags

pa

gtan nas mi mdzad pas thugs sgam zhing des pa'i sgo dang po'ang 'di tsam nas dod cing / lo der mdzod 'dzin bsod nams shin tu bro 'tshal bas nyin gcig rje rdo rje 'dzin chen
po nyid gdan 'dren gyis phyag dbang skabs rje nyid la hor shel gyi phreng ba sogs phul/ mi ring bar mdzod pa de dus las yol bar gang gi yab rje nyid thugs ngal che tshul
gyi skabs rje nyid kyis thugs gso zhabs brtan gsol 'debs sogs zhu gnang dang khong 'das dus phur bzlog glo bur ba de'i gdab las nyi ma bzhud la khad byung ba'i ling ga'i
g.yas ngos su 'ug pa kho skya log ge yod pa dang / gdab kha dngos dpal 'bar gyi 'od la mdzad pa sogs thugs dran gsal por 'khrungs pa dang / yab rjes stsal ba'i rakSha'i
phyag phreng der shin tu gtsigs chen gyis de la kI la ya/ hrIHShtI/ pakShiM rnams rang byung du bzla bar mdzad pa dang / gzhan yang gzigs snang la dpal mgon zhal dang pu
tra lcam sring dur khrod bdag po bsam yas chos skyong a tsa ra mi nag sogs 'dug gsungs pa lan cig min pa yang yang rgyal yum mchog la bka' stsal zhing / gtsug lag khang 'ga'
zhig gi ming nas smos te 'di na 'di yod gsung pa'i bka' yang yang yum mchog la stsal ba dang / de mtshams shig nas gzim shar bde chen 'od gsal du phebs/ gzhi dgon bum
'dzin byams pa rab brtan bzang po sngar nas yang yang 'byon mu des bzhugs g.yab shar du rnam 'joms/ seng gdong sngon mo/ gur/ khro bcu'i rjes gnang sogs gnang / bla ma de
rwa lo'i rnam sprul nyams rtogs can yin gsungs kyang rje rdo rje 'chang nyid kyi de dus gzigs snang la/ rje grol mchog gi dbu bla rgya sgom legs pa rgyal mtshan gyi sku
'dra bzhin gzigs shing / khong dpon g.yog gis/ gang la ser sna ma gdangs ma brjid che ba zhig mdzad pas de la rje nyid thugs shin tu 'dzin pa zhig 'khrungs/ de dag gis

kyang rje nyid la 'di nga'i bla ma yin zhes thugs mnyes po dpe bral du mdzad/ skabs shig 'od gsal du gzim shar dpe khri'i logs la spre'u chen po mi tshad tsam zhig gar byed
pa dang / yang lan cig mi gnyis gri ring khyer nas rje nyid la mtho 'tshams bgyid tshul 'khrungs pa 'di dag kyang mdo las/ rin chen chos kyang dkon la rtag tu 'tshe ba'ang
mang / /zhes gsungs pa ltar bar chad kyi ngo zhig yin na'ang yab rje sogs dam pa gong ma'i thugs rje dang rje nyid kyi thugs bskyed kyis nyer 'tshe mi mngon dbyings su
yal/ de tsam la yum mchog bstan 'dzin bsod nams bzang mo de gra pa bgres po 'dra ba zhig res 'ga' rtser bzhugs nyir byon te rje nyid la thugs lhag par brtse nyams mdzad
pa rnams thugs kyi dpal be'ur yang dag par mnga' ba lags// // ! dgung grangs lnga pa chu glang lo tsam la 'od gsal gyi ngang duu sa skya ma btab gong gi lung pa 'di'i dbyibs
rnams gzigs nas/ 'dir ma 'ongs pa na dpal ldan sa skya zhes pa'i dgon chen zhig yong rgyu yin dgongs pa thugs la 'khrungs pa dang / slob dpon 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis
sems can zhig dmyal ba nas bton pa dang / sa chen/ rtse mo/ chos rje khu dbon te bzhi lhan cig tu gzigs pa dang / rje btsun rin po che mnyam bzhag gi phyag rgya can la mchod
pa'i lha mos mchod pa 'bul ba sogs lan gnyis gsum mi 'dra bar 'khrungs pa ste klu sgrub dang rje btsun gong ma lnga'i zhal de dus ka gzigs shing de lo chos khri thang
mo cher gser zangs kyi rgya phibs gnang ngo // // ! dgung grangs drug pa shing stag gi ston rje btsun a Ni drung gis mgon po'i sku mtshams grol ba'i sbyin sreg tshoms dmar
du gnang skabs drag yol 'gang dkar ma bkram pa gzigs pas/ 'di 'dra'i yol ba'i rnam dpyod ang dgongs pa 'khrungs byung gsung ba ni phyis su'ang drag yol der gtsigs chen
mdzad skabs thos lags/ de lo thugs la dgyes pa'i sngar gyi bu rdzi

bkra shis rab mdzes chu nad kyis mnar bas de mi 'tsho bar mkhyen te gan du yang yang thebs pas rgan mo bsam pa rdzogs/ de 'das pa gsan pas dam pa rnams ni byas pa shes shing
drin du gzo ba yin pas na/ spyan chab kyi rnam pa mdzad cing snying rje'i kun slong bsam gyis mi khyab pa 'khrungs/ de tshab dpal rtse sde pas zhabs 'gyur hur bskyed kyis
zhus kyang phyis su de nyid la bar chad zhugs nas gdan sa chen po dang ha cang 'brel chags pa ma byung bar gleng zhing gnas gsar rje phebs theng gnyis pa'i skabs so//
// ! dgung grangs bdun pa shing yos snron zla'i yar tshes dge zhing bkra shis pa'i tshes brgyad kyi nyin sku yon gyi thog ma/ thon mi sambho Tas/ bslab pa kun gyi gzhi 'dzin
cing / /rig byed smra ba rnams kyi rgyu/ /ming tshig brjod pa kun gyi gzhi/ /yi ge'i sbyor ba bshad par bya/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar gyi don dang ldan pa'i kA li ljags klog
gi dbu 'dzugs rgyu'i snga dro sgo rum gzim spyil dkar po dang / dbu rtse rnying ma'i 'jam dbyangs gzi 'od 'bar ba mjal bar phebs pas bse mgon chen po'i sku mdun gyi sa
stegs steng nas rgya khab gzhan las pa ldabs kyis ring ba zhig /bse mgon yid bzhin gyi nor bus bslu med rten 'brel gyi che bas stsol bar mdzad pa'ang / rje btsun 'jam pa'i
dbyangs kyi mtshan la rdo rje rnon por gsungs pa bzhin rje nyid kyi mkhyen rab sU tse'i rtse mo ltar rno bar 'gyur ro/ /zhes gsungs pa'i lung bstan du gor ma chag pas
khab de'ang rgyun ring gi bar thugs tshags mdzad cing / yab rje mchog nas ka phreng sogs 'bul gnang skabs tshegs med du mkhyen pa sogs thugs rab kyi bdag por mnga' gsol
gyi sgo dang po'ang 'di nas dod de/ ji skad du/ chos kyi ma mo ma bslabs thugs su chud/ /ces pa'i gras su bzhugs shing / de skabs yab rje mchog gis mtshon legs so'i rten
'byung gras gra tog gser gsum gyi glegs bam phyag tu son pa ni/ rgyal ba'i bka' mdo rgyud dgongs

'grel man ngag dang bcas pa'i bdag por 'gyur ba'i 'bad med lhun grub kyi rten 'brel du gdon mi za bas rje rdo rje 'chang nyid kyang 'di la de dus ka rten 'brel dge ba zhig
yin nam dgongs pa 'khrungs pa don gnas su shes ldan gzur gnas kun gyis mkhyen gsal ltar lags/ zhag shas nas gnas slob bzod pa bkra shis kyis/ sku zhabs rin po cher thugs
brel gyi stabs gdung brgyud rin po cher sku yon kho bos zhabs 'gyur zhus na gsung ba bzhin la de bzhin gyi zhal bzhes stsal bas bzhugs g.yab shar du sger mchod gnang ste/
rten khri der brten bcas sgros ldan chung ngu dang / rig 'dzin bla brgyud sman thang ba'i phyag bris ma 'grems par mdzad de snga dro thugs gnyer phur sgrub sogs khyug tsam
gyis bde blag tu khong du chud/ de nas yab rje mchog gis sgrub thabs brgya rtsa'i rjes gnang re dang / sa skya bka' 'bum ljags lung thun re/ phyi dro skyor sbyangs phran
bu re mdzad/ 'di tsam zhig la re zhig rje rdo rje 'chang nyid a lce drung zung bcas gnas bcur bzhugs skabs shig rje nyid kyi rdzu 'phrul gyis spos kyi red bu zhig zhal
bar btsugs steng sku lus kyi lcid reng bur bkal te bzhugs pas sku mched zung ha las par gyur ba'i tshe ci yang ma gsungs shig bka' stsal/ ces a Ni drung 'di'i gsung las
yang yang thos so// // ! dgung grangs brgyad du phebs pa me 'brug lor phur sgrub kyi thugs 'dzin rnams sngon du song nas thog mar phebs shag mdzad kyang / yab rje mchog nas
phur sgrub chugs nyer sgo rum du brtag sgril mdzad pas ma 'thon pa ni/ de lo lha chen khyam stod ag glen nam ang lan ka brgyad kyi ya gyal gsum nyen gcong dogs gnas gang
yang med bzhin du hor zla bdun pa'i tshes bcu gsum nyin glo bur rdib gzhom byung bas/ thog ma'i la nyer de ltar mi rung ba 'phur shes ma hA kA las dgongs te ma gnang bar
'khums so/ /de tsam nas bzung sngags 'chang chos

kyi rgyal pos mdzad pa'i brag rdzong ma mchan bu bcas thugs la zin nas zhal 'don chag med kyis nyin ltar yi ge bdun ma sogs stong phrag re dang / sngags 'chang dang a mes zhabs
kyi sku bstod shlo ka re brgya tshar chag med 'don par mdzad/ de nas yab rje mchog sku 'khor rags bsdus bcas gzhis rtser rgyal ba yab sras mi'i dbang po bcas zhal rgyas
thog mjal phyag bka' drin che ba nas/ smin drug zla nang gdan sar phebs skabs kyi bca' sgrig rnams sngar srol bzhin mdzad de/ rje rdo rje 'chang nyid a lce drung thung
bcas nas bla brang zam sner phebs bsu/ mjal dar bstar ba/ byin rlabs zhu ba sogs mdzad nas rim gyis gzim chung du dga' spro'i dpal la longs spyod par gnang / mi ring bar
kun rdzob ltar snang du beg ge'i snyun lci ba 'dogs bcas bzhes gnang skabs yab rje mchog nas bka' dbang rjes gnang byabs khrus ljags chu sku glud rdzong chog sogs mdzad
pas gegs med snyun las grol ba'i tshul bzhes so// // ! dgung grangs dgur phebs pa me sbrul lor rje nyid kyis/ /dpal sa skya pa'i yab chos gras khro bo'i rgyal po phyag na
rdo rje 'byung po 'dul byed kyi ljags bsnyen zla gcig dbang khang smin grol bde chen du grangs bsnyen mthar phyin mdzad skabs lho phyogs nas 'di yin med pa'i sgra phir
mang po zhig dang / 'od 'khyug 'khyug byung bas ci yin dgongs rab gsal der gzigs pas sprin nag gi khrod na gur lha brgyad yongs rdzogs bya nag thams cad kyi kha na sgog nyag
re re thogs pa zhig 'khrungs/ gzhan yang rje btsun rin po che gzigs snang byung ba'i tshul 'bum thang ldebs bris la gsal ba bzhin dang / de lo skyabs mgon mthu stobs
dbang phyug nyid phun gling du thog mar phebs skabs drung 'khor gyis gzhas sogs bsu ba dang / skabs shig thar rtse rdo rje 'chang nam mkha' bsam grub nas yab yum sku mched
bcas la tshe dbang zhig

stsal dus/ tshe bum zan grub ma de las 'chi med tshe chu'i rgyun dngos su phebs pa'ang yab rje mchog la nyung ngu/ rje rdo rje 'chang nyid la mang tsam/ 'jam mgon gcung rin
po che dang yum mchog drung la gtan nas ma byon pas phyis kyi rten 'brel yang de ltar du gyur cing / de dus tshe dpag med lha dgu'i sgo nas 'chi bslu dang rjes 'brel gyi
bka' dbang thog me tog dkyil 'khor la 'bul gnang skabs kyang yab rje'i de sangs rgyas tshe dpag med la babs/ rje rdo rje 'chang nyid kyi de rin chen tshe dpag med la babs/
'jam mgon gcung dam pa dang yum mchog drung gi de gzhal yas khang nang du lhung tsam byung zhing / gur khro bcu dang zhal bsnyen dus kyi rjes gnang yang gsan/ yang thar
rtse rdo rje 'chang nyid nas yab rjer sgrol dkar/ rje nyid la dbyangs can lha mo/ /gcung dam par zhal sgrub dus kyi thang ka bcas stsal ba'ang brtags shing dpyad na/ yab
rje mchog la sku tshe bsring thabs sgo gang zab mdzad dgos pa dang / rje rdo rje 'chang nyid shes bya'i dkyil 'khor la sgra dbyangs lha mo lta bu'i mkhyen rab rgyas par
'gyur ba dang / gcung dam pa nyid la gnyan mgon zhal bzhi pa shin tu 'go zhing 'ches pas na de nyid bsten sgrub kyis phrin 'chol dgos pa'i brda yang dag pa rnams rtsa ba'i
bla ma dam pa gang nas lkog gyur rjen ston du gor ma chag go/ // ! dgung grangs bcu pa sa rtar dbang khang phu'i mgon khang srid gsum zil gnon du lha mchog rdo rje gzhon
nu'i dus grangs kyi ljags bsnyen kha skong sbyin sreg bcas mthar phyin du bka' drin che zhing / thun dbar la yab rje mchog nas sa skya bka' 'bum gyi ljags lung dang /
de lo sgrol ma g.yu mkhar mo'i steng gi dri gtsang khang 'di nyid rten brten pa bcas gang gi yab rje nas gsar bskrun mdzad pa'ang yum mchog nyid phebs gong gi mnal lam de
nyid lkog gyur rjen gsal du

mngon no// // ! dgung grangs bcu gcig tu phebs pa sa lug lor kha'u sman chab skabs mar lam skyed lhas su rgyab ri'i brag grum phyir 'phen na rung min zhus skabs yab rje mchog
gi bka' las/ nged rang nas rab gnas bgyis na mi skyon zhes gsungs te/ yab sras zhal rgyas nas phyag nas mdzad pas da lta'i bar du'ang ma lhung ba ling nge yod pa 'di yin
par gleng zhing / de nas gzhi thog pho brang gi shar brgyud nyen ches pas zhig gso mdzad skabs rje rdo rje 'chang nyid a lce drung zung bcas la bzhugs gnas shing gsar
bskrun gyi gyang ldebs dang shing bsgrigs sogs la tshon dang mthing zhal sogs grub bstun/ yab rje mchog nas gur lcam dral dang zhal gyi thugs 'dzugs dang / gnas slob nas
gdugs dkar rgyal mtshan 'dzugs chog gnang zhing / nang du nyer mkho'i yo byad rnams 'grig rjes rje rdo rje 'chang nyid kyis sku yon gyi rim pa spyi dang / bye brag rgyal
sras lam bzang sogs thugs 'dzin mdzad do/ /de dag gi don bsdu na/ 'jam mgon gzhon nur gyur pa'i 'khri shing gang / /rgyal sras spyod pa'i yal 'dab gsar bu'i dus/ /bag chags
bzang po zab brling gting tshugs pas/ /byis spyod dri bzhon ngal te gshin rjer bros/ /'khrungs ma thag nas dran pa'i lcags kyu yis/ /skyed byed dang bcas mi ngas gnyis
'thung snar/ /btab ste snying rje'i yul du rjes bzung nas/ /rdo rje ri bo'i gtos kyi rnam thar bskyangs/ /yon tan kun gzhi kA li nas brtsams te/ /brda tsam mod du bde blag
thugs chud pas/ /ma bslab kun mkhyen mi 'gyur mkhas pa'i gtam/ /skyengs te sngon byung rdzu la brten par nges/ /gaml-i ma hA kA las dngos grub mtshon/ /rdo rje rnon por
gsal 'debs dam bsgos shing / /dngos nyams gzigs snang ngang du bde stong gi /ye shes mchog gi ro yis thugs rgyud gtams/ /ma bcos lhun grub dam pa'i

gshis lugs la/ /byas shes drin gzo'i ri mo bsub tu bral/ /rgyal dang rgyal sras mchog gi rnam thar ni/ /lha rigs gzhon nu'i thugs kyi rgya mtshor 'khyil/ /zhes kyang smras
so// // ! rtsa ba'i sa bcad bzhi pa khams gsum chos kyi rgyal po'i gser khri rin po cher dbang bskur te bstan pa dang 'gro ba'i phan bde rlabs po che spel tshul la/ khams
gsum chos kyi rgyal po'i gser khri rin po cher mnga' gsol ba dang / bstan 'gro'i phan bde spel tshul rnams lo khams dang sbyar te bshad pa gnyis las/ dang po ni/ skye ba
gzhan du sbyangs pa dang / /mkhas pa du ma bsten pa dang / /rnam par dpyod pa'i blo gros kyis/ /shes bya kun la 'jigs med thob/ /ces gsungs pa ltar/ nges pa'i don du rje
btsun 'jam pa'i dbyangs las gud na ma mchis kyang / rnam par mi nas mir gyur ba'i skye ba nyi shu rtsa lngar de nyid kyis rjes su bzung bas shes bya rig pa'i gnas lnga dang
/ bcu dang bco brgyad la sogs pa mtha' dag phyin ci ma log par mkhyen pa'i 'jam mgon sa skya paNDi ta chen po kun dga' rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po sku dbon dang bcas pa'i
chos kyi khri rin po che mkhas pa zil gnon du grags pa ga la bar/ lha dang bcas pa'i 'gro ba mtha' dag gi mchod sdong chen po khams gsum chos kyi rgyal por dbang bskur
ba'i sngon du 'gro ba rten 'brel gyi sgo 'phar brgya phrag dbye rgyu'i sku rim du/ sa lug dbyug zla'i nyer drug la dmar chen gtor bzlog dang sbrags rgyal gsung bka' 'gyur
rin po che zhal dbye ba/ mi shigs rdo rje'i tshe srog sgrub pa'i cho ga bcas dang / bsnyen sgrub las gsum mthar phyin gyi zor las pa lngas nyer dgur gtor zor 'phen pa/
smin zla'i tshes gsum lhag pa lha mtshams kyi 'grub sbyor dang ldan pa'i nyin mchod zhing bya khra ma'i 'bruu spungs la/

bstan srid je mthor rgyas pa'i rten 'brel gyi dar cog sgreng ba sogs dang / mgo zla'i mjug phur bzlog sgrub zhag lnga'ang gnang ngo // // ! dgung grangs bcu gnyis su phebs
pa lcags spre'u rgyal zla'i tshes gcig nyin lha mchod sngon 'gro'i skyabs mgon yab sras sku 'khor/ /ban tshang bla rigs sogs dang bcas tshoms chen du dga' ston bzhugs gral
sngar rgyun bzhin rgya cher stsal/ tshes gnyis nas bzung rje rdo rje 'chang nyid ban tshang pa'i 'khor tshogs dang bcas mgon khang khag rnams kyi gtor spod skabs yongs
grags kyi khag bzhir lha mdung / rnga ril dar cog can kha btags bcas bstan 'gro'i bde skyid dar ba'i thugs smon can gyis 'bul ba mdzad/ tshes gsum nas yab rje rdo rje 'chang
gis mgon khang steng 'og /bdud 'dul phug /skyed lhas/ bsam brling dus mchod rnams su phyi sgrom nang gzungs sogs ma tshang ba med pa'i ru mtshon 'dzugs chog /spyi bye
brag gi bstan pa dar rgyas yun brtan gyi phrin 'chol gnyer gtad sogs thugs bskyed rlabs po che'i sgo nas sgrub 'dzugs skabs rje rdo rje 'chang nyid kyang phebs/ de nas zla
nang de'i yar tshes la gser khri rin po cher mnga' gsol gong / rgyal sras lam bzang gi gsung bshad kyi dga' ston stsol ba la sku na'i stabs thugs spobs sbyang phyir du/
gnas slob bzod pa bkra shis nas bskul ma bzhin gzhi thog bla brang gi shar phyogs khang gsar bsod nams dpal 'byor gling du/ gong gi sku mched 'jam mgon gcung rin po che/
a Ni drung/ yum mchog /rje btsun drung gsum/ gnas slob gsol gzim sogs bcu phrag brgal tsam la tshogs chen mor ji ltar stsol ba bzhin gyi bshad lung nyin gsum ma zhig bka'
drin che ba ni sku tshe 'di nyid du chos 'chad mdzad pa'i sgo dang po'i skabs so/ /zla ba de'i nyer gsum nyin

'chams mgon bcu dgu spyan 'dren bcas dus mdos kyi tshogs dbur yab sras zung phebs shing / nyer lnga'i nyin snga bar grol nas mnyen chas 'chams lha khang chen mo'i rdo gcal
du mdzad/ nyer brgyad nyin las mkhan sgo ma ru 'dren bcas kyi gar 'chams rngam brjid dang ldan pa kun gyi yid 'phrog pa dang / nyer dgu gtor zor 'phangs nas/ gnam gang la
chos srung rnams la gtang rag phrin 'chol zung 'brel gyi bskang ba brgya tshar du grags pa dang / hor lugs kyi dbang du btang na lcags spre'u gsar tshes kyi snga dro bstan
srung mgon po mnga' gsol rgyas par mdzad rjes gzhi thog pho brang gi tshoms chen mor skyabs mgon dam pa yab sras dkon mchog gi grangs ldan gyi dbu g.yas/ chos grwa nyi
zla zung gi bya ba las kyi sne mo ba/ mchod yon rin po che rnams kyi legs skyes stob mi/ gzhan yang gzhis byes kyi ser skya mchog dman 'os babs rnams la lo gsar gyi dga'
ston gya nom par bstar zhing / tshes gnyis gsum bzhi rnams la gser khri rin po cher mnga' gsol dngos gzhi'i dga' ston snga ma gnyis kyi tshe yab rje mchog nas gzhi thog
pho brang gi yang steng du lha bsangs dang / de nas sngar srol ltar bca' bsgrigs sngon du btang nas/ nyin dang po/ lnga bdo'i mgon po zas gtsang sras pos chos kyi 'khor lo
bskor ba'i skabs su lha dbang brgya byin gyis phul ba'i chos dung rin po che dkar po rgyang grags nyi ma rtse shar la gsung bskul gyis/ mkhas pa zil gnon nam/ 'khor lo
gsum ldan nam/ chos khrir thang mo che sogs mtshan mchog gsum ldan gyi gser khri rin po che ga la ba'i mdun du/ chos grwa rnam gnyis kyis gtsos sdom brtson sde snod 'dzin
pa'i dge ba'i bshes gnyen rnams kyis gral gyi gzhi bzung / skya ser khri

phrag longs ba'i tshogs kyi khrod du/ srid zhi'i gtsug rgyan 'jam mgon mi srid bzung ba skuu mched sku mtshan dang dpe byad kyis spras shing lta bas chog mi shes pa sku 'khor
dang bcas pa rnams/ 'phags pa rta thul ltar spyod lam dul zhing / tshangs pa'i rgyal po ltar blo gros dang ldan pa'i sgo nas phyags legs par phebs te/ gser khri rin po
cher sku gsung thugs 'gyur ba med pa lhan ne lhang nge lham mer phebs bstun gsung rab klog pa maNDal 'bul ba sogs sngar rgyun gyi phyag len bzhin grub 'phral/ gnyis med
gsung ba don kun grub kyis rigs can gsum la chos kyi 'khor lo bskor pa'i tshul ji lta bar rje rdo rje 'chang nyid kyis/ sems bskyed gsal 'debs nas brtsams 'jam mgon sa skya
paNDi ta chen pos dbus gtsang khams gsum du tshogs chos su legs par gdams pa'i bstan bcos chen po thub pa'i dgongs pa rab tu gsal bar byed pa'i mtshan don nas bsam gtan
gyi phar phyin yan chad legs par stsal/ nyin bar mar gong bzhin bca' bsgrigs sngon 'gro'i sngar gyi 'phro nas sku gsum ye shes kyi rnam gzhag yan chad/ nyin gsum par skyabs
mgon yab sras gsum char gong gi dge mtshan dang bcas phebs te/ rje rdo rje 'chang nyid kyis sngar gyi 'phro nas mjug gi sbyar byang bar tshang la ma nor ba/ kun gyi
yid 'phrog pa gsung 'jam zhing snyan la dag cing gsal ba nye ring med pa tshangs pa'i dbyangs lta bu'i sgo nas der 'dus kun gyi rna ba'i bdud rtsir sim pa/ bsnyengs pa mi
mnga' ba'i spobs pa gzengs mtho ba'i ngang nas stsal bas kun kyang dga' bde'i dpal la lhag par sbyar ro/ /de ltar gyi skabs rten 'brel gyi legs skyes phun sum tshogs pa
bstar ba ni/ rgyal dbang thams cad mkhyen gzigs mchog nas khyad du mtshar ba'i dgu tshan dgu /sa skyong yab sras nas kyang de bzhin sogs mdor na gzhis

byes nas dngos 'bul rmugs 'dzin dbang po'i gan mdzod zhal dbye bar co 'dri ba dang / dge 'dun pa skye bo'i tshogs dang bcas pa la mang ja gdan non sbyin 'gyed stob pa sogs
dang / gdan sa chen po'i rten khyad mtshar rnams la mchod pa snyan shal spyan gzigs/ gzhan yang zur 'bul gyi rnam gzhag dgos pa rnams la'ang de bzhin bcas mdzad cing / brgya
dpon nas mol gtam phul grub rjes yab rje chos kyi rgyal pos/ gang gi rigs sras dam pa sku mched zung khams gsum chos kyi rgyal por mnga' gsol ba'i legs tshogs kyis mtshon
bdag gzhan gyis dus gsum du bsags pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba rnams chab mi 'tshal ba'i phyir/ yon tan rin po che sdud pa las/ ci ste mtshan ma med na de ni bsngo ba yin/
/zhes gsungs pa ltar/ 'khor gsum yongs su dag pa'i gsung bsngo'i rgyas btab rjes yab rje nyid rje rdo rje 'chang sku mched kyi sku mdun du zhal byang gzigs kyis bzhengs nas
'jam mgon sku mched la/ rgyal srid rin po che sna bdun bkra shis pa'i rdzas brgyad sogs kyis mnga' dbul smin rgyas dpon slob lhan rgyas nas gnang ba'i shis brjod/ rgyal
mtshan rtse mo nas rgyal ba'i sku gsung thugs kyi bkra shis shog gi bar ban tshang dbu byed che bas jeng drangs/ tshogs pa byings bcas nas 'brug stong dus gcig la ldir
ba lta bu'i gsung gdangs kyis mtha' brgyan par mdzad de/ 'jam mgon sku mched gang gi rgyal tshab tu mnga' gsol legs byas kyi rten 'brel dge bas mtshon 'dzam gling na sgrun
zla dang bral bar mkhas grub gzur gnas du mas bsngags pa'i rje btsun sa skya pa'i gdung rabs rin po che srid mtha'i bar du byon nas gser khri rin po cher mnga' gsol gyi
rten 'brel 'bad med lhun gyis grub pa'i dge mtshan srid na gsal ba ni nam mkha'i khams shin tu dwangs

shing nyi 'od gsal ba 'ja' dang 'od kyi gur khang 'khyil ba/ dkar phyogs lha rnams me tog gi char snyil zhing der 'dus kyi skye dgu mtha' dag dga' mgu yi rang gi dad pa'i thal
sbyar dang chabs gcig gnas tshul de ltar 'byung 'gyur gyi smon lam 'debs pa dang skyabs mgon rdo rje 'chang yab sras rnam gsum gyi ngo mtshar mdzad pa'i gleng mo sgrogs
pa la gcig tu gzhol bar gyur cing / de'i sang nyin gegs med don ldan gyi dga' ston chen mo'i thog rje rdo rje 'dzin nyid la yab sras zung gis mtshon gzhis byes ser skya
drag zhan rnams nas legs so'i sgo brgya rnam par dbye ba'i skabs so/ /de dag gi don bsdu na/ gnam bskos lha yi rang 'dra'i rigs bdag khrir/ /rgyal tshab mchog tu mnga'
gsol nyi zla zung / /mthon por 'gyur med shis pa'i me tog char/ /snyil la phyogs bcu'i rgyal dang rgyal sras kyang / /de tshe gdul bya'i blo gros 'dab brgya pa/ /yongs su
'byed pa'i dam chos tsha zer ni/ /'jig rten kun gsal bcu gnyis bdag po yis/ /rnam grol sbrang rtsi'i bcud du 'dzum par bskyangs/ /phyi nang rten 'byung skyes kyi bdog pa'i
dngos/ /mi zad nam mkha' mdzod kyi spun zla ru/ /lhun grub phrin las phyogs kyi bu mo'i rnar/ /grags pa'i gdugs dkar dkar phyogs lha yis bzung / /zhes kyang smras so//
// ! gnyis pa bstan 'gro'i phan bde spel tshul rnams lo khams dang sbyar te bshad pa la/ thos rtsom gnyis rtogs sla ba'i phyir so sor phyogs bsdoms su bshad pa dang / bsam
sgom 'chad rtsod kyis mtshon lugs brgya'i mdzad phrin kun gsal gyi tha gru ltar yangs shing rgya che ba'i nang nas bka' 'bangs kyi tha shal mu to ba bdag gis cha shas
tsam zhig rnyed pa rnams go rim bzhin lo khams so so'i nang du ji mdzad ma 'khrul bar ston pa dang gnyis las/ dang po la/ thos pa mdzad pa'i tshul dang / rtsom pa

mdzad pa'i tshul gnyis kyi dang po la/ spyir dam pa'i chos nyan pa'i phan yon dang / bye brag theg chen gyi chos nyan bshad kyi phan yon gnyis kyi dang po ni/ byang chub sems
dpa'i sde snod las/ /thos pas chos rnams shes par 'gyur/ /thos pas sdig las ldog par 'gyur/ /thos pas don med spong bar 'gyur/ /thos pas mya ngan 'das pa thob/ /ces gsungs
la/ de'i don rnam bshad rig par/ de la rkang pa bzhi po 'dis ni rim pa ltar/ phyi nang gi grub mtha' shes pas blang dor gyi gnas shes pa dang / tshul khrims kyi bslab
pa thob nas nyes spyod las ldog pa dang / sems kyi bslab pa thob nas don med pa'i 'dod pa spong ba dang / shes rab kyi bslab pa thob nas de la brten te zag zad mngon du
byas nas myang 'das thob pa ste bzhi'am/ yang dag pa'i lta ba rnyed pa dang / las dang / nyon mongs pa dang / skye ba'i kun nas nyon mongs las brgal ba ste bzhi dang / chos
'dul ba la dad pa rnyed pa dang / rab tu byung ba dang / dbang po'i sgo bsrungs pas 'dod pa las 'dod chags dang bral bas gnod pa spong ba dang / bden pa rtogs nas myang
'das thob pa ste bzhi la bshad do/ /lung rnam 'byed las/ mang du thos pa la phan yon lnga yod de/ phung po la mkhas pa dang / khams la mkhas pa dang / skye mched la mkhas
pa dang / rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba la mkhas pa dang / de'i gdams ngag dang rjes su bstan pa gzhan la rag ma las pa yin no/ /gzhan yang rnam bshad rig par bcom ldan
'das kyi chos nyan pa la phan yon lnga gsungs te/ ma thos pa thos par 'gyur ba dang / thos pa yongs su byang bar 'gyur ba dang / som nyi spong ba dang / lta ba drang por
byed pa dang / shes rab kyi tshig dang don zab mo rtogs par 'gyur ba'o/ /zhes sogs mang du gsungs

so// // ! gnyis pa bye brag theg chen gyi chos nyan bshad kyi phan yon ni/ gzhi'i dus su theg dman gyi dge ba zil gyis gnon cing rigs gsos thebs pa dang / lam gyi dus su sgrib
pa ma lus par spong bas bsod nams gzhan las lhag pa dang / 'bras bu'i dus su rnam mkhyen thob par nges pa'o/ /dang po ni/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin par/ stong gsum
gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi sems can de dag thams cad dgra bcom pa nyid thob par 'gyur la/ dgra bcom pa de dag gi sbyin pa las byung ba'i bsod nams bya
ba'i dngos po dang / tshul khrims las byung ba'i bsod nams bya ba'i dngos po dang / sgom pa las byung ba'i bsod nams bya ba'i dngos po gang yin pa de la/ kun dga' bo 'di
ji snyam du sems/ bsod nams kyi phung po de mang ba yin nam gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das mang lags so/ /bde bar gshegs pa mang lags so/ /bka' stsal pa/ kun dga' bo de bas kyang
su zhig byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po la shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa dang ldan pa'i chos tha na nyi ma gcig ston na/ de bsod nams kyi phung po ches mang du
skye'o/ /zhes pa nas/ kun dga' bo 'di ni byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de'i chos kyi sbyin pa ste nyan thos kyi theg pa thams cad dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi theg
pa pa'i gang zag thams cad kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad zil gyis gnon pa'o/ /zhes sogs gsungs so// // ! gnyis pa ni/ rgyud bla mar/ gang zhig byang chub don du gnyer
bas gser zhing nor bus spras pa ni/ /sangs rgyas zhing rdul mnyam pa nyin re chos rgyal rnams la rtag 'bul la/ /gzhan gang 'di las tshig gcig thos shing thos nas kyang
ni mos na 'di/ /sbyin pa las byung dge ba de las bsod nams ches mang thob par 'gyur/ /blo ldan gang zhig bla med byang chub 'dod pas bskal pa du mar yang / /

lus ngag yid ni 'bad pa med par tshul khrims dri med srung byed la/ /gzhan dag 'di las tshig tsam thos shing thos nas kyang ni mos na 'di/ /tshul khrims las byung dge ba de
las bsod nams ches mang thob par 'gyur/ /gang zhig 'di na srid pa gsum gyi nyon mongs me 'jil bsam gtan ni/ /lha dang tshangs gnas mthar son rdzogs pa'i byang chub 'pho
med thabs sgom la/ /gzhan gang 'di las tshig tsam thos shing thos nas kyang ni mos na 'di/ /bsam gtan las byung dge ba de las bsod nams ches mang thob par 'gyur/ /gang phyir
sbyin pas longs spyod dag ni sgrub byed la/ /khrims kyis mtho ris bsgoms pas nyon mongs spong byed la/ /shes rab nyon mongs shes bya kun spong de yi phyir/ /'di mchog
nyid de de yi rgyu ni 'di thos yin/ zhes so// // ! gsum pa ni/ mdo sde rgyan las/ gang zhig tshig gam don sgo nas/ /tshigs bcad gnyis 'dzin rab sbyor la/ /sems can blo ldan
mchog de yis/ /yon tan rnam bcu thob 'gyur te/ /khams ni zad par brtas pa dang / /'chi ba'i tshe na rab dga' thob/ /ci ltar 'dod par skye ba dang / /kun tu tshe rabs
dran pa dang / /sangs rgyas rnams dang 'phrad pa dang / /de la theg mchog thos pa dang / /mos pa blo dang bcas pa dang / /sgo gnyis byang chub myur thob pa'o/ /zhes gsungs
shing / gzhan las kyang mang du gsungs mod kyi mang bas 'jigs nas 'dir de tsam las ma spros la/ de dag kyang rnam bshad rig par/ mdo don che ba nyid thos nas/ /nyan pa
dang ni 'dzin pa la/ /nyan pa po ni gus byed pas/ /thog mar dgos pa brjod par bya/ /zhes pa bzhin yin pas/ khams gsum chos kyi rgyal po 'brel tshad don ldan gyi rdo rje slob
dpon chen

po de nyid ni bskal pa dpag tu med pa'i snga rol du bcu gsum rdo rje 'dzin pa'i go 'phang la mnga' gsol du zin na'ang / gang gi ba tshwa can chu klung gi mdo lung sogs kyi
