don bzhin/ dus 'dir/ 'gro ba ma lus pa srid pa'i gcong rong las sgrol ba'i ded dpon chen po'i tshul bzung nas/ mdo rgyud man ngag dang bcas pa'i zab rgyas kyi bdud rtsi'i
'byung khungs yongs 'dzin dam pa bsnyen tshul ni 'di lta ste/ rje rdo rje 'chang nyid kyi zhal sgo las byon pa'i rje btsun sa skya pa'i gdung rabs gdan rabs bcas kyi lo
rgyus ngo mtshar srid na 'gran bral zhes bya ba las/ yab rje rdo rje 'chang dang thar rtse rje/ /gnas gsar rje dang brag rtsa rje btsun drung / /gzhi dgon rab brtan bzang
dang rta nag mkhan/ /tshul khrims bzang dang ngor chen bsod nams bzang / /sangs rgyas ye shes dpal ldan chos skyong zhabs/ /gong dkar bsod nams blo gros rnam mkhyen grong
/ /chos dbang rgya mtsho chu ri bkra shis don/ /kun dga' chos 'phel rin chen bzang po ste/ /gong dkar rnam lnga rin chen mi 'gyur zhabs/ /'gro mgon thub dbang de sras rig
'dzin mtshan/ /mkhan chen dbang phun mkhan chen kun dga' zla/ /seng ge rgyal mtshan sha ri mnga' bdag che/ /rgyal dbang skal bzang rje dang mchog sprul zhabs/ /dpal ldan
no min han dang 'on rgyal sras/ /lo nas sems dpa' chen po smin grol gling / /khri chen rin chen rnam rgyal sras mchog bcas/ /'bri gung rje dang bsam sdings yang zab rje/
/kun dga' sangs rgyas zhal lu ye shes grags/ /dngos grub sdings dang kun dga' don gsal sogs/ /gus pas bsten nas ris med chos rgyun zhus/ /nyams len med kyang dbang lung
man ngag 'khrid/ /gzhon dus brtson khul slob ma bstan phan dang / /btang snyoms dam nyams gsog pa grangs med yod/ /ces gsungs pa ltar bla ma dam pa de rnams las zab pa
dang

rgya che ba'i chos tshul mtha' yas pa zhig bzhes te/ dus phyis gsan pa rgya mtsho'i mthar son pa'i dpe gcig pur 'os par mdzad pa'i tshul rnams ni ha cang mang ches pas 'dir
ma spros pas rje rdo rje 'chang chen po de nyid kyi gsan yig rin po che pod chen gnyis kyi steng nas shes par bya ba'i dbang du zhus nas/ gnyis pa rtsom pa mdzad pa'i tshul
ni/ ji skad du/ chos rnams thams cad bka' dang bstan bcos gnyis su 'dus/ /legs par gsungs dang de yi dgongs 'grel te/ /de yis dbang gis shAkya'i bstan pa 'di/ /'jig rten
khams 'dir yun ring gnas par 'gyur/ /zhes dang / rgyud bla mar/ gang zhig rgyal ba'i bstan pa 'ba' zhig gi /dbang byas rnam g.yeng med yid can gyis bshad/ /thar pa thob
pa'i lam dang rjes mthun pa/ /de yang drang srong bka' bzhin spyi bos blang / /zhes gsungs pa ltar gyi brjod don dang ldan zhing / dpyad gsum rnam par dag pa'i bstan bcos
tshar du dngar ba rnams kyi nang nas rags pa tsam zhig brjod na 'di lta ste/ gsol 'debs brgyud bdebs dngos dang zhal skong skor/ 1) gdung rabs la sogs rnam thar bsgrigs
rtsom skor/ 2) sgrub dkyil bsgrigs chags bsnyen thabs sbyin sreg skor/ 3) dkar chag bca' yig debs dang dpyad khra'i skor/ 4) bskang mdos phrin bcol gtor bzlog ru mtshon
skor/ 5) dril lan sogs sna tshogs pa'i skor/ 6) dang drug las dang po ni/ yab rje rdo rje 'chang la gsol 'debs yon tan rin chen 'byung gnas sogs tsho bzhi/ rje btsun kun
dga' bstan pa'i nyi mar gcig /sa skya pa'i gdung rabs gsol 'debs don gnyis lhun grub pa ma bsam pa lhun grub zhal skong / dus mchod bla brang gdung rabs gsol 'debs/ rin
sgang gdung rabs gtso bsdus gsol 'debs/ kun dga' don gsal gyi ngor mdzad gdung rabs

gsol 'debs tshigs bcad gcig /nang chen bla ma'i ngor mdzad gdung rabs gsol 'debs/ thar rtse rdo rje 'chang la gnyis/ gnas gsar rdo rje 'chang la shlo ka gcig dang rgyas pa
gnyis/ rje de gnyis la zhabs brtan re re/ yang nam mkha'i mtshan can dang ratna'i mtshan can la zhabs brtan tshigs bcad re re/ brag rtsa rdo rje 'chang la gsol 'debs gnyis/
'jam mgon sangs rgyas ye shes la zhabs brtan gsol 'debs re re/ gong dkar bsod nams blo gros la gcig /gong dkar chos dbang rgya mtshor gsum/ rin chen mi 'gyur rgyal mtshan
la gsol 'debs/ 'jam mgon dpal ldan chos skyong la zhabs brtan dang gsol 'debs/ rgyal dbang bskal bzang rgya mtshor zhabs brtan gsol 'debs le tshan/ mchog sprul rin po
che blo bzang bstan pa'i dbang phyug 'jam dpal rgya mtsho dpal bzang por gsol 'debs/ smin gling khri chen 'gyur med rin chen rnam rgyal la gsol 'debs/ smin gling gdung rabs
spyir gsol 'debs dang zhabs brtan/ sdom gsum brgyud 'debs ma rig g.yul rgyal/ gnam kha'u par gsol 'debs/ bu ston rin po cher gsol 'debs/ paN chen shAkya mchog ldan la
bstod pa/ ngor e waM chos ldan gdan rabs gsol 'debs/ tshar lugs bla ma gtso bsdus gsol 'debs/ tshar lugs bla ma gtso bsdus la phyag 'tshal/ sgar chen dang kun dga' dbang
rgyal la bstod pa re re/ yang dag brgyud 'debs/ lam zab brgyud 'debs kyi kha skong / chos las pa bkra shis dar rgyas kyis zhus brgyud 'debs kha skong kha shas/ bde mchog
nyung ngu'i lung brgyud gsol 'debs/ mkha' spyod ma'i brgyud 'debs ngor chen dang tshar chen gyis mdzad pa'i kha skong rnams phyogs bsdoms/ mi 'khrugs pa'i brgyud 'debs/
tshe dpag med kyi bla brgyud

gsol 'debs le tshan/ 'jigs byed ro langs brgyad bskor gyi bla brgyud gsol 'debs kha skong bcas/ dbu ma lugs kyi sems bskyed brgyud 'debs/ khams gsum rnam rgyal gyi dbang brgyud
gsol 'debs/ gsang 'dus rim lnga'i 'khrid brgyud gsol 'debs bu mdzad kha skong / zhal bzhi bsnyen dus kyi rjes gnang bla brgyud gsol 'debs/ rmor chen la gsol 'debs le
tshan dang de gsham mnal lam du rtsom gnang gi tshigs bcad gcig bcas/ thub bstan mkhan chen klu dbang rgya mtsho dang ngag dbang bstan 'dzin rgyal mtshan gnyis la gsol 'debs
re re/ rtse gdong sprul sku'i yang srid myur 'byon gsol 'debs/ chos gter gling sprul sku myur 'byon gsol 'debs/ 'gyur med kun bzang klong grol la gsol 'debs/ rdor brag
rig 'dzin la gsol 'debs/ rgyal tshab dam pa ngag dbang 'jam dpal bde legs rgya mtshor zhabs brtan/ tho yon blo bzang nor bur brtan bzhugs/ dwags grwa bzod grags ngor mdzad
gsol 'debs zhal gsung ma/ ri khud sprul sku'i bzhed skong kun blo rgyang 'bod/ mkhyen rab skal ldan gyi ngor mdzad zhabs brtan gsol 'debs/ dwags grwa bkra shis yar 'phel
gyis zhus le tshan gsum/ 'jig rten dbang phyug la smre sngags/ smon lam bde dga' rgya mtsho/ rgyud sde bzhi'i lha tshogs la gsol 'debs/ rje btsun sgrol mar gsol 'debs/
khe smad dpal lhun nas zhus yab sras rnam gsum gsol 'debs/ khe smad sgrol 'bum ngor mdzad gsol 'debs/ kye rdor rgyu dbang zhal ngo nang brgyud la gsol 'debs/ stag rtse
byams pa lha dbang rig 'dzin la gsol 'debs/ thub bstan dge 'phel rje btsun rin po cher gdung rabs myur 'byon gsol 'debs/ bdag nyid chen po bzang po dpal la gdung rabs myur
'byon

gsol 'debs/ rje rdo rje 'chang sku mched kyi zhabs brtan bco brgyad yum bgres ngor mdzad/ yang gser can shangs pa slob dpon gyi ngor mdzad zhabs brtan/ skyabs gnas dam pa rnams
la zhabs brtan gsol 'debs dge slong bskal bzang mchog grub kyi ngor mdzad/ rje rdo rje 'chang sku mched brtan bzhugs gsol 'debs re re/ padma dpal ldan gyis zhus zhabs
brtan/ yang brtan bzhugs tshigs bcad re byas pa tsho gsum/ gcung rin po cher gcig /phur lcog pa chen por gsol 'debs/ bden tshig bkra shis 'gyur med/ bden tshig sa bstan
gsal 'bar/ a ti lug pan e dhi ni no mi na han zhus gsol 'debs/ gsol 'debs ma dag phung khams ma/ gong dkar blo nyi sogs kyis zhus pa'i gsol 'debs tshigs bcad gcig gi gsham
na rgyal mtshan 'dzugs chog dang bcas pa/ spu bla bsod grags kyis zhus yul sde rgyas pa'i smon tshig tsho gnyis/ gong dkar kun snang grwa tshang sogs rgyas pa'i bden tshig
/smon tshig kun mkhyen mngon gyur ma/ zhwa dmar sprul skur zhabs brtan gsol 'debs/ rje nyid la gsol 'debs dad ldan re skong / brtan bzhugs gsol 'debs nyes bral thar
mchog /bden tshig phan bde ganggA'i chu rgyun/ bden tshig 'gyur med g.yung drung / byang gling sprul sku myur 'byon gsol 'debs dang zhabs brtan/ dwags po zhabs drung rigs
bdag ngag dbang lhun grub dar rgyas no min han la gsol 'debs rab 'byams zhing bzhugs ma/ gser can shAkya 'gro mgon ched stsal zhabs brtan gsol 'debs/ thub brtan mkhan chen
padma rgyal mtshan la gsol 'debs/ smon lam dus gsum dpal 'bar/ e rte ni blo bzang chos grub kyis zhus sku bstod/ 'gyur med dpal sgron gyis zhus zhabs brtan/ gzim 'og sprul
sku'i ngor mdzad gsol 'debs shlo ka gcig /sgrol dkar brgyud rim

gsol 'debs/ bsod 'od kyis zhus yab sras rnam gsum zhabs brtan/ shing phag nag zla'i bco brgyad la 'jam mgon sa paN dngos su gzigs skabs thugs smon/ brgya dpon bkra shis 'od
zer gyis zhus smon lam/ stobs 'phrog dbang po'i gsang 'khrid brgyud 'debs lam rim smon lam bcas kyi zhal skong / dam bzang ngor mdzad zhabs brtan shlo ka gcig /de mo gong
mar gsol 'debs/ rje rdo rje 'chang yab sras rnam gsum zhabs brtan yid lhung dpon ngor mdzad pa/ 'gro mgon bstan pa sangs rgyas kyi sprul sku myur 'byon gsol 'debs/ zhu
chen tshul khrims rin chen gyi yang srid myur 'byon phrin gsol/ dwags grwa mkhan pos dgon der dbu ma 'jug pa'i gzhung 'dzugs skabs zhus pa'i smon tshig /bde mchog brgyud
'debs kha skong / rdo rje phur pa dang gu ru drag dmar gyi dbang brgyud kha skong / sgrol dkar tshe 'khrid brgyud 'debs kha skong / rje rdo rje 'chang la gsol 'debs rten
'brel zab don/ thar rtser ganydzi ra dang rgyal mtshan phul skabs kyi smon tshig /paN chen thams cad mkhyen gzigs chen por gsol 'debs/ yang can mkhan po ngag dbang shAkyar
bstod pa/ brtan bzhugs gsol 'debs 'chi med rdo rje'i srog rtsa dang 'chi med 'od snang / sgrub thabs brgya rtsa'i bla brgyud gsol 'debs le tshan gnyis/ zham 'bring ba 'od
zer gyi ma'i ched du gnang ba'i smon lam tshigs bcad gcig /rtse gdong bdag chen ngag dbang nor bu bsod nams dbang rgyal/ kun dga' tshe dbang rig 'dzin/ ngag dbang nor
bu rgyal mtshan rnams la gsol 'debs/ bektse'i rjes gnang gsan skabs kyi gsol 'debs mi mthun kun zhi/ 'jigs byed nang mchod 'bul tshul kha skong / drag po sgrol dbang gi brgyud
'debs kyi kha skong / phar tshad brgyud 'debs kha skong / zhe chen bla slob nas zhus pa'i

brtan bzhugs/ zhe chen sprul sku'i brtan bzhugs/ gdung rabs zhabs brtan lha ldan kun sbyin ngor mdzad/ bstan rgyas gling mchog sprul myur 'byon gsol 'debs le tshan/ yar 'brog
thar gling rgyas phyir thugs smon/ yab sras rnam gsum gsol 'debs glang thang lcags ri sprul sku'i ngor mdzad/ sme brtsegs dud khar bstod pa/ gnod sbyin pho dgu mo dgur
bstod pa/ nye gnas bkra shis ming can gyis zhus pa'i yi dam chos srung sogs kyi sku bstod/ dge byed lor bsam yas chos skyong la khrab ldan sogs gsar phul thog gi smon tshig
bcas te gsol 'debs brgyud 'debs dngos dang zhal skong skor rags bsdus tsam mo// // ! gnyis pa gdung rabs sogs rnam thar bsgrigs rtsom skor ni/ yab rje rdo rje 'chang
gi rnam thar/ gnas gsar rdo rje 'chang chen po'i rnam thar/ 'dzam gling byang phyogs kyi thub pa'i rgyal tshab chen po dpal ldan sa skya pa'i gdung rabs rin po che byon tshul
rnam par thar pa ngo mtshar rin po che'i bang mdzod dgos 'dod kun 'byung gi kha skong rin chen 'dzad med srid zhi'i dpal 'byor lhun grub/ sa skya pa'i gdung rabs dbang
rgyal lhun po/ /sa skya pa'i gdung rabs rin po che byon tshul kha skong bcas bsdoms shing lhag par dus mchod bla brang ba'i gdung rabs kha yod lag yod du bgrangs pa gdan
rabs bcas kyi rnam thar lo rgyus/ a mes zhabs kyi rnam thar nying khu/ rnal 'byor ma'i bla brgyud rnam thar nyung ngu / dpal ldan lha mo'i lo rgyus/ sgro mo lung pa mang
thos bsod nams chos 'phel gyi rnam thar brag rtsa ba chen pos mdzad pa 'phro can gyi zhal skong rnams dang / gzhan yang lung rgyun spel phyir dbur tshigs bcad re bsnon
par mdzad pa/ rgyal tshab dam pa/ sangs rgyas rin chen/ sa lo/ dkon mchog lhun grub/ sngags 'chang yab sras gsum gyi rnam thar bsdus pa

dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ mus chen sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan gyi rnam thar 'bring po ste/ gdung rabs sogs rnam thar bsgrigs rtsom skor ro// // ! gsum pa sgrub dkyil bsgrigs chags
bsnyen thabs sbyin sreg skor ni/ byang gter lcags sdong lha mang tshar lugs dbang chog /gdugs dkar gyi dkyil chog /gdugs dkar kyi chog khrigs/ 'od zer dri med kyi cho
ga'i las rim/ gzungs gra lnga'i mngon dkyil nag 'gros ma/ gzungs gra lnga rdo rje 'phreng ba lugs kyi bdag 'jug /paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang gis mdzad pa'i gra lnga'i sgrub
dkyil dbang chog la dogs dpyod/ gur mgon lha bcu gnyis ma'i sgrub dkyil/ de'i mtshams sbyor/ rang bzhin 'byung ba'i gtsug tor rnam par rgyal ma'i dkyil chog dang de'i
bstod pa/ mi 'khrugs pa'i dkyil chog gshin po rjes 'dzin dang bcas pa 'khor lo bde mchog lU'u hi pa'i sgrub dkyil/ 'khor lo bde mchog nag po pa'i sgrub thabs 'bring po/
/bde mchog dril bu pa'i lugs kyi phyi rdul tshon gyi dkyil chog /gsang 'dus 'jam pa'i rdo rje'i sgrub dkyil/ de'i dbang gi mtshams sbyor/ 'jigs byed ro langs brgyad skor
gyi sgrub dkyil/ rwa tshar gnyis kyi thun mong ma yin pa'i bzhed pa 'jigs byed bcu gsum ma'i mngon dkyil lhan thabs cha lag bcas/ de'i bshom dang thig rtsa/ gshed dmar lha
lnga'i sgrub dkyil bdag 'jug gi yi ge /de'i bla brgyud shog gcig /ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub kyi tshe dpag med lha dgu'i sgrub mchod kyi bdag 'jug gsal byed/ kye rdor
sgrub thabs kyi rnam bshad lung rgyun spel phyir mtshan dang dbur tshigs bcad bsnan pa/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i sgo nas dus mtha' ma'i cho ga /sgrol ma maNDal bzhi pa'i
cho ga rmor mdzad zur 'debs/ sgrol ma maNDal bzhi chog

rgyas pa/ yang sgrol ma maNDal bzhi chog /byad 'grol gser lde'i chog khrigs/ sbyong rgyud nas gsungs pa'i tsha chog /sbyong rgyud nas gsungs pa'i ro sreg sngon 'gro'i phung
po chas 'jug gam rus cho ga zur bkol/ ri khrod ma'i bum chog /rnam sras mchod chog /zhing lha mchod chog /rgyal zla'i tshes gcig tshoms bar mgon khang gtor 'dzug 'don khrigs/
sha brgya zan brgya'i glud gzhung / gtsug tor dri med kyi gzungs bklag thabs dang mchod rten gdab tshul/ tshe dbang mda' 'phel ma/ rten 'brel bsrung ba'i byin rlabs
bya tshul/ gsang 'dus mi bskyod rdo rjer brten pa'i gshin po rjes 'dzin gyi cho ga /rdo rje gtum mo'i las byang / gur las gsungs pa'i mkha' 'gro rigs lnga bsdus pa'i sgrub
dkyil/ rta mgrin yang gsang lha dgu'i dkyil chog /de'i dkyil 'khor du slob ma rjes su bzung ba'i cho ga /sambu Ti'i dkyil 'khor du slob ma rjes su bzung ba'i mtshams sbyor/
kye rdo rje'i sgrub thabs ma nor don tshang de mo mchog gi dgongs bzhed bzhin mdzad pa/ sgrub thabs brgya rtsa'i gras kye rdor dpa' gcig nag 'gros ma/ bcu gcig zhal
gyi maNDal sgrub mchod/ kye rdor bdag bskyed bsdus pa dang de gsham kha rag gsol mchod gnyan sgrol yan lag drug pa'i sgrub thabs rjes gnang bcas/ spyan gzigs gtso 'khor
gsum gyi sgrub thabs rjes gnang / spyan gzigs sgrub thabs shin tu nyung ngu/ tshe dpag med 'chi bslu'i zur 'debs/ khro bo stobs po che'i sgom bzlas/ rdo rje gzhon nu dang
mkha' spyod ma'i sgrub thabs re re/ sgrol dkar tshe 'khrid zla ba'i chu rgyun gyi nyams len snying po bsdus pa dang de'i zur 'debs/ gu ru drag dmar gyi rjes gnang / che
mchog padma thod phreng gi sgrub thabs rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum gyi rnam gzhag /phyag rdor 'chi bdag 'joms pa'i bdag bskyed/ khro mo sme brtsegs bum chog

rjes gnang dang bcas pa/ dzam dkar rjes gnang / dgra nag nas gsungs pa'i dbyangs can dmar mo'i sgrub thabs/ khyung nag gi rjes gnang / mkha' lding gser mig 'khyil ba'i rjes
gnang / khyung khra'i sgom bzlas dang bsnyen sgrub bya tshul/ sgrol dkar sgrub thabs shin tu bsdus pa/ gtsug tor 'bar ba'i rjes gnang / 'byung 'dul me dbang rjes gnang /
rnam snang sgyu dra nas gsungs shing sgrub thabs brgya rtsa nas bshad pa'i srung ba lnga gtso rkyang rjes gnang / shangs lugs rta mgrin gsang sgrub mngon rtogs/ khro rgyal
rta mchog rol pa'i sgom bzlas/ bgegs mthar byed kyi sgom bzlas/ tshe dpag med dze tA ri'i lugs kyi sgom bzlas/ rig byed ma'i gnad yig gsal byed/ rig byed rjes gnang thun
mong dang thun mong ma yin pa'i rnam gzhag /rig byed ma'i chos skor dngos grub 'byung gnas kyi gsal byed/ ku ru kulle'i rjes gnang bya tshul/ gur mgon dkar po'i tshes
sgrub/ zhal dkar po tshe 'phel gyi bdag mdun sgrub tshul/ bram nag shan pa drug skor gyi bdag mdun rnam gzhag /grib ma khrus sel gyi nyams len/ phag dkar shes rab gsal byed
kyi nyams len/ rgyal sras kun gyi 'jug ngogs theg chen spyi bye brag la 'jug tshul/ bcu gcig zhal lha lnga'i rjes gnang / tshe dpag med lung lugs kyi nyams len/ dbyangs
can dkar mo'i rjes gnang / yang dag zla gam dgu pa'i sgom bzlas/ dam tshig rdo rje'i sgrub thabs/ 'dod rgyal rjes gnang gsal byed/ ma Ni bum sgrub/ phyag rdor rnam sras
sbags sgrub ngag 'don/ sa chen kun dga' blo gros dang 'jam dbyangs dmar ser sbags sgrub/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan gyi bla ma'i rnal 'byor/ 'jam mgon sa skya paNDi
ta'i bla ma'i rnal 'byor/ rdo rje phur pa la brten pa'i

bla ma'i rnal 'byor nyams len/ dus 'khor bla ma'i rnal 'byor/ gur gyi mgon po'i sgo nas bla ma'i rnal 'byor/ nA ro mkha' spyod dang gshed dmar gnyis kyi 'khrid 'chad tshul/
bde mchog rdo rje mkha' 'gro'i rgyud las gsungs pa'i yig brgya'i las tshogs khrus dang sbyin sreg gsal byed/ lha mo 'od zer can ma'i sbyin sreg /bde mchog nag po lugs kyi
gzhi bsnyen 'bring po bya tshul/ rta mgrin gsang sgrub bsnyen thabs sbyin sreg bcas/ dge mdzad rdo rje'i bsnyen sgrub kyi lag len zur 'debs/ gsang 'dus mi bskyod pa'i bsnyen
thabs sbyin sreg /'jigs byed kyi bsnyen thabs sbyin sreg /'byung 'dul bsnyen thabs/ seng ge sgra'i bsnyen thabs sbyin sreg bcas/ thugs rje chen po'i bsnyen sgrub bya
tshul/ sangs rgyas mnyam sbyor yang dag zla gam dgu pa dang gcig pa'i bsnyen sgrub sbyin sreg bcas/ rdo rje gzhon nu'i bdag nyid rtsa ba'i dkyil 'khor gyi sbyin sreg rdo
rje gzhon nu'i las bzhi'i sbyin sreg /de'i sbyin sreg phrin las rgya mtsho'i nying khu/ kun rig bsnyen sbyin la cho ga dang bzlas grangs phral tshul/ kun rig thig tshon
byin rlabs/ dpal chen yang dag thig tshon byin rlabs/ gur drag sbyin sreg bsnyen thabs bcas/ khyung khra'i zhi ba'i sbyin sreg /rnam 'joms ba ri lugs kyi zhi ba'i sbyin
sreg /rnam 'joms bir lugs zhi ba'i sbyin sreg dang de gsham bstod pa ring thung / rnam rgyal sbyin sreg /gur lha brgyad drag po'i sbyin sreg pho rkyang drag po'i sbyin sreg
/brag rdzong ma la brten pa'i zhi ba'i sbyin sreg /tshe dpag med lha dgu'i rgyas pa'i sbyin sreg /ku ru kulle'i sbyin sreg /tshogs bdag thabs 'khor sbyin sreg bcas/ sangs
rgyas sman bla'i bsnyen yig /bla ma zhi khro'i bsnyen yig /mi 'khrugs pa'i bsnyen thabs sbyin sreg bcas/ rnam rgyal gyi rab gnas/ bde mchog dang gsang 'dus 'phags lugs
kyi

rab gnas 'bring po/ so 'brang 'khor lo bcu gsum ma'i rab gnas dang 'dogs tshul thun mong min pa'i gsal byed/ rdo rje phur pa'i rab gnas rgyas pa/ kye rdo rje la sbyar ba'i
rab gnas rgyas pa'i zin bris/ yang kye rdo rje sogs la sbyar ba'i rab gnas 'bring po/ /mgon po'i rab gnas rgyas pa'i zin bris/ ku ru kulle sngon mo'i char 'bebs dang sad
srung / nag po chen po la klu chen brgyad bskor gyi char 'bebs/ nag po chen po'i man ngag rlung gnon/ rdo rje drag po rtsal gyi char 'bebs/ thugs sgrub dang dgongs 'dus btsa'
sad bsrung pa'i gsal byed/ bu ston rin po ches mdzad pa'i thog dang ser bas g.yos sogs bsrung thabs nag 'gros/ gtad hrul zangs gling zur 'debs bka' rgya can 'dod gsol
bcas/ tshogs bdag gi 'gab 'dre bse gdong can mnan thabs/ rdo rje gzhon nu'i sgo nas phung sri mnan pa'i man ngag ling dpe bcas/ jag 'ching ra ru ma'i gsal byed bcas/ lha
brgyad dkyil 'khor gyi bkra shis/ oM AHhUM gi bdud rtsi mchod tshig don ldan bdud rtsi/ lcags sdong ma'i rgyun khyer dang de gsham rdo rje rab brtan ma'i gtor 'bul bcas
te sgrub dkyil bsgrigs chags bsnyen thabs sbyin sreg skor rags bsdus tsam mo// //! bzhi pa dkar chag bca' yig debs dang dpyad khra'i skor ni/ mkha' spyod be'u bum gyi dkar
chag /'bum thang dngul gdung rin po che'i dkar chag /thub pa 'od zer 'gyed kyi dkar chag /tshoms chen nyams gso'i skabs mgon khang chen mo'i dkar chag /sde dger gdung
rabs sogs bris thang bcu bdun gnang ba'i dkar chag /pha sgar zur sbug gnyis su bzhugs rgyu'i rten rnams kyi dkar chag dang 'dod gsol tshong tshe brtan dbang phyug nas ma
Ni rdo bskos bzhengs pa'i dkar chag /lha chen skas

ring gsar bzhengs skabs kyi dkar chag rje rdo rje 'chang gi bka' bzhin zhal dkar nas mdzad pa/ gsang sngags bde chen gling gi bca' yig /thub bstan lha khang chen mo ba'i bca'
yig /gdan sa chen po'i bya ba las kyi sne mo ba rnams kyi bca' yig /rtse thab pa'i bca' yig /lha chen g.yos khang gi bca' yig /chos grwa lho byang thun mong rung khang
gi bca' yig /bar thab pa'i bca' yig /dmangs thab pa'i bca' yig /mgo zla'i bka' 'gyur bca' tshe/ rtse gdong chos sde pa'i bca' yig /bsam yas lcog grwa pa'i bca' yig /chos
'khor lhun po pa'i bca' yig /rgyun sgrogs gzhi grwa'i bca' yig /hor rtsa bod rtsar song ba'i spyi 'gro/ yang de dang 'dra ba mdo khams lho byang la gnang ba/ lha chen spyi
bsod par gnang ba'i spyi 'gro/ rta nag thub brtan par gnang ba'i spyi 'gro/ glang nag bkra shis chos sder gnang ba'i spyi 'gro/ bar lding rdzong chung dpon slob byams
par gnang ba'i spyi 'gro/ shel rdzong dga' bo bar gnang ba'i springs yig /khri tshang bsam 'grub kyis skus springs yig /gling kha rin chen chos dbang nas zhus pa'i springs
yig /sga 'dra'i gzhi bdag la springs yig /de'i ka ba lho mar sbyor gnang gi yi ge /hor khang gsar pas zhus pa'i springs yig /bsam yas spyi pas zhus pa'i springs yig /dngos
grub sdings pa'i thang ka'i rgyab yig /rnam rab klong rtsa lho pas zhus pa'i springs yig /dbon tshe dbang rnam rgyal la gnang ba'i thang ka'i rgyab yig /'dam thog bseb
rong rgyal por sprengs yig /rta nag sdings dga' bya bzang par gnod byed la springs yig /kha'u sman chab kyi gzhi bdag la springs yig /ming bsgyur can gyi springs yig rnams
dang / rje btsun sa skya pa'i gdung rabs rin po che gras thang bzhengs tshul/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang gi lam 'bras

bka' rgya thim pa'i gzigs snang 'bri tho/ sgrub thabs rgya mtsho'i bris thang bzhengs tshul/ yab rje'i bla mchod zhal thang bri tho/ de'i mchod thang rgyab gzungs bri tho/
zhal gtor chen skabs zor las pa rim can nas sgrub bsnyen gyi rten bla rdo bram gzugs kyi ri mo can gyi bzhugs khang gi tho/ chu spre'u dngos grub gling dkar bdud 'bur sku
gsar bzhengs kyi byin rten gzungs bzhugs tho/ thar rtse rdo rje 'chang gi sku spur snyan shal gyi zhal byang / gzim 'od nas mkha' spyod be'u bum gsar bzhengs sbyar byang
/ rnam sras sku bzhengs tshul/ pu trar rdor gong phul ba'i zhal byang / chu spre'u sgo rum nang so smug chung bcas su snyan shal zhal byang / rje rdo rje 'chang sku mched
dbus phebs skabs bco brgyad du sbyor gnang gi snyan shal zhal byang / gos sku zhal 'byed skabs kyi tho chung / lha chen mkhan gsar bsko skabs phun sum tshogs pa'i bkra
shis kyi tho/ /thub bstan rnam rgyal gyi mkhan gsar bsko skabs kyi tho/ 'jam 'don bya tshul/ dus mdos skabs 'chams sku 'thon tshul/ dus mdos nyir dgur mgon po 'khor bcas
kyi sku 'chams mdzad tho/ dus mdos chen mo gtong tshul/ dus mdos zor las pa'i nyer mkho/ g.ya' lung 'jag gshongs kyi sku 'bum nyams gso'i gzungs tho/ lcang can gung gi snyan
shal zhal byang / rnam 'phyang chu stod sa paN 'khrungs tshes thog gser khrir skyabs mgon sku gdung mchog nas rnam 'grel gzhung skyor mdzad skabs 'phan phul ba'i zhal
byang / yab rje'i dgongs rdzogs bla mchod skabs kyi chos spyod tho/ dpe khang chos mdzod chen mo'i debs kyi mgo brjod dang sbyar byang/ phyA phrin nor bu mchog rgyal sa
lugs ltar gtong tshul/ sgrol ma g.yul mdos gtong tshul/ phur sgrub chen mor nyer bar mkho ba'i yi ge /lcags 'then mi 'dra ba'i khyad par gyi yi ge /hor zla gsum pa'i mgon
mdos/ bzhi pa'i dam

tshig bskang gso/ mus chen mchod 'bul/ drug pa'i tshes bzhi/ drug pa'i bco lngar zhal dro lhums zhugs dus ston mchod 'bul/ dus mdos gzabs ma/ dmag zor ma'i mdos/ 'dod khams
ma'i bskang gso dngos grub rol mtsho dang rjes 'brel mdos gzhung / lcags yos dbo zlar zhag bzhi 'dod khams rje khol gyi mdos chog /zhal gyi mdos/ pu tra ming sring gi gtor
chen/ tshogs bdag /rje rdo rje 'chang gi gsung rtsom bektse'i gtor bzlog /hor zla bzhi par grags blo ba'i dgongs rdzogs gsang 'dus las byi nas bzung mchod phreng mchod
sprin rgya mtsho 'dzugs par mdzad dus dang / sa glang dmar chen gtor bzlog mdzad skabs/ rdo rje gzhon nu'i smad las rjes gnang / rdo rje gzhon nu dang gur zhal sogs kyi
gtor bzlog chig sgrub dang sgrub grogs nyung ngu'i bya tshul rnams kyi debs dang / phur bzlog gi dzam 'gros kyi tho/ rdo rje gzhon nu'i byin dbab kyi rol yig /rgyan mchog
dus mchod dpyad khra/ dkar bstod gsar rtsom 'dzugs gnang gi dpyad khra/ bka' 'gyur rin po che zhag bzhi pa tshugs dus kyi dpyad khra/ rje rdo rje 'chang sku mched sku dogs
skabs dge 'dun bsnyen bkur gyi dpyad khra/ me bya rta zla'i nyi shur gnang ba'i dpyad khra sogs te dkar chag bca' yig debs dang dpyad khra'i skor rags tsam smos zin nas//
lnga pa bskang mdos phrin 'chol gtor bzlog ru mtshon skor ni/ dam tshig bskang gso'i ngag 'don/ dam tshig bskang gso'i sngon 'gro bshom yig zur bkol/ mgon po bcu bdun
ma'i bskang ba/ mgon po gyi ljangs lugs bcu bdun ma'i gtor bsngo/ mes srong kun phan gyis zhus brag rdzong bdag bskyed sngon 'gro'i lha brgyad zhal gtso 'khor bcas kyi gtor
bsngo/ stobs 'phrog dbang por bskang bshags phrin bcol mdor bsdus/ sde dge bu skyes kyis zhus gtor chog khyer bde/ gtor chog

nyung ngu sde dge bu sgos zhus pa/ dur bdag gtor bsngo gur zhal rdo rje rab brtan ma tshe ring ma bcas kyi gtor bsngo/ khu spe mkhan slob kyis zhus gtor bsngo nyung ngu/ rtse
drung bskal bzang bstan dar gyis zhus gtor bsngo nyung ngu/ lcags sbrul spu hrang pa dgon drug phyogs bsgrigs skabs zhus ngor yang gsang bdag bskyed sngon 'gro'i phyag
bzhi ma ning rnam sras bcas kyi gtor bsngo bskang ba phyogs bsgrigs/ tsi dmar gtor bsngo bsdus pa/ bse khrab pa'i gtor bsngo/ rnam sras gtor bsngo/ stobs 'phrog dbang po'i
gtor bsngo/ yi dam chos srung rnams kyi gtor bsngo bskong ba phyogs bsgrigs/ dmar po skor gsum gyi gtor bsngo/ tshogs bdag gtor bsngo/ gur gyi mgon po'i thugs dam bskang
ba'i rim pa rgyal dbang rjer phul ba/ tshangs pa zhi drag gi gsol mchod/ rta mgrin dang tsi dmar zur 'brel mchod phrin/ tsi dmar gtor ma'i las mtha' rnams kyang rgyal
ba'i dbang por phul ba/ legs ldan ma'i sku phebs skabs kyi dam bzhag dang / mdung dmar can phyag mtshan bzhi pa'i 'bur sku gnang skabs de'i gtor bsngo bskang ba/ legs ldan
ma zhi drag mchod tshul/ mchod phreng / gtor 'bul bsdus pa/ de'i phrin las rnams glo bo rgyal bor gnang ba/ mgon po che chung / lha mo zung / yam shud dmar po/ /pu tra
ming sring rnams la bskang thung grangs gsog ched mdzad pa/ 'on rgyal sras rin po che'i ngor mdzad dam tshig bskang gso'i reg zig /nag po chen po'i bzlog mdos bya tshul/
mgon mdos kyi shom yig /mdos thams cad kyi dkris byed tshul/ tsa tu rmu kha'i gtor mdos zung 'brel gtong tshul/ pu tra'i zor

mdos kyi dmod bcol/ pu tra ming sring gi drag po'i gtor chen/ gtor bzlog dang gang la sbyor rgyu'i dmod bcol dang de gsham g.yul mdos dmod bcol/ chos rgyal sku lnga dang che
btsan yab rkya bdun gyi rten mdos gsal byed/ phur bzlog bshad pa'i mtshams sbyor dang de'i dmod bcol/ nag po chen po'i man ngag drug cu pa'i lhan thabs/ yang de'i lhan
thabs/ de'i bshad pa'i mtshams sbyor/ de'i skabs su nyer mkho'i sngags dang / mchod pa/ bskul rnams phyogs bsgrigs/ lha brgyad zhal gtso 'khor tsi dmar mched bdun bcas la
bstod bskul las bzhi'i dmigs pa bcas/ tsi dmar gnad bskul/ rdo rje gzhon nu'i gtor bzlog 'bring po/ /'jigs byed drug cu pa ngor lugs kyi skabs su mkho ba'i zin bris/ stobs
'phrog zhing skyong dbang po'i bsnyen sgrub bya tshul/ de'i dmigs pa'i lhan thabs/ de'i dmod bskul/ gur zhal gtor bzlog gi zur 'debs/ chos srung dmod bskul bsdus pa/ gur
lcam dral gsar bskrun phrin 'chol/ gur zhal sogs kyi phrin 'chol/ 'gor thub pa'i rgyal tshab dpal ldan sa skya zhes yod pa'i phrin 'chol/ rdo rje rab brtan ma'i snyan
shal phrin 'chol/ yang der bstod cing phrin las 'chol ba/ tsa tu rmu khar phrin 'chol kA li mdzes phreng / dbon lha rgyal nas bskul ngor sde dge'i gdung rabs myur 'byon phrin
'chol/ lha btsun ngag dbang lhun 'grub dar rgyas kyis zhus pa'i phrin gsol/ rje btsun sa skya pa'i gdung rabs myur 'byon phrin 'chol gtso bsdus/ dkar bdud lcam dral
phur srung dang bcas pa'i bstod pa/ ma hA kA lar bstod pa bstan srung dgyes pa'i lha'i rol mo/ /grang chen bektser brag rtsa rje'i sprul sku myur 'byon phrin 'chol/ me stag
bstan pa spyi rim gtor bzlog skabs kyi phrin 'chol

chos skyong gtso bsdus kyi phrin 'chol/ mtshan ltas ngan pa zhi phyir gsal byed rdor gling du mdzad pa'i 'phrin 'chol/ gur lha bcu gnyis ma'i mchod gtor phrin 'chol sngags
bcas/ bka' blon thon ngor mdzad pa'i rgyal chen rnam lnga sogs la phrin 'chol/ gnam the dkar por phrin las bskul tshig /tsi dmar sku rten khri smon par sku chas phul dus
kyi phrin bskul/ rgyal chen rigs lnga'i phrin gsol shlo ka gcig /me glang dbyar mjal dus tsi dmar la thod bcings khrab gdan sogs phul dus kyi phrin gsol/ dus mchod du pu
tra dmar por drug ldan rten sogs phul dus kyi phrin 'chol/ gur lcam dral gdong bzhi pa sogs la ru mtshon 'dzugs chog rgyas pa/ de'i rnam gzhag dbyangs rol chog bsgrigs/ gur
lha brgyad kyi ru mtshon 'dzugs chog /stobs 'phrog dbang por ru mtshon 'dzugs chog /me bya khri phebs skabs skyed lhas su thug chog gsal byed/ de'i mnga' gsol/ dmag zor
ma'i ru mtshon 'dzugs chog /mgon po'i gsang ba'i las mkhan lngar ru mtshon 'dzugs chog /gsang ba'i las mkhan pu tra lcam sring la mnga' gsol gyi tshigs bcad thun mong ma
yin pa/ gnod sbyin dregs pa lcam dral gyi thug chog /tsi dmar la brten pa'i ru mtshon 'dzugs chog /de'i mnga' gsol/ bse khrab pa'i ru mtshon 'dzugs chog /yam shud dmar
po'i phyi rten 'dzugs chog /'dod khams ma'i gsol kha dang mnga' gsol bya tshul/ dur bdag dkar bdud phur srung bcas kyi mnga' gsol/ bektse lcam dral gyi mnga' gsol/ rje btsun
sa skya pa'i bla ri dang bla mtshor gnas pa'i sman rgyal gnyis kyi gsol mchod/ stag 'tsher gangs mchod gtong tshul/ gnod sbyin rnam gnyis mchod chog /bsam yas

dbu rtse rigs gsum gling bzhi gling phran jo mo gling gsum sogs kyi gnas srung rnams la gser skyems 'bul tshig /khyung lung lha mo'i gsol kha/ srid zhi'i mgron la gtor 'bul
bsdus pa/ smyug la khu sbe chos sde'i gzhi bdag thog rgod bkra shis kyi gsol kha/ bse khrab pa'i gsol mchod/ yang phur srung mar mchod gtor 'bul tshul/ 'go ba'i lha lnga
dang brtan ma bcu gnyis mchod tshul/ pho lha skya ser gsol mchod sogs bskang mdos phrin 'chol gtor bzlog ru mtshon skor rnams rags bsdus su brjod zin nas// // ! drug pa
dri lan sogs sna tshogs pa'i skor ni/ gnas gsar rdo rje 'chang la 'jigs byed skor gyi dri ba lan bcas/ gzhan yang lha chen mkhan po chos bkra shis/ zhal dkar mkhan po ngag
dbang shes rab/ zhe drung sogs la dri ba mdzad lan bcas mang du mchis shing / thub bstan rnam rgyal dpal mgon zhal la bcol dam gnyer gtad kyi yi ge /chos srung la gnyer
gtad bka' bsgo/ rje btsun sa skya pa'i gdung rabs la brten pa'i bka' bsgo/ bka' bsgo'i yi ge spyir btang dmigs bsal bcas/ cha zhabs khams drung bcu dbon klung rta 'dzugs
yig /brul gtor bka' gdams lugs/ chu gtor grangs gsog byed tshul/ lan gtor gtong tshul/ 'byung bzhi gtor ma/ rnal 'byor ma'i tshogs mchod/ yang tshogs mchod bdud rtsi 'khyil
ba/ bar do ngo sprod kyi gdams ngag rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum/ theg chen lam gyi snying po/ /lo glud lag len dang bcas pa/ rnam sras rigs chen bco lnga'i gtor ma'i rnam
gzhag /sa skya bskor dpon ma Ni bar nye mkho'i yi ge /mgon dkar dmag zor bsang mchod/ rnga gzungs/ khams ab la sku skyer 'jigs byed bris thang rgyab yig /gnyan phul byung
bas

bzhengs pa'i sa chen zhal thang phyag nas ma 'dzam gling 'od gsal gyi sgo khyim sku brnyan gzungs gzhug la phul skabs de logs kyi yi ge'i 'dra shus/ yig bskur rnam gzhag /lcags
byi rgyal dbang rin po cher zhabs brtan skabs zhal bzhes zhu tho/ bsam yas rab khyung grwa tshang par phur 'tshams skyon 'don zin bris/ gdung chos su char 'bebs zin
bris/ a dkar thang sgar thog mdzad pa'i khrus gsol/ lcags byi tsi dmar sku phebs skabs dang / tshal gung thang du drag shugs dbang po/ /yang der bse khrab pa/ rgyal po shing
bya can/ dwags grwar bse khrab pa/ stag khu chos skyong rnams phebs skabs stsal ba'i yi ge /lha khang mkhan chen chos bkra shis 'thon skabs kyi brtags yig /gnas gsar
rdo rje 'chang la drag po sgrol dbang stsal skabs thol byung gi ljags rtsom yan lag bdun pa/ shi gson gdags yig /rtse gdong g.yag rwa lnga'i rten bshad/ rol 'chams sogs kyi
skabs kyi nyer mkho/ sku gsung thugs rten gyi 'dod gsol/ thub dbang 'jam dbyangs phyag rdor bcas kyi 'dod gsol/ skyed lhas rtag gtor gyi 'dod gsol/ yum bskal bzang bde
skyed bu khrid ma'i dgongs rdzogs rten gyi 'dod gsol/ gang de'i spur rus la sangs rgyas kyi mtshan 'bum bris su bstar ba'i 'dod gsol/ 'bum thang dngul gdung rin po cher
phul ba'i 'dod gsol/ bla brang shar thar rtse rdo rje 'chang gi sman sku 'dod gsol/ brag rtse rdo rje 'chang gi 'dra sku'i 'dod gsol/ 'gro mgon bstan pa sangs rgyas kyi nang
rten dngul gdung rin po che dang / gzim 'od rjes sgrub 'jam dbyangs kyi 'dod gsol/ bsam brling smon bde 'phel chen nas zhus pa dang / sangs

rgyas bzang po'i rje sgrub rdor sems sku'i 'dod gsol/ 'phags sde slob dpon gyis zhus 'dod gsol le tshan/ glo bor gnang ba'i legs ldan zhi drag gi sku'i 'dod gsol/ /phur sku'i
'dod gsol/ chos drags kyi sku'i 'dod gsol/ 'dar par stsal pa'i tshar chen rin po che'i sku'i 'dod gsol/ bdud 'dul mchod rten nyams gso skabs kyi 'dod gsol/ dgongs rdzogs
mchod 'bul thog yab rje thub chen 'dzam gling g.yas bzhag /sngags 'chang chen po/ /chos srung rnams bcas la snyan shal gyi 'dod gsol/ spos skyed rten gyi 'dod gsol/ bum
sgrub skabs kyi 'dod gsol/ sbal gdod chos mdzad zhal gyi snang brnyan 'dod gsol/ ji srid zhi dga' tshal du de mo rin po che'i snang brnyan 'dod gsol/ mda' dbon phu lung
pa'i ngor mdzad rgyal chen lnga'i 'dod gsol/ tsi dmar gsol go gsar bskrun skabs 'dod gsol/ 'on khri smon chos skyong snyan shal 'dod gsol/ spos dkar bla mas dgon de'i bla
ma bzang po'i sprul sku myur 'byon ched zhus 'dod gsol/ yer par bzhugs pa'i klu dbang gi sku'i 'dod gsol/ 'on rgod tshang du gnang ba'i sku rnams kyi 'dod gsol/ gdung chos
mgon sku'i 'dod gsol/ dpal rab rnga chung dang DA ru'i 'dod gsol/ pad tshal gyis zhus 'dod gsol/ gzim 'od nas rje rdo rje 'chang nyid/ tshe dpag /rnal 'byor ma/ gur rnams
gsar bskrun gyi 'dod gsol dang / mkha' spyod ma'i bris thang 'dod gsol bcas te de rnams kyi sgo nas dpyad gsum rnam par dag pa'i bka' rtsom rnams rags rim tsam smos
zin cing / da dung 'dir ma 'thus pa pod long tsam yod tshod bcas ljags rtsom gyi phreng ba tshar du dngar ba rje rdo rje 'chang chen po nyid kyis bstar bar mdzad pa 'di dag
ni/ ji skad du/ dge sbyong phal cher thos pa nyung / thos pa de

dag brtson pa nyung / /sdom brtson phal cher bkur ba nyung / /bkur ba de dag sdom brtson nyung / /sbyin bdag chos la dad pa nyung / /dad pa can gyi mchod bya dman/ /mchod pa
de dag log 'tsho'i rgyu/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar snyigs ma lnga ches cher bdo ba'i dus 'dir chos don du gnyer ba sogs nyung ba dang / don gnyer yod pa rnams kyis kyang dam
pa gong ma'i gsung zab brling dang ldan pa rnams myur du mi rtogs pas/ dam pa gong ma'i gsung la gzhi mdzad de nag 'gros 'ba' zhig tu bkod par mdzad pa 'di ni thugs rje
dang dgos pa khyad par can du 'khums pas/ rjes 'jug rnams spro dga'i 'dzum sgros bzhad pa'i 'os su gyur lags/ de dag gi don bsdu na/ bcu phrag rig byed nye ba'i yongs 'dzin
las/ /brgyad khri bzhi stong chos phung 'dod 'jo'i dpal/ /mang thos rna ba brgyad pa'i blo gros su/ /ris med 'khyil ba'i gtam 'di srid na gsal/ /rgyu des don gnyer legs
bris skal bzang can/ /so so'i ring lugs sde bzhi'i gdong 'bab dpyid/ /snying gi bdud rtsir bzung ba'i rgyun 'di ko /bsregs bcad brdar ba'i gser bzhin ngang tshul bzang
/ /bde skyid 'byung gnas bstan 'dzin rin chen snying / /dbus gtsang khams kyi yul grur nyer bkram nas/ /rang rang 'dod don 'bad med 'jo ba'i gsos/ /bskrun 'dir mi dad blo
ldan su zhig mchis/ /dpal mgur longs spyod 'khor lo'i lding khang na/ /rang 'dra'i rdo rje rnon po zlos pa'i gar/ /cir yang bsgyur 'dis legs bshad char bzhin nyil/ /skye
dgu'i tsha gdung sel ba'i grogs kyi mchog /ma rtogs log rtog the tshom mdud pa'i rgya/ /'grol byed dam pa'i zhal lung sor mo'i 'phrul/ /mthong grol nag 'gros bklags chog
'di na ho/ /thugs la bzung zhing skal ldan rigs kyi bu/ /zhes kyang

smras so// // ! gnyis pa bsam sgom 'chad rtsod kyis mtshon lugs brgya'i mdzad phrin kun gsal gyi tha gru ltar yangs shing rgya che ba'i nang nas bka' 'bangs kyi tha shal mu
to ba bdag gis cha shas tsam zhig rnyed pa rnams go rim bzhin lo khams so so'i nang du ji mdzad ma 'khrul bar ston pa la/ dgung grangs bcu gnyis pa lcags sprer gser khri
rin po cher mnga' gsol grub nas rim gyis/ rje rdo rje 'chang gang gi bsti gnas gsar pa byang mar gong 'khod kyi zhal ngo sogs bka' chos rin po che zhu mi rnams kyi steng
/ phyag gnyer mgron gnyer sogs 'ga' zhig 'phar ba'i nyi shu skor la/ sa lo'i yig steng nas rje btsun 'jam pa'i dbyangs dmar ser gyi rjes gnang stsal skabs yab rje rdo rje
'chang nyid kyis thog steng nas ci 'dra byung 'gro'am dgongs te gzigs pas/ grub 'phral rje rdo rje 'chang nyid la de lta bu'i gnang tshul rnams sgo gangs nas legs par 'dug
ces dbugs dbyung gzengs bstod kyang stsal to/ /de nas rim gyis lo nad der 'brum nad dang 'bur yan gnyis char byung ste byings kyis dbye dka' ba'i dogs gnas che skabs/
yab rje mchog tu mdzod 'dzin rgyal mtshan rin chen nas gnas tshul yang yang zhu gnang gi phyir phebs su 'brum pa min tshul kho na byon pa ni/ gzhan ngo srung ched dang gtam
sbir sna tshogs kyis bstan lar gnod dogs re zhig 'brum pa min tshul kho na gsung mur yum mchog nas thugs sgrub tshes bcu'i cho ga brgya tshar grangs gsog 'grub nyer rdo
rje tsher mas bro 'tshal skabs bad rlung yin tshul gleng rkyen gyis spang blang ji bzhin pa ci yang ma gnang zhing / rnga rol me nyi sogs spang bya blang byar mdzad kyang
nyam nyes su ma gyur ba'i grub rtags 'di ni rje rdo rje 'chang nyid kyi'ang chu yos lo'i mdzad pa 'og tu 'chad rgyu dang mtshungs pas yum sras kyi grub mtshan ngo mtshar
can du 'khums so/ /de nas

sku mched rnams gzim skyil gsar pa las 'phos te rje nyid rtse'i sku yon khang dang / a lce drung sku mched gzim shar rgyal yum dang zhal rgyas skabs mchog dman mtha' dag yab
rje rdo rje 'chang rgyun sku gcong che ba'i stabs da lam ci 'dra yong ngam snyam ci bya gtol med du gyur pa'i ngang nas/ rje nyid kyis mtshon zhal ngo rnams dang phyag
gnyer chos sde lho byang drung ser skya cha zhabs khams drung sogs nas rang rang gi 'byor tshogs dang chabs gcig rten 'brel gyi gnad dang ldan pa'i zhabs brtan rdo rje'i
re khA can/ sngon 'jam mgon sa skya paNDi ta chen pos gang gi yab dpal chen 'od po dang / bu ston rin po ches grub dbang zla seng la phul ba sogs kyi rgyun bzang dang zang
zing gi dngos po phongs med du spungs te spyi bye brag gi rim gro bsgrub pa dang / lhag par mdzod 'dzin nas zhabs pad yun ring du bstan pa'i zhal bzhes zhus skabs/ ngos
la 'brum nad kyis skyon mi yong sems las mi dgos phebs pa bzhin yab mes gong ma'i rnam thar ltar gyi lha 'brum dkar po bzhes te zhag bcu skor la sangs dengs kyis/ gzhi thog
dbang khang theg chen rin po che'i bzhugs khri'i steng nas rje rdo rje 'chang chen po sku mched lnga sogs skal ldan gyi slob bu bco lnga tsam la/ rnal 'byor dbang phyug
birWa pa'i bzhed gzhung / yongs rdzogs bstan pa rin po che'i nyams len/ gsung ngag rin po chen lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa tshogs bshad smin grol cha lag dang bcas pa gnang
ba gsan pa'i mgo tshugs te/ snang gsum rgyab chos su bla ma rgya bod/ gong ma lnga/ tshogs nyan/ dkar brag /zhang brag /dpal tshul/ buddha shrIH ngor chen/ mus chen/
kun mkhyen rnams kyi rnam thar/ gsung ngag khog phub legs bshad 'dus pa'i rgya mtsho/ sa skya bka' 'bum lung 'phros gang 'gro/

sems bskyed chen mo/ slob ma rjes 'dzin/ zhal gso'i ljags bsnyen rnams snron zla'i tshes dgu'i bar la gnang skabs su'ang yab rje rtsa ba'i bla ma dam pa la sngar dang ye mi
'dra ba'i thugs dad bcos min du rje rdo rje 'chang chen po la 'khrungs pa ni gzhung nas gsungs pa bzhin gyi bla ma'i byin rlabs thugs rgyud la zhugs pa ni dam pa'i rnam
thar du gor ma bkum/ de lo'i bsam brling lha mo mchod la rje rdo rje 'chang a lce drung sku mched bcas phebs/ de tsam nas bzung rje nyid skabs 'ga' ma gtogs lha mchod la
phebs pa ni rnam pa kun tu'o/ /de mtshams nas 'di khul la nad de je cher mched pas yab rje mchog nas gsung chos 'phro shol mdzad de thub bstan skyong ba'i mel tshe chen po
rnams la phrin 'chol dang / zhal ngo rnams la 'jam nag /khyung khra nag /rta mgrin skyer sgang / rnam 'joms/ sme dud sogs kyi rjes gnang dang / brgya bzhi/ ma mdos/ glud
rdzong rigs la thugs 'grus dang / ljags chu/ bsrung ba/ rim gro'i zhal bkod rnams bka' drin che skabs gzhung zhabs rin po che nas mda' dpon pad lcang lha rdzong sku tshab
sogs mngags pas 'o brgyal rma thog shu brtsegs kyi rjes su snyeg pa lta bu dang / rim gyis don dam rdo rje lta bu'i sku mchog brnyes su zin pa'i rje rdo rje 'dzin chen
pos kyang kun rdzob ltar snang dang bstun par mdzad de snyun bab lci bar bzhes rung / spyi bye brag gi bsod nams kyi mchod sdong chen por 'gyur med rdo rje gsum gyi rang
bzhin du mdzad pa'i sku drin yang bskal par gzhal ba'i go skabs dang bral/ de lo'i gro bzhin badzra kI la ya'i sgrub mchod kyang dbu rtse rnying mar tshugs shing rtsa 'chams
nang du mdzad nas brub 'chams sa tshogs su mdzad chog dang / nad thag phal cher khrums zla'i nang chod nas sgo rum steng 'og sogs su gtang rag mdzad de zla sked tsam
la zhal

ngo zhabs phyi rags bsdus bcas kha'u zhes pa pi cing gi skad du bzang po zhes pa dang / spo kha'u zhes pa ngan pa zer ba'i brda ste gong bzang po'i yul grur bdud rtsi sman
chab la phebs te dbyug zla nas lam 'bras kyi 'phro rgyu dbang / aShta'i bzlas lung / rgyud gsum dang rjes 'brel pod ser dmar/ rtsa rgyud brtag gnyis/ bskyed rim rnam bshad/
de la rtsod spang ngor chen dang kun mkhyen gyis mdzad pa/ yang kun mkhyen dang a mes zhabs kyis mdzad pa'i bskyed rim rnam bshad so so dang / bdud rtsi ril bu dang rdor
dril/ bgrang phreng dgang blugs bum pa rnams kyi bshad pa tsho gnyis/ kye rdor mngon dkyil rnams a mes zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ zhar byung du rdo rje phur pa'i mngon rtog
rgyas pa chos rje bla ma/ bsdus pa sa lo/ de'i dkyil chog a mes zhabs/ gur drag phrin gzhung rgya gar shes bzang / dbyug gu ma'i rgya gzhung klu sgrub dang / bod gzhung a
mes zhabs kyis mdzad skor/ gtor ma brgya rtsa sngags 'chang chen po/ /'od dpag med kyi nyal 'pho a mes zhabs/ rdo rje mkha' 'gro'i sbyin sregs lo/ sku dang gsung thugs ma/
gtum chen ma/ bdud rtsi lnga mchod/ nag po mchod rten/ chos nyid ma/ bskang gsar/ lha mo/ zhal/ pu tra/ dkar bdud rnams kyi sgos bskang rgya gar ba/ sa lo sogs kyis mdzad
pa/ dmag zor ma/ dur bdag /pu tra/ dkar bdud/ tsi dmar/ bse khrab pa rnams kyi bskang ba dang 'phrin 'chol/ sa skya'i rje btsun ma rnams a mes zhabs dang / gdung rabs
myur 'byon bskang phrin sngags 'chang kun dga' bkra shis/ rgyal gsol log 'dren tshar gcod yab rje mchog gi gsung / bstod pa srin sngon gang gsum/ ma skyes hUM yig rngams
'bar rab 'byams sangs rgyas bstan srung rgyas bsdus rnams kyi sde

tshan/ spyi stab srid zhi dpal 'byor ma sogs bskang skor/ chos spyod rab gsal lha mthil par mar bzhugs dang ma bzhugs kha shas/ bstan pa gso chog mangga'i mtshan gyi gsung
sogs ljags lung phon che ba dang / gsung ngag cha lag lam zab phyi nang/ bir bsrung phyi nang/ bla ma rin 'byung / tshar gsum khugs pa rnams kyi byin rlabs bcas zla gsum
tsam gyi ring chos char bdud rtsi'i zil dngar 'bebs par mdzad pa'i rgyu lam dbang gi bka' sgrub sogs kyi skabs rje rdo rje 'chang nyid kyis kyang zhal rgyas mdzad pa lags/
de skabs kyi bar seng rnams la yab rje mchog dang / dbu byed ye shes rgyal mtshan/ brtson 'grus ye shes sogs las bde kye gsang gsum sogs gdan sa chen por bzhugs pa'i cho
ga phyag len dbyangs rol sogs gsan sbyangs mtha' chod pa bka' drin bskyangs/ smin zla tsam la nad khrun yongs rdzogs chod nas mgo zla'i bde mchog sgrub mchod dang dus mdos
sogs rje rdo rje 'chang nyid kyi thugs 'gan bzhes shing / dus mdos kyi nyer gsum nyin gang gi yab rje dam pa nyid 'chams sku rnams la snyan shal 'bul bar phebs nas gral
gsham du tshogs phyag mdzad pa'i tshe/ rje rdo rje 'chang nyid bzhugs khri'i steng mi tshugs pa lta bu'i 'tsher nyams byung zhes bka' stsal to/ /de dag gi don bsdu na/
dmar ser dhIHyig spro bsdu'i ngang mo yis/ /skal ldan yid kyi chu bya'i sna drangs nas/ /mtha' bral mkhyen rab chu gter chen po'i ngogs/ /rab tu sbyar 'di chos sgo gsum
par nges/ /phyi nang rkyen gyis mi brdzi rdo rje'i skur/ /col chung tsher ma'i ming gi pho nya des/ /bag ma phyir bsnyags la 'dod 'bras sbyin pa'i sgo/ /phyi phral skyengs
te mi mngon dbyings su dengs/ /mngon gyur sa la dbang ba'i bi rU'i gzhung / /DA ki'i zhal rlangs 'thul ba'i cha lag bcas/ /chos kyi 'khor lo'i mdzod du

nyer bzung nas/ /mkhas mang dbus su rdo rje'i khri la 'gyings/ /zhes kyang smras so// // ! dgung grangs bcu gsum du phebs pa lcags bya rta zla'i nang yab rje mchog nas dgung
keg rkyen sel la dmigs sgo rum du tshe sgrub bcad rgya dang / slar pho brang du byon skabs rje rdo rje 'chang sogs nas rtags rten 'brel bzang min zhu gnang gi phyir phebs
su/ ltas kyang bzang bar rang ma byung / bzlas pa 'gro chung / bse mgon bzhugs khyim du bas 'grib pa lta bus mi mthong / yab rje de nyid yang yang rmi ltas su phebs pa
zhig byung gdung spun rang la gsung ngag slob bshad 'di phral du 'phrod re byed ces yang yang gsungs pas rje nyid kyi thugs la skyo snang drag po zhig 'khrungs/ nag zla'i
mjug tsam la gzim shar mgon khang du yab sras zhal rgyas nas pu tra'i mdos zor sgrub gnang gis phyir 'phen mdzad/ sa ga'i ril sgrub la rje nyid la'ang phebs shig pa gnang
yang gsang 'dus sgrub mchod la thog mar phebs rgyu dang thug pas dgongs zhu mdzad/ snron zla'i lha mo mchod la yab rje nyid ma phebs na legs tshul zhu bar mdzad pas/ 'di
lo cis kyang 'gro slar mi shes gsungs nas phebs pas rtsa skyed kyi thad tsam du rgyu mtshan med par thugs la skyo shas drag po 'khrungs byung zhes rje rdo rje 'chang nyid
la bka' stsal/ de nas mangga'i mtshan can gyi yig steng nas grub thob tshe dbang zhig stsal ba rje nyid kyis kyang gsan/ tshes dgu nas bzung yab rje rdo rje 'chang nyid
la 'di yin med pa'i snyun gzhi sku shed nyams stobs che zhing gsol dang je zhan du 'gro ba las snyun zug sogs cher med pa zhig bzhes skabs/ gsol sman sku rim sogs 'thud
shol med pa dang / lhag par mkha' 'gro bsun bzlog yang yang / gzhan yang gang 'tshams kyi mdzad sgo rnams rje rdo rje 'chang nyid kyi dbu g.yas tshang mas bka' drin che
mur dang

bzhes yong re dang / yab rje mchog nas kyang gsung ngag slob bshad gnang shag gi mur brag rtsa rdo rje 'chang dang / thub bstan mkhan chen tshul khrims bzang po'ang byon pas
mkhan chen la sngar nas rkyen sel zhu mu bzhin tshe dbang gur drag khro bcu'i rjes gnang sogs gsan zhing / gzim chung nas khyogs la gdan 'dren zhus dus mkhan chen des ag
gsung ba dang spyan chab mdzad/ de dus gsung 'phros rang bzhin gyi skabs nged nas chos rnams ma 'phrod pa byung na thar rtse dang / brag rtsa ba sogs la zhus shig gsungs/
tshes bcu gsum par sku khams res 'jog dang de nas je zhan gyis spyi sger nas zhabs brtan sku rim rnams bstud mar mdzad mu'i bcu dgu nas thugs dam nyams bzhes rnams sngar
las yun ring bar mdzad pa dang / mgul glo dang mnal yer ba sogs la glo gcog mnal 'gugs kyi gto dang / rje rdo rje 'chang nyid la ljags sngags 'bul dgos kyi bka' bzhin
la thugs 'tsher shin tu che ba 'khrungs kyang / bla ma mnyes byed gang yin bya/ /zhes dang / sems dge ba la nyes pa med/ /ces sogs thugs mtshor dgongs te man ngag sdud sud
nas 'byung ba'i sngags dang gto sogs yang dag mdzad/ nyer bzhi'i nyin bzhugs g.yab tu bzhugs skabs bzhugs stan phyogs bzhir bsgyur gsung ba bzhin mdzad dus spyan nam mkhar
had kyis gzigs/ de skabs rje rdo rje 'chang sku mched yum mchog rnams nas spyi sgos bstan pa rin po cher dgongs nas zhabs pad brtan dgos kyi gsol 'debs mdzad pas/ 'dun
pa gang drag bgyid gsungs pa las gzhan ci yang bka' ma stsal/ de dus snron zla'i mchod 'bul nyer lngar mdzad skabs yin pas chos grwa lho byang nas kyang zhabs brtan gsol
'debs dang / rje rdo rje 'chang nyid kyi mgon des zla rer chag med gnang ba'i gur drag phrin gzhung bka'

drin che bas nyin phyed yan la gsal 'gyur med kyang de nas je zhan gyis gnas slob de spyan chab mdzad bzhin par rje nyid kyi sku drung du byung bas/ thugs skyong ngal gyis
gsung chen po shor byung zhes bka' stsal/ de mtshams nas gzim chung du phebs dgos kyi bka' bzhin mdzad pas gzhan rnams zhabs brtan gso 'debs mdzad mu dang / mdzod 'dzin des
snyan sgron mang du zhu ba'i skabs yab rje mchog nas rje rdo rje 'chang nyid la spyan cher gyis gzigs nas/ sna'ang grang mor song ba dang dbugs 'di'i stabs bcas nam phyed
tsam las mi thub pa 'dra gsung bas thugs 'thor nas ci mdzad gtol med ltar gyur pa'i sgo nas bzhugs gnas su byon te/ gsol 'debs la rtse gcig tu thugs gzhol ba'i skabs
su gzim chung zangs drar 'od 'khyug pa dang / zangs dra skad 'byin pa sogs rje rdo rje 'chang nyid kyis mngon sum du gzigs pas dpa' bo mkha' 'gro'i bsu ba yin par thag chod
dgongs pa 'khrungs / gang ltar yab rje rdo rje 'chang nas rtogs ldan chos nyid rang grol byon byung bzhugs stan things gsungs pa yang yang phebs mu'i thor 'go ma zin tsam
la zhing 'di'i gdul bya re zhig rdzogs te/ dag pa chos kyi dbyings kyi ngang du bde bar gshegs pa'i tshul bstan 'phral/ dbu las rlangs pa skya bun gyis byung bas dbu
zhwa'ang chu rgyun can du gyur pa dang / de nas spur chas rnams gsol te mchod rdzas dbus su bzhugs su gsol/ nyer drug nas rje rdo rje 'chang sku mched sogs kyis gnas bcur
dgongs rdzogs bla mchod bka' drin che zhing / de'i tshe spyir dbyar dus dang / sgos paN chen thams cad mkhyen pa'i mchog sprul rin po che gang gi gdan sar phebs nye'i stabs
mi dbang chen po sogs gtsang phebs dang / lhag par dgongs bskor ma 'gugs par gsang rgya dam por mdzad/

gnam gang la sku gdung rin po che gnas bcur phebs pa nas bzung dgung zhag zhe dgu'i bar rje rdo rje 'chang sku mched gnas slob sogs sgrub grogs lngas dpal kye rdo rje'i ras
dkyil steng nas dgongs rdzogs sgrub mchod mdzad skabs nam mkha' g.ya' dag cing me tog gi char nyil ba sogs byung ba'i rkyen gyis/ 'ga' zhig gi blor zhing khams brjes pa
min nam snyam pa shar rung gleng brjod ma nus/ sku rim du zhal 'phangs te mang ja mchod 'bul sogs mdzad pa dang / rje rdo rje 'chang chen pos drug pa'i bdag med sgrub mchod
la'ang phebs/ dgongs bskor 'khor bstun yab yum zung gi gzim chung dngos thog nas 'jal/ mang 'gyed/ brgya mchod sogs grangs mang dang / 'dus sder bla ma mchod chog tshar
kha shas/ gtsang dbus gnas rten la mchod 'bul/ dgon du mar mang skol sogs dang / gdan sa gzhung nas 'dus tshogs su bde kye gsang gsum/ bdag med ma/ mkha' spyod ma/ kun
rig rnams kyi sgrub mchod zhag bcu bzhir mchod gtor gzabs shom/ bsnyen bkur gya nom pa/ grol nyin gzim chung nas 'gyed dang / gzhung nas mang ja sogs bsnyen bkur rgya che
ba mdzad/ zhal ngo so so/ chos sde rnam gnyis/ drung ser skya/ bla tshang khag /mi sde byings sogs nas rang 'byor dang bstun pa'i dge sgrub/ gdung 'bul/ rten bzhengs zhal
thebs sogs dpag med dang / gro bzhin ser 'du nyin gnyis la bsnyen bkur bzang ba/ gsum par thang ston mchod 'bul bsnyen bkur/ sbyin gtong sogs bla ma gong ma'i dgongs rdzogs
dang cha 'dra'i bsngo smon sogs rje rdo rje 'chang sku mched nas yang dag par gsal/ gzhan yang 'phral yun gyi dgongs pa zab mo rdzogs pa'i thabs bla na med pa rje rdo
rje 'chang chen po'i bka' gsang gis legs par

'doms nas/ zla ba de'i tshes mgor mgon khang khag bzhir phrin bcol sngon 'gro'i yab rje'i bsti gnas phun tshogs 'chi med rdo rje'i gur khang du/ rje rdo rje 'chang nyid dpal
kye rdo rje'i gzhi bsnyen la bzhugs stan 'jags pa ste 'di ni gzhi bsnyen thog ma'i skabs so/ /smin zla'i nang thar rtse rdo rje 'chang gis tshoms dmar du sbur bzhu mdzad
pa'i nub mo rje rdo rje 'chang nyid la bla mas rjes bzung gi mtshan ma 'di ltar 'khrungs te/ ser khang steng gi nam mkhar nyi zla'i 'og tsam na 'ja' sprin dmar po'i dbus
su yab rje de nyid sku mdangs dmar zhing sngags chas sku bem dmar po dang sa zhu bzhes shing / g.yon skyabs sbyin g.yas gos dmar la lam zab bir bsrung sogs kyi phyag dpe
yin dgongs pa zhig gril nas/ sku 'khris kyi nye gnas brgyud rje rdo rje 'chang nyid la stsal nyams can bzhugs pa la/ bzhugs g.yab g.yam skyor shar 'khris na'ang yab rje
de nyid bzhengs nas nam mkha' bzhugs pa'i yab rje rang gi sku la bshad pa mdzad pa zhig 'khrungs pa ni/ dus phyis rje rdo rje 'chang nyid rje btsun sa skya pa'i gser chos
kyis mtshon snyigs ma'i dus 'dir yongs rdzogs bstan pa rin po che'i mnga' bdag mdzad pa la sgrun zlas dben par 'byung zhing / skyabs gnas kun 'dus yab rje rdo rje 'chang
nyid kyis rnam kun rjes su 'dzin pa'i brda yang dag par gdon mi za zhing / de dus spur sgam nas gdung rus phran bu zhig rje nyid la byon pa ni/ phyis su gdung 'dzin gyi
go sar bzhugs dgos kyi brdar ngos 'dzin mdzad cing de nas gdung rus rnams 'gad gtsang btul nas sAtstsha dang bla ma yi dam sogs kyi sku par grangs mang gser mtshal sogs
kyis bsgyur ba rnams phyi rten/ nang rten/ dbu gser 'dra sku sgros gtsang / dus mchod thub dbang gnas brtan 'jim sku sogs kyi gzungs

dang / byin rten phran bu/ gdung 'gyed sogs gang 'tshams mdzad cing / gzhan yang zhal thang kha shas/ dus ja/ dus dran mchod 'bul/ kye rdor sgrub mchod/ ser 'du bcas so so'i
dkar chag dang / gtong debs su gsal ba bzhin zab dgongs chos dbyings de bzhin nyid du rdzogs thabs thugs bskyed spyi bye brag mang du mchis kyang 'dir de tsam mo/ /rgyas
pa ni yab rje de nyid kyi rnam thar du gsal zhing / de nas rje nyid kyis gdan sa chen po'i sbyin bdag 'ga' zhig la grub thob dang grub rgyal gyi tshe dbang tshar kha shas
yang dag par stsal ba'i dus su tshe chang phyogs kun tu lud par gyur to/ /de dag gi don bsdu na/ kye ma skyabs gcig mahA gu ru'i sku/ /zho 'thungs rus skyes rdo rje'i
rang bzhin de/ /snyigs ma'i rang mdangs chos bdud 'thab mo las/ /rten 'brel sgo brgyas bzlog pa'i gnas ma gyur/ /mkha' 'gro'i dbang phyug sgyu 'phrul gshog rgyangs kyis/
/sa 'di'i snod bcud dor nas dag pa'i mkhar/ /gshegs pa'i rjes su sku gdung za ma tog /bsod nams rten du stsal ba'ang ngal bso'i grogs/ /dgongs zab chos dbyings de bzhin ro
gcig tu/ /je cher mngon par rdzogs pa'i phyi nang rten/ /ring bsrel rnam bzhi'i gang bu gsar bskrun gyi/ /bka' gsang 'doms mkhas rgyal sras sems dpa' che/ /dag snang 'od
gsal nam mkha'i dkyil 'khor nas/ /gdod ma'i mgon po'i rang zhal chu 'dzin g.yos/ /byin rlabs zim char kun gzhi'i sa gzhi'i ngos/ /byon 'phral bde stong gsos kyi ngang du
'byams/ /ye shes byin zas sbyangs pa'i gdung rus dum/ /slar 'byung rten 'brel brda ni 'di na ho/ /sngags 'chang rgyal sras mchog gi ngang tshul gyis/ /'gran bral 'khon
rigs spel zhes 'doms min nam/ /zhes kyang smras so// // ! dgung grangs bcu bzhir phebs pa chu khyi lor thar rtse rdo rje 'chang nam mkha' bsam

grub kun dga'i mtshan dpe'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i drung du dge bsnyen gyi sdom pa yang dag pa bzhes shing / de'i dus su mtshan 'bul rgyu'i tho rengs thar rtse ba chen
por/ bud med sngon mo pi wang bsgyur bzhin pa zhig gis ngag gi dbang phyug kun dga' blo gros bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po zhes lung bstan pa bzhin du mtshan gyi
mnga' gsol mdzad pas/ rjes su rje nyid kyi gsung las/ kho bo la sngags 'chang gos dkar can du dgos pa'i brda de dus nas ka byung zhes yang yang gsungs/ de nas mi ring bar
mkhan po dbang phyug phun tshogs/ kun dga' zla 'od/ nam mkha' sangs rgyas/ grags pa/ kun dga' sangs rgyas sogs las slar yang thub pa 'od zer 'gyed spyan 'dren gyis/ mdo
las/ khyims pa rnams ni me 'obs na gnas pa lta bu'o/ /rab tu byung ba rnams ni bsil khang na gnas pa lta bu'o/ /zhes dang / klu sgrub kyis/ khrims ni rgyu dang mi rgyu'i
sa bzhin du/ /yon tan kun gyi gzhi rten legs par gsungs/ /zhes dang / sum brgya par/ nyon mongs dgra g.yul rgyal byed tshul khrims te/ /dge tshul brtul bzhugs chu lon brtsigs
pa dang / /'chi ba'i mche ba 'byin par byed pa'i thabs/ /rdzogs pa'i byang chub dpal nod dbang bskur yin/ /zhes sogs gsungs pa rnams thugs mtshor bskyil nas rab tu
byung bar mdzad de sngar gyi mtshan gyi steng du sangs rgyas bsnan pas/ de nas bzung ngag dbang kun dga' blo gros sangs rgyas bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po zhes
snyan grags don ldan khor yug ri bo'i khongs su'ang rgyu ba de nyid yongs su grags par gyur cing / de lo gdan sa chen po'i phur sgrub kyi tshogs dpon 'gan bzhes mdzad pa
nas bzung skabs 'ga' ma gtogs lo khams nang du 'khod min la ma ltos par rnam pa

kun tu'o/ /dbyug zla'i nang rje btsun sa skya pa'i yab chos bcom ldan 'das snying po kye rdo rje man ngag lugs kyi smin byed kyi dbang cha lnga zhal ngo rnams dang / las tshan
khag /chos gra nyi zla zung gi dge 'dun bcas la stsal ba de ni smin byed kyi dkyil 'khor du zhal slob rjes su bzung ba'i sgo dang po dang / mgo zla'i dus mdos chen mo'i
tshogs dpon gyi thugs khur yang bzhes shing / brag rtsa rdo rje 'chang blo gsal bstan 'dzin rgya mtsho'i sku drung du dbang / rjes gnang / lung sogs mang du gsan/ de nas
sde dge dpon bsod nams mgon po chibs bskyod kyis nyer bdun nyin gdan sar 'byor nas dus mdos ma grol bar gang mtshams kyi bdag rkyen yang dag par bka' gsang gis gdams so/
/de dag gi don bsdu na/ bag yod so thar khrims kyis sgo gsum mdzes/ /yab mes lugs bzang 'khrul med don ldan bskyangs/ /skal ldan smin grol lam gyis rjes su bzung / /rten
'brel mchod yon nyi zla'i dkyil 'khor rgyas/ /zhes kyang smras so// // ! dgung grang bco lngar phebs pa chu phag rgyal zla'i 'gor/ gang gi mdo smad sa skyong chen po nas
zhal rgyas kyi dga' ston dngos 'bul rmugs 'dzin dbang po'i gan mdzod zhal dbye ba lta bu sngon 'gro'i legs skyes gya nom pa stob par mdzad/ skabs 'dir zhu 'os 'di dag
kyang gleng ste/ rje rdo rje 'chang chen po de nyid ni bla ma gong ma rnams kyi rnam thar la zang zing gi dngos 'bul 'di dang 'di zhes brjod nyog can du so sor mang du smos
pa dang / don yod med la ma ltos par skye bo phal pa mang po'i ming bkod pa dang / brjod don bla ma de de'i ngo mtshar med pa'i rjod byed mdzes mtshon can dang / ngo mtshar
che chung ji ltar yang yin lugs drang po de mi bkod par a pha'i gsol zhal gtsang ma'i dpe bzhin sgro btags mang du bsnyad pa rnams

la ni rnam pa kun tu mi dgyes pas/ 'dir yang rdo rje'i gsung de nyid tsi ttar bcangs te bgyis pa'i khul du lags/ de nas khong dpon g.yog sogs la kye rdo rje man ngag lugs kyi
dbang chen 'ga' dang / grub thob dang ras chung pa'i tshe dbang sku dngos rnams la sgo rum ye shes mgon po'i sku drung du gur lha brgyad kyi rjes gnang dang sgrags bka'
bsgo sogs thugs 'dod kyi re ba yongs su chos kyi sgo nas khengs par mdzad/ de nas dad pa'i rtsa ba brtan po dang ldan na mthong thos dran reg kun don ldan du 'gyur ba'i
dri gtsang khang rnams su mchod 'bul gnas gzigs bsngo smon sogs yang dag pas mtshams sbyor rnams mdzad rjes gdan sa nas 'thon nye'i phebs phyag sogs lugs zung gi bdag rkyen
yang dag pa stsal nas/ bla ma gong ma rnams kyi phyag len phra mo tshun chad mi nyams dar rgyas su mdzad pa'i dam bca' thugs kyi dpal ber dam du bzung ste/ bde kye gsang
gsum/ bdag med ma/ mkha' spyod ma sogs gdan sa chen po'i tshugs sgrub mchod rnams kyi rdo rje slob dpon nar mar bka' drin che ba'i bar mtshams rnams su dbang bskur/ rjes
gnang / lung sogs/ chos 'chad kyis dus 'da' bzhin pa nas/ sa zla stobs kyi mgon po rnal 'byor dbang phyug gi dus chen dang bstun rgyun gyi bza' ba'i dam tshig bdud rtsi
ril bu sgrub pa'i sngon du kye rdo rje'i ljags bsnyen kha gso bdun phrag dang / chig sgrub thog mar gnang skabs phye ma dang / de nas ril bu 'phel che ba/ mdog legs pa/
ro bro ba sogs myong grol bdud rtsi ril bu zhes mtshan snyan dang ldan pa bskrun te kun ngo mtshar gyi dpal la 'god par mdzad/ dbyug zla'i yar tshes dge bar mgon khang
rnams su phrin 'chol mthar phyin gyis bcu bzhi 'khon dkon mchog rgyal po dang rje btsun brtse ba chen po'i dus chen gnyis 'dzom thog rje

rdo rje 'chang chen po nyid sku 'khor dang bcas/ 'dzam gling rten gyi gtso bo jo zhal rnam gnyis sogs dbus gtsang gi rten grags che rnams la mchod cing bsnyen bkur ba dang
/ ris med rgyal bstan rin po che dar rgyas yun brtan thugs smon gyi mtshams sbyor/ 'phags mchog phyag na padma'i sgyu 'phrul rol gar 'chang ba rgyal ba'i dbang po mchog /mahA
paNDi ta thams cad mkhyen gzigs chen po sogs la mjal phyag legs skyes bstar ba sogs kyi ched du/ gdan sa chen po dpal ldan sa skya nas chibs kyi kha lo bsgyur te bkra
shis dar rgyas kyi maNDal du gsol tsha/ dgon rgyas su bzhugs zhag /de nas rim gyis lcang gshongs/ lcags ri dang rtse na kha sogs su bzhugs zhag gis bsam grub sbug tu bla
brang mchog nas gzim gur/ bzhugs khri/ gnam rgyan sogs sngon 'gro'i thabs bsur mgron gnyer bgres pa/ gsol dpon chen mo/ dpon tshang chen mo sogs kyis mtshon drung 'khor
'ga' zhig dang / gzhis rdzong mi sna sogs kyis chibs bsus gsol ston zur gsos rnams legs paradagyes bzhes dang / de nas thams cad mkhyen gzigs chen po'i sku'i gan du phebs
skabs de zhabs kyi mdzod 'dzin chen po sku 'khor nas phyag mdzod 'gag tu bkra shis pa'i lha'i reg bya phul nas phyag gser gyi 'khor lo dbu gtsug tu bzhes/ rim gyi ma hA
paNDi ta chen po'i sku mdun du mjal dar rtse sprod bka' drin che nas mchog gi sprul pa'i sku rin po cher khri 'bul du/ tshan pa so so'i 'gor bkra shis pa'i mdzod btags kyis
jeng drangs/ dngul srang lnga bcu yod pa'i thum gnyis/ gos rgyan bzhi sprin ris yug /pho rta bzang ba/ tsan dan dmar po dum/ ljon lo 'khor drug bzhi/ 'bru dkar ltang
gnyis rnams so sos gtsos pa'i tshan pa bcu gcig /gtsos med kyi tshan pa bcu gnyis rnams gser

khri rin po cher mnga' gsol legs skyes su bstar bas rten 'brel gyi sgo brgya bzang dgur 'dzom pa dang chabs gcig /mjal rten du'ang bkra shis pa'i lha'i reg byas jeng drangs/
sa snying / rin gnyis bre chen/ rta pho/ ljon lo 'khor drug dang 'bru dkar ltang zung rnams kyis gtsos dang gtsos med kyi tshan pa rnams dgyes rdzas su phul ba bdag gir
bzhes nas/ mnyes gshin brtse ba'i gsung mchid zhib lhug dang / tshang mar gsol ston rgya che mu med lta bur stsal rjes mjal slog tu'ang rin gnyis kyis gtsos/ gos yug re
yod pa'i tshan pa bco lnga tsam dang / mdzod 'dzin chen po nas bzung sku 'khor ba tshang mar gsol ras gya nom pa stsal/ de zhabs kyi phyag mdzod rin po cher yang / dngul
srang lnga bcu'i thum sogs kyis gtsos tshan pa bde 'byung gi grangs ldan dang / mjal slog tu'ang dngul bre chen/ tshan pa bu ga'i grangs ldan bcas dang / de dus kyi sne shan
par sku gnyer dpon/ mgron gnyer/ lho gling pa bcas mchis shing / dngul gdung rin po che rnam gnyis kyi dbus dri gtsang khang rnams su mchod 'bul/ snyan shal/ ris med
pa'i bstan bstan 'dzin rgyas pa'i thugs smon gyi mtshams sbyor dang / 'dus tshogs dge 'dun sum stong tsam la bsnyen bkur dang thugs 'dod bzhin dngul gdung 'gag tu phyag dbang
/ chibs bsu skyel ba rnams la'ang gsol ras sbam mtho ba stsal ba sogs thugs brel rnams rim grub kyis chu shar du thab skyel dang bcas phebs te/ gser can bla spyi nas
ser phreng sogs kyis dgon par gdan drangs shing / gnas gzigs thugs smon mchod 'bul mang ja bsnyen bkur dam 'gyed 'dus tshogs la 'jam dbyangs dmar ser gyi rjes gnang / spyi
sger mjal phyag

dmangs phyag sogs 'gro don la thugs gzhol ba'i skabs shig zur khang sde pas/ rje btsun sa skya pa'i yab chos dmar po skor gsum gyi be'u bum pusta ka gsum phul bar phyis su'ang
rje rdo rje 'chang chen gyi gsung las/ ngos 'grul thog ma'i skabs 'byor ba'i be'u bum 'di dag rje btsun sa skya pa'i bstan srid la rten 'brel gyi la nye shin tu bzang
ba byung zhes yang yang gsungs shing da lta'ang dpe khang chos mdzod chen mor bzhugs su gsol ba lags/ de nas rim phebs kyis zangs mkhar sprul sku dang rin rdzong 'bras yul
skyed tshal sogs nas chibs bsu mjal zhu legs 'bul dang bcas der 'dus skya ser bgrang yas la khrom dbang / grwa tshang la bsnyen bkur dam 'gyed bcas stsal ba ni de skabs
sa dgon yongs la mdzad do/ /sang nyin byams chen gnas gzigs mchod 'bul smon lam snyan shal sogs kyang de skabs gnas gzigs thams cad kyi skabs su mdzad do/ /ngur smrig dang
kyog po gnyis nas ser phreng gis bsu skyel gyis rim pa/ de nas dpal de'u/ gzim phug /stag khu/ zhe re skyed tshal/ gsal byed rdo gling / snye thang rnams nas ser phreng
sogs kyis chibs bsu skyel dkar spro legs 'bul/ gnas gzigs/ 'gro don rnams mdzad rjes gsol tshigs sgang du gong sa mchog nas stsal ba'i chibs bsu brtse mgron sogs bcu gnyis
tsam dang / shod nas kyang de bzhin gyis sngun bsus mjal gur du phebs thog mi rje mchog gis mtshams zhu mgul dar sogs bstar bzhes dang / 'chi med dga' tshal bzhugs sgar
du phebs 'phral yang dga' ldan khang gsar nas mgron gnyer ched mngags kyis rtse shod du mtshams zhus lha dar sogs dang / bkur gsos bdag rkyen bla na med pa spyi sgos
nas mchod yon bstan lar dgongs pa'i gzigs bskyangs bka' drin che

zhing / smin zla'i tshes gsum nyin gzim chung nyi 'od 'khyil par rgyal dbang thams cad mkhyen gzigs mchog gi mjal phyag la rje rdo rje 'chang nyid kyis phyag 'bul mdzad pa
dang bstun rgyal ba'i dbang po mchog kyang gser khrir sku bzhengs kyis phyag len mjal dar phan tshun 'bul gnang / dbu thug sogs kyis dbug dbyung gzengs bstod dang / gsol
ja'i skabs phan tshun mnyes gshin pa'i bka' gsang rmad du byung bas dus 'das rjes/ mgron khang du dkar spro'i thog /rtse drung thugs dad can rnams kyi re skong dang / tshes
dgur legs skyes rten 'byung bstar bar mdzad pa'i sngon du 'gro ba maNDal gyi tshom bu/ mi shigs rdo rje'i re khA can gyis bzhugs stan/ sku gsung thugs kyi rten rnams dang
bcas gang gi spyan sngar 'khod de maNDal 'bul ba/ 'gro la bde skyid ma sogs kyi gsol 'debs/ zhal bzhes zhu ba rnams bka' drin che 'phral 'bul tshan bcu phrag lnga dang
nyag ma lngas lhag pa la gtsos yod nyer gcig /de phyin gtsos med rnams mchod yon zhal rgyas kyi legs lam bslu med rten 'brel gyi bdog pa brda mtshon tsam du phul bar rnam
kun don yod kyi rjes 'dzin mkhyen pa'i mtha' 'doms dang bcas mdzad sbyor gyi thog /lha ldan gyi yul gru mtha' dag 'ja' dang rmugs pas gang zhing / dgung g.ya' dag pa/
nyi ma'i 'od zer mngon par 'bar ba/ bar snang thams cad du me tog gi char pa bu yug tu 'tshubs par 'dug ces lha ldan skye dgu phal cher nas gleng mor bsgrags par gyur to/
/gnas de'i jo shAka rnam gnyis kyi dbus 'phrul snang gandho la chen po'i rten ji snyed pa'i spyan sngar/ stong mchod rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum de bas nang bzhin gyi 'bring
po'i mchod 'bul snyan shal/ rgyal bstan de 'dzin ris su ma phyed pa dar rgyas yun brtan thugs smon gyi mtshams sbyor sogs

dang / bcu gnyis la mi'i dbang por legs 'bul gyi snga rol du mi dbang yab sras/ dA las yab sras sogs drag bsdus rnams la bla ma zhi khro'i tshe dbang sogs thugs 'dod bzhin
stsal rjes legs skyes rnams brims shing / gong smos bzhin de skabs gdan sa chen po rtse gdong rten brten par bcas rje rdo rje 'chang nyid kyi phyag tu nor bdag po'i tshul
gyis son par gyur to/ /de nas ra mo cher mchod 'bul sogs gong bzhin dang / bcu gsum la ri bo gru 'dzin du chibs bskyod de jo bo lo ki shwa ra/ gser gdung chen po zhal rnam
gnyis kyi dbus rten ji snyed par mchod 'bul dang / bcu drug la rnam gser brgyud gsang ne'u thog tshogs khang gsar bzhengs la phyag nas/ sgrol ma rtsod rgyal/ rnam snang
gangs can/ gdung rten nga long ma sogs la mchod 'bul rgya che/ 'dus sder bsnyen bkur/ rnam gser du khrom dbang / 'jam dbyangs dmar ser dang 'byung 'dul rjes gnang sogs
stsal zhing / de skabs kyang gong lha sa'i ltas dang mtshungs pa byung zhes bla grwa kun ngoms bzhin du gleng mo 'khrol bar grags/ de nas lha ldan du zhi ba lha dang drung
'khor 'ga' zhig la sgrol dkar spyan bdun ma'i rjes gnang tshe dbang sogs dang / spyi sger gyi re ba mtha' dag nye bar skong bar mdzad/ de skabs gong ma'i tA shing bcas
thun gang ba'i dge rtsa ba 'byor bas tA shing dwa las tsang jun sogs la'ang legs skyes bstar bar mdzod 'dzin pa bkas mngags shing / rim gyis gong sa mchog sa skyong yab sras
sogs nas phebs phyag bdag rkyen bla med du stsal te nyer bdun la rtse shod phebs skyel ba rnams dang bcas lha ldan nas chibs bsgyur gyis yer ba dang yer la brgyud/ na
lendra zhes rgyun gyi dbang por 'bod pa'i gnas su phebs te rten ji snyed par mchod 'bul sogs dang skya ser 'dus tshogs la khrom dbang / bco brgyad du tshe rta sbags sgrub

dang 'jam dbyangs dmar ser rjes gnang / dpal ldan rtse'i bdag chen rdo rje 'chang gi thugs dam ma zhal bzhi rdo sku'i drung ban tshang ba'i 'khor tshogs dang bcas nas gsung
bskang phrin 'chol/ de skabs so sos/ legs 'bul zhabs brtan gya nom pa rnams dgyes bzhes kyis bod lo gsar ba'i dga' ston kyang gnas der mdzad do/ /rgya zhol/ la mo tshang
ba/ 'bum stod du gsung bskang dang bde chen chos sde/ shing tshang / dgod kha'am rgod khal la brgyud bsam yas su shar sgo zung khang du bzhugs te/ bsam yas mchims phu dang
bcas pa'i gnas rten rnams la mchod 'bul snyan shal thugs smon/ rab tu gnas pa'i me tog 'thor gnang bcas dang / chos skyong chen por dbu 'ching khrab gdan mdung ral gri
zhags pa rnams dgyes rdzas su stsal bas rnam bzhi'i phrin las sgrub pa'i zhal bzhes kyang phul/ de dus gong sa rdo rje 'chang lnga pa chen pos rin chen mi thod brgya dang
brgyad las grub par rin chen sna bdun 'bur dod khyad mtshar can gong ma de nyid kyi sku tshe ril por phyag bcangs gnang zhing / bar skabs lums pa bar dang rten du 'byor
bas des rmor chen rdo rje 'chang la phul ba rim gyis bsam yas sku rten par byung ba de rje rdo rje 'chang chen po'i phyag tu babs pa yar lam thar rtse rdo rje 'chang la
phul ba da lta thar rtse'i nang rten gras su bzhugs bar thos lags/ gang ltar rab grwa 'dus spyi spyi sger so so/ sku rten pa/ rdzong dpon sogs kyi dngos 'byor zad mi shes
pa dang chabs gcig zhabs pad yun brtan gyi tha tshig zhu ba dang / tshes bcu'i gar 'chams gzigs 'bul/ skya ser bgrang yas la khrom dbang / a ra pa tsa na'i rjes gnang /
gzhan yang phur chung gtor bsngo sogs kyi ljags lung stsal ba sogs bstan 'gro'i mdzad sgo rnams grub nas rim gyis phebs pa'i tshe rtse thang 'bras

gling dang nyi skor gyi rdo zhig la blo gros chos kyi rgyal mtshan zhes pa'i yi ge rang byon du byung ba bzhin/ de dus kun gyis rje rdo rje 'chang nyid la mtshan de bzhin du
gsol ba dang / rab 'byams pa mdo sngags chos 'phel gyis brtsams pa'i rje nyid kyi brtan bzhugs nang na'ang de bzhin 'khod lags/ mgo zla'i nyi shur khra 'brug dang nyer
gcig snga dro gnas gsar rdo rje 'chang chen po chibs bsur byon dus nas bzung rje nyid kyi rigs bdag de nyid rnyed par gnang ba yin te/ de yang / 'jam mgon mkhyen brtse'i
dbang phyug rang lugs snyan brgyud bstan pa rin po che'i mnga' bdag yin pa dang / rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan 'jam mgon a mes zhabs kyis dbu blar mdzad pa dang /
gnas gsar stong dpon sa skya pa'i sku nye yin pa sogs sgo du ma nas 'brel legs lam che ba bcas de dus rdo rje 'chang nyid kyi thugs dgongs la yab rje de nyid kyi gsung sgros
kyi zur la yar klungs dbon rin po che zhes dgyis nyams mdzad pa dang / gzhan phyogs lhung gi gtam yang du ma gsan pa bcas dbon rin po che de bzang ngan ji 'dra yin nam
dgongs pa las mtha' gcig tu nges pa'i bzang ngan ma 'khrungs shing / de gong gdan sa nas chibs ma bsgyur gong du thar rtse rdo rje 'chang nam mkha'i mtshan can gyis yum
mchog dang mdzod 'dzin pa bcas la/ yar klungs zhabs drung du sku rus sku yon sogs gang sa nas dbu blar bzhes thub pa zhig byung na legs tshul dang / rjes su phyag bris
kyi'ang brda sbyar bar brten mdzod 'dzin nas de rtsis kyi snyan sgron zhu rtsis bcas gang ltar khra 'brug tu zhal 'dzom thog /bla ma sku lta bas chog mi shes shing gsung
'jam zhing snyan pa gzigs pa tsam gyis thugs dad dbang med du 'khrungs pa zhig dang / rje rdo rje 'chang nyid zhal gzigs phyogs kyi rten 'brel sa rga'ang ma log par byang
gzigs la zhabs drung nyid lho gzigs su thog mar zhal rgyas/ rim

gyis gtam snyan bzhugs khrir chos sde'i thab bsu'i thog chos rje khu dbon gyi lo rgyus sogs zhib rgyas su phul/ bod kyi mkhar chags pa'i thog mar grags pa yum bu bla mkhar
gtsug lag khang du mchod 'bul sogs kyi skabs/ rgyal rabs chos 'byung lo rgyus kyi bshad pa chu 'bab ltar gnang bas thugs yid 'phrogs te/ yab rje rdo rje 'chang / thar rtse
rdo rje 'chang / brag rtsa ba chen po rnams nges shes gting nas rnyed pa'i bla ma dam par rang yin kyang / da lta'i sku gsung thugs kyi mdzad spyod 'di la dpags na bla
ma 'di de bas lhag pa zhig med kyang mi zhan nges par 'dug dgongs pa'i thugs mos dang bcas bla brang gi sgo spe mkhan chen gzhon nu blo gros kyi gzim chung du gdan 'jags/
sang nyin sgrol dkar gyi gsung chog rgyas pa sngon 'gro'i zhabs brtan gyi tshe/ sku gsung thugs rten/ maNDal/ zhal dkar stegs bcas/ gding ba/ gos kyi bla bre sogs rten 'brel
gyi rdzas gya nom pa dang / spyi so nas kyang dngos 'bul bla med bcas mdzad sbyor gyi mthar sku gsung thugs 'gyur med rdo rje gsum gyi rang bzhin du bzhugs te chos kyi
'khor lo rgya cher bskor ba sogs bka' mdo rgyud dgongs 'grel dang bcas pa nas drangs pa'i lung rig gi legs bshad stsal pa thugs kyi dpal ber sim pa sogs kyi rkyen gyis/
da cha bla ma 'di'i zhabs pad bsnyen nas gsung gi bdud rtsi ngom med du gsol ba zhig byung na ci ma rung dgongs pa'i dad mos lhag par yang 'khrungs pa ni/ rgyal sras shAnta
de was/ da ni bdag gis ci nas kyang / /rigs dang mthun pa'i las brtsams te/ /skyon med btsun pa'i rigs 'di la/ /rnyog par mi 'gyur de lta bya/ /zhes byang chub sems
dpa'i spyod pa bla na med pa'o/ /de'i tshe mdzod 'dzin gyis/ yab rje mchog sogs bla ma dam pa 'ga'

zhig la rje nyid nas zab chos gsan tshul/ da lta gsan mu bcas des na rnam 'dren dam pa nyid kyang dbu blar phebs dgos tshul zhib rgyas zhus par/ da lam chos 'brel zhig phul
te 'gyangs min nas phebs pa'i zhal bzhes stsal/ sang nyin bka' chos stsal rgyu'i do nub de rje nyid thugs spro dga' bde stong gi ngang du dus 'das shing / de nub zhabs drung
gi mnal lam du yab rje bsod nams rin chen de nyid kyis zhabs drung nyid la sbyor khrus rgyas pa zhig stsal ba 'khrungs pa'i sang nyin sgrol dkar yid bzhin 'khor lo'i
rjes gnang thun mong ma yin pa gsung bshad shin tu rgyas pa dang bcas gnang bas/ gang gi thugs rje'i dang rje nyid kyi thugs dad kyis byin rlabs 'phral du zhugs te ston
dang bstan pa gzhan nas mi 'tshol ba'i dad mos dang bcas yongs rdzogs snyan brgyud bstan pa rin po che'i mnga' bdag tu gyur pa'i rten 'brel gyi sa rga 'bad med lhun grub
tu 'grig par gyur to/ /gnas der khrom dbang dang 'dus tshogs su 'jam dbyangs dmar ser gyi rjes gnang / gnas gzigs skabs gnas bshad kyang zhabs drung mchog nas stsal dus 'du
khang steng gi tshar chen rnam thar kyang ris ma'i 'dar gdong 'khrugs pa'i zhing bkod kyi thad du/ 'di ci 'dra lags gsungs pas/ 'dir 'dar gdong 'khrugs nas phan tshun
'thab tshun 'chab mo byed ci tshar chen rin po ches mchod g.yog la thog kha nas mi rkang bus gsungs pa dang ser ba babs shing / ma chen rdo bkras kyis tshar chen la mthu
mdzad dgos zhus pas zhal gyis ma bzhes par ngo nag thug ge bsdad pa sogs kyi zhing bkod yin 'dug gsung / de skabs thugs rtog ci yang ma 'khrungs kyang rjes su gnas tshul
de 'dra ngan can gyis zhus pa min nam snyam pa'i dgongs pa tshom dogs 'khrungs kyang / sgo gang sa nas zhib 'jug mdzad pas ci yang tshom gzhi ma byung bas thugs bag phebs/
sri gcod 'bum par thab

skyel skabs de skor tshong dpon de ne tso'i lo rgyus zhib pa dang mchod rten la bskor ba mdzad nas srid las thar tshul/ byas lha khang skor gyi rten bshad rnams bka' drin che
ba sogs legs lam mchog tu dge ba'i sgo dang po dod par gyur to/ /de nas rim phebs kyi rnam sras mon mkhar ring mo nas/ bye tshogs su paN chen gyi rdza sku dang khyung
po'i thugs rten sogs la mchod 'bul thugs smon khrom dbang 'dus tshogs la rjes gnang sogs stsal/ chos skyong chen pos bka' bzhin phrin las sgrub pa'i tha tshig kyang phul
lo// // ! dgung grangs bcu drug tu phebs pa shing bye'i rgyal po lo gsar gyi lha ba sangs rgyas pa'ang der mdzad de chibs bskyod kyis gra thang du gur gyi mchod gar dang
/ pu tra ru 'dren bcas kyi 'chams gzigs 'bul/ 'dus tshogs la a ra pa tsa na'i rjes gnang tshe dbang gong ma lnga bstod kyi ljags lung byings la khrom dbang byams gling gnas
gzigs sogs mdzad nas/ bdun phun chos 'khor du'ang khrom dbang dang rta mgrin gsang sgrub kyi rjes gnang 'ga' zhig la mgon po khro bcu'i rjes gnang sogs spyi sgos kyi re
ba rnams bskangs te/ rim gyis rab smad rnam rab gong dkar rdo rje gdan du 'jam dkar dmar ser dzam dmar srog sgrub lha brgyad rjes gnang rnams dang rta zla'i tshes gcig
lha bsangs/ de nas yob la brgyud gzim phug stag khu spe skyed tshal 'og sogs thams cad du khrom dbang / stag khu sper 'jam dbyangs dang 'byung 'dul/ spos skyed du 'jam dbyangs
dang mi g.yo ba dkar po'i rjes gnang rnams kyis so so'i blo kha rdzogs par mdzad de gam la brgyud thar gling rgyal rtse sogs su rang rang gi 'dor sbyar dang bstun pa'i
mjal phyag dngos 'bul brtan bzhugs spyi sger nas bstar ba rnams zab bzhes dang / thar gling 'dus tshogs la 'jam dbyangs dang mi g.yo ba'i rjes gnang / skya

ser mang por khrom dbang / rgyal rtser yang de bzhin bgyis/ gur par 'jam dbyangs dmar ser/ sa paN bla ma'i rnal 'byor/ 'byung 'dul bla ma mchod chog rnams dang / rkyang 'dur
bde can dang ngor e waM chos ldan du'ang de bzhin/ dge sdings gzhis khar khrom dbang sogs mdzad de rta zla'i nang chibs bsu sogs sngar rgyun bzhin gyis gdan sa chen po
dpal ldan sa skyar phyags legs par phebs te dga' ston gtang rag sogs kyis dus 'da' ba'i skabs so/ /de dag gi don bsdu na/ mdo khams sa skyod blo gros kumbha'i snod/ /brgyad
ldan zhi bsil re ba'i bcud kyi rdzogs/ /snying po bde chen len pa'i dkyil 'khor du/ /zung 'jug yi ge bzhi ldan ngo bo bzhengs/ /'chi med myong grol bcud len rdzas sngags
dang / /ting 'dzin nus mthus bskrun pa'i dge mtshan ltas/ /lhun grub gsal des kun gyi yid 'phrogs nas/ /bden gtam lce rtse'i ngos nas yang yang rgyug /gangs ljongs lha
gcig pad dkar 'chang ba yi/ /thugs rje spro bsdu'i rten 'brel jo zhal zung / /nyid kyi sgyu 'phrul zlos pa'i gar dang bcas/ /dbus gtsang sbyin dang bde gshegs mchod kyis
bskyangs/ /zhes kyang smras so// // ! de nas hor zla gnyis gsum gang rigs kyi bdun phra gcig ring sgrol dkar yid bzhin 'khor lo dang tshe rta sbags sgrub kyi ljags bsnyen/
sgrol dkar gyi sbyin sreg bcas bka' drin che zhing / sa ga'i mjug nas zla gcig ring khyad 'phags mgon khang du gur gyi mgon po'i ljags bsnyen yi ge bcu gnyis ma 'bru 'bum
sbyin sreg bcas mdzad pa ni gur gyi ljags bsnyen dang po'i skabs dang / chu stod zla ba'i tshes 'gor rje btsun rig byed lha mo'i ljags bsnyen zhag bdun sbyin sreg bcas
gnang skabs rnams la dngos nyams kyi ltas ya mtshan yod tshul rnams zin bris ma mchis shing / 'on kyang rig byed ma'i

ljags bsnyen grol 'phral tsan dan dmar po'i phreng ba phyag 'byor sogs gzhung nas bshad pa'i 'grub rtags 'khrul med byung zhes gsung zer gyi zur las rnyed/ de lo'i badzra kI
la ya'i sgrub mchod kyi rdo rje slob dpon mdzad de skal ldan gyi slob bu brgya dang nyer lnga de'i dkyil 'khor du smin grol la 'god par mdzad pa'i rgyun lo yun ring po'i
bar du mang nyung ci rigs re dang / de lo gser mdog dbon por kye rdo rje'i rgyu dbang dang tshe dbang / gdan sa'i las chen pa sogs mtshams pa'i rigs rnams la lam dbang
/ gong ma'i rnal 'byor ma dang bstun mkha' spyod rdo rje btsun mo'i byin rlabs tshar lnga stsal zhing de'i zla mjug la 'jam mgon gnas gsar ba chen po gdan sar phebs te/ bod
lo gsar pa'i yar tshes dge ba nas bzung kha'u brag rdzong pa'i lugs sam tshar lugs su'ang grags pa tshe thung dbang po yang rab tshe gcig la sangs rgyas pa'i thabs thun
mong ma yin pa yongs rdzogs bstan pa rin po che'i nyams len gyi gdams pa gsung ngag zab mo slob bshad ces grags pa 'di nyid ni/ kun mkhyen klu sgrub rgya mtshos/ tshogs
par bshad pa'i drang don za zi'i gtam/ /rnam par spangs te slob bu mchog dag la/ /gces par bskyangs pa'i nges don snying po'i bcud/ /zab mo slob bshad khyongs par byin gyis
rlobs/ /zhes gsungs pa'i gsung ngag lugs gnyis kyi mchod tshul yang 'di lta ste/ mus chen 'khor lo sdom pa yan la tshogs slob kyi tha snyad mi snang yang mgon des bdag
chen rdo rje 'chang la zab gnang 'ga' zhig zur du stsal ba nas de ltar du grags pa'i gdams ngag zab mos mtshon lo ngo phyed gnyis tsam gyi bar du gnas gsar 'jam mgon la
bzhugs pa'i zab chos re gnyis tsam ma gtogs mtha' dag par bum pa gang byo'i tshul du bzhes mu'i zhal gyi chos

skor gsan skabs shig 'od gsal du/ rje bla ma dang mjal zhing thugs dges pa'i rnam 'gyur du ma zhig mdzad pa'i ngang nas chos srung che chung gnyis la bstod pa shlo ka bdun
re rtsoms shig gsung pa 'khrungs pa'i rgyu mtshan zhabs drung du phul bas/ btang rag zhig dang bstod pa zhig mdzad dgos kyi brdar 'dug /ces gsungs pa'i bstan srung dgyes
pa'i lha'i rol mo zhes bya ba 'di ljags rtsom mdzad do/ /de dag gi don bsdu na/ rim gnyis zab mo'i mchog thun dngos grub brnyes/ /gzhi lam 'bras dus smin grol gdams pas bskyangs/
/tshad ma snyan brgyud bzhi sogs gnas gsar rje'i/ /zab chos bum pa gang byos thugs brgyud gtams/ /zhes kyang smras so// // ! dgung grangs bcu bdun du byon pa shing
glang lor mdzod 'dzin rgyal mtshan rin chen gyis bskul ma zhus don bzhin/ 'dzam gling mdzes pa'i rgyan mchog sprul pa'i gandho la chen po 'di'i shar nub byang gsum gyi
spen bad gsar spo dang sbrags go 'phang cher bstod cing / lho mar kha sgron bcas gtsug lag khang mdzes pa'i zhabs tog rgya cher bskrun pa'i gsung gsang lhug par grol ba'i
tha tshig rdo rje'i ri mo spyi bo'i rgyan du bkod de/ 'go bzo 'ul mi bcas nas sla bcos bab col du ma song bar rgyu 'bras kyi blang dor snying khongs su bcangs te bgyis
pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba ni/ sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po'i rnam thar du/ gdan sa chen po 'di nyid kyi khang phran re la zhig gso byas na yang mchod rten re bzhengs pa'i
phan yon dang 'dra bar bla ma gong ma rnams kyi gsung las 'byung ba thugs la bzhag gsungs pas na/ de lta bu'i dge ba'i rtsa ba rgya chen po rnams la lta smos kyang ci 'tshal
