zhing / las mi rnams la'ang spyi sger nas ja chang rtsam sha sogs 'du long phun sum tshogs pa de dus las bzang ba ma dran/ zhes da lta'ang ngag rgyun du chags

shing / de lo khal kha 'ga' zhig la/ seng gdong sngon mo'i rjes gnang lung bcas dang / bla ma chu bzang par grub rgyal ma'i tshe dbang / gnas gsar rdo rje 'chang chen po dang
/ rtse gdong sprul sku/ chu bzang bla ma bcas la gur lha brgyad kyi rjes gnang dang / yang gnas gsar rdo rje 'chang chen por kye rdo rje man ngag lugs/ yang dag /bdag
med lha mo bco lnga/ a ra pa tsa na lha lnga/ phur pa'i stod las smad las rnams kyi dbang bka' dang / ri khrod ma'i byabs khrus/ lcags sdong lha mang / dkar bdud kyi rjes
gnang rnams dang / gong ma lnga'i bka' 'bum na bzhugs pa'i bde mchog thugs rje chen po/ mi g.yo ba'i skor rnams dang / sa lo'i bla mchod/ chos spyod rab gsal/ bskang ba/
bstod 'bum/ nyams rtogs gong 'phel/ phyogs bcu mun sel/ ri khrod ma'i mdo rnams kyi ljags lung dang / chu stod zla nang zhe re skyed tshal sprul skur kye rdor rgyu dbang
dang grub thob tshe dbang / dza sag bla ma bstan 'dzin chos dar gyi mi sna kha shas la/ bzang spyod/ ltung bshags/ shes snying rnams kyi ljags lung yang stsol bar mdzad
do/ /de dag gi don bsdu na/ 'dzam gling rgyan gcig sprul pa'i dri gtsang khang / /mngon mtho mdzes pa'i dbu 'phang bla na 'phags/ /phan tshun chos kyi bang mdzod 'jo ba'i
zla/ /stong gsum nor bus bkang yang sgrun skabs bral/ /zhes kyang smras so// // ! dgung grangs bco brgyad du byon pa me stag lo bkra shis lha khang gi zam sner chos kyi
rgyal po 'phags pa rin po che'i zhal gzigs pa'i tshul 'bum thang ldebs bris la gsal ba bzhin dang / rta zla'i yar tshes la mgon khang khag bzhir phrin 'chol sngon 'gro'i
nyer dgur gdan sa chen po rtse gdong gi phyogs su chibs kyi kha lo bsgyur te/ rim gyis

thub bstan gser mdog can gyi chos grwa chen por byon thog tshe dpag med sprul sku'i rjes gnang zhig stsal te/ dbo zla'i tshes drug la gdan sa rtse gdong du phyags phebs nas
bstan rgyun mi nyams srid mthar spel ba'i chos sbyin rgya cher mdzad tshul ni 'di lta lags/ gong ma lnga'i sku bstod kyi ljags lung gis chos sgo phye ste/ rim gyis 'jam
dkar ma ti lugs/ sgrol dkar bka' babs bdun ldan/ tshe dpag med chag lugs rnams kyi rjes gnang lung bcas dang / bcom ldan 'das snying po kye rdo rje/ dpal chen yang dag /phur
pa/ gsang ba 'dus pa/ mi bskyod rdo rje rnams kyi smin byed kyi dbang rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor steng nas dang / dkar bdud lcam dral gyi rjes gnang / skya ser 'dus cher
khrom dbang grub rgyal ma/ kye rdor man ngag lugs kyi sgrub dkyil/ gdan sa'i chos spyod dang bskang ba bstod pa yongs rdzogs kyi khar rje rdo rje 'chang chen po'i zhal
sgo las byon pa'i yab rje bsod nams rin chen gyi sku bstod le tshan/ yang dag gi brgyud 'debs/ de'i sgrubs thabs tshigs bcad ma rnams dang / bdag chen rdo rje 'chang gis
mdzad pa'i bskang bsngon rgyal ma/ sa los mdzad pa'i glo bo mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub dang zha lu lo chen gyi sku bstod/ sgrol ma'i mtshan brgya 'gyur bcos/ dkar cha
bzhi rnams dang / chos rje bla ma dam pas mdzad pa'i rdo rje phur pa'i sgrub thabs rgyas 'bring / de'i dkyil chog rtogs par sla ba/ sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal pos mdzad
pa'i gtor bsngo chen mo/ phur chung / drug cu pa'i zin bris/ 'jam mgon a mes zhabs kyis mdzad pa'i tsi dmar bskang ba le tshan/ bse khrab pa'i bskang ba/ yab rje bsod
nams rin chen gyis mdzad pa'i bskang ba rnams kyi ljags lung sogs bsten mkhas bgyi ba lhur

bzhes kyi chos sbyin mtha' yas pa zhig gis 'dir ma zad sku tshe ril por 'da' bar mdzad pa rnams kyang / dbyig gnyen gyis/ chos sbyin nyon mongs can min pas/ /mdo sogs ji bzhin
yang dag ston/ /ces dang / bslab btus las/ chos kyi sbyin pa zang zing med/ /bsod nams 'phel ba'i rgyu yin no/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar gyi sgo nas legs par 'doms pa sogs
gdan sa de'i 'gro don rnams mdzad zin nas rje btsun sgrol mas lung bstan pa'i gnas ngor e waM chos ldan gyi chos grwa chen por dbang rjes gnang sogs kyis skal ldan rnams
chos char gyi tshims par mdzad nas/ 'og min stug po bkod pa'i zhing dang mtshungs par rdor 'dzin bye ba'i gtsug rgyan rje btsun rin po che sogs gong ma mang por rje 'brang
bcas nas bsngags brjod kyi me tog 'thor bar mdzad pa'i gnas gdan sa chen po dpal ldan sa skyar phebs te/ sa ga'i rnal 'byor dbang phyug birWa pas sa drug gi rtogs pa rnams
nyin re bzhin rim gyis brnyes pa'i dus chen dang bstun myong grol bdud rtsi ril bu'i sgrub pa rnams grol rjes/ khal kha chos rje ngag dbang lhun grub dar rgyas la kye
rdo rje'i rgyu dbang / ku ru ku lle lha lnga dang 'khor lo bde mchog nag po pa'i dbang rnams dang / gtsug tor 'bar ba'i rjes gnang / 'jam mgon a mes zhabs kyis mdzad pa'i
bde kye gnyis kyi sgrub dkyil/ rtsa ba rdo rje'i tshig rkang / gtsug 'bar bstod pa rmor mdzad kyi lung rnams sgyi chu bla ma sgang stod chos mdzad la'ang stsal zhing /
gzhan yang rig byed ma dang tshogs bdag thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa khyad par zhar byung dang bcas pa'i rjes gnang / kag chol 'dod pa'i rgyal po thun mong ba/ dmar
chung skor gsum/ mgon dkar yid bzhin nor bu/ ber gcer rnam gnyis/ dud sol ma thun mong ba rnams kyi

rjes gnang lung bcas dang / de'i bskang ba sangs rgyas rin chen dang mgon dkar sgrub skor tshar chen/ mkhyen brtse/ ngag dbang chos grags kyis mdzad pa'i lung rnams dang /
gzhan yang khal kha tshe brtan rgya mtshor kye rdo rje'i rgyu dus kyi dbang zab mo stsol ba dang chabs gcig zha lu grang chen slob dpon sogs slob bu nyer gsum tsam yang smin
par mdzad cing / zha lu pa tshor mkha' spyod rdo rje btsun mo'i byin rlabs gnang ba'i tshe nang mchod kyi dkyil du ba~M yig rang byon 'khrungs pa kun gyi mig gi bdud
rtsir stsal ba'i ngo mtshar gyi mdzad pa dang sbrags tshar mdzad sgrub dkyil ljags lung rnams kyi sgo nas las can dag pa'i gdul bya mang po rjes su bzung bar mdzad do/ /de
dag gi don bsdu na/ sa 'dzin rtse mo'i gdong du mig stong pa'i/ /khab bzhin bkra ba'i skye dgur chos sbyin sgo/ /brgya phrag dbye zin slar yang mtha'i 'gro'i rgyud/ /smin
grol lam du nang gi phag mo bstan/ /zhes kyang smras so// // ! dgung grangs bcu dgur phebs pa me yos gro bzhin zla nang chos sde nyi zla zung sogs la sgrub thabs brgya
rgyam gyis mtshon chos char mtha' yas pa zhig dang / gzhan yang grang chen dbu byed/ spor bla ma/ grang chen slob tshab sbyin pa rnams la las gshin bcu gsum ma dang / dpa'
gcig gi rjes gnang / bcu gsum ma'i bskang ba/ tshar mdzad bcu gcig zhal gyi rjes gnang / de'i smyung gnas bya btang rjes mdzad pa rnams kyi lung dang yang skabs sna tshogs
su gdan sa'i zor las sogs la gur khro bcu/ lha brgyad/ zhal sgrub bsnyen/ pu tra/ de'i zur bka'/ bran bdud/ dkar bdud rnams kyi rjes gnang so so'i yig lung rnams dang
/ yang ngor gyi 'bul khag bla ma dang nyi shar ba sogs la dmag zor ma dang / dur bdag rjes gnang sogs tshar kha shas stsal bar mdzad cing / de lo gzhan yang chos char mang
du

phab tshul mchis kyang de tsam las spro ma nus/ de mtshams nas gung 'gyur med tshe brtan dpon g.yog rnams phebs pa'i tshe rje rdo rje 'dzin chen po nyid kyis/ bla brang phun
tshogs gling du mjal phyag sogs lugs gnyis kyi bdag rkyen phun sum tshogs pas khong dpon g.yog rnams dga' spro 'dzum mdangs kyi dpal la sbyor bar mdzad skabs/ 'jam mgon
mthu stobs dbang phyug nyid gzhi thog dbang khang na gzim dpon kun phun dang bcas bcom ldan 'das snying po kye rdo rje'i gzhi bsnyen la bzhugs pa'i skabs te/ de'i snga rol
tu a tsar zhig nas shel bum che ba zhig tu chu bo ganggA'i chu khyer ba dang mjal 'phrad kyis gsung gleng mang du mdzad pas yam bu dang gorSha'i lo rgyus 'dra las gzhan
mi snang zhing / sku mtshams thog gung sku rkyang la mjal phyag dbu tshugs su mdzad pa bzhin bka' drin che/ bcad rgya mthar phyin 'phral yul chen ban tshang pas/ las mkhan
ru 'dren bcas kyi 'chams gzigs 'bul yang mdzad do/ /de dag gi don bsdu na/ gnyug mar gnas sogs bslab gsum rgyan phreng can/ /bsdu dngos rnam bzhi snying po'i gsos kyis
sbyangs/ /stobs ldan sa spyod dregs pa'i che bskyungs nas/ /zhabs sen ral pa'i do ker bla nang bzhes/ /zhes kyang smras so// // ! dgung grang nyi shur phebs pas 'brug lor
rje rdo rje 'chang sku mched zhal rgyas nas dpal gur gyi mgon po'i ljags bsnyen zla gang ma zhig mdzad pa 'di ni rje nyid kyi gur gyi sngags bsnyen gnyis pa'i skabs dang
/ de nas 'jam mgon sangs rgyas ye shes la grub chen brgyad cu/ nyi sbas sgrol ma/ snar thang brgya rtsa/ sa skya bka' 'bum gyi ljags lung rnams zhal rgyas nas gsan skabs
'jam mgon mthu stobs kyi mtshan can gang la sku

khrag brtas pa lta bu'i snyun gzhi lci ba zhig bzhes skabs ngor pa dpon slob rnams kyis 'jigs byed drug cu pa/ rnam rgyal stong mchod sogs dang / chos grwa lho byang nas kyang
sku rim rgya che/ lhag pa rje rdo rje 'dzin nyid kyis tshe sgrub rnams la thugs brtson lhur bzhes mdzad pas re zhig nas sku lus las 'bu mtho gang tsam zhig mngon sum
du 'thon pas 'phral du snyun gzhi las grol ba'ang rje rdo rje 'chang nyid kyi sku drin du yang dag par 'khums lags/ rta zla'i nang yul chen ban tshang par kye rdo rje'i rgyu
dbang / kun rig /tshe dpag med lha dgu/ gur drag rnams dang / nag zla'i nang ngor gyi grwa rgyun kha shas dang sku drung sku skye bcas la sa paN bla ma'i rnal 'byor/
ku ru kulle'i rjes gnang thun mong ba/ dmag zor ma'i rjes gnang lung bcas rnams stsal zhing / 'dren mchog sangs rgyas ye shes la grangs chen bco brgyad kyi ljags lung nas
bzung chos bka' rgya cher phul ba rnams dam pa de nyid kyi gsan yig na gsal ba bzhin dang / snron zla'i nang klu sdings zhabs drung rin chen mi 'gyur rgyal mtshan la phur
dbang / dkar bdud dang las gshin bcu gsum ma'i rjes gnang lung bcas dang / gdong dga' chos sde pa 'ga' zhig la lam dbang / lha brgyad dang pu tra'i rje gnang lung bcas
dang / spyi shing bla ma ngo g.yog la yang phur dbang sogs bstan 'gro'i bgyi ba 'ba' zhig gis dus 'da' bar mdzad skabs mdzod 'dzin pa'ang bro 'tshal gyi mu dang / de mtshams
nas rje rdo rje 'chang nyid gzhis rtse rin rtse sogs la phebs skabs te/ rje nyid kyi gsung las/ de lo ngas ni gzhis rtse rin rtse sogs la'ang srid pa bar do'i rnam thar
zhig bskyangs/ zhes gsungs shing / de'i tshe gdan sa'i lugs zung gi thugs khur rnams gang dang zhal mi gnyis pa'i 'jam mgon

mthu stobs dbang phyug nyid kyis bzhes shing / rje nyid dbang phyogs su chibs bsgyur gyis skyer kha tshal zhes par bzhugs stan 'jags te ngo mtshar mkhas grub kyi mdzad par
gzhan dring mi 'jog pas dus 'da' bar mdzad skabs shig /de lo gzhis rtser char dkon po zhig byung ba'i rkyen dang / brnyad kyis 'tshol ba'i yang phyir te rje nyid la char
'bebs dgos tshul gsol ba bzhin mdzad ma thag lung pa chus gang ba'i drag char zhig 'bebs par mdzad pas 'dod rgyal gyi sgrar bshos kyi ming la bag tu 'bod pa bzhin skye bo
kun gyis da gzod sa skya bdag chen rin po ches bag byin song / zhes gleng ba dang lhan cig dad mos dang dga' mgu lhag par che ba'i dpal la 'god par mdzad/ ces dang / de
nas rin rtser phebs skabs tshe dbang zhig dang gur khro bcu'i rjes gnang zhig dbang dA las nas zhus stsal mdzad cing / gnas der pha bong chen mo zhig mchis pa de med pa mdzad
dgos tshul gsol ba bzhin la yang / mtshan gang zhig la pha bong de lhag ma tsam las mi snang ba'i rdzu 'phrul 'ga' zhig ston par mdzad ces rgan thog 'ga' zhig gleng
bar thos lags pas dgos gal che dus rdzu 'phrul gyi bkod par rdugs pa'i gras ni dam pa de nyid nam yang min pas/ rje rdo rje 'chang nyid kyi gsung las kyang / kho bo ni bla
ma gong ma rdo rje 'chang dang zhal mi gnyis pa mang pos rjes su bzung / bsnyen sgrub las gsum mtha' dag rang yid ches nges bgyis pa'i mthu las las bzhi ci sgrub kyang
yi dam chos srung gi byin rlabs 'jug nges pa rang yod rung drag las sogs ni cher ma bgyis shing / gal te rdo rje 'chang gi rgyud sde nas bshad pa nyams su len dgos pa zhig
yin na'ang mtha' rdugs pa'i gras ni min

no/ /zhes yang yang gsung las thos so/ /gzhis rtse phyogs nas ngor du chibs bsgyur gyi skabs dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed zhal phyag yongs su rdzogs pa zhig gzigs shing / thar rtse
phebs 'phral thar rtse rdo rje 'chang gi gsung las/ de ring sku zhabs rin po che la las gshin rigs gsum gyi rjes gnang sbrel nas 'bul dgos 'dug pas bka' sgrub da ci nas
tshar zin pas gsol ston grol 'phral 'bul lo zhes stsal ba'i ngo mtshar phan tshun 'gran res ni/ sngon gyi dus su rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan dang kha che
paN chen shAkya shrI sogs 'khrul zad gong ma'i rnam thar dang mtshungs shing / gzhan du de skabs rnams su sku gegs kyi rnam pa nyam nga ba de dag khro rgyal ma he'i zhal
can gyi sgo nas ngal ba 'bras med du mdzad pa ni gor ma chag go /lo de'i gro bzhin grang chen sku rim pa rnams la khro bcu'i rjes gnang dang gtor bzlog gi ljags lung bcas
dang / gsang 'dus sgrub mchod dang bstun dbang cha kha shas skal ldan rnams la stsal zhing mdzod 'dzin rgyal mtshan rin chen dus las yol bar byang bu lam ston gyis mtshon
rjes 'dzin gyi bgyi ba rnams yang dag par mdzad cing mi ring bar mdzod 'dzin pa shes rab phun tshogs las khur du bka' yis mngags so/ /de dag gi don bsdu na/ zag med bde
chen mgon po'i rang zhal gzigs/ /dam pa phan tshun don yod 'chad nyan 'gran/ /nang gi zug rngu'i rang gzugs phyir dbyung nas/ /dad ldan slob bu'i re ba'i yol go rdzogs/
/dbang phyogs yul du e raNDa yi gsog /sngon du mdzad nas tha tshig don gyi 'bras/ /'dren byed bdud rtsir byin yang ma tshims par/ /sna tshogs sgyu ma'i 'khrul

'khor zo chun 'khyud/ /thar pa'i dkyil 'khor gtso bo'i he ru kas/ /gdon bgegs 'joms pa'i las kyi gshin rje gsum/ /pho nya'i snga rol ye shes dbyings gzigs nas/ /slar yang mdzod
'dzin byas shes drin gzos drangs/ /zhes kyang smras so// // ! dgung grangs nyer gcig tu phebs pas sbrul rgyal zlar spang shar bla mar rdo rje phur pa'i dbang dang grub
rgyal lugs kyi tshe dbang / de'i gnam gang nas bzung bdun phrag gsum gyi bar lha chen sprul pa'i ganbho la'i steng gi sngags 'chang bdud kyi stobs 'phrog ngag dbang kun
dga' rin chen gyi gzim spyil po Ta la smon gnas yid 'ong tshal du/ gur gyi mgon po'i phyi 'khrid brag rdzong ma thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa'i rtsal 'don bcas mdzad
pa ni/ dbyig gnyen gyis/ tshul gnas thos dang bsam ldan pas/ /sgom pa la ni rab tu sbyor/ /zhes gsungs pa bzhin/ thos pas phyi'i sgro 'dogs bcad/ de rjes bsam byung gi
dpyad pas dag par mdzad de ji bzhin sgom pa'i ngang la thugs gzhol zhing / tshar chen rin po ches/ rten gyi dkyil 'khor gsang ba'i dam rdzas dang / /rab zab bsad dang bskyed
pa'i 'khrul 'khor dang / /zab gsal ting 'dzin ma nor gsang ba'i sngags/ /rtse gcig 'bad pas bsnyen sgrub mthar phyin shog /ces gsungs pa'i 'bras bu mngon gyur gyi 'grub
rtags kyang gsal bar 'khrungs pa zhes thos lags/ 'khrid 'di nyid rje bla ma gnas gsar pa'i drung du gsan skabs mnal lam 'od gsal gyi ngang du bka' rtsom 'di ltar yang
mdzad do/ /kha'u brag rdzong nag po'i ri khrod du/ /zab don du ma'i 'byung gnas chos kyi rje/ /se lo

'jam pa'i rdo rje rdo ring bar/ /snying nas gsol ba 'debs so byin gyis rlobs/ /zhes gsungs pa 'di 'dra'i rigs gzhan yang rje nyid la mang du 'khrungs kyang gsang 'os 'ga' zhig
ni 'od gsal de las bzhengs nas thugs dran cher mi gsal ba'i tshul mdzad lags/ rta zla'i nang sa ngor bstan pa'i sbyin bdag chen po mdo smad sa yi thig le sde bzhi dge
bcu'i dpal mngon par 'bar ba'i rgyal khab nas/ sa skyong blo gros rgyal mtshan sku 'khor rnams gdan sa chen por chibs bskyod mdzad thog rje rdo rje 'chang chen po'i dpal
gyi mgur nas zab rgyas chos kyi bdud rtsi grol bar mdzad pa ni 'di ltar mthong ste/ thog mar sku tshe mi 'gyur rdo rje'i rang bzhin du bya ba'i phyir rje btsun sa skya pa'i
yab chos dze tA ri'i lugs kyi 'chi med dbang po'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba/ ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma'i zhal bcud dpal ldan birWa pa'i zhabs kyis legs par bkral
ba kye rdo rje man ngag lugs kyi rgyu dbang dang lam dbang / grub pa'i slob dpon chen po nag po pa'i lugs kyi rnal 'byor gsang mtha'i smin byed zab mo'i dbang / pha bla na
med pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi gtso bo dpal gsang ba 'dus pa 'phags lugs su grags pa mi bskyod rdo rje'i dbang / rje btsun sa skya pa'i yab chos rnying ma 'khon rog shes rab
tshul khrims kyis rkyen 'ga' zhig la brten rnying ma'i chos skor rnams g.ya' lung 'jags gshongs kyi sa'i char gter du sba bar mdzad dus yang phur gnyis chos skyong bka' gnyan
pa'i stabs sba bar mdzad ma thub pa nas bzung / bsnyen cing sgrub par mdzad pa'i dpal chen yang dag zla gam dgu pa dang / phrin las lhun grub sa phur lha lnga bcu rtsa
gcig gi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba dang / gzhan yang rdo rje

'jigs byed ra lugs ro langs brgyad bskor/ bde mchog gong zhal can/ yab chos rtog pa nas gsungs pa'i ku ru kulle lha lnga rnams rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor chen po sgrub cing
mchod pa'i sgo nas dbang rnams smin rgyas chos rgyal dges pa'i mchod rdzas su 'bul bar mdzad/ rjes gnang skor la/ bod kyi rdo rje gdan dpal ldan sa skya 'di nyid chags pa'i
thog mar gyur pa sgo rum mam/ sgo rim mam/ sgo bsrungs sogs sgra bshad 'jug dang ldan pa'i ye shes mgon po'i drung du lha brgyad thun mong bas 'go drangs/ skabs mtshams
ji ltar rigs par/ kha 'u'am kha'ub ces kyang gleng ba'i me 'bar gyi brag la dngos su thim pa'i tsa tu rmu kha bsnyen dus kyi rjes gnang / sngon sngags 'chang chos kyi
rgyal por dam nyams lha sa rdzong pas nyin mtshan dus drug tu 'tshe ba'i skabs shig nor skyong yam yum gyis bstan dgra de dag la mngon spyod kyi las mdzad par gzigs snang
sogs 'khrungs pa'i ngo mtshar dang ldan pa dpal dur khrod bdag po'i rjes gnang / rje btsun rin po che sogs gong ma mang por mi la mi lab pa'i tshul gyis ci gsung phrin las
sgrub pa'i dam can mon bu pu tra'i zur bka'/ yang phur rnam gnyis kyi srung ma dkar bdud lcam dral/ gur gyi mgon po lha brgyad thun mong ma yin pa/ gur khro bcu/ dbang
lha dmar po skor gsum gyi rjes gnang sogs yab chos de rnams dang / paN chen dmar po nas brgyud de zhang pa la bka' babs pa'i dmag zor lha mo/ smad lugs g.yor po ba nas brgyud
bu ston rin po cher bka' babs pa'i ngal bsos po ser chen lha dgu/ khro dbang rdo rje gzhon nu'i smad las drag po sgrol ba'i

rjes gnang / tsa turmu kha dkar po tshe 'phel/ yab chos 'jam dpal dpa' gcig /sgrol ma dkar mo'i rjes gnang rnams te zab rgyas gdams pa'i bsil zer gyi bdud rtsis sa spyod thugs
kyi kunda dkar gsal bzhin ras kyi me tog phyogs kyi bu mor ngom pa'i dga' ston la bkod pa'i mthu la brten nas/ sa bstan nor 'dzin dpal mo'i ljongs 'dir dar zhing rgyas
la yun ring gnas pa'i thugs smon rgyal sras mchog gi spyod pas dus 'da' bar mdzad do/ /sa zla'i nang rags rdzong dgon lag bcas par kye rdo rje'i rgyu dbang dang mkha' spyod
rdo rje btsun mo'i byin rlabs kyang stsol bar mdzad de/ snron zla tsam nas 'jam mgon mthu stobs dbang phyug nyid bstan srung rgya mtsho'i bsti gnas bdud las rnam rgyal
dpal mgon dga' ba'i tshal du brag rdzong ma'i ljags bsnyen sbyin sreg bcas mdzad skabs tsam nas bzung rje nyid kyis phur sgrub chen mor gsung bshad kyi dga' ston stsol
gnang gi sngon 'gro phyag dpe 'dzin sbyangs/ phrin 'chol sogs mdzad rjes gro bzhin badzra kI la ya sgrub cing mchod pa'i 'dus pa rgya mtsho'i dbus su legs bshad kyi dga'
ston lhug par grol ba dang / mdos chang dang sku rim chen mo'i zor 'dzin gyi rdo rje slob dpon bka' drin che rgyu'i ljags bsnyen rnams mu sbrel gyi thugs brel rnams 'byung
'gyur dang / dbyug zla'i nang spyi sger bstan 'gro'i nyer 'tshe zhi phyir rje nyid kyi bka' gsang rmad du byung bas 'doms te/ gang gi gcung 'jam mgon mchog nas sgo rum
bla ma lha khang du bzhugs yul gyis bse 'bag nag po 'phur shes kyi sku drung du zhag 'ga' bskang phrin la thugs brtson gyi mur/ nyin gcig bse mgon bzhugs yul nas sku mdun
la rgyang gis mdzad pa lta bu dang / nyin gcig sa lotstsha ba'i phyag

rnga gnang mur lpags ldebs la 'od 'khyug pa nye gnas dang thun mong du gzigs shing / de skabs mkha' 'gro 'du ba'i dus kyi tshe zhig rje rdo rje 'chang nyid nas dam can mon
bu pu tra'i thun mong ma yin pa'i gsang rten gnyis gsar bskrun gyis/ chos kyi rgyal po 'phags pa rin po che'i bla brang gzhi thog dbang khang mdar bskang phrin la thugs gzhol
ba'i sgo nas srod chen thog gnang ba'i nub mo 'gag pa rab brtan gyi rmi ltas su/ gzhi thog rtse'i thog kha'i sgor sgo lcags byed rgyu yin bsam pa la mi mgo rlon pa khrag
'dzag 'gel bzhin 'dug pas 'jigs snang cher shar ba dang / sgo rum 'khor tshoms su ldir chom du mas tshig gsal ba la g.ya' g.ya' zer ba thos pas don chen zer ba de bla
ma lha khang mdar nyal ma nus par gzhan du bros pa sogs kyi tshul 'di'ang / sngon sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po la bstan dgra ma rungs pas 'tshe ba'i skabs shig /byas
'gyur rdo rje'i brag rdzong na dpon slob 'gas mgon po drug cu pa'i gtor bzlog sgrub gnang mur kye bos kyi bskul tshugs pa dang bstun/ nub phyogs kyi nam mkhar mi nag dung
long can gnyis gros byed pa'i tshul gyis nged rang tsho thog mar rin spungs la phyin/ de nas lha sa rdzong la phyin pa drag zer ba zham 'bring ba gnyis kyi mngon sum du
mthong ba dang tshul mtshungs pas zhing bcu tshang pa'i bstan dgra zhig gi rnam shes mi bskyod pa'i zhing du 'dren par mdzad pa ni gor ma chag /de nas dum tsam zhig nas
'khar rngar sor mo bsnun pa lta bu'i sgra zhig byung nas ldir chom rnams yar 'ong ste dbu rtse rnying ma'i gser phibs steng song ba 'dra mo zhig byung ba'i sang nyin dbu
rtse'i gser phibs khar yang khrag

rlon 'thor re ba dang / 'khor tshoms lho 'gram la che ba rta dang chung ba ra lug gi rmig rjes 'dra mo gdan nas la mang du byung ba sogs ni kun gyis dgongs gsal ltar lags/
de nas chu 'bum/ pha sgar/ go 'jo sogs kyi bla gnyer tshong dpon rnams bcas la/ tshe dpag med/ kun rig /gur drag rnams kyi dbang stsal zin 'phral/ 'di yin med cing don gyis
stongs pa'i thugs bsun 'o brgyal can zhig gis thugs rgyud 'khrugs bzhin du/ drug cu pa'i zor 'dzin sngon 'gro'i ljags bsnyen skabs dngos nyams kyi mtshan ltas du ma 'khrungs
tshul dang / dngos gzhi zor gyi dus nyin gnyis gsum lingga 'phar zhing lingga'i steng la 'ja' tshon gyi mdangs chags pa sogs lha dbyer 'bungs che dgos pa'i mtshan
ma 'khrungs shing / de mtshams nas bod dpon sku mched dus gzing je gsal gyis thams cad yang bya thabs kyis dben pa'i 'jigs zhum zla sbrel du byung ba dang / de nas dus mdos
gtor spod sogs kyi tshogs dbur 'jam mgon gcung rin po ches phebs/ de'i tshe stod phyogs kyi bros shor rnams lhags dogs dang / 'dar sde pa sku mched la srog skyob mdzad
pa sogs sgo gang sa nas thugs 'tsher ba'i rang bzhin dang / de'i dus bsam yas sku rten pa 'byor ba'i zhal ya chos 'brel sogs 'jam mgon gcung rin po ches mdzad cing / sku
rten pas lha chen rtse'i sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po'i sku la smon lam gyi mtshams sbyor bgyis dus sku brnyan de'i dbu mtshams nas zil pa 'thon pa zhig byung 'dug cing
/ mgo zla'i bde mchog sgrub mchod grol 'phral khal kha bstan dar bla mar kye rdor rgyu dbang dang rje btsun sa skya pa'i gser chos bcu

gsum nyin gnyis la rdzogs pa/ khyad 'phags mgon khang du lha brgyad kyi rjes gnang / de skabs tho rengs snga ba nas bzung sgrub mchod yan la rdo rje gzhon nu'i bsnyen mtshams
sngon 'gro'i stod las rdul mtshon gyi dkyil 'khor sgrub gnang gis dbyangs nyis rdzogs sum rdzogs kyi gtor bsngo yan chad/ bde mchog sgrub mchod grol nas khal khar chos
'chad sa ma rub tsam gyi bar de nas snga 'phros bskang gso bcas srod chen zin tsam la grol bar mdzad pa sogs so skye'i blo yul las brgal ba 'phags chen byang chub sems dpa'
bdag pas gzhan gces kyi rnam thar lhur bzhes 'di 'dra ni rje rdo rje 'chang de nyid la snga phyi rnam pa kun tu mang du mchis kyang 'dis mtshon par bya'o/ /nyer gsum
nyin phur bsnyen la bzhugs gdan 'jags rgyu'i snga dro dkar bdud kyi rjes gnang zhig stsal te lha mchog rdo rje gzhon nu'i bsnyen mtshams la thugs gzhol ba'i tshe dkar bdud
phur srung rnams dgyes pa'i rnam 'gyur du ma dang bcas zhal yang yang bstan pa'i rkyen gyis bstod pa rgyas pa 'di'ang de dus mdzad cing / tho rengs kyi cha 'ga' zhig tu
srung ma de dag gis mchod pa kha gso ba dang / mchod me spor ba dang / rje nyid bzheng bar bskul ba sogs bstan srung mngon sum bran du 'khol ba'i ngo mtshar mdzad pas dus
'da' ba'i skabs so/ /de dag gi don bsdu na/ zag med bde chen mgon po'i ting 'dzin las/ /bzhengs 'phral stobs kyis mtho ba'i sa spyod mchog /zab mo'i dkyil 'khor dbyings
su rjes bzung nas/ /yab mes mdzad bzang don gyi snying por zhugs/ /bstan 'gro'i phan bder 'bab pa'i zer 'bum gyis/ /ngo mtshar ltas bzang grol ba'i lang tsho

can/ /las bzhi'i 'dzum phreng g.yo ba'i g.yar lam du/ /dar dir sgra 'byin dkar phyogs mthu ldan rnams/ /bar med drug ldan dus su chos 'khor che/ /g.yel med phar phyin bzhi
pa mthar son nas/ /yengs med thos bsam sgom pa'i rnal 'byor dus/ /'bral med bstan srung bran 'khol bla ma rje/ /zhes kyang smras so// ! dgung grangs nyer gnyis su phebs pa
lcags rta lo phur pa'i ljags bsnyen skabs dbo zla'i tshes dgu'i tho rengs 'jam mgon gnas gsar pa chen po nyid zas gtsang sras por dngos su gzigs grol 'phral chos sde nyi
zla zung gi dge 'dun rags bsdus rnams la bka' chos kyi bang mdzod rgya cher 'jo bar mdzad nas/ nag zla'i nang 'jam dbyangs gzi 'od 'bar ba'i zhabs mthil la ljags bldag
mdzad pa'i mur sku'i g.yon 'khris de na 'phags pa klu sgrub dang zhi ba lha'i snam sbyar brtsegs pa zhig gzigs pa dang / 'jam mgon a mes zhabs kyis lan gsum gyi bar du zhal
bstan te rjes su bzung ba lags/ snon zlar chos rje dpal ldan chos skyong gi dbon por tshe dbang grub rgyal ma dang / lcags khu rin gling bla ma/ thub bstan mkhan zur bcas
la tshe rta zung 'brel gyi dbang stsal zhing / zla mjug nas chu stod tshes 'go bar yang bskyar gzhis rtser chibs kha bsgyur thang gnyis pa'i skabs bkra shis bde legs
su bzhugs sgar gyi tshe'ang sgo du ma nas 'jigs shing nyam nga ba zhig mchis na'ang / bslu med las 'bras kyi rten 'brel dang / rje rdo rje 'chang nyid kyi thugs rje thugs
bskyed phrin las las shar ba'i mthun 'gyur gyi rol mo 'khrol ba sogs kyi mthu las nye zho'i gdon bgegs kyi bsam sbyor dmigs med kyi dbyings su rgyas btab nas rim gyis gdan
sa chen por legs

par phebs te/ /phyi nang gsang ba'i 'gal rkyen zhi phyir lha khang rtse mgon khang du gsung bskang nyin gsum ma zhig mdzad rjes 'char 'phar gyi bstan don mdzad sgo rnams rje
btsun gong ma rnams kyi thugs bskyed las mi 'gong bar mdzad de/ dbyug zlar gur grwa brgyad la rta mgrin yang gsang gi dbang dang / lha brgyad/ zhal/ dur bdag /pu tra/ bran
bdud/ dkar bdud/ khro bcu rnams kyi rjes gnang dang lung 'ga' zhig bcas legs par stsal nas/ mgo zla'i nyer dgur gtor bzlog grub 'phral dbu rtse rnying mar bdun phrag
gcig bla ma gong ma rnams kyi phyag bzhes dang mthun par thugs sgrub mdzad de mgo zla phyi ma'i yar tshes brgyad la sgo rum gzim spyil dkar po'i mgron khang steng 'dzugs
chog rgyas par gnang ba'i 'go gzungs gzhug bsham tshul nas mjug 'dzugs chog gi bar tshang ma/ rje btsun gong ma'i yig cha gung bsgrigs kyi thog yang dag pa'i lam nas 'dren
par mdzad skabs bstan srung dgyes pa'i mtshan ma'ang gsal bar 'khrungs shing / bcu drug nas bdun phrag gcig ljags bsnyen sngon 'gro'i bcom ldan 'das snying po kye rdo rje
man ngag lugs rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor la brten pa'i sgrub mchod mdzad pa'i bar rnams su ban tshang pa 'ga' zhig la zhal dkar po tshe 'phel dang / gang gi a lce drung
la bcu gcig zhal gyi rjes gnang dang 'brel bar rje nyid kyi gsung rtsom bsnyen yig gi lung dang ngor pa 'ga' zhig la sgra mi snyan gyi tshe dbang rnams gnang mu'i nyer
drug nas bcom ldan 'das snying po kye rdo rje'i gzhi bsnyen zla drug gi bar du bka' drin che skabs lhag pa'i lha'i zhal gzigs pa'i rtags 'khrungs tshul gyi gsung yang snang
ba bcas 'di ni rje rdo rje 'chang nas kye rdor gzhi bsnyen gnyis pa'i

skabs dang / de'i tshe de'i dus su gdan sa'i lugs zung gi mdzad sgo rnams 'jam mgon mthu stobs kyi mtshan can mchog nas gang gi bka' lung gi khur bzod par mdzad cing / de lo
mes srong sde pa kun phan dam chos rgyal mtshan la gnang rgyu'i gur gyi bris thang thun mong ma yin pa zhal bkod gnang skabs sngar gyi gur lha brgyad steng / dmag zor rgyal
mo be con thod khrag lte ba'i thad kar mgo sprod du bzung ba zhig 'khrungs pa'i khrod nas dbu mdzad dbang phyug chos 'byor yin snyam pa zhig gis byang sems dkar po ka
pA la gang rje nyid la phul ba dang / gzhan yang gnyan mgon zhal bzhi pa'i skor la gzigs snang ngo mtshar can mang dag yod gsung ba las chos skyong bka' gnyan pas reg zig
dang bral zhing dpal mgur las kyang ma grol/ 'chi bdag las kyi gshin rje phur khang gi sgo tshad dang mnyam pa zhig kyang bka' nyan pa'i tshul gyis gzigs so/ /de dag gi
don bsdu na/ gzhis byes zhing sar chos char rjes thob tu/ /dbang phyogs sa 'dzin phrag nas nye zho yi/ /chu 'dzin dbyings dag mtshams sprin bla gos can/ /phan bde'i tsha
zer g.yo ba'i snang byed 'khrungs/ /de tshe dan stod gzim spyil dga' tshal du/ /phyogs las rnam rgyal ru mtshon 'dab brgya'i phon/ /rten 'brel byin rlabs dri bsung 'thul
bzhin par/ /bstan srung dgyes pa'i mchod rdzas nyid du grub/ /mngon gyur sar chags bi rU'i gdams ngag gnang / /stan gcig lha sngags rol pa'i bde stong dang / /mnyam du

ljags bsnyen grol

la khad rigs bdag thar rtse ba nyid phebs pas/ rje rdo rje 'chang thugs dges pa'i gsung las/ bla ma dang yi dam dbyer med du 'grub pa 'di rten 'brel shin tu legs gsungs shing
las bzhi'i sbyin sreg sogs grub nas zhal rgyas/ chu stod zla nang 'jam mgon gcung dam par gsang 'dus mi bskyod pa dang / rigs bdag thar rtse bar lcags sdong ma'i tshe
dbang rgyas pa/ dkar bdud phur srung dang sgar chen sku 'bring rnams kyi sku bstod/ thugs rje chen po'i mig 'byed gsar rnying bcas kyi ljags lung / khrums zla'i gsang 'dus

bcas dang / dbyug zla'i tshes gnyis nas lam gtor dang drug la gdan sa 'og rtse gdong gi phyogs la chibs bskyod de bcu gcig la rtse gdong du phebs nas zhag gnyis lcang can
mgon khang du phrin 'chol zab rgyas kyis bcu bzhis mchod thog gdan sa de nyid du phur pa sgrub mchod gsar 'dzugs mdzad gong gza' skar sogs gzigs yul du ma gyur kyang 'grub
sbyor rang 'grig dang grol nyin nyer bdun la'ang 'grub sbyor rang 'grig bcas rje rdo rje 'chang nyid kyi thugs bskyed dang / yul phyogs de'i bde skyid bla nar 'phel ba'i
bslu med rten 'brel gyi 'jug sgo bzang por grub cing / de'i tshe rje nyid nas rdo rje slob dpon gyi khur bzhes thog grwa sum cu skor gyis sbyor dngos rjes gtsang theg
pa khur blangs su mdzad pa'i rgyun da lta'ang kun gyi spyod yul du gyur pa 'di bzhin dang / 'chams chas sogs mkho dgu'i yo byad/ mchod pa bsnyen bkur/ 'dzugs ston sogs gya
nom

pa rgya che mu med du mdzad nas zla mjug dus gtor dang / tshes gcig la gye re mdo mchod gzhis khar gtor spod rdzong ri gnas gzigs sogs dang / bzhi'i snga dro ngor 'bul sdud
bla rnying sogs la mkha' spyod ma'i byin rlabs dang / lcang can mgon khang nyams gso gsar bskrun ltar du mdzad/ drug la bdud 'dul mgon khang gtor spod dang chabs gcig zhal
bzhi yum chen sring mo bzhi dang bcas dngos su bzhugs pa'i sprul pa'i g.yag rwa lnga sogs mgon khang steng du gdan 'dren gyis mtshan yang bsil tshal mgon khang du mnga'
gsol zhing de dang lhun rtse'i gtor spod sogs grol nas/ rang phyogs bu chen pa dang bsnyen gnas ma chos sde ba bcas la bcu gcig zhal gyi rjes gnang dang rgyal sras chos
rdzong pas mdzad pa'i smyung gnas po bstod kyi ljags lung / de nas rim bzhin rin sgang gtor spod/ khrom dbang / mkha' spyod ma'i byin rlabs/ rje btsun sa skya pa'i gdung
rabs rin po che byon tshul chen mo/ sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po'i rnam thar/ rje nyid kyi ljags rtsom gdung rabs zhal skong nyung nguu / sman bla mched bdun/ rnam 'joms/

bdud rjes gnang bcas dang / rdo rje las rim rtsa 'grel 'grel chen 'bum nag /phur pa'i dkyil chog /phur bzlog /gur drag /de'i brgyud 'debs/ las mtha' gsal byed/ dkar cha
bzhi/ slob dpon padma'i bla ma'i rnam 'byor/ rje rdo rje 'chang nyid kyi zhal sgo las byon pa'i phur pa'i las bzhi'i sbyin sreg /dmod bskul/ dkar bdud bstod pa rnams kyi
ljags lung dang / drag po sgrol dbang sogs te de tsam gyis zhing de'i gdul bya rnams smin grol lam bzang gi dpal la re zhig 'khod zin nas gser can du phebs te ma gcig grub
pa'i rgyal mo lugs kyi tshe dbang dang / de nas rim phebs kyis ngor e waM chos ldan 'dus tshogs

la 'jam dbyangs dmar ser dang sgrol dmar rjes gnang yig lung bcas dang / rnal 'byor dbang phyug sa skya pa chen po la rje btsun 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyis dngos su stsal ba'i zhen
pa bzhi bral gyi 'khrid yig rje btsun rin po che/ sa skya paN chen/ nub pa rig 'dzin grags rnams kyis mdzad pa dang / rje nyid kyis 'jam mgon sangs rgyas ye shes kyi
sku bstod dang brtan bzhugs le tshan gyi ljags lung khrom dbang bcas dang / klu sdings su zhabs drung khu dbon/ khang sar thar rtse'i dbon/ klu sdings ban tshang / bla brang
khag gi zhabs phyi rnams bcas la mi g.yo ba dkar po'i rjes gnang lung bcas dang / thar rtse rje nam mkha'i mtshan can khu dbon/ klu sdings khu dpon/ khang gsar dbon/
rje sangs rgyas ye shes kyi dbon sku mched sogs la rje btsun rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i byin rlabs tshar gnyis/ lam zab phyi ma/ dur bdag rjes gnang bcas stsal zhing de skabs
thar rtse rdo rje 'chang nas sngon du gcen lung la phebs skabs shig thams cad mkhyen pa dpal mchog rgyal mtshan gyi yab gzhis mkhas snga lho pa zer ba zhig gi nang du bzhugs
dus rje de'i phyag rol gur mgon 'di nyid gzigs pas/ de dus thar rtse rjes phyag rol de gdan sar phyag 'byor yong ba'i phrin 'chol mdzad pa dus su smin te/ mkhas snga
lho pas thar rtser khyer te 'di spus 'gyur mdzad dgos zhus pa bzhin/ thar rtse rdo rje 'chang dges pa'i gsung gis gang gi lo rgyus dang bcas rje rdo rje 'chang nyid la
phul pa da lta'ang dpal sa skya'i phyag rol drag gras gur mgon lha dgar grags pa 'di lags/ gzhan yang rje de nyid kyi phyag babs sgra dbyangs/ snyan grags sogs rol cha mang
dag mchis so/ /de'i tshe bla brang so so nas legs 'bul dang / spyi bye'i blo khams dang 'tshams pa'i

mdzad pa rnams grub rjes gdan sa chen po dpal ldan sa skyar phebs gdong rten 'brel phun sum tshogs pa'i sgo 'phar gcig tu phye te/ 'phags chen gong ma'i spyod tshul mtha' dag
bdag gir bzhes pa bla ma zhi ba lha nyid thugs bskyed kun bzang smon lam can gyis nye bar drangs te/ dngos 'bul gyi bdog pa gya nom pa dang bcas zhabs pad ga la bar bsnyegs
pa'i dge mtshan gser zhal la longs spyod pa'i skabs thugs bzhed kyi chos sgo dbye bar mdzad pa la/ gza' skar shis par rje btsun sa skya pa'i yab chos rnying ma rdo

tas shangs sreg shing du bsgyur ba/ dkyil chog rdo rje las rim rtsa 'grel/ 'grel ba 'bum nag /sa skya pa chen pos phur pa'i mngon rtogs dang las byang / rje btsun rin
po che'i sgrub thabs dang tho yig /bla ma dam pa'i sgrub thabs rgyas bsdus/ dkyil chog rtogs par sla ba rnams dang / sa lotstsha ba'i brgyud 'debs dngos grub rgya mtsho/
bsnyen sgrub gsal byed bdud rtsi'i 'od can la sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal pos mchan mdzad/ gtor bzlog gnam lcags rdo rje'i me dbal/ 'khor lo rtsibs bcu dang ltas ngan brgyad

las bzhi'i sbyin sreg

dmod bskul/ dkar bdud phur srung gi bstod pa/ gnas gsar rdo rje 'chang gi gsol 'debs dang zhabs brtan/ rje rdo rje 'chang sku mched kyi zhabs brtan le tshan ljags lung rnams
dang / rje btsun sa skya pa'i thun mong ma yin pa'i gdams ngag gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i rtsa ba rdo rje'i tshig rkang rnal 'byor dbang phyug birWa
pas shar phyogs nag po par gdams pa'i man ngag zab mo mkha' 'gro'i zhal rlangs 'thul le ba'i ljags lung stsal ba bcas zhal slob mchog gi thugs kyi bum bzang re ba'i bcud
kyis gtams par gyur cing / de'i zla mjug zhal gyi bsnyen mtshams sngon 'gro'i gtor bzlog zor 'dzin mdzad dus kyang dngos nyams kyi mtshan ma bzang po 'khrungs shing de

go ram pa dang / zur 'debs le tshan thar rtse paN chen gyis mdzad

pa/ drug cu pa drag bskul yongs rdzogs bcas kyi ljags lung / rgya khag bla mar sgrub thabs brgya rtsa dang seng gdong sngon mo'i rjes gnang lung bcas shar ri mnga' bdag la
'jam dbyangs dmar ser/ tshe rta sbags sgrub/ lcags sdong lha mang rnams dang chu mo sprul skur yang a ra pa tsa na lha lnga dang / 'jigs byed ro langs brgyad bskor gyi dbang
/ bya gshongs mkhan por grub rgyal ma/ lam dbang sogs te mdor na bstan pa'i bya ba thos bsam sgom gsum dang / mkhas pa'i bya ba 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum gyis rnam pa thams
cad du dus 'da' bar mdzad pas dgung grangs bcu gnyis nas nyer gsum 'di'i bar du'ang kye rdor rgyu dbang tshar lnga bcu nga bgrangs/ lam dbang nyi shu lhag tsam/ bde mchog

yang rje rdo rje 'chang nyid kyi thugs nyams su nyin zhag phrugs rer sgom sgrub chag med kyang nyer bdun tsam re bzhes par mdzad pa ste/ de dag kyang rje nyid kyi gsung las/

'gro/ /zhes dang / zhi ba lhas/ 'di 'dra'i dal ba rnyed gyur nas/ /bdag gis dge goms ma byas na/ /'di las bslus pa gzhan med de/ /'di las rmongs pa'ang gzhan med do/

te/ /da gzod dam pa'i mgon po nyin skar tsam/ /kye ma ma hA gu ru slar bzhengs shig /ces kyang smras so// ! dgung grangs nyer bzhi pa chu spre'u gsar phral bzhugs thab

pa dang tshogs bdag gi 'gab 'dre bse gdong can yang gnon par mdzad/ nag zla'i nang rje rdo rje 'chang sku mched nas brag rdzong ma'i las tshogs shwa bzlog rgya chen sgrub par

nas 'phags chen blo gros rgyal mtshan sogs gong ma mang po'i bzhugs gnas tshoms dmar steng 'og /dngos grub gling sogs la nyams gso gsar bskrun lta bu dang / khyad par dngos

zhib gleng mdzad/ de nas thar rtse rdo rje 'chang gi bka' bzhin rje rdo rje 'chang sku mched nas gu ru drag dmar gyi ljags bsnyen bdun phrag gnang skabs kyi nyer dgur a

sngon 'gro phrin 'tshol skabs skyed lhas su rtag gtor 'dzugs gnang gis rje btsun sa skya pa'i gdung brgyud rin po che chad med myur du 'byon pa'i ched du zhag shas phrin

pa zhig dang / yang

skabs shig gser gyi rdo rje gnyis phyag tu 'bul mkhan zhig 'khrungs pa rnams kyi 'bras bu mngon gyur kun gyi spyod yul du gyur pa 'di bzhin dang / smin zla'i bcu gsum la bdag
mo phebs pa'i ston mo gzhas sogs gzabs 'chor dang / khyad par gong sa rin po ches gzim 'gag 'dod 'jo sku tshab tu ched mngags kyis legs gsol tshad med stsal ba sogs gzhis
byes mtha' dag nas rten 'brel gyi sgo brgya phye bar mdzad skabs cung zad 'tshub nyams kyi rtags 'ga' zhig kyang byung zhing / de nas gzhung zhabs mchog nas zhol khang
chos mdzad ched mngags kyis zhag shas gsung bskang nyin gang mtshoms chen du mdzad pa'i dbu dang / mdos chung mdos chen sogs gang gi bka' yis 'jam mgon gcung dam par legs
par 'doms so/ /de dag gi don bsdu na/ snod bcud phun tshogs gling du mi mthun gegs/ /mthar dbyung nag po chen po'i ngo bor bzhengs/ /slar yang gdug can 'gong po'i kha
gnon che/ /drag po dmar chen sreg blugs bcas la gzhol/ /de tshe dpal mgur grol ba'i gzigs mo ru/ /rigs bdag nyid kyang lhags shing bdud rtsi gsol/ /'phags chen bsti ba'i
pho brang rten brten pa/ /gsar bskrun byin rlabs me char dbyings nas g.yos/ /chos dbyings mnal ma'i dgongs zab 'gengs pa dang / /me 'bar gnas su grub mtshan gsal bar bstan/
/'byung 'gyur re ba'i rten 'brel 'jug sgo brgya/ /ci yang tshar du dngar ba thugs mtshor bskyil/ /zhes kyang smras so// ! dgung grangs nyer lngar phebs pa chu bya rta
zla'i tshes gcig la rlung chen tshad med byung ba bal yul nas gzhan la me 'jug byas par gleng zhing / de nas mang mkhar gnas gsar bas 'chams gzigs 'bul dang / tshes drug
nas bzung yongs rdzogs

bstan pa rin po che'i nyams len gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i gdams ngag 'jigs bral stobs kyi mgon po dpal ldan birWa pa nyid la ye shes kyi mkha' 'gros
dngos su stsal ba'i man ngag mkha' 'gro'i zhal rlangs can thog mar 'chad pa'i sgo dbye bar mdzad de/ zhal slob kyi gtso bo 'jam mgon mthu stobs dbang phyug gi dbu g.yas
skal ldan rnams la zla gsum tsam gyi ring stsol bar mdzad pa'i chos kyi rnam grangs ni rje rdo rje 'chang nyid kyi ljags rtsom gdung rabs rin po che'i zhal skong nang gsal
bzhin dang / snron zla'i tshes lnga nas 'bum thang gtsug lag khang rten brten par bcas nyams gsos 'bum dngul gdung du bskrun pa ring bsrel rnam bzhis phyur por bkang ste
sa rgyan gnam rgyan mchod spyad gdan rabs sogs ngo mtshar gyi bkod 'doms bla na med pa'i 'go tshugs par mdzad/ de mtshams nas gsol thab lhor spo gnang gis chu stod zla
nang rje btsun rig byed lha mo sngon mo'i char 'bebs la thug gzhol ba'i skabs shig /rdo rje phug na 'jam mgon mthu stobs dbang phyug nyid de sngon nas sku snyun pa'i 'phrod
gzhes gnang mur rje nyid la 'phral du phebs brda zhig byung bar rtab rtab por byon pas sku rlung gi rnam pa 'dra mos dran med du bzhugs 'dug pa la rje nyid nas thabs sna
tshogs kyi 'du ci yang zhig mdzad pas/ dar tsam nas ljags dbugs kyi rgyu ba sleb tsam byung zhing / de skabs thar rtse dang gnas gsar rje gnyis char bzhugs pa la skyabs
'jug ljags gul gsung brtag bcas zhu gnang la gnyis ka'i gsung du 'phral 'tshubs las skyon mi yong gsung ba bzhin phyi dro nas thugs dam mdzad khul dang / mi ngo ni cher
mi mkhyen cing gsung yang mi mdzad pa bcas rje rdo rje 'chang nyid nas bcar bzhugs kyis nyin gang khyol/ mtshan mo zham 'bring pa rnams sku drung du

bkas mngags te rje de nyid gzim phug gi mdar bzhugs pas nam phyed tsam nas mnal bde mor khugs pa'i gnas tshul snyan du son/ sang nyin nam langs 'phral sku 'khris su phebs pas
zhal 'don gnang thub tsam 'dug pas thugs bde/ /de nyin 'jam mgon gnas gsar ba nas tshe dbang sogs stsal ba nas rim dwangs kyis phur sgrub sogs la phebs/ de'i tshe thar
rtse dang gnas gsar rje gnyis char nas bdag mor rten 'byung dngos po'i gnang cha dang legs slob zhal ta stsol bar btsun mor sku dngos phebs/ ston 'gor thar rtse rdo rje
'chang ngor du phebs gong gsung las/ rje rdo rje 'chang de nyid mkhyen rab la sa skya paN chen dang / mnga' thang phrin las la 'phags chen blo gros rgyal mtshan dang / mthu
stobs nus rtsal sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po dang mtshungs pa yong nges rang lags/ zhes lkog gyur rjen gsal gyi lung bstan thog tu khel ba stsal rjes rig 'dzin pho
brang gi sgo bsgrigs sogs shin tu 'grig par mdzad de phebs skyel zhu mi rnams la da ni gzim chung ya gir yang de tsam mo zhes 'gyangs min nas zhing brje ba'i gsung dang /
ston nas dgun 'go'i bar gnas gsar rdo rje 'chang nas gsar rnying du ma'i chos bka' mang du stsol bar mdzad mthar dbus phyogs la chibs bsgyur/ khrums zla'i nang chos lhun
mkhan po/ thub bstan mkhan po sogs la mkha' spyod ma'i byin rlabs dang dur bdag rjes gnang lung bcas dang / ngor bla brang khag so so ba mang po dang khyad par thar rtse'i
zhabs gras chu nad kyis non nas lnga lam du chas pa gnyis bcas la bla ma zhi khro stsal 'phral nas de gnyis bder song zhing / dbyug zla'i nang thub bstan grwa rgyun pa
'ga' zhig la 'jam dbyangs dmar ser rjes gnang dang gdung rabs ya rabs kha rgyan gyi

lung / rgyang mkhar bla ma yab sras la tshe dbang lcags sdong ma/ lha chen drung ram kun dga' tshul khrims sogs kha shas la phur pa'i sbyin sreg /phur chung gtor bsngo rnams
kyi ljags lung / zla nang der khal kha ching wang bde chen skyabs kyi mi sna dbang phyug sogs nyi shu skor dang / sne shan sog po dpon g.yog bcas sngar bla med kyi dbang
gis smin nges nyer lngar rje btsun sa skya pa'i gser chos dmar po skor gsum/ dmar mo skor gsum/ dmar chung skor gsum/ seng ge sgra/ 'jam nag /khyung khra/ dzam dmar srog
sgrub ste bcu gsum du grags pa'i rjes gnang lung bcas/ 'od dpag med kyi nyal 'pho dang rong ston chen pos yum la gnang ba'i 'pho ba bcas stsal te/ dga' mgu'i rnam 'gyur
brgya phrag g.yo ba'i dpal la 'god par mdzad/ smin zla'i nang 'jam mgon gcung dam pa'i dbus zhal ngo rnams dang / chos sde nyi zla zung gi dge 'dun kha shas/ 'jam mgon gnas
gsar ba/ de'i phyag mdzod/ rje drung ngag dbang lags/ gser mdog bla ma dpon g.yog sogs nyer lngar 'khor lo bde mchog lU nag dril gsum gyi dbang chen dang dril bu lus
dkyil gyi dbang / 'jam mgon gnas gsar ba chen po zhal dkar rje drung bcas la pu tra/ las gshin khrag mdog yab yum/ bse bya bzhi bskor bcas kyi rjes gnang dang / dpon g.yog
tshang mar sgra mi snyan gyi tshe dbang / zhal dkar gser bla sogs kha shas la bde mchog bong zhal/ kye rdor rgyu dbang / lam dbang / nA ro mkha' spyod dang dpyal lugs phag
mo skor gsum phag dkar rnams dang / sgrub thabs rgya mtshor grags pa'i rjes gnang tshang ma/ 'jam dbyangs dmar ser/ mi g.yo ba dkar po/ khyung khra/ gnyan sgrol/ dzam
dmar/ gza' yum/ rdo rje shugs/ sna tshogs yum/ gtsug

'bar/ gnas bcu/ legs ldan mched gsum/ bka' gdams lha bzhi/ sme dud/ dmag zor ma/ rdo rje rab brtan ma'i rjes gnang rnams dang / lung la/ rje btsun sa skya pa'i gdung rabs rin
po che byon tshul/ bde mchog chos 'byung / lU nag dril gsum gyi bskyed rim rnam bshad/ mkha' spyod ma'i sgrub dkyil rnams a mes zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ rje btsun rtse mo
dang grags pa rgyal mtshan gnyis kyis mdzad pa'i dril bu dbang chu sgrub thabs/ kun mkhyen gyis mdzad pa'i mngal sgong gnyis kyi sgrub thabs/ dmag zor ma dang rdo rje rab
brtan ma gnyis kyi bskang gso'i lung rnams stsal ba sogs nyin mtshan khor yug lta bur chos kyi 'khor lo bar med du bskor bar mdzad pa yang / ji skad du/ gang la phan phyir
nga yi chos/ /tshul bzhin bstan pas mchod 'gyur gyi/ /me tog byug pa mar me yis/ /rgyal ba yang dag mchod ma yin/ /zhes dang / byams pa seng ge sgra'i mdo las/ gang gis
ganggA'i bye snyed sangs rgyas zhing / /rin chen bdun gyis yongs su bkang byas nas/ /dga' rab sems kyis rgyal la phul ba dang / /gang gis sems can gcig la tshigs bcad byin/
/rin chen sbyin pa shin tu rgya chen des/ /tshigs bcad byin pa snying rjes bsgrubs de la/ /char yang mi phod bgrangs su'ang ma yin na/ /gnyis dang gsum du bsam du ga
la yod/ /ces pa dang / ganggA'i bye snyed 'jig rten gser dag gis/ /bkang ste gang la sbyin pa byin pa bas/ /dus ngan tshe na tshigs bcad gcig brjod pa/ /de yi phan 'dogs
ci 'dra de la med/ /ces dang / seng ges zhus par/ chos kyi sbyin pas skye ba dran/ /zhes gsungs pa sogs bstan la byi dor gtsang ma'i cho gas dus 'da' ba las gzhan pa'i rang
don nyi

tshe'i bsam sbyor ni rje dam pa de nyid la rmi lam tsam du'ang mi mnga' zhing / de nas 'char 'phar gyi thugs brel spyi dang bye brag la gzhol bar mdzad pa'i skabs so/ /de dag
gi don bsdu na/ DA ki'i zhal rlangs 'thul ba'i gsung ngag gi /cha lag dang bcas zil dngar drod gsher dus/ /skal ldan blo gros gshin po'i zhing sa cher/ /rnam grol thar
pa'i sa bon dang po bskrun/ /rim bskyed myu gu mchog la mi mthun rlung / /grang reg gtum po thugs rje'i tsha zer gyis/ /sbyong tshe rnam 'dren zung gi gsang ba'i lung /
/phan tshun rtse dgar chas pa'i bshes su gyur/ /thar pa'i rtser son grub dbang gsang lung gis/ /mgon khyod zhing bcas 'byung 'gyur tha tshig bsnyad/ /ya gyal 'dren pa'i gsung
gsang lhag ma'i bcud/ /ngom med gsol nas 'gro rgyud smin cing grol/ ces kyang smras so// // ! dgung grangs nyer drug tu phebs pa shing khyi'i dpyid chos grwa lho byang
sogs skal ldan mang por gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa thang gnyis pa stsal skabs gsung ngag sngon mar ma gnang ba'i lung rjes gnang sogs mdzad pa'i rnam
grangs ni/ gsung ngag rin po che byung tshul dang kye rdo rje'i bsnyen thabs gnyis a mes zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ rje nyid kyis mdzad pa'i brgyud 'debs rnams kyi kha skong
sgar chen dang kun dga' dbang rgyal gyi gsol 'debs/ rtse gdong bdag chen gsum gyi sku bstod/ yab rje'i sku bstod skyabs gnas ma/ rnam thar gsol 'debs/ gnas gsar rje dang
thar rtse rje'i sku bstod/ de gnyis kyi zhabs brtan/ sangs rgyas ye shes kha'u pa a Ni drung bcas kyi gsol 'debs rnams dang / kun mkhyen gyis mdzad pa'i bdag med ma'i sgrub
thabs dbang

gi tho yig lam dbang bskur gso dbang chu'i sa chog gsal byed a seng ma'i don 'grel/ lam 'bras bla brgyud gsol 'debs le tshan/ rnam bir byin rlabs bya tshul/ kye rdor rgyud
dang mthun pa'i smon lam/ dbang gi sngon 'gro'i sems bskyed le tshan/ brda 'grol nges pa'i dpal ster rnams dang / gzhan yang gtor bsngo chen mo sogs kyi ljags lung dang sangs
rgyas klu dbang 'od zer can ma khro mo sme brtsegs/ tshe dpag med dkar po/ seng gdong dmar mo/ tshogs bdag dkar po/ tshe dpag med sprul sku rnams kyi rjes gnang lung
bcas rnams yang dag par bka' drin che zin 'phral/ rje rdo rje 'chang sku mched nas tshoms dmar du zhal gyi dam tshig bskang ba nam langs sa rub lta bur bskul res kyi sgo
nas sgrub gnang dang / de nas gong smos bzhin 'bum thang gtsug lag khang phyi nang gcong zom can la bla ma gong ma du mas nyams gso nyan ka sogs rgyun chags su mdzad kyang
gtan brling khel ba ma byung ba'i stabs rten brten par bcas yongs rdzogs gsar bskrun gyis rnying pa gyang zegs phran bu tsam yang med pa lta bur bkas 'doms zin pa gnam
sa bar gsum mdzes byed mchod tshogs kyil phyur por bkang ba rnams kyi cha gzhi ha lam grub dus gang gi yum mchog dam pa nyid snyun bzhes kyi mu dang / sa ga'i gsang 'dus
sgrub mchod thog gser can grwa bskor ba bcu lhag dang de'i bla ma dpon g.yog sogs la 'dod 'bras bzhin gsang 'dus mi bskyod pa'i dbang dang / khams pa grwa rgyun bsnyen mtshams
pa bdun tsam la lha brgyad rjes gnang / snron zla'i nang sgrub mchod thog chos grwa lho'i dbyar chos pa rnams dang gser can grwa bskor ba mus pa bcas la 'khor lo sdom
pa nag po pa'i dbang tshar gsum dang / yab

rje rdo rje 'chang bsod nams rin chen gyi dgongs rdzogs kye rdor sgrub mchod thog gdong dga' chos sde ba sogs skal ldan gyi skyes pho mo mang ba dang / sa stod gzhis gnyer/
g.yang chos rgyal sras/ gnya' nang pa dpon g.yog sogs mi grangs brgya dang brgya phyed la kye rdo rje'i rgyu dus kyi dbang tshar drug dang / yang gdong dga' ba phal cher
dang chos sde byang pa 'ga' zhig bcas bdun rer khro bcu'i rjes gnang tshar gsum gro bzhin phur sgrub thog 'jam mgon gcung rin po che a lce drung chos sde lho byang kha shas
la dwags rje btsun ma dpon g.yog kha shas rdzong ri rab 'byams pa sogs la phur dbang tshar gnyis dang / yang la dwags rje btsun dpon g.yog stod sgar dpon rang dkyil khang
pa ngo g.yog rdzong ri ba sogs mang tsam la tshe dbang lcags sdong ma/ sngon 'gro gzer lnga'i nang rdor sems sgom lung / rgyal rtse mes srong nas zhus pa'i rje nyid
kyi gsol 'debs kyi ljags lung rnams bka' drin du stsal ba'i sgo nas gdul bya mang po thar lam du rjes su bzung / de'i tshe yum mchog nyid gzhi thog pho brang na bzhugs shing
/ phur sgrub skabs snga phyir sna tshogs su 'bum thang gzungs gzhug 'od zer dri med de'i dkyil chog grangs gsog gis sgrub par mdzad pa dang / skabs 'ga' gzhi thog tu
phebs te rgyal yum dam pa'i rkyen sel la rje rdo rje 'chang sku mched nas thugs gzhol ba'i skabs shig /yum gyi gsung las/ do nub gzhi thog tu bzhugs la sang nyin tshogs dung
byung bstun byon cig gsungs pa bzhin mdzad nas sang nyin phebs khar yum gyi sku drung du byon gsungs pa ltar byon pas yum gyi gsung las/ da lam bdag nad 'di'i kha nas
thar ba zhig mi yong bas des na nyid rang ni sku na dang babs lugs

gnyis la mkhyen rlabs rgyas pa sogs blo kyog ma dgos/ 'on kyang bstan 'gro'i mdzad par thugs brtson che gshis sku 'khrugs ma byung bar mdzod/ gcung po 'di thugs sems chung
la sku gcong che zhing zhabs 'debs ma thugs gyong ba sogs 'o brgyal rang byung dogs dang sku tshe'ang ha cang ring ba zhig ma byung dogs pas nam bzhugs bar sku mched da lta
bzhin thugs mthun pa dang dbu 'don yang dag mdzod/ gzhan yang rje btsun drung rnams dang zhabs phyi sogs la zhal mngags du ma mdzad mthar rgan mo nga'i 'das shul gang
mdzad na'ang nyid rang nas mkhyen pas des ma 'thus pa gang yang zhu rgyu med gsung ma thag rje nyid kyi thugs la lta ba bka' rtags kyi phyag rgya bzhi gsal 'debs lta bur
'khrungs pa'i mur dar tsam mnyam par bzhag rjes gsung lan du/ da dung sku rim 'phrod pa zhes sogs yang dag zhu bas yar bskyed bzhes thub tsam e yong / ci ste ji gsung bzhin
thog bab shar tshe gang ci'i zhal chems 'gyod med zhu gsung bas yum mchog nyid thugs dgyes pa rab gyi rtser son/ de nas phur sgrub ring dang khrums zla'i bcu gsum phar
res 'jog gis de nyin dbang khang na dpal gsang ba 'dus pa 'jam pa'i rdo rje'i sgrub mchod gnang skabs glo bur du da ni gshegs par nye bas re zhig yar byon na gsol ba bzhin
mdzad pas mi ngo'ang mi mkhyen cing spyan phan tshun du gzigs thub tsam mchis pas de ma thag rje rdo rje 'chang chen pos bdud rtsi ril bu khrus chur sbyar ba/ sangs rgyas
kyi 'phel gdung rin po che rnams gnang bas dar tsam nas thug dran gsal zhing / bcu bzhi'i shar gyi skya rengs shar tsam la sgrub mchod kyi tshogs dung gsan ma thag yum
nyid phyag thal mo sbyor bzhin pa'i mur dgongs pa chos kyi dbyings

su zhugs 'phral/ gang gi zhal chems bzhin gzim 'od lags nas mkha' spyod ma'i 'pho ba gsal 'debs sogs dgongs zab rdzogs thabs kyi mdzad sgo mtha' dag rje rdo rje 'dzin nyid
kyi gsung gis legs par 'doms nas dgun dus kyi tshe 'jam mgon dpal ldan chos skyong dang zhal rgyas/ mgo zla'i nang tsha rong sde pa snyan grags khu bo bcas dang las chen
pa sogs chos sde lho byang 'ga' zhig la tshar lugs grub rgyal tshe dbang lung bcas dang rnam 'joms byab khrus/ bde mchog sgrub mchod dang bstun gling tshang bla ma chos rgyal
mtshan sogs nas gsol btab bzhin bde mchog nag po pa'i dbang / dgun chos pa rnams la lcags sdong ma/ brgya dpon sogs bsnyen mtshams pa 'ga' zhig la lam dbang / de mtshams
nas khams phyogs hor khang sar dpon g.yog brgya skor rje rdo rje 'chang nyid kyi snyan grags sgra 'dzin gyi bu gar lhung pas dad pa'i yid kyi khye'u chung dbang med
du khug ste dngos 'bul rgya che ba dang bcas mjal phyag la bcar ba gzhung sne shan bcas la'ang lugs zung gi bdag rkyen spyi dang bye brag bla ma zhi khro'i tshe'i dbang bskur
ba bcas legs par stsal to/ /de dag gi don bsdu na/ yongs rdzogs bi rU'i nyams len gzhung shing che/ /tshad ma snyan brgyud bzhi ldan chos kyi sgo/ /thabs shes brda yis
phye ba'i dkyil 'khor du/ /snod rung dam tshig ldan kun rjes su bzung / /drin gyis bskyangs pa'i skyed byed ma ma'i gsung / /gang thugs dag pa'i me long 'phos ma thag
/don ldan bslu med dam pa'i thugs rje yis/ /lcags kyus 'di phyi kun tu yang dag drangs/ /shing rta'i srol 'byed rgyal tshab mi pham mgon/ /sdom brtson ngur smrig zol gyis
nyer lhags nas/ /

mgon khyod zhal rgyas mnyam bzhag rjes thob tu/ /mdo smad hor sogs mang por 'dod 'jo grol/ /ces kyang smras so// // ! dgung grangs nyer bdun du phebs pa shing phag rgyal zla'i
bcu gnyis la rje rdo rje 'chang chen po'i rigs bdag dam pa lugs zung gnyis char nas sku drin gzhal bar dka' ba thar rtse rdo rje 'chang nam mkha' bsam 'grub kun dga'
mtshan dpe'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po zhing 'di'i gdul bya re zhig rdzogs pa'i dgongs rdzogs kyi rim pa spyi dang bye brag rje rdo rje 'chang sku mched nas dngos dang brgyud
nas mdzad dgos rnams yang dag par bka' drin che mthar/ bsam yas mkhan gsar bsod 'od 'dam thog bla ma bstan yar sogs mi bdun tsam la rje btsun sa skya pa'i zab chos
bir bsrung dang lam zab phyi ma'i byin rlabs/ rje nyid kyi gsung rtsom mgon po'i char 'bebs ljags lung / yang lcags la mi chen dpon gyi mgron gnyer bstan 'dzin gzhung sne
shan pa/ rtse gdong 'bul sdud bla ma mkhyen rab/ 'brug bla sprul sku sogs la 'dod 'bras bzhin 'khor lo bde mchog nag po spyod pa'i rdo rje lugs kyi dbang / mkha' spyod ma'i
byin rlabs dang de'i 'pho ba'i lung / yang lcags mgron dpon g.yog chos grwa lho byang 'ga' zhig 'bul sdud bla ma sogs skya ser mang tsam la grub rgyal ma'i tshe dbang
/ sde dge mkhan rin po che dpal ldan chos skyong / sku tshab dpon po lha rgyal/ rdzong gsar bla ma yon tan rgya mtsho/ ri bo che'i ma Ni ba brgyad/ gzhung sne shan pa sogs
brgya phrag brgal tsam la bla ma zhi khro dang rta mgrin skyer sgang rjes gnang / rdzong gsar bla ma dang ri bo che'i ma Ni ba sogs la rdo rje gzhon nu'i smin byed kyi
dbang / lho byang dge 'dun bsnyen mtshams pa bdun la lha brgyad dang dkar bdud kyi rjes gnang / tshos sgo bskor chen pa sum cu tsam dang gdan sa'i mnga' zhabs dan khrod
pa rnams

sogs skyes pho mo drug brgya brgal tsam la grub rgyal tshe dbang tshar gnyis rnams stsal ba dang / rta zla'i nang ngor thar rtse'i 'bul sdud gdong spras bla ma sangs rgyas
lhun grub ngo g.yog bcas la lcags sdong lha mang dang dbyug gu ma'i sgrub skor gyi ljags lung dang ka leb bla gsar sogs la 'byung 'dul rjes gnang / dbo zla'i nang sde dge
gnyer ba bsod nams bkra shis kyi tsha bo a kham dpon g.yog nyer lnga tsam la tshe dpag med lha dgu/ kun rig phur dbang rnams dang / nag zla'i nang dpon lha rgyal dpon g.yog
dang 'dam bla bstan yar sogs mang por sgrol dkar lugs gnyis dang drag dmar gyi rjes gnang / dbon po rkyang par mgon po lha bcu gnyis ma'i rjes gnang lung bcas rnams stsol
bar mdzad/ de'i tshes bco brgyad tho rangs sgo rum bla ma lha khang du 'jam mgon sa skya paNDi ta sku gzi brjid dang ldan zhing zhal 'dzum par bcas dngos su gzigs pa
nas bzung sku bstod shes bya thams cad gzigs pa'i sogs shlo ka gcig phreng 'khor re chag med du mdzad/ gzhan yang 'gro mgon 'phags pa rin po che thang gsum tsam gzigs pa'i
gcig 'bum thang ldebs bris la yod pa 'di bzhin dang / rgya gar shar phyogs za hor gyi rgyal khams de dpal ldan sa skya nas brtsis pa'i lho nub na yod par nam mkha' 'ja'
tshon gyis gang ba dang / skabs shig mus kyi spang steng zhig na bla ma rab byung bgres po sku bem drag chem me ba zhig gsol nas chos 'chad mdzad rgyu yin dgongs pa dang
/ yang mus gyi 'du khang ka bzhi ma kha lhor bstan zhig na bla ma bgres po de ga bzhugs nas rdo rje snying 'grel gyi bshad pa mdzad pa dang / yang dpal chen pho brang rnying
dus yongs rdzogs 'khrungs pa'i g.yab kha nub bstan zhig tu gung tshigs mdzad kyin bzhugs pa dang / zha lu'i ldebs bris la mdzad pa bcu gnyis kyi

bshad pa gnang mu nas bden bzhi'i chos 'khor bskor ba'i bshad pa'i tshe gos ser gyi snam sbyar bzhes nas gnang ba sogs sngon gnas rjes dran lta bu ya mtshan mtshar du che ba
de rnams kyang 'khrungs shing / nag zla'i nang nas chu stod zla skad bar kun rdzob ltar snang du rdo rje'i sku brnyes rje rdor 'dzin chen po nyid la sku khrag brtas pa'i
snyun gzhi bstud mar bzhes tshul gyi skabs 'jam mgon dpal ldan chos skyong nas sku rim gyi zhal bkod dang nyid nas kyang sku gegs sel thabs sgo gang zab mdzad cing lhag
don rje nyid kyis thugs dam tshe sgrub rnams la brtson par bka' drin che bas rim gyis snyun gzhi dbyings su dengs/ lo de'i ril sgrub gang gi gcung dam pa nyid kyis thugs
'gan bzhes shing de'i tshe rje btsun gong ma'i bdud rtsi ril bu'i sta rnams mang du spel bar mdzad/ de nas chu stod zla mjug tsam nas thub bstan mkhan po bstan 'dzin rgyal
mtshan/ ri khud sprul sku bsod nams dbang phyug /sde dge dme shod bla ma yon tan rgya mtsho sogs skal ldan rnams la slar yang zab rgyas kyi bdud rtsi 'di ltar grol bar
mdzad do/ /grub chen brgyad cu sgrub thabs brgya rgyam tshe dbang grub rgyal ma dang bla ma zhi khro lcags sdong lha mang dang / 'chi med 'dod 'jo'i lugs rdo rje'i srog
shing yang snying kun 'dus sgra mi snyan tshe'i rdzong chung / gur lha brgyad/ khro bcu/ trakshad/ dmag zor ma/ zhal bsnyen dus/ bektse/ dur bdag /pu tra/ bran bdud/ dkar
bdud/ las gshin rigs gsum/ dmar po skor gsum rnam sras/ phyag rdor/ khang brtsegs/ zhang blon/ tshogs bdag chags pa rdo rje sogs rjes gnang dang / dpal 'khor lo bde mchog
nag po pa/ dril bu phyi nang / gsang 'dus 'phags lugs/ ye shes zhabs lugs/ 'chi med rnga sgra/ mi 'khrug lha dgu/ rigs

gsum spyi dbang / sbyong dkyil bcu gnyis/ gshed dmar lha lnga/ dri med rnam gnyis/ gur drag /a ra pa tsa na lha lnga/ yang dag /phur pa'i stod las/ rta mgrin yang gsang / ku
ru kulle lha lnga'i dbang rnams la 'jam mgon mthu stobs dbang phyug nyid kyang phebs shing de dag la gzhan yang / snar thang brgya rtsa/ jo lugs dang nyi sbas sgrol ma/
sa paN bla ma'i rnal 'byor/ gnas bcu/ sman bla/ klu dbang / 'jam dbyangs dmar ser/ dkar po shes rab 'khor lo/ /smra seng 'jam nag /dbyangs can dkar dmar dang shes phyin
dkar mo/ /nor rgyun ma/ so 'brang / gza' yum/ gtsug 'bar/ 'od zer can ma/ 'jigs byed dpa' gcig /tshe dpag med dkar po/ mi g.yo ba dkar sngon/ bcu gcig zhal/ don zhags/ sgrol
ma dkar dmar/ rnam rgyal/ rnam 'joms/ 'byung 'dul le tshan/ u tsa rya/ gtum khyung / gnyan sgrol dang rjes 'brel mtshan brgya'i lung / ri khrod ma/ rta mgrin skyer sgang
/ nag po grub rgyal jo lugs/ seng gdong sngon dmar/ sme brtsegs ljang dud khro mo bcas/ phag dkar rdo rje shugs/ khyung khra/ sna tshogs yum/ bde mchog lhan skyes/ dzam
ser nag dkar/ dzam dmar le tshan/ a pa ra tsitta/ bka' gdams lha bzhi rnams kyi rjes gnang lung bcas dang / gro bzhin phur sgrub thog phur dbang bcas te/ dus gnas thams
cad du zang zing dang bral zhing bsod nams 'phel ba'i rgyur 'gyur ba chos sbyin 'ga' zhig gi dus 'da' bar mdzad de sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa rin po che nam langs nyi shar
lta bu zhig byung na ci ma rung dgongs pa'i thugs bskyed gzhar yang mi bskyud pa 'di ni/ klu'i rgyal po rgya mtshos zhus pa'i mdo las/ chos

byin pas ni zag pa zad pa'i mngon par shes pa rnam pa dag par 'gyur ro/ /zhes dang / rin chen phreng bar/ chos kyi ched dang de bzhin du/ /gzhung gi don dag dran pa dang /
/chos kyi sbyin pa dri med pas/ /tshe rabs dran pa thob par 'gyur/ /zhes sogs mang du gsungs pa'i don yang thugs la 'dogs par mdzad do/ /de nas mgon khang khag bzhir phrin
'chol sogs sngon 'gro'i dbyug zla'i nyer lnga'i nyin rje rdo rje 'chang sku mched rin po che zhal rnam pa gnyis sku 'khor ba rnams dang bcas gtsang dbus su chibs kyi kha
lo bskyod par mdzad pa de ni rje nyid kyis dbus phyogs su phebs thang gnyis pa ste maNDal du gsol tshigs dgon rgyas su bzhugs zhag de nas rim bzhin lcang gshongs dang rgya
mdud/ sred rgod dang lcags ri/ snar thang dang gzhis rtser zhag gsum/ nam tshang dang gser can te der gang blo ma'i rig gtad zhig stsol bar mdzad/ de nas gling phu ba'i
gzhis dang rtse gdong du zhag bcu gcig /der tshe dpag lha dgu/ kun rig /lam dbang / khrom dbang / pu tra'i zur bka'/ bran bdud rnams bka' drin che nas snum ri dang rgya
ma kha/ nya mo dang se shing kha/ khu lung dang rin spungs su khrom dbang / byams chen du 'byung 'dul gyi rjes gnang dang ngur smrig /chu tshad kha dang ram pa/ lung bzang
dang dpal de'u/ phan la rtsa dang shags smad/ chu shur dang gsal byed rdor gling / gnam dang snye thang bkra shis sgang / stod lung mda' dang lha sar zla gcig zhag bdun
bzhugs shing de'i tshe gong sa rin po che cung zad sku ltem tshul bzhes skabs yin gshis mjal phyag sogs ji 'dra yong ngam gsung mu dang / rong sner phebs dus rgyal rtser
'brum dogs sogs gang sar yid gnyis kyi khyogs la 'chang bzhin par phebs kyang rgyal ba yab sras bka'i dgung blon rnams sogs che btsan tshang mas gzigs bskyangs phun sum
tshogs pa dang / spyir sger lha sde mi sde drag gzhan mtha' dag nas zhabs kyi padmor

'dud cing phu dud che ba sogs te/ ji skad du/ dam pa rgyang na gnas na yang / /'khor 'dab phan pas ring nas skyong / /zhes dang / rgyal po rang yul che ba tsam/ /dam pa gang
du phyin sar bkur/ /zhes rten 'brel gyi chos nyid du mchis lags pa dang / lhag par gru 'dzin pho brang chen po nas kun gzigs bdun pa chen pos bdag rkyen dbu 'don gyi mdzad
pas spyir bag dro zhing / yang sgos de sngon gzhan nas mjal phyag zhus pa'i nyen bslangs/ sku khams la gnod pa 'dra yang byung tshod mchis kyang rje rdo rje 'chang zhal
rnam pa gnyis la phebs phyag gnang ba'i nub mo mtshan gzim 'jam pa dang / zhabs brtan phul ba nas sku la yar bskyed bzhes pa sogs gong sa de nyid kyi rnam thar lcang skya
rdo rje 'chang gi gsung rtsom de na'ang bsngags brjod bcas 'khod par gnang 'dug pa bzhin rje rdo rje 'chang chen po de nyid ni dus dang gnas skabs thams cad du grub mtha'
ris su ma phyed pa'i mkhas grub la gus shing / de dag gi gsung gi bdud rtsi bzhes pa'i dbu bla yang gong gsal ltar dang / khyad par rgyal ba yab sras 'di rnams snyigs
dus bstan 'gro'i mgon du bsams bzhin phebs pa yin dgongs pa'i thugs dad rang byung bcos min du mchis pa'i rten 'brel gyi gnad dang / 'phags mchog phyag na padma nyid kyi
thugs rje rnams lhan cig 'dzom pa'i ngo mtshar bla na med pa las byung ba'o/ /de nas 'dzam gling skye 'gro kun gyi bsod nams kyi zhing mchog dam pa dang / yang sgos bod
kha ba can pa'i bsod nams kyi bgo skal du rnyed pa jo bo rin po che'i sku drung du rab gnas chig sgrub mdzad pa de'i tshe/ gang gi gcung rin po ches gzim chung khams gsum
du sme brtsegs kyi sku khrus dang / spor sde par lam zab bla ma'i rnal 'byor dang kye rdor bsnyen thabs kyi ljags phu lung / gong ma bdag po chen po'i sku tshab shu am
pas mjal zhus thog 'jam

mgon gcung rin po cher lhag par dges pa'i rnam 'gyur yang bstan par grags la de skabs rje rdo rje 'chang chen po nyid nas chos char bdud rtsi'i zegs mas 'gro blo smin par mdzad
pa'ang 'di lta mthong ste/ mda' dpon pu lung pa sogs la bla ma zhi khro/ zhi ba lha/ spel bzhi spo ra ba sogs la kye rdor rgyu dbang tshar gnyis/ mgron gnyer bskal bzang
/ wag ri bla ma sogs la mkhal spyod ma'i byin rlabs/ mda' dpon 'bum thang pa sku ngo lnga ra tshe ring ma'i rjes gnang / gung paNDi ta sku 'khor tshang mar sna tshogs
yum gyi rjes gnang dang 'chi med 'dod 'jo/ yang dbus mda' dpon sogs la rgyu dbang dang rtsis dpon phun tshogs la rdo rje'i srog shing / karma dang bu lags kyis thogs drangs
sbra zhol ba phal cher la grub rgyal ma/ gsang phu dang shel grong gnyis su khrom dbang / rnam gser du bla ma zhi khro/ bka' blon thon pa 'khor bcas la sgrol ljang dang

mda' dpon/ spel bzhi/ spo ra zha lu rab rgyas bla ma/ khal kha thon dar gyi mi sna bcas la lha brgyad rjes gnang / dza sag la gos sngon can rjes gnang / khal kha ma gtogs

rjes gnang / khri khang du dza sag 'khor bcas la bla ma zhi khro dang sku ngor sgrol dkar/ dum ri chos sder ltung bshags/ byams smon/ smon lam bcu pa/ byams pas dam bcas
pa'i gzungs/ mi mjed ma/ sgrol bstod nyer gcig rnams kyi ljags lung bcas stsal zhing / de nas la mo dang btsang thog dge ldan gnas gzigs/ sa sgang dang bde chen du sgrol
