mkhar du glang pa gser gling par

'byung 'dul rjes gnang / mes srong pa/ glang mthong ba/ bde rgyas pa rnams tshang ma dang gser gling bla ma bcas la tshe dbang lcags sdong ma dang gnod sbyin rnam gnyis kyi
mchod chog lung / de nas gang ro sgang mkhar du mes rje dang gnas chung bar 'jam dbyangs dmar ser rjes gnang dang gnod sbyin drag bskul lung bcas/ zhang chag dang dbang
ldan phu shar/ lha g.yang na kha dang bar tshor rnam 'joms byabs khrus dang bla ma zhi khro/ de nas rkyang 'dur zhag bzhi kun rig gi dbang tshar gsum khrom dbang bcas dang
/ bar tsho bar bde mchog yab bka' yum bka' dur khrod bdag po dang nor rgyun ma'i rjes gnang / skyid bde sbug par 'jam dbyangs dmar ser rjes gnang / de nas a drung skyed
tshal 'og dang pa nam klu sdings/ pad tshal du lcags sdong lha mang / sme dud/ mi g.yo ba dkar po rnams dang / gnod sbyin rnams gnyis mchod chog lung / de rjes khyung ram
/ khyung rgyab/ rgyan gong / zha lu rnams dang / ri phug tu chos khrir tshogs chen la bu bstod phan bde'i 'byung gnas/ brtan bzhugs phyogs las rnam rgyal/ dus gsum sangs
rgyas/ rtsa brgyud bla ma/ dpal ldan bde chen rnams kyi ljags lung / de nas lcags dang ngor e waM chos ldan du khrom dbang dang tshogs chen la rnam rgyal rjes gnang / khang
gsar la gdon 'grol/ gling khang du bla ma zhi khro/ thar rtser lcags sdong ma/ khri pa sogs la mkha' spyod ma'i byin rlabs/ klu sdings su 'byung 'dul me dbang rnams
dang / 'jam mgon gcung rin po ches tshogs chen la 'jam dbyangs dmar ser dang / thar rtser tshe dpag med dkar po'i rjes gnang zhig stsol bar mdzad cing / de skabs 'gro mgon
'phags pa rin po

che'i thugs dam rten thub pa'i dbang po'i dngul sku mthong ba don ldan 'di nyid phyag tu son tshul ni/ rje nyid kyi gsung las/ 'gro ba'i mgon po chos rgyal 'phags pa rin po
che'i thugs dam rten dngul sku khyad 'phags 'di me byi zla ba bzhi pa sngon ma'i tshes bdun rgyal phur gyi 'grub sbyor nyin yon tan rin po che du ma'i 'byung gnas dpal e
waM chos ldan gyi rten brten par bcas pa spyi dang / khyad par thar rtse rdo rje 'chang chen po'i nang rten dngul gdung rin po che la kye rdo rje'i rab gnas 'bring po phul
ba'i cho ga grub nas gling khang du 'jam mgon dpal ldan chos skyong gis kho bo mched 'khor bcas la dga' ston rgya cher stsal ba'i thog sku 'dra rin po che 'di lo rgyus
dang bcas gsol ras su gnang ba dang / thar rtser slebs skabs dbon rin po che dpon g.yog rnams nas sgrol dkar gyi brtan bzhugs gnang ba sogs mdor na rab gnas la shis pa'i
rten 'brel mtha' dag ma bsgrigs lhun grub tu 'grig pa'i rten khyad par can 'di sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' blo gros sangs rgyas bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang pos
dpal sa skya'i sde bstan pa gdung brgyud dang bcas pa'i 'thas su khyad 'phags gtsug lag khang gi rten gras la bzhugs su gsol ba 'di bzhin ji srid bstan pa rin po che nam
gnas gyi bar de srid du bzhugs pa'i phrin las mgon po che chung lcam dral 'khor dang bcas pas mdzod/ ces gsungs shing / yang de lo tshe sgrub slob dpon tsha bo blo bzang
don ldan gyis phul ba'i chos kyi rgyal po 'phags pa rin po che'i phyag cha'i gras ljon dmar las grub pa'i dgang blugs kyang gtsug lag khang der sbyor bar mdzad lags/ de
nas bye spe dang gangs can gnas gzigs/ sred rgod khro phu dge sdings su khrom dbang dang bla ma zhi khro/ rdzi lung dang sngon mo rdzong mdun

rdo rje gdan par shes snying lung / de nas bya gshongs su shes phyin dkar mo'i rjes gnang dang bsam myur ma'i lung / e bar 'jam dpal mtshan brjod kyi ljags lung rnams mdzad
pa mtshon don tsam du bkod pa'i sgo nas spyi dang bye brag gi gdul bya rnams rnam grol thar pa'i khang bzang du 'dren par mdzad cing / gzhan ma rje de'i mdzad pa ni nam
mkha'i mtha' dang mnyam na de dus kyi mdzad pa ji snyed pa brjod pa yang de dang 'dra ba ste 'di yang gnad don du shes dgos shing / de nas sle'u dang ra ma se lung / bkra
shis dar rgyas nas gdan sa chen po dpal ldan sa skyar chibs kyi kha lo bsgyur te bkra shis dang dge legs kyi dga' ston gtang rag sogs kyis dus 'da' ba'i skabs so/ /de dag
gi don bsdu na/ 'dzam gling bstan 'gro'i skyed tshal sbubs yangs su/ /ngal 'tsho'i mtsho skyes 'jam mgon gzhon nu'i dus/ /lugs zung blang dor snang ba'i bshes gnyen de/
/kye ma kun gsal dag pa'i dbyings su 'dzegs/ /'on tang gsung zer zegs mas bskyangs pa dang / /gang gi thugs bskyed 'dzom pa'i rten 'byung gnad/ /phan bde'i sbrang rtsi 'jo
ba'i dpyid dpal du/ /lhun grub phrin las rgyas dang lhan cig brtan/ /dbus gtsang ra yig gnyis pa'i khyu tshogs kun/ /'dod 'bras sbyin pa'i bcud kyis nyer myos te/ /dga'
ba'i rnam 'gyur 'bum g.yos dar dir gyi/ /bstod dbyangs 'khor mor sgrogs pa'ang dngos po'i gshis/ /zhes kyang smras so// ! sa ga zla nang rje rdo rje 'chang nyid kyi thugs
bskyed rlabs po ches ji srid bskal pa'i bar du zhal gyi dam tshig bskang gso gsar 'dzugs mdzad de de'i tshogs dbur rje rdo rje 'chang sku mched zhal rgyas su phebs shing
/ tshugs gong gtso gtor mdun rgyab bye nas gzhig cing gtor dar mchod me'i khar lhungs

grabs kyis me nyen yang che tsam byung ba sogs ni/ lo de'i ston bdag mos dbus la phebs pa dang phyi lo 'jam mgon mthu stobs dbang phyug nyid zhal mi bzhugs pa'i snga ltas su
ngos 'dzin mdzad/ snron zla'i mjug nas chu stod zla mjug bar rje nyid tshe dpag med lha dgu'i ljags bsnyen sbyin sreg bcas bka' drin che skabs/ 'jam mgon gcung dam pa nyid
tshogs dbur phebs mu yin pa bzhin bde mchog sgrub mchod dus de gras kyi grwa gzhon zhig phyogs la 'khyar/ kye rdor sgrub mchod dang bstun rgyu dbang gnang dus kyang dbang
yol shor rkyen gyis dkyil 'khor phyed tsam la skyon pa sogs mi dge ba'i mtshan ma'ang byung ba dang / chu stod tshes bzhi'i dge tshar phebs gong rje rdo rje 'chang nyid
ljags thun la bzhugs mur zhabs brtan 'bul gnang dang chabs gcig phyag 'tshal thugs smon sogs mang po zhig mdzad mthar khong rang gi rgyun gyi zhal 'don phyag phreng de
rje nyid la phul nas phebs song bas rje nyid kyi thugs la de dus ka phyi lo zla tshes de la zhing brje ba'i brdar gzigs/ de tsam na gong dkar rdo rje 'chang chos dbang
rgya mtsho gdan sar phebs nas bka' chos gnang ba'i 'go tshugs dang / gro bzhin tsam nas bzung bdag mos dbus la phebs rtsis mdzad mu dang / phur sgrub thog phur dbang tshar
'ga' zhig stsal rjes khrums zla nas klu sdings zhabs drung mi 'gyur rgyal mtshan/ rje drung ngag dbang / yon tan rgya mtsho sogs la sman bla/ klu dbang rgya gzhung klu
sgrub kyis mdzad skor/ rig ral gyi sgrub thabs/ rong ston gyi bstod lung bcas dang / bka' gdams lha bzhi/ gang blo ma'i rig gtad/ 'jam dkar/ dmar ser/ 'od zer can/ gza' yum/
rnam rgyal/ gtsug 'bar/ mi g.yo dkar sngon/ bcu gcig zhal/

don zhags lha lnga/ seng sgra ngag bsrung 'grol bcas/ gnyan sgrol mtshan brgya bcas/ ngo lugs dang nyi sbas sgrol ma/ dbang sgrol/ sgrol dkar rjes gnang dang rgya gzhung sgrub
thabs le tshan bum chog gtor chog sgom srung bris srung ltas ngan g.yang len byad 'grol/ gnas dang chom rkun srung ba lam srung rnams dang / sgrub thabs/ rjes gnang /
sbyin sreg /tshe khrid rnams kyi lung dang / rta mgrin dbyug tho can/ skyer sgang zla rgyal lugs/ dbyangs can dkar mo/ sme brtsegs/ dzam ser nag dkar gsum/ de'i chu sbyin
sogs yig rnying / gos sngon can/ rnam sras rigs can bco lnga dang snyan grags sgrub/ a pa ra tsitta/ sgrub thabs rgya mtsho dang rgya gzhung gi lung / las gshin bcu gsum/
sna tshogs yum/ rdo rje shugs/ khyung khra/ seng gdong nag mo/ rig byed ma'i rjes gnang thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa gsang sgrub byin rlabs lung bcas/ tshogs bdag
dmar chen/ chags rdor phyag bzhi pa/ 'dod rgyal/ dmar chung skor gsum/ dzam dmar dang de'i yig rnying sgrub skor lung / zhal bsnyen dus/ dur bdag dmag zor/ tshe ring mched
lnga rnams kyi rjes gnang lung bcas dang rigs gsum spyi/ tshe dpag med lha dgu/ 'chi med rnga sgra/ mi 'khrugs pa rnams dang sbyong dkyil bcu gnyis/ phur pa'i stod las
rnams kyi dbang dang / smad las rjes gnang / drag dmar nyang lugs dbang dang phrin gzhung brgyud 'debs las mtha' gsal byed rnams kyi lung dang / bde mchog lhan skyes byin
rlabs dang dpyal a mo gha sangs rgyas rin chen bcas kyi khrid yig lung / phag dkar/ dpyal lugs phag mo skor gsum/ nA ro mkha' spyod/

chos nyid dngos ston rnams kyi byin rlabs dang be'u bum lung rnams kyis skal ldan de dag smin cing grol bar 'dzad/ de'i tshe gong dkar rjer dpal rtse sogs yog dkyil chen mo
rnams gsan bzhes mdzad rjes khrums zla'i nyer gsum nas 'jam mgon mthu stobs dbang phyug nyid kye rdo rje'i gzhi bsnyen la 'jug par mdzad cing / dbyug zla'i tshes 'gor bdag
mos dbus la phebs pa dang stabs mtshungs su 'jam mgon gcung rin po che nyid thog mar sku rlung 'dra bas rim gyis snyun lci tsam bzhes tshul dang / de dus mdzod 'dzin pa'ang
dbus su phebs/ rje nyid kyis dam pa rnams kyi ngo mtshar rnam thar la gtso bor gyur pa chos 'chad sogs 'char 'phar gyi bsten mkhas bgyi ba rnams dang gang ci'i rim
gro'i zhal bkod bcas tshar phyin mdzad/ smin zla'i nang a Ni drung dang gang gi yum mchog dam pa de nyid kyi nang rten dngul gdung rin po che gsar bskrun mdzad rgyu'i nang
gzungs gdung tsha rnams la phyag nas dang mgo zla'i nang khang gsar dbon chos skyong bzang po/ /or du su blo bzang tshogs gnyis/ tshe ring pi si sogs la kye rdor rgyu dbang
dang dmar po skor gsum gyi rjes gnang sogs 'dod chos kyi bdud rtsis blo gros kyi bum pa 'gengs par mdzad rjes dus mdos phrin 'chol gyi nang so grub nas rta mgrin yang
gsang gi sgrub pa mdzad pa'i skabs sa skya tshogs kyi dar chen la rlung gnon sgrog thag 'dogs mi thang du lhung nas tshe'i dus byas par tshang ma ya nga zhing rnam rtog
za ba zhig byung ba de bzhin rjes su dgongs tshe/ me glang lo'i dpyid rgyal dbang rin po che dang dbyar 'jam mgon gcung dam pa nyid zhing brje ba'i ltas su ngos 'dzin mdzad
pa bzhin don la'ang de ltar du 'khums so/ /de dag gi don bsdu na/ ji

srid bskal mang snyed kyi rdzing bu ru/ /nar mar 'babs pa dam tshig gso ba'i rgyun/ /tshugs pa'i sgrun zlar mi shigs rdo rje'i srog /mA sa ri bong can gyi ngang du grub/ /de
tshe rjes skyes dam pas lkog gyur dang / /'grogs nas phyis 'byung ltas kyi mel tshe g.yos/ /rnal 'byor dkyil 'khor gtso bo'i he ru kar/ /bzhengs te skyed byed drin gzo'i
cho ga bsgrubs/ /bsnyon bral dam pa'i las su che ba ni/ /'chad rtsod rtsom sogs gsungs phyir drin can rjes/ /khor yug kun tu bstan pa'i byi dor la/ /dal med gzhol 'dir
mi dang blo ldan su/ /zhes kyang smras so// ! dgung grangs nyer dgur phebs pa me glang rgyal zla'i nang rje rdo rje 'chang sku mched kyi rgyun tsha rnams la zhal dkar ngag
dbang lags nas dbu rtser rab gnas brgya tshar mdzad skabs nyin gcig 'jam dbyangs gzi 'od 'bar ba'i spyan gnyis nas chab zegs pa zhig byung zhing / rta zla'i nang ngor pas
'jigs byed drug cu pa dang / gong dkar dpon slob rin po che nas kyang gtor bzlog mang du gnang mu'i/ dbo zla'i tshes bzhir gong sa rgyal dbang rin po che chos dbyings
su thim tshul gyi dgongs rdzogs 'bul bar mdzod 'dzin lha sar phebs shing rje nyid nas dgongs rdzogs su bde kye gsang gsum sogs kyi sgrub mchod gnang / de'i tshe klu sdings
zhabs drung rin po che zhabs 'bam gyi snyun lci mos ngor du khyogs la gdan 'dren mdzad rjes gza' skar legs mdzom nas/ mus chen sems dpa' chen po'i thugs dam ma ras bris
tshe dkyil zhal phye nas tshe dpag med lha dgu'i sgrub mchod brgya tshar gyi dbu tshugs mdzad/ de dus zla sked tsam la gang nas 'ong med pa'i bud med sprul gzugs 'dra ba
lung pa du ma'i mi nor ngo shes pa zhig byung

ba ni dus rtags lta bu yin 'dra gsungs/ mdzod 'dzin gdan sar 'byor nyer 'jam mgon gcung dam pa nyid la chab bsags kyi 'go zug dang bye tshogs sku rten pa'ang 'byor/ de sngon
nas bla ma dam pa du ma dang chos skyong 'ga' zhig gi lung / gzhan yang mo rtsis sogs la babs pa'i tshe dbang rjes gnang sogs tshang ma rje rdo rje 'chang nyid nas mdzad
pa dang mnyam du tshe chog /gtor ma/ bka' bstan gsung sgrogs/ mdos/ gtor bzlog /bskang ba/ sbyin sreg /sAtstsha sogs sku rim sgrub 'os kun chos sde nyi zla zung / ngor/
chos lhun/ zha lu sogs su mdzad cing / gzhan yang rtsis bon nas byung ba'i gto bcos sogs gang 'tshams mdzad skabs shig rje nyid lha khang rtser phebs te bye tshogs sku rten
par sku gsol thog lung zhu nan tan mdzad pas rbod gtong gi cho 'phrul yin tshul gyis 'jam mgon dpal ldan chos skyong gi gsung bzhin bgyis pas 'thus zhes stsal zhing /
phad bur lcags glang sogs bcug pa zhig zhags pas bcings te brag chung gi rir gnon la de'i khar mchod rten byin can gzhag /ces dang / yang nam mkhar yul gyis gzigs te/ lam
gyi gzhi mdor lha babs mchod rten bzhengs/ gzim chung gtso bo'i shar lhor rgyal mtshan dkar po 'od ldan tshugs gsungs pa las sku srog la skyon 'byung min nges sbyar zhu
bar mdzad kyang lan med du yal/ de skabs gzim chung shar na rje rdo rje 'dzin nyid bzhugs pa bzhin gtso bo yin pas de'i shar lhor rgyal mtshan dkar po 'dzugs dgos de bzhin
ring min nas sngags 'chang gos dkar lcang los mdzes pa'i skur bzhengs dgos kyi brda dang / mchod rten ni g.yul thang gsham gyi 'di nyid/ lha babs ni gdung brgyud rin po
che

tshar du dngar ba phebs par brtags pas chos skyong gi bka' lung yang gsal por stsal/ sa ga'i tshes 'gor 'jam mgon gcung dam pa'i sku mtshams grol kyang sbyin sreg ni gnang
ma thub/ de'i tshes bcu drug nyin g.ya' lung 'jag gshongs kyi 'khon sku 'bum la nyams gso gsar bskrun nang gzungs bcas legs par mdzad/ de dus lan gcig rje rdo rje 'dzin gyi
'od gsal du sgo rum bse mgon chenapo yin dgongs pa'i mgon po'i zhal 'bag sngo thal char lhags kyis gdungs pa 'dra ba zhig ltag sgo rdo skas 'gor gzhan la 'gro tshul gyis
byung bas thugs khral 'khrungs pa zhig dang / yang / bse mgon bzhugs khyim na mal lo'i thugs dam ma yin zer ba'i rus krong gzi brjid can zhig mchis par bse mgon gyi tshab
yin 'dra dgongs pa zhig dang / lan cig sku mched phyag sbrel gyis phebs bzhin pa'i mur sku skye de'i rnam pa med par byis pa lo lnga'i tshod tsam zhig mchis pa'i mthar/
rgya dkar nag gandho la'i steng khri zhig la 'jog gnang thog mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags kyi skur 'gyur ba dang / lan cig chos dung rin po che 'jam mgon gcung dam
pa nas bzung gnang gi mod du 'jim rlon bzhin zhig pa dang / skabs shig mon pa zhig nas gzhi thog la bsdigs te mda' 'phen pa dang / ban de zhig gis rje nyid ma gtogs sku
'khor tshad mar bsnun cing bsdigs pa sogs ltas ngan pa bstud mar 'khrungs pas bzlog thabs kyang de dang de'i gnyen por ci dgos ye shes kyi gzigs pas 'doms par mdzad cing
/ gcung dam pa nyid la'ang sngon du ljags bsnyen skabs rje 'bangs nyer lnga'i gras dran pa nam mkha'i sku skye yin dgongs pa'i mod gter zhig 'don par mdzad pas/ gro ga dang
dar dmar la gter

chos dhA ki dhA ki zer ba'i glegs bam zhig rnyed pa dang / yang nyid kyi khong nang na byis pa mche ba skya zing nge ba zhig skye la khad yod dgongs pa dang / yang ljags thun
skabs dngos su rang sems kye rdor yab yum gyi rnam pa mtho gang tsam zhig rlangs pa bun ne 'thon nyams 'khrungs pas thugs skyo lhang nge ba dang / da nged gcong can 'di'i
gdung gi go sa mi yong bas gang ci'i mtshams la bla ma rin po che rang thugs bsam cher bskyed mdzad dgos gsung pa dang / skabs 'gar rim gro gsol sman sogs kyis dga' mo
yong 'gro zhes thugs gso'i tshul mdzad lan du/ bdag la zla ba brgyad par dri med rnam gnyis dang mi 'khrugs pa'i gsung chog rnams gnang rogs mdzod gsung pa sogs sku mched
thugs yid gcig 'dres kyi mdzad pas dus 'da' ba'i mur 'jam mgon dpal ldan chos skyong spyan 'dren gyis rjes gnang / 'chi bslu/ phrin 'chol/ zhal bkod sogs tshang ma rtag
'grus su mdzad cing / rje der brtag par bskyar zhus mdzad pas 'jam mgon gcung dam par rim gro phran bu dang / 'u bu 'di pas sku zhabs gcen gyi zhabs brtan la brtson dgos
'dug /ces zhus par mi gnang bar rje nyid kyi sku gegs sel thabs stsal bas gzhan dag na re/ ci gsung / zhus par mi gnang ma zhus par stsol ba 'di 'dra ya mtshan zhes sgrogs
pa'ang byung mod/ 'jam mgon de nyid kyis mngon mkhyen gsal por stsal ba yin grang / skabs shig rje rdo rje 'chang nyid nas phyag rdor u tsarya'i rjes gnang mdzad dus
'jam mgon gcung rin po che'i sku sha'i pags hrag la tsha 'khyug 'khyug 'khrungs pa dang / mkha' 'gro bsun bzlog mdzad skabs bsu ba rnams phyir slog pa'i mtshan ma mus chen
la 'khrungs pas

da cha yar bskyed bzhes pa zhig e yong gsungs mur gdugs dkar byad 'grol sogs mdzad/ zha lu nas bla grwa nyi shu skor gyis bu lugs bzlog chen bzhi/ tshe chog /don zhags sogs
dang / bla ma ye shes grags pas slob dpon mdzad de gdugs dkar mdos 'phen rgyu'i snga dro khong la khrag rlung snyun thub byung ba sogs 'tshubs nyams dang / de mtshams nas
'jam mgon gcung rin po che'i gsungs las/ bde mchog nas a lce drung mched byon na gsung bar rje nyid kyis ston ka tsam byon pas 'thus gsungs pa yin tshul mdzad pas/ ston
sgug long mi yong lags gsungs pa dang / rje nyid kha'ur sman chab la phebs grabs kyi nyer bsdogs mdzad pas/ 'jam mgon dpal ldan chos skyong gi gsung las chab kyang 'gyangs
pa dang gtar kha ni de lo nas bzung ji srid 'tsho ba'i bar mi rung gsungs pa'ang don gnas bzhin de nas bzung gnang ma dgos shing / sman pa zung nas chu gtar gnyis ka bshol
na zhabs la snyun gzhi byung dogs gleng ba ltar chu stod tshes lngar chab la phebs rtsis kyis tshes bzhir zhal dkar dkon rgyan la gang ci zhib gleng gnang bas/ da nangs
phyag rtsa gdeng khel zhig mi 'dug pas chab bshol cis kyang gnang dgos zhus don bzhin dang / de nas je zhan bcas sku drung du phebs pas bla sman pa mchi ma 'byin cing
'dug pas de 'phral bdud rtsi 'phel gdung sogs zhu bar mdzad cing / 'jam mgon dpal ldan chos skyong spyan 'dren mdzad pas des kyang spyan chab nyil bzhin du da sku zhabs
rin po che 'dir ma bzhugs gsung pas gzim spyil du phebs nas thugs dam gsol 'debs la brtson par mdzad pas dar tsam zhig nas dgongs pa chos dbyings su thim pa'i tshul gsan

pas/ rkyen sel rim gro sman zas spyod sogs gang la'ang 'gyod med de tsam zhig ni bgyis/ las dbang bzlog med 'di 'dra ang gsung ba'i mur zham 'bring pa rnams nas thugs gso dang
sbrags dgongs rdzogs skor gyi zhal bkod dang / sku bstod sogs gsol btab la de ring mang ja zhig dang / gzhan rnams 'jam mgon dpal ldan chos skyong sogs la zhu rtsis yin/
gsol 'debs da lta 'ong gsungs nas 'gro la rjes brtse ma 'di skad cig la stsal/ kye ma thub dbang bstan pa'i sogs shlo ka gcig ni lo de'i dpyid gong sa rin po che sogs
bstan 'dzin gzhan gshegs pa'ang thugs dran gyi gsung yin gsungs/ dar tsam nas 'jam mgon dpal ldan chos skyong spyan chab kyis brnangs pa tsam gsung 'dar bzhin du de ring
bdag sogs gdul bya kun gyi bsod nams dus gcig tu zad pa'i gnas tshul ngan pa de 'dra mthong byung bas da cha skyabs mgon dam pa nyid zhabs pad yun bzhugs kyi dgongs pa g.yel
med nas/ bstan don lar rgya tshang mar thugs bskyed zab sgron zhu dgos la'ang rim bzhin gsan bzhes thugs rje che dgos zhes dngos po'i 'bul cha dang bcas mdzad pas/ bka'
las/ spyir bdag rang bsod nams dman pas gzhon nu nas yab rje rdo rje 'chang gshegs/ gdan sa'i khur byis pa zhig la babs/ bar skabs su ya hud yong la khad kyi snang tshul
du ma'ang byung / khyad par nu bo de bdag rang la 'khri zhing gdan sa 'dzin par med ka med rang yin kyang / sdod ring lus gcong zhing da lo nad yun ring por byed sgo
kun 'thud ma shor bar byas khul dang / khyad par sku zhabs nyid nas de lta bu'i thugs brtson mdzad kyang gegs chag bzlog med kyi snang tshul 'dir bdag ni tshig pa za rang
drags kyang bya thabs mi 'dug pas sku zhabs

nas de lta'i thugs ngal mi bzhes par 'phral yun gang cir 'di nas kyang zhu cha mang du mchis pas de bzhin thugs khur che bzhes zhu gsungs pas thugs gsos te gnas skabs kyi gsung
gleng dang / 'jam mgon des spur drung thugs dam gsal 'debs sogs dang dus mtha'i zhal bkod tshang ma gnang ba dang chabs gcig rje rdo rje 'chang nas kyang thugs dam gyi
rtsis gang zin mdzad de tshes lnga nas bzung kye rdor sgrub mchod la thugs gzhol ba'i skabs dang / chos sde nyi zla zung nas kun rig sgrub mchod/ bzang spyod 'bum ther/
ban tshang pas kye rdor sgrub mchod rnams dang / zhag gsum nas thugs dam grol rtags je gsal gyis 'jam mgon mus chen ngag dbang lags rnams nas gsung chog dang / tshes bdun
la spur chas zhal bkod kyis spur bzhu'i gnas 'ga' zhig brtag sgril gnang bar phun gling tshoms chen 'thon pas der bca' sgrig dang brag rtsa rje'i dgongs rdzogs 'char can
yang gnang / chos brgyad snga dro mchod phreng rgyas pa'i dbus su sku spur spyan 'dren gyis phun gling sgo 'phyor du nye skor skya ser tshang mas byin rlabs zhus rjes
tshoms chen du gang gi 'jam mgon dpon slob rnams kyis kye rdor sbyin sreg sgo nas bzhu sbyangs mdzad pas chab nad can gyi sku spur de ni brlan med ltar skad cig la me mchod
bzhes pas 'jam mgon thugs dges te gsung chog gi mtshams shig la bum sgor thugs rtog mdzad pas dbu yongs rdzogs de phyogs su dud de dbu thod logs la kha sar pa Ni 'dra
ba'i bzhengs sku gsal ba gzigs shing / nang ltas dang bstun nam mkha' la'ang ngo mtshar 'dra yod 'gro dgongs gzigs pas nyi ma gsal zhing 'ja' dkar phon tsam byung bas/ 'o
ya gi ka yin 'dug gsungs

shing phyag thal mo mdzad/ thugs dam grol nas zhe dgu'i bar rje rdo rje 'chang nyid kyis kye rdor sgrub mchod nar ma'i nyin re bzhin de'i lho sgo'i gsung chog dbang bskur bcas
dang / zhag bdun pa'i thog mtshan byang sreg pa/ dkyil 'khor gshegs gsol sogs bdun tshigs rnam dag gi phyag bzhes kyi sgo nas rjes 'dzin dang / tshes bcu nas zhag gsum
ring sku gshegs kyi ljags bsnyen kha skong bcu cha'i sbyin sreg spel tshig can bcas mdzad/ spur khang dang gdung rus bsdu ba sogs 'jam mgon des mdzad nas spur sgam tshur
'byon dus mchod phreng nyung ngu'i sil snyan gyi sgra snyan du lhung bas thugs skyo lhang gi mur/ e ma 'dus byas thams cad ni mi rtag pa zhes gsungs pa'i snang tshul ni
'di 'dra dgongs pa'i ngang du dar tsam zhig 'byams/ bcu bzhi nas zhag lnga'i ring ngor du dge 'dun lnga brgya skor la bsnyen rgyas dang / dbus lho byang la dgongs rdzogs
sgrub mi ched mngags kyis lha sar jo zhal rnam gnyis/ rang byon bcu gcig zhal/ byams pa mched lnga/ byams pa chos 'khor/ lo ke shwa ra rnams la snyan shal/ byang chen rgyal
tshab rin po che/ bsam yas/ khra 'brug /yar klung shel brag rnams kyi rten gtsor yang snyan shal/ rnam grong rdo rje 'chang la bsngo rten sman par/ gos jus yug /gong
dkar 'dus sde nas gur rigs bsdus/ kye rdor bka' babs bzhi/ gza' yum/ bdag med ma/ gsang 'dus mi bskyod pa/ 'jam rdor/ sgrol ma bcu bdun/ gur sgrol/ a ra pa tsa na/ rigs gsum
spyi/ bde mchog lU nag dril gsum/ phag mo so bdun/ 'jigs byed ro langs brgyad bskor/ bcu gsum ma/ zhe dgu ma/ sgyu ma chen mo/ kun rig /rnam bir/ gshed dmar lha lnga/
bcu gsum ma/ dgra

gdong rnams kyi dkyil 'khor sgrub mchod dgos cha yon bcas dang / bkra shis chos sder gnas gsar rdo rje 'chang chen por na bza' cha tshang / phyag phreng rgyan bcas/ rdzab gsol/
phur pa sogs phyag cha rnams dang / chibs sga 'khor/ brgyad tshan gsum rnams dang / 'dus spyi nas kye rdor man ngag lugs/ bdag med ma/ gur rigs bsdus / rdo rje sgrol
ma/ rig byed ma/ gsang 'dus lugs gnyis/ 'jigs byed bcu gsum/ phyag rdor 'khor chen/ bde mchog lU nag /mkha' spyod ma/ mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho/ sangs rgyas mnyam sbyor/ gdan
bzhi/ sam pu Ti/ gur lha brgyad/ kun rig /rigs gsum spyi/ mi 'khrugs pa/ tshe dpag med/ 'od zer can/ rnam rgyal/ dus 'khor rnams kyi sgrub mchod dgos cha yon bcas/ zha
lur rdor dbyings rtsa lugs/ 'grel lugs/ rtse mo dang dpal mchog rigs bsdus/ dpal mchog rdor sems/ khams gsum rnam rgyal/ chos dbyings gsung dbang / 'jam dpal rigs bsdus/
'jam dpal gsang ldan/ kun rig /mi 'khrugs bcu gsum/ 'chi bdag 'joms pa/ rnam snang mngon byang / dri med rnam gnyis/ gra lnga/ gnas bcu/ don zhags/ gdugs dkar/ phyag rdor
'gro bzang / rnam rgyal/ sman bla/ 'chi med rnga sgra rnams kyi sgrub mchod dgos cha yon bcas/ gzhan yang gtsang dbus dgon sde nyis brgya dang zhe bdun tsam la mang skol
bsngo rten rnam gzhag sogs dang / paN chen thams cad mkhyen drung ljags bsngo rten dngul srang lnga bcu/ ja 'khor/ chibs sga 'khor rnams kyis mtshon brgyad tshan gsum bcas/
tshang ma'i dngos po gang song bsdoms ja 'khor drug don gsum lhag

tsam/ dngul srang chig stong sum brgya nyi shu skor/ dgu tshan brgyad tshan re/ bdun tshan kha shas/ lnga tshan so gsum/ gsum tshan nyis brgya bcu gcig /snam bubs brgya dang
go lnga/ kha btags chig khri drug stong bdun brgya brgal tsam/ mar khal brgya dang bdun cu skor/ gser zho brgya dang don drug bcas song zhing / spur rus btul zin nas gdung
tsha mchod dgu ma 'bum ther gtsug tor dri med snying po can dang / bla ma yi dam chos srung nor lha'i sku khri phrag brgal tsam gyi sAtstsha rnams chos grwa lho'i dge
'dun res bskor gyis khur bzhes 'go pa lde phyung pa bkra shis 'od zer gyis bgyis te thog mar tshoms dmar/ de nas lha chen thigs g.yab shar du tshugs/ gro bzhin tshes bzhi
nas thigs g.yab lho sogs su bde kye gsang gsum/ bdag med ma/ mkha' spyod ma/ kun rig /tshe chog /rnam rgyal/ bstan pa gso chog zhag bdun rnams dang rje rdo rje 'chang nyid
nas zhe dgu'i kye rdor grol nye yin pas skabs shig sku gshegs de snyun med sngar gyi rang chas su 'khrungs pas rang bzhin gyi gsung gleng mur deng sang 'o brgyal mi 'dug
gam gsung pas/ skyon ci yang mi 'dug bdag gi zhe dgu them dus gur mgon lha brgyad kyi dbang zhig bskur grogs mdzod gsung pa 'khrungs pa bzhin nyer lngar zhe dgu them
dus mgon po'i dbang chen gras lha brgyad dkyil chog khol sgrub kyis dbang bskur mdzad/ de skabs gzhung zhabs rin po che/ sde dge sa dbang / 'brug sde srid sogs kyis gtso
mdzad gzhis byes che phra du mas zhabs 'debs dngos po gser dngul ja sogs mang du 'bul bar mdzad/ khrums zla'i 'gor gdung tsha rnams grub pas rje nyid lha khang rtse'i smon
gnas yid 'ong tshal du bzhugs

'jags kyis phyag nas grangs gsog dang sbrags sku gshegs kyi zhal chems bzhin dri med rnam gnyis mi 'khrugs lha dgu rnams rdul dkyil thog nas ci rigs dang / phyi dro'i tshe
mgon khang du slad kyi phrin 'chol sogs la thugs brtson mdzad/ de nas rje rdo rje 'chang gi thugs dgongs la sku gshegs de'i zhe dgu zla mchod sogs la dge ba rgya cher ni
mdzad zin/ lo mchod kun rig ni btsugs/ gzhan dge rgyun rang ma byung yang chog /da ko gdan sa mdzes rgyan dngul gdung khyad 'phags shig byung na sku gshegs kyi dgongs pa
rdzogs thabs kyang de bas lhag pa med pa dang / khyad par gdan sa chen po 'di la zhabs tog tu dgongs te thog mar dus mchod gtsug lag khang bkod legs mdzad rjes der bzhugs
yul bgyid 'khrungs par sku dogs che skabs shig gso mi rung ba'i rgyu mtshan sogs snyan sgron bzhin lha mthil sprul pa'i gtsug lag khang chen por sku gsung gi rten khyad
mtshar bzhugs kyang thugs rten khyad 'thon ma bzhugs par dgongs/ mchod sdong 'dzam gling 'od gsal 'di nyid bzheng rgyu'i thig rtsa thar rtse paN chen gsung la sangs rgyas
phun tshogs kyis mchan gnang bzhin mdzad rjes byang chub mchod rten gyi shing bkod sogs bka' yis 'doms rjes/ dbyug zla'i nang chos gra lho byang pa/ yul chen pa/ nyi shar
pa/ chos lhun pa sogs brgya skor la gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i smin grol bsdus tsam zhig mdzad pa ni 'di nyid 'chad thang gsum pa'i skabs so/ /'di
lo mthong ba don yod nyams gso gsar bskrun lta bu'i gtsug lag khang steng ma gsar bzhengs kyis phebs 'grul skabs phyag 'byor gyi sku rten rnams bzhugs su gsol/ de mtshams
nas 'dzam gling na blo ldan gzur gnas kun gyi bsngags

brjod kyi me tog 'thor zhing 'dud pa'i yul du gyur pa mtshan mchog gsum ldan gyi gdung rabs rin po che 'jig rten na phan bde'i btsas su che ba 'di nyid spel ba'i phyir sdom
brtson ngur smrig gi brtul zhugs las slar ldog ste sngags 'chang gos dkar lcang los mdzes pa'i skur bzhengs su gsol bar/ lcang skya rdo rje 'chang / gnas gsar rdo rje 'chang
/ 'jam mgon dpal ldan chos skyong / gzhung zhabs rin po che dgung blon chen po rnams dang bcas sde dge sa skyong / zhu chen rin po che rnams kyis thog drangs mdor na
rje btsun sa skya'i bstan pa rin po che thugs la bcangs so cog nas gdung brgyud rin po che'i sku che ba'i lo rgyus zhib gleng gis jeng drangs te/ gdung 'dzin gyi go sa rin
po cher phebs dgos pa'i gsol 'debs nan tan chen pos mdzad pa'i rkyen dang / rje rdo rje 'chang nyid kyang snyigs dus kyi bstan pa'i me ro gso ba la sngags 'chang chos
kyi rgyal po dang 'jam mgon a mes zhabs kyi rnam thar lhur bzhes don thog tu 'gyur ba'i thugs bskyed dang / skye 'gro'i bsod nams mi dman pa sogs sgo du ma nas rten 'brel
'grig ste ston mjug gza' skar legs mdzom thog chos lung rgyal po'i sras mo gzhon pa phun tshogs tshe ring de nyid gsang rgya 'dzol med du padma 'dam na gnas kyang 'dam gyis
ma gos pa bzhin du khab bzhes mdzad/ mgo zla nas bzung rje nyid kyis rje btsun sa skya pa'i gdung rabs myur 'byon sku rim du gdugs dkar nyer bdun ma'i sgrub mchod brgya
tshar grangs gsog dang bdag mor kye rdor rgyu dbang dang de tshe dpag med lha dgu'i dbang / sgrol ma nyer gcig sogs rjes gnang kha shas/ khyad par so sor 'brang ma'i rjes
gnang brgya tshar rnams mdzad pa tsam nas bzung rje btsun sa skya pa'i gdung brgyud rin po che ma 'ongs srid mtha'i bar du 'byon pa'i ched kho nar gnang ba'i mdzad pa
gcig pur bltas kyang sku tshe ril po byol ba dang 'dra

ba lags so/ /de dag gi don bsdu na/ gnam lo sgra gcan 'bar ba'i glang dar gyis/ /kha ba ri pa'i legs byas gsog pa'i rten/ /phyag na padma 'jam dbyangs nyi zla zung / /kho bo'i
snang ba 'phrogs so kye ma hud/ /'on kyang drang srong chen po'i bka' lung gis/ /bde gshegs bstan pa byang phyogs 'phel ba dang / 'grib pa'i tshul gsungs rdzun bral tha
tshig la/ /kun kyang re zhig ngal bso bsten pa'i grogs/ /ngan de'i gnyen por dam bcas byang chub sems/ /dpal gyi rdo rje slar byon tshar bcad dang / /mnyam du bstan pa'i
me ro nyer gsos te/ /dgongs dbyings rdzogs pa'i snang ba'i zer phreng sbyin/ /gsung ngag legs bshad 'dab ma grol ba dang / /sngags 'chang utpal dkar po'i gos bzang can/
/sngon med gsar du bzhad pa'i dge mtshan ni/ /srid gsum che dgu'i gtam gyis bsus par nges/ /zhes kyang smras so// // ! dgung grangs sum cur phebs pas stag dpyid 'go mar
gong bzhin gyis bla ma yi dam sogs kyi sku par rnams dang / rje rdo rje 'chang nyid nas sku par stong du nye ba/ mchod pa rgya mchod dgu bsdoms nyis brgya skor 'debs par
mdzad/ rta zla nas mchod sdong gi zangs dngul/ gser/ phra rgyan sogs bzo gra'i bka' 'doms mdzad pa'i zangs dngul gser phra rgyan skor rje nyid kyi zhal sgo las byon pa'i
gdung rabs zhal skong bzhin dang / de'i tshe gzhung zhabs rin po che/ sde dge sa skyong sogs drag zhan du ma/ zhal ngo so so/ chos sde nyi zla zung sogs dgon sde mang po
phyag gnyer drung gras/ bla gnyer tshang gzhis mi ser skya sogs kyis phra rgyan gser dngul zangs sogs mang po'i zhabs 'debs phul/ nag zla nas bzung rje rdo rje 'dzin nyid
kyis rnam rgyal stong mchod ji song bar gsog gnang skabs/ gter ston rig 'dzin tshe dbang bkra shis kyis/ de'i gter chos zhig gi lung bstan las/ sa skya bo'i nang gi kun
dga'i ming : rkyen bar chad dam

sel dogs zon zab: /lha phur pa bsgrub na mchog tu shis: /rkyen der grol bod khams phan bde spel: /zhes sogs kyi lung dang auDy-in padma'i tshe chu ngo ma lo rgyus bcas stsal
ba bzhes shing / de dang chabs gcig rnam rgyal gyi sku gzungs 'bum ther bzhugs pa'i rnam rgyal mchod rten bzhi bzheng dgos tshul bzhin ngo mtshar rten bzhi'i gras rnam
rgyal sku 'bum gyi byang ngos su mchod rten 'di bzhi bzhengs gnang dang / brgya dpon bkra shis 'od zer nas rab gnas brgya tshar mdzad/ chu stod zla nang nas bzung rje btsun
sa skya pa'i gdung rabs myur 'byon ched du gzungs gra lnga'i sgrub mchod brgya tshar mdzad pa'i cho ga rer gtso mo'i sngags nyis brgya nyer gcig dang / lha mo bzhi'i sngags
zhe gnyis re 'khor sngags nyer gcig re bcas dang bstun bdag mor dbang bskur brgya tshar mdzad mu'i zla nang der ri khrod ma'i bum chog ljags rtsom gsar bsgrigs steng
thog mar gnang ste/ sgo rum du gsung bskang dang sbrags gsang rgya'ang grol zhing phun tshogs gling du phebs/ mi ring bar rje nyid kha'ur sman chab la chibs bskyod skabs

dang / gro bzhin phur sgrub grol nas mkhan chen gsar bsko dang bca' yig le tshan du ma 'di rnams ljags bsgrigs mdzad/ khrums zla'i nang shing bzo tshang ma grub pa'i

rus/ theg chen spur sha /nam mkha' rgyal

shes rab 'byung gnas kyi spur rus/ mus chen sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan dang sgar chen gyi dbu thod dum/ klu sgrub rgya mtsho'i spur rus/ ngag dbang chos grags kyi gdung thal/
a mes zhabs kyi thugs dum gdung rus/ bsod nams mchog ldan gdung rus/ ngag dbang rnam rgyal kyi dbu thod dum/ bsod nams dbang phyug gi gdung rus/ bstan pa rab rgyas kyi
tshems ring bsrel can gyi dum bu/ bzang po rgyal mtshan gyi gdung rus/ sngags 'chang kun dga' bkra shis kyi gdung rus gdung thal/ mtshal gtar ril bu/ yab rje rdo rje 'chang
gi spur chab zegs 'dam rnams dang / yang rgyal po 'od zer go cha/ 'khon dkon mchog rgyal po yab sras/ 'u yug pa rig seng / shes rab rgya mtsho/ rgyal tshab/ lha mchog
/'phags chen/ sa lo/ /dkon mchog lhun grub/ spyan snga ngag chos/ bdag chen kun legs/ sngags 'chang yab sras/ tshar chen/ mkhyen brtse/ nam dpal/ dbang phyug rab brtan/
ngag dbang chos grags/ a mes zhabs yab sras dbon/ bco brgyad chen mo khu dbon/ bzang po rgyal mtshan/ ka spe ba/ yab rje rdo rje 'chang rnams kyi dbu lo/ /gzhan yang gong
gi bla ma rnams kyi na bza'i dum bu/ gong ma lnga/ bdag chen/

sa lo/ spyan snga/ grol mchog /tshar chen/ mkhyen brtse/ sngags 'chang yab sras gsum/ shes 'byung / ngag chos/ rtse gdong khri chen khu dbon/ a mes zhabs yab sras dbon/ sangs
rgyas phun tshogs/ tshul khrims dpal bzang / yab rje rdo rje 'chang / rje rdo rje 'chang sku mched bcas kyi bdud rtsi ril bu phon che ba/ thang stong rgyal por tshe dpag
med kyis dngos su stsal ba'i tshe ril/ mkhyen brtse'i skye bdun ril bu sogs skye bdun duu ma jo bo'i phyag bris ma'i dpe dum/ bla ma gong ma'i gtor skam sne 'dus/ 'jam
dbyangs ril bu/ rten 'dam ril nar/ ba so'i dbang bum byin can rnams dang / chos 'khor nang yab rje rdo rje 'chang / a mes zhabs/ sngags 'chang chen po/ tshar chen/ go ram
rje/ rdo rje gdan pa/ rdzong pa kun rgyal/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang / gong ma lnga/ lo chen a ti sha /birWa pa/ bodhi satwa/ padma 'byung gnas/ klu sgrub/ sangs rgyas rdo
rje 'chang gi sku bcas bsdoms chig khri chig brgya don gcig /dbu gzungs lam zab/ kye rdor bka' babs bzhi/ bdag med ma/ gur/ sam/ dus 'khor sa lugs/ bde mchog lU nag dril
gsum/ sa phur/ gsang 'dus 'phags lugs/ 'jigs byed sa lugs/ kun rig /a ra pa tsa na lha lnga/ tshe dpag med lha dgu/ sems bskyed dbu ma lugs so thar/ gur zhal rnams kyi
bla brgyud dang / sa skya pa'i gdung rabs rnams brgya dang bcu gsum gser bris tshar gcig steng grub chen brgyad cu/ yang dag sa lugs/ dri med rnam gnyis kyi brgyud pa rnams
bzhugs

pa'i rtser sangs rgyas kyi ring bsrel rje nyid kyi phyag babs ji tsam 'dod pa 'jos kyang mi zad pa'i gter chen 'di nyid nas bco lnga dang de skabs 'phral 'byor nyer lnga/ khyung
po'i thugs byon ring bsrel gsum/ gtsug tor rnam rgyal gyi gzungs/ 'od zer dri med gzungs mdo yug bris/ gdugs dkar sku gzungs 'khor lo rnams bzhugs par rje nyid nas
rgyal mtshan 'dzugs chog dang rab gnas bsdus pa duu ma/ rgyas pa kye rdor dkyil chog dang 'brel ba zhi rgyas sbyin sreg bcas mdzad dus shangs 'ba' ra sprul skus bum pa bcud
ldan kha rgyan can gyis thog drangs dngos 'bul gya nom pa'ang mchod sdong gi drung du bzhes shing / da'u dpon don yod nas gser srang brgya phrag gi 'bul ba'ang zhi ba'i
sbyin sreg thog 'byor ba sogs ma bsgrigs lhun grub kyi la nye phun sum tshogs shing / bum pa ni da lta tshogs chen rnam rgyal sogs la mdzad pa 'di dang / gser de las 'og
nas 'byung ba'i bum sgo'i gser sku rdo rje 'chang bskrun par mdzad/ tshul 'di ni bdag cag gi ston pa mnyam med shAkya'i rgyal pos chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba'i tshe lha'i
gtso bo zung nas gser gyi 'khor lo dang dung dkar po phul ba sogs dang mtshungs par sems shing / de'i tshe dpon la dge bsnyen gyi sdom pa phog ste kun dga' rgyal mtshan
du ming 'dogs mdzad/ dpon des zhabs brtan gsung rtsom zhus par byon dang 'byon 'gyur gyi zhabs brtan gsol 'debs bkra shis 'gyur med g.yung drung gnang nas re zhig tshogs
'don ma mdzad par slar chu lug lo nas gnang chog byung ba'ang ma 'ongs mngon mkhyen gyi rten 'brel bla med du sgrigs par mdzad pa gor ma chag /rten bzhengs 'di nyid kyi
gzungs sogs skor zhib par bkod cing gzhan rje nyid kyis rten bzhengs gnang

bar bltas nas sku tshe ril po khyol ba dang 'dra bar mdzad pa gzhan rnams kyang 'di dang cha 'dra na'ang mang bas 'jigs te rgyas par spro ma nus/ de nas gser dngul sogs kyi
g.yogs ma grub pa'i shing 'bum de nyid la/ thub bstan lha chen gyi mkhan rabs nyer bzhi pa brtson 'grus ye shes kyis kye rdor rab gnas 'bring po brgya kha yar dang / mgo
zla nas rje rdo rje 'dzin nyid kyis gshed dmar sgrub mchod brgya tshar gyi dbu tshugs par mdzad do/ /de dag gi don bsdu na/ rigs rus phun tshogs 'od gsal lha lam nas/ /sku
mched nyi zla'i gzigs pas bstan 'gro'i tshal/ /'byed snang nyin mtshan brdal ba'i ngo mtshar gyi/ /ya gyal sngags 'chang gos dkar kunda'i gnyen/ /'dzam gling bsod nams
mig gis mi mngon dbyings/ /'dzegs phral pad dkar spungs pa'i ring bsrel gyis/ /nyer gtams chos sku'i rten gyi za ma tog /br-ikShas spras pa'i phyi rol mchod sdong smin/
/dam ye dbyer med byin rlabs spro bsdu mkhan/ /phun tshogs rten 'brel lhun grub tsha zer dbang / /gang 'dul sku yi zlos gar gling bzhi ru/ /sgyur mdzad drin can bla ma rdo
rje 'chang / /zhes kyang smras so// ! dgung grangs so gcig tu phebs pa sa yos dpyid gser sku rdo rje 'chang gi bzo gra dang rim gyis gser zangs g.yogs rnams mdzad mu'i
dbo zla nas gong gi gshed dmar sgrub mchod 'phro sa ga tsam la grol bar mdzad pa'i dngos chog brgya dang dgu la gtso bo'i nye snying chig 'bum chig khri bdun stong chig brgya
nga gnyis/ gtso bo'i snying po rtsa sngags yum dang 'khor sngags rnams chig khri sum stong chig brgya nga gnyis re rnams ljags bzlas su bstar zhing / rta zla sngon ma'i
bcu bdun la sde dger dpal ldan chos skyong dang phyi ma'i bco brgyad la tshe 'dzin dpal bskyed bu 'khrid dam tshul khrims dpal rgyas dbang mo'i yum

phun tshogs tshe ring ma gshegs pas snga ma'i nyi dros tsam la sa skya'i nam mkha'i dbyings thams cad sprin kha dog lnga ldan sngar mthong ma myong bas gang ba zhig byung dus
'jam mgon de zhing brjes pa rje nyid kyis mkhyen pa dang bcas/ rje de'i dgongs rdzogs su lo star dus dran gyi thog byams chos sde lnga klog 'don yang mdzad/ dbo zla'i
nang phun tshogs tshe ring ma'i dgongs rdzogs su 'jam dbyangs kyi sman sku ngo mtshar can 'di'i sku rgyu rten 'dam dpe bral mar grags pa sogs byin rlabs phon che ba dang
rin po che dang sman sna'i tshogs kyi phye ma 'jim par bsres nas rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan gyi nang rten 'jam dbyangs gzi 'od 'bar ba'i sku dbyibs 'dra gang
lon mdzad nas ring bsrel rnam bzhis phyur por mdzad de rab tu gnas pa'i byin rlabs kyi gzi byin g.yos te bzhugs su gsol ba dang / yang a Ni'i drung kun dga' bstan pa'i
nyi ma dang rje nyid kyi yum mchog bsod nams dpal gyi dbang mo zung gi nang rten dngul gdung rin po che byang chub mchod rten phyag tshad can dbu zhabs bar gsum gyi gzungs
ring bsrel/ sku gshegs zung gi gdung 'dam la sAtstsha/ bla ma yi dam sangs rgyas byang sems chos srung nor lha'i sku par grangs mang bskrun pa sogs kyis gtams te phra
rgyan mchod rdzas dang bcas ngo mtshar 'phrul gyi bka' 'doms tshar phyin mdzad rjes dam ye dbyer med du byin gyis brlabs te lus can bsod nams gsog pa'i zhing mchog dam par
mig gi spyod yul du gsal ba 'di dang / yang rab 'byams rgyal ba kun gyi spyi gzugs khyab bdag dpal ldan bla ma dam pa bka' drin mtshungs med thar rtse rdo rje 'chang nam
mkha' bsam 'grub kun dga' mtshan dpe'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po zhes snyan pa'i ba dan srid pa gsum na gsal ba de nyid kyi sman sku yid bzhin gyi nor bu gsar bskrun
mdzad pa 'di nyid kyi rgyu ni/ sa 'jim gtsang mar rdzas nyer lnga'i thog drangs bzang zhing gya nom

pa du ma dang / rten 'dam dpe bral ma la slar yang rje nyid nas byin rten mang du bsre bar mdzad pa'i lde gu dang lhan cig sbrus pa las grub pa'i thar rtse ba nyid kyi sku
shin tu 'dra lon zhing mi bskyod rdo rje'i phyag rgya can du bzhugs pa 'di nyid kyi nang gzungs gtso bo yab rje bsod nams rin chen gyi thugs dam rten yun ring mdzad pa'i
'jigs byed kyi sman sku chung ngu rwa lo'i mngon rtogs rin chen snying po dang mthun pa la 'dod gsol gyis spras pa/ rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas dang khyung po'i ring bsrel bcas
khyon dgu/ rje nyid kyi phyag tsha grangs mang / thar rtse rje'i thugs dam phyag phreng ba so de nyid kyi gdung 'dam dang gong ma mang po'i gdung 'dam las bskrun pa'i
sku par mang po/ dbu zhabs bar gsum gyi gzungs ring bsrel gyis phyur bar mdzad de 'dus tshogs nas rab tu gnas pa'i me tog tshar kha shas dang / rje rdo rje 'chang nyid kyis
kye rdo rje la brten pa'i rab tu gnas pa'i me tog gnad smin phul dus kyi gsung las/ ye shes sems dpa' phebs pa'i rtags kyang shar bas dgos 'dod re skong 'di nyid la rje
de rang gi dbu zhwa/ gos ber/ zhal dkar stegs bcas/ spyi blugs/ 'thor snod/ rdor dril/ nang mchod/ thod DA/ bum pa sogs bsod nams kyi zhing mchog der phul ba yin cing /
rje de'i sku drin ni nam du yang khyer mtha' ma mchis so/ /rgyu mtshan ci'i phyir na/ yab rje rdo rje 'chang de nyid zhi bar gshegs dus rang nyid byis pa na phra lugs gnyis
kyi blang dor la rmongs pa'i dus chos 'jig rten gyi mgo 'don tshang ma dam pa 'di'i sku drin gyis bskyangs pa'o/ /zhes gsungs/ de mtshams nas dbus kyi chos skyong khag
gi lung bstan las ru mtshon mang po dgos tshul bzhin nang so/ dus mchod dga' ldan smug chung rnams kyi nang dang bsam brling mgon khang steng bcas su so so'i thug chog
gsar bsgrigs ltar 'dzugs par mdzad pa dang /

yang spyan ltas shig la rtag 'tsher gangs mchod dgos tshul 'khrungs par yang de bzhin gsar bsgrigs thog mdzad/ snron zla'i nang rje btsun sa skya pa'i gdung rabs rin po che
'phel rgyas 'byung phyir dus mchod du/ zang tsha bsod nams rgyal mtshan dang bzang po dpal zung gi sman sku ring bsrel rnam bzhi'i gong bur bskrun te ji srid 'khor ba ma
stong bar du rje btsun sa skya pa'i gdung rabs rin po che rgyun mi chad par 'byon pa'i thugs bskyed bla na med pa dang bcas bla brang go bzhi las gdung rabs rin po che'i
'byung khungs su gyur pa dus mchod 'di nyid du bzhugs su gsol zhing / zla nang der mgon khang khag bzhi dang dngos grub gling rnams su rje nyid nas bdun phrag re'i ring
snga dro sgrol dkar yid bzhin 'khor lo'i bdag mdun bum bzlas rnams dang de'i rgyas pa'i sbyin sreg /phyi dro chos skyong so so'i bskang phrin bcas dpal gyi zhal zas re 'dod
don nam 'grub bar gta' mar bzung gnang gis skyed lhas su bdag nyid chen po bzang po dpal gyi sku bstod gsar bsgrigs mdzad pa dang bstun/ kun dga' tshe ring sogs kha shas
sku 'bum rnam rgyal la mchod 'bul gyi sgro btags te slar yang gsang rgya'i thog chos lung du rgyal yum sku drin can ma de nyid spyan 'dren par mngags te/ chu stod zla
nang gsang khog nas gdan sar phebs par bcom ldan 'das dpal gsang ba 'dus pa mi bskyod rdo rje'i rdul dkyil du smin par mdzad de rjes su gnang ba du ma dang / lha sku bde
stong dbyer med don dam pa'i gshis las ma g.yos kyang ltar snang mthun sdeb kyi la nyer shar ba'i rim gro rnams rim bzhin mdzad de gro bzhin phur sgrub dang bstun phun gling
du tho rengs snga bar phebs/ skabs shig rje nyid kyi 'od gsal du rgyal yum nyid dang lhan du brtse chen lha khang du phebs song bar gzim chung gi sgo 'gag de na rnal
'byor pa rus pa'i rgyan can bag dro ba zhig bzhugs 'dug pa des sna drangs brtse chen lha khang sa chen sku 'dra rin po

cher yab yum nas phyag gnang ste yab kyis yum la rten bshad gnang rtsis kyis/ phun sum tshogs pa mnga' ba gser gyi ri bo 'dra/ /zhes sogs bkra shis tshigs bcad gsum sngon 'gro'i
rten bshad mdzad skabs sku 'dra rin po che gzhan las gsal zhing dgyes nyams che ba zhig 'khrungs pa ni/ yab yum sku drin can las gdung brgyud rin po che zhal rnam pa
gnyis 'byon pa'i slar 'byung gi rten 'brel bla na med par yid gnyis dang bral/ khrums zla'i stod la gong gi gser sku rdo rje 'chang yang tshar phyin nas nang gzungs kyi

pa sde srid gtsang ba'i nang rten gras 'jam dbyangs bsod nams dbang po'i phyag babs de dang / gnyan phul byung ba gtsug tor rgyal pos gzhong par mdzad pa'i sa 'jam zhal sprod/
sa chen gyis phyag nas brgya tshar dang rje btsun sku mched kyi phyag nas dang thugs dam rten byin can/ sangs rgyas kyi 'phel gdung lnga rnams kyis thog drangs ring
bsrel rnam bzhi grangs mang nyung tsam ma gtogs mchod sdong nyid dang cha 'dra bzhugs par gza' skar dge ba nas 'thor nas sgrub par mdzad de rje nyid kyis rdo rje slob dpon
dang / mkhan po 'dus tshogs bcas nas kye rdo rje'i dkyil chog dang rjes 'brel rab gnas zhag bdun ma rgyas pa'i sbyin sreg /'o thug sgrub pa/ gzhan yang gtsug lag khang
rnams su sna lnga'i mchod pa/ dge 'dun bsnyen bkur mchod phreng bstar ba/ phyi bskor la me tog 'thor ba/ 'phen sku zhal dbye/ ston mo'i thog spyi sger legs skyes bzhes pa/
'go bzo bar gnang cha/ mnga' zhabs la 'bru 'gyed gzhas sogs cha lag tshang ba'i tshul gyis mdzad cing / gser sku rdo rje 'chang la na bza' sogs dang /

las zur sbug pha sgar sogs nas sbyin bdag dad can rnams kyis phul gras dkar shel gyi mchod dpyad/ rgyu sna tshogs las grub pa'i me tog phon bcas phyag tu son pa bzhin slob

bzhi/ sprul pa'i lha khang chen mo rnams kyi thog drangs gtsug lag khang ji snyed bzhugs pa la/ bar skabs su si tu byang rgyal dang lha sa rdzong pa sogs bstan dgra gdug

du/ /ma bsgrigs lhun grub la nye ci yang 'khrungs/ /byas shes drin gzo'i ngo mtshar phyag rjes ni/ /'jam dpal phug pa'i 'gram par rgyu ba byed/ /gdams pa'i mdzod sgo

dbyung gzengs bstod dang bcas sa skya pa'i gdung rabs 'byon par lung bstan pa dang / slob dpon bram ze mchog sred kyis sba sder la lcags dkrol ra ma lug gi rgyan btab pa zhig
tu gsol ja dron mo stsal ba dang / mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags mnal lam du 'khrungs tshe mgon des mdzad pa'i pod chen drug gi 'grel par ljags lung zhu 'dod kyis glegs

mtheb la gzug gzer 'khrungs pas bla sman rgyal tshing nas dreg yin tshul zhus/ je lod kyis mar lam skyed lhas mgon khang la'ang phebs ma bde/ sgang mkhar yum mchog nas
dbu mthing bzhes skabs chibs gzhol ba'i tshe zhabs nad sing dngas su gyur pas zhabs phyi kun de gar ha las/ skyes pho mos glu gzhas kyis sngun bsus gdan sar phebs pas zhabs
skyon ci yang ma byung ba ni 'phral du 'tshubs kyang 'gyangs min nas thugs 'dod 'grub pa'i la nye bzang bar ma zad dbu mthing bzhes 'phral snyun las grol tshul de bzhin
rje nyid 'byung bzhi la rang dbang thob pa'i dgongs gzhi khyad par can no/ /de'i sang nas yang sngar bzhin snyun gzhi des zla phyed tsam bskyed ma bzhes pa'i tshul gyi
thugs nyams 'ur te sman bcos rnams cham gyis bskyur nas sngar nas 'od gsal du 'khrungs shing phyis su rjes gnang yang gsan pa 'jam dpal nA ga raksha'i sgom bzlas srung
skud bcas mdzad pas/ zhag shas nas klu mang po zhig shi ba'i mtshan ma 'khrungs te snyun las grol ba'i tshul mdzad/ snron zla'i mjug nas zla

gcig ring rnam 'dren dam pa gnas gsar rdo rje 'chang chen po'i sku drin gsab ched dang / rje btsun sa skya pa'i sde bstan pa gdung brgyud dang bcas pa'i sku rim du rwa tshar
thun mong ma yin pa'i lugs dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed bcu gsum ma'i sgrub mchod brgya tshar grangs gsog mdzad skabs kyi chu stod zla ba'i tshes bcu gcig nyin gnas gsar rdo
rje 'chang zhi bar gshegs pas dgongs rdzogs kyi'ang go chod byung ba sogs lkog gyur rjen gsal gyi thugs mkhyen yin pa la ni bsnyon du med cing / dgung zhag nam rdzogs par
mkha' spyod ma'i sin dkyil sgrub mchod chag med kyi sngags sdom oM gsum ma nyi khri dgu stong bzhi brgya tham pa/ sku bstod lnga stong nyis brgya go gnyis/ mchog sprul
myur 'byon zhe dgu rnams mdzad cing / de lo ga ya dha ra'i bum chu'i snod gas pa dang bsam brling lha mchod dus gur kar chag pa rnams ni dbu bla 'di zhing khams brje ba'i
rtags dang / rje de nyid ni rnam kun nyin mtshan khor yug tu bstan 'gro'i don 'ba' zhig gis dus 'da' ba las rnam g.yeng gi dri ma phra mo tsam gyis ma gos kyang / 'jam mgon
gnas gsar ba de nyid gshegs pa nas bzung srod tho rengs nyin par gung tshigs skabs sogs yud tsam re bzhugs skabs thugs la skyo shas dang / khyad par da ni rje btsun gong
ma'i thugs dam chag med kyi rim pa kha gso ba rnams kyang zhu yul shin tu dkon pa 'dug dgongs pa'i thugs 'dun dung dung lhang lhang bcas nges 'byung gting nas 'khrungs
pa'i zhal 'don dge sbyor la rgyun las kyang thugs brtson gyis rtsa ba'i bla ma dam pa rnams kyi dgongs rdzogs dang skye 'gro sems can thams cad kyi don du smin rgyas mdzad/
rje de'i dgongs rdzogs dang bstun lo re bzhin 'jigs byed bcu gsum ma'i rdul dkyil sgrub mchod shom rgyas pa dang bcas zhag bzhi'i khongs su ya ma rA dza bzhi stong brgal
tsam dang / gsol 'debs bzhi brgya lhag tsam re mdzad cing phyi lo dus chen nyin dpal sa skya'i lha chen thig g.yab

gtsug lag khang du de nyid kyi 'dra sku rin po che gsar bskrun ring bsrel rnam bzhis phyur por mdzad de rab tu gnas pa'i me tog gis mnga' gsol bar dbu zhwa/ na bza'/ phyag
phreng / phyag cha/ mchod pa'i yo byad bcas de nyid kyi nyer spyad ngo mas spras te bzhugs drung sna lnga'i mchod pa 'bul gnang dang / gzhan yang gsung gi bdud rtsi bzhes
pa rnams bstan 'gro'i ched so so'i skal ba dang mthun par spel gnang dang / rje btsun sa skya pa'i bstan pa'i rtsa ba 'khon rigs dri ma med pa'i gdung rabs spel bar bka'
stsal sogs ngal ba lhur bzhes kyis dpal ldan bla ma dam pa'i dgongs rdzogs su stob pa dang / sngon du dgung grangs nyer gnyis thog gi spyan ltas ngo mtshar can de bzhin
dang / de lo khrums zla'i tshes gsum tho rengs gnas gsar rdo rje 'chang dpon g.yog tshang ma sa skya'i bla brang phun tshogs gling gi dbang khang du mjal bar ga ya dha ra'i
bum chu'i snod la skyon tshul de zhu gnang la skyon med 'gro gsung zhing / rje de la dgongs rdzogs 'bul rten yin dgongs pa'i khyad mtshar gyi gos phon chen 'bul nyams
dang / zhabs gras sbyin rgya ma yin snyam pa zhig gis/ yig brgya mtshal dam ma zhig phul nas rje bla ma snyun skabs pad dkar sprul sku'i lung bstan de 'di yin zer ba kha
phye nas gzigs pas tshigs bcad kha shas byung ba thugs dran mi gsal ba'i tshul mdzad/ yang skabs shig gnas der gnas gsar rdo rje 'chang nyid bzhugs te maNDal tshom bu du
ma bkod pa zhig gi mthar mchod gtor bshams nas phur pa'i dbang sngar gsan ma myong ba zhig stsal ba dang / gzhan yang rnam 'dren de yang yang phebs te rje btsun sa skya pa'i
zab chos kha shas la bskyar chos mdzad pa dang / sku'i rnam 'gyur zhi khro du ma'i sgo nas lugs gnyis kyi blang dor stsol ba sogs mtha' yas pa zhig 'khrungs pa ni 'khrul
zad rje btsun gong ma rnams kyi rnam thar kho na ste sa skya pa chen por 'jam pa'i dbyangs gtso

'khor/ rnal 'byor dbang phyug /zhang ston chos 'bar sogs dang / slob dpon rin po cher/ mnal tshe 'od gsal dag gis mnyam par 'jog /mthu stobs dbang phyug yi dam gang rung la/
/nyin mtshan gang yang the tshom gcod mdzad pas/ /zhes dang / rje btsun rin po cher/ mnal tshe chos rnams glegs bam gyi/ /tshul gyis khong du chud gyur pas/ /de yi mod
la chos kun gyi/ /de nyid gzigs pa khyod la 'dud/ /ces dang / 'jam mgon bla mar/ srid pa kun tu legs par sbyangs pas na/ /rmi lam na yang chos kyi sgo rnams kun/ /dge ba'i
bshes kyis dngos su 'doms par mdzad/ /ces sogs mang du gsungs ba bzhin dam pa'i khyad chos sha dag go /de nas dbyug zla'i tshes bcur 'bum thang sa paN phyi rten nyams gso
gsar bskrun lta bu mdzad nas rje nyid kyi rgyun gyi phyag tsha lnga stong bzhi brgya don bdun sogs nang gzungs grangs mang bcas byin rlabs kyi gzi byin 'phro bar mdzad
pa dang / mgo zla'i bde mchog sgrub mchod thog tshogs yongs la DA ma ru/ nang mchod/ 'thor snod gsar bskrun rnams sbyor 'jags kyis sgrub mchod dang dus mdos sogs kyi tshogs
dbur phebs pa'i skabs so/ /de dag gi don bsdu na/ dag snang 'od gsal me long dngas pa'i mkhar/ /dam pa'i zhal mthong lung bstan chu 'dzin g.yos/ /gsang rgya dbyang rnga'i
sgra grol zug rngu'i gdon/ /gdengs can dbyings su mi bzad thog gis bsgral/ /rigs bdag zhing sar dgongs pa'i char zim ni/ /mi mngon dbyings nas gzigs pa dge bas phab/
/snang brnyan myu gu bskrun tshe dge mtshan ltas/ /ci yang bzhad pa'i snye phon g.yur za ldem/ /thun gsum mnal tshe rnam 'dren mtshan mo'i mgon/ /zab chos bdud rtsi'i thigs
phreng slar yang spro/ /'jam mgon phyi rten kunda gzhon nu dang / /

gsang mtha'i khams su snang ba'i byi dor 'gran/ /zhes kyang smras so// ! dgung grangs so gsum du phebs pa lcags sbrul rgyal zla'i tshes gnyis nas bzung 'di yin med pa'i snyun
gzhi thub zhig bzhes pas nub gcig gzim shar gyi gnam sa bar gsum li khrir gzigs pas da lta rang sku tshe 'phos rgyu yin 'dra dgongs pa'ang 'khrungs mod/ sman bcos rim
gro dang thugs dam zab mo'i mthu la brten rta zla'i mjug nas rim dengs kyi tshul bzhes mur gzim shar mgon khang du zhal gyi dam tshig bskang gso mdzad pas sku lus sor chud/
de nas rdo brag rig 'dzin chen pos lung bstan gdung rabs myur 'byon sku rim du gra lnga dang dmar po skor gsum gyi sku par grangs mang dang / de dag gi sku gang legs bzhengs
dgos babs pa bzhin gra lnga lugs sku rnams sde dger yon sbyar gyis zhus/ gong gi sku par grangs mang de dag dang gdung rabs myur 'byon ched dmar po skor gsum bzheng
rgyu'i bca' bsgrigs la rten 'brel rang 'grig lta bur de dag gis mtshon sku par mang po de sngon nas gsar blugs grub 'phral yin pa bzhin brgya stong sogs phyag btab grangs
mang dang / sku rgyur byin rlabs rten 'dam mtshal sogs dbang rdzas dmar po sne mdzom 'jim gtsang la byin rlabs mdzad pa dang bsres te tshoms bar mgon khang du tshul khrims
bkra shis sogs nas shin tu gsang bar bzhengs te thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa'i gzungs bcas snron zla'i mgor grub 'phral rje nyid kyis phyag nas tshar gcig dang
/ chos las pa bstan 'dzin rin chen gyis brgya tshar mdzad/ gzhan yang gdung rabs myur 'byon ched rmang mkhar thub bstan dge 'phel du lho byang dge 'dun brgyad grwas rje
btsun rin po che'i bla ma'i rnal 'byor dang phrin 'chol sogs zla gcig ring bgyis shing zla mjug brtse chen lha khang rgya cher bskrun par mdzad pa dang / chu stod zla nang
phur sgrub phrin 'chol gong

tsam la ri nag rtser bye ma ngu ba'i kha gnon gyi rigs gsum mchod rten gsar bskrun dang / skyed lhas phrin 'chol la yum gyi gnas gzigs ched yab yum lhan du phebs te byas 'gyur
du nub gcig bzhugs/ gnas gzigs grub nas mar lam lha 'khren lta bu'i rgyum lam gyi sked tsam phebs dus rbab rgyugs shig byung yang ma skyon/ bsam brling du'ang zhag gcig
dang mar lam ri nag rtser mchod rten rnams la phyag nas 'bring po mdzad rjes dri bya sder ma'i lhag tsam du byon dus nam mkha' dbyings shin tu dngas par dpon po ri'i thad
du sprin dum zhig 'dus te zim char 'bab pa dang / brag chung nas bde gling lcags ri'i bar 'ja' tshon 'od skor lta bu zhig kyang shar bas thugs la ya mtshan che ba zhig
'khrungs/ gro bzhin phur sgrub grol nas slar yang gra lnga sgrub mchod drug cur nye ba gsog gnang gis yum la dbang grangs gsog mdzad/ de sngon nas sde dge zhu chen rin
po ches/ gzim chung 'phrod min yang brtags ngos gdung brgyud myur 'byon gang ci'i mtshams la thugs bsam che bskyed dgos tshul gnang ba bzhin yab rje rdo rje 'chang gi gzim
chung 'chi med rdo rje'i gur khang rgya bskyed de rten 'brel khyad zhag bcu skor la tshar phyin pa mdzad nas mtshan yang 'dzam gling phun tshogs dpal 'bar du gsol te gu
ru drag dmar sgrub mchod kyis thog mar byin gyis brlabs/ de rjes rdo rje phur pa'i ras dkyil sgrub mchod kyang mdzad pas byin chags shing thugs bag phegs pa byung gsungs/
khrums zla'i nyer gcig la dpal sa skya'i rgyab ri seng ge'i gdong can gyi mig g.yon mtshon byed brag 'bur thad nas glo bur du zhig ral byung bar kun thugs rtog za ba'i
skabs rje nyid kyi 'od gsal du/ 'jam dbyangs gzi 'od 'bar ba'i sku drung na rje nyid bzhugs par rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan gyi zhabs gras yin dgongs pa'i grwa pa zhig
dang gsung gleng mur

brag ri zhig tshul de gsungs pas/ grwa pa de na re/ 'di rje btsun rin po che zhing khams brje skabs kyang byung bas chos rje bas rje'i dgongs rdzogs dang gdan sa'i sku rim
gnyis char la dmigs nas 'jam dbyangs gzi 'od 'bar ba'i sku 'di bzhengs pas skyon ma byung / da lta'i 'di'ang dpal sa skya pa'i bstan srid la gnod pa'i lcags glang zhig 'thon
nye yod pas zer mur rje nyid kyi thugs snang la/ thang sku zhig gi ldebs la ri sngon po gnyis phan tshun nas rgyugs pa'i sne 'dzoms mtshams nas glang sngon po mig khra
hrig ge ba zhig rwa nyug ge 'thon nyams byed pa 'khrungs pas gra pa des sngar gyi 'phro las/ da lam yang 'jam dbyangs gzi 'od 'bar ba'i sku tshad dang mnyam pa'i 'jam dbyangs
kyi sku zhig bzhengs nas phan ngo che zhing / de mtshungs nyin gcig nang yum rgyas pa tshar gsum bklags pas phan nam zer ba zhig 'khrungs pa bzhin smin zla'i bcu dgu
la thigs g.yab lhor dbu rtse 'jam dbyangs gzi 'od 'bar ba dang mnyam pa'i rje btsun 'jam dpal dbyangs sman 'dam las grub pa byin rlabs kyi gzi 'bar grang gser leb byugs
can sku rgyan na bza' mchod cha sogs dang / gzungs gzhug skabs thugs kar gzhug rgyu'i 'jam dpal gyi sku zhig thigs g.yab rten khrod nas 'tshol bar mdzad pas mangga'i mtshan
can gyi phyag babs li sku mkhyid gang tsam zhig phyag tu thebs pa'i gsham yig la sbyin bdag gi ming bsam 'grub phun tshogs kyis bzhengs zer ba'i tshig sgra legs pa de
bzhin ma bsgrigs lhun grub kyi rten 'brel lta bur byung bas/ bstan srid lor rgya la nges par phan pa zhig yin no gsungs pa'i sku 'dra rin po che 'di la dbu zhabs bar gsum
gyi gzungs ring bsrel dang bcas pas phyur bor gtams shing / khyad par ri bkra ngan pa bzlog pa'i 'dod gsol bcas 'bul gnang gis kye rdo rje la brten pa'i rab gnas 'bring
po dang / gzhan

tshar 'ga' zhig bcas dam ye dbyer med du byin gyis rlob par mdzad do/ /de lo gzhung zhabs rin po che nas sku rim thugs brtson 'ga' zhig gnang dgos byung ba ltar 'dir yang smin
zla'i nang / rje rdo rje 'chang nas bdud 'dul phug tu bskang phrin gnad smin la zhag shas thugs gzhol/ de nas mdos chung gi tshogs dbur phebs kyang de dus mtshan 'grul
bsrung dgos stabs gtor rgyag la ma phebs/ dus mdos thog sde dge gnyer pa sngo ye sogs dang hor kre bo dpon sde dge'i sras mo bcas dang / gnas gsar rje'i phyag mdzod sogs
kyang 'byor pas so so'i blo dang mtshams pa'i lugs zung gi bdag rkyen dang / phyag mdzod nas bodhi'i tsitta'i phyag phreng rgyan ldan zhig phul/ de nas lha chen mkhan po
chos bkra shis sogs zhal slob 'gar mtshan nyid kyi yig cha rgya bod mang pos mdzad pa'i ljags lung phon chen yang stsol bar mdzad do/ /de dag gi don bsdu na/ gnyan mgon
dam tshig bskang ba'i g.yar lam du/ /mi mthun g.yul rgyal dbang lha grub pa'i mod/ /brtse chen snying po dri gtsang khang bu rgyas/ /bye ma ngan pa'i kha gnon rigs gsum
rten/ /bskrun che ya mtshan ltas bcas yum mchog nyid/ /slar smin mdzad rjes gzim spyil gsar pa ni/ /byin rlabs gzi byin 'bar ba dang bcas pa/ /yang dag grub pa'i byin chags
bag phebs 'khrungs/ /sngon tshe rdor 'dzin dus kyi gsang ba'i gtam/ /dag snang ngang du gleng ba'i bden tshig don/ /ji bzhin mdzad 'phral ngan rtags dbyings dengs nas/
/'char 'phar bstan 'gro'i don chen nyid la gzhol/ /zhes kyang smras so// // ! dgung grangs so bzhir byon pa chu rta dbo zla'i nang gdung rabs myur 'byon ched du dgongs rje
nyid nas khyad byang mgon khang du gtor bsngo chen mo'i nang gi chos skyong tshang mar gtor bsngo brgya rtsa gsog gnang dus gong gi phyag phreng de mdzad chog byung bas
phyag mdzod 'jam dpal gyis phul yang don la gnas gsar

rdo rje 'chang de nyid kyis gdung rabs myur 'byon rten 'brel bsgrigs sam snyam gsungs/ gzhan yang gdung rabs rin po che myur phebs ched smin grol gling / rta nag thub bstan
mkhan po bstan 'dzin rgyal mtshan/ dza lung pa 'gyur med gsang sngags bstan 'phel rnams kyis 'khor lo/ za yig /rim gro'i zhal bkod sogs tshang ma chos sde rnam gnyis/ ngor/
bkra shis chos sde/ gong dkar/ sde dge lhun grub steng sogs gtsang dbus khams kyis dgon rnams kyis thog drangs sangs rgyas bstan pa'i ris med grub mtha' dang / rtsis
bon nas sgrub dgos sogs tshang ma dang / jo zhal rnam gnyis mtha' 'dul yang 'dul ru gnon gyi gtsug lag khang / rgyang dang rgyang 'bum mo tshe sogs sngon gyi gnas rnying
du mar zhabs tog dgos tshul bzhin rtsad gcod mdzad pas mtshal ris ye shes sgrol ma rten brten pa bcas deng sang gang bzhugs su la yang zhu rgyu ma byung / 'dan klong thang
sgrol ma'ang sku chung ngu zhig las med skad bcas tshang mar mchod 'bul rgya che nas sne 'grel par ci smin mdzad/ de nas zhal dkar sman ram par bskul ma mdzad pa bzhin
srid 'bebs sman dang zas spyod tshang ma yig lam nas phul ba dang bcas gang sar snyan zhu 'dzol med zhus pas phyis su'ang 'di la thugs 'dogs lhag par che/ gang ltar snga
phyi bar mtshams kun tu rje btsun sa skya pa'i gdung rabs myur 'byon kho nar thugs brtson 'di nyid gcig pu'i sku drin yang bskal pa rgya mtshor khyer mtha' mchis min blo
ldan gzur gnas dag gis dpyod par zhu/ nag zla'i yar tshes la rgyal yum/ lha chen mkhan po/ mus chen/ zur 'chad grub dbang sogs la ku ru kulle ngor lugs thun mong dang thun
mong ma yin pa tshar lugs kyang de bzhin bcas kyi rjes gnang / lha lnga'i dbang / lha lnga gsang sgrub byin rlabs/ tshogs bdag ngor lugs/ tshar lugs

thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa/ chags rdor/ dkar po/ phyag bzhi pa/ 'dod rgyal ngor lugs/ tshar lugs thun mong ba/ dmar chung skor gsum rnams gnang skabs shig spyan ltas
su/ dpon po ri'i rtse nas lha rgyal 'then pa'i skad gsal por gsan pa dang / gzhi thog ltag gi bskor lam du mi zhig gis tsandan dmar po'i 'khur po shin tu che ba zhig 'khyer
yong ba dang / yang lha khang rtse'i mdzod nag nang khug ma ser po zhig na TaM ka nyung ngu las mi snang bar mi zhig nas da 'di TaM kas myur du khengs yong rgyu yin
zer ba 'khrungs pa 'di la ni/ phyi ltar na slar 'byung sa khyi lo rje nyid nas rigs sras dam pa nyi zla zung la rnam sras rigs chen bco lnga'i rjes gnang stsal skabs mdzod
'dzin kun dga' phun tshogs kyi thugs rgyud bskul ba ltar dngul bre chen brgya rtsa sogs rje btsun sa skya pa'i 'thas su gan mdzod 'dir 'jog par mdzad pa dang / nang ltar
na khams gsum dbang du sdud pa'i gdung brgyud rin po che myur du zhal gzigs kyi brdar gor ma chag /de lo gong sa rin po che blo bzang bstan pa'i dbang phyug 'jam dpal rgya
mtsho dpal bzang po gru 'dzin gser khri rin po cher mnga' gsol skabs rje nyid phebs bzhed thun mong ma yin pa mchis rung gdung rabs rin po che nyag phra bas bcad rgya
dang / zhabs dreg /zhabs 'bam sogs sgo du ma nas phebs ma bde bas mdzod 'dzin pa shes rab phun tshogs la bka' 'doms bzhin phebs/ de nas chos gra lho byang gi spyi chen bzod
rgyan gyis gzhis rtse bkra shis sogs bkug nas/ thub bstan lha chen gyi rung khang ngam g.yos khang dpal 'byor rgya mtshor khro chen gsar blugs skabs/ der shis brjod dang
khro chen gyi mtshan ljags sgrig mdzad pa dang mnyam du dbyar chos chen mo'i tshogs dung dkar po rgyang grags gsung bskul dus gcig mdzom pa'i rten 'brel bzang por lhun
gyis grub ste mtshan yang 'dod dgu rgya mtshor gsol zhing rje nyid nas sgrub gnang gi tshogs bdag zab

'khor yang 'jug par mdzad/ snron zla'i tshes bcu phun tshogs sbyor nyin rje rdo rje 'chang nyid nas lo gnang dus kyis sa bcud bum gter 'char can sgrub gras kyi gsung chog de
grub 'phral gung tshigs dang bstun chos lung nas rgyal po bsod nams don grub sras 'khor rags bsdus bcas 'byon pa'i gnas tshul gyi thog mar mthong smon na da lta bzhugs
yod zer ba gsan pas/ smon pa'i sgra de bum sgrub kyi tshig sgrar legs shing / de nyin rgyal yum mchog dbu sil grub nas sku rgyan bzhes skabs bcas sang nyin mjal 'dzom thog
ma dang rang 'grig dang lung srol gyi sos bskor zhes gos rgyan gzabs 'chor skra bkru bza' btung 'byor pa dang bcas rten mjal bskor ba glu gzhas rkang bro sogs skyid nyams
byed srol nas/ chu zam sogs zhabs phyi rnying gras kyis thog drangs sde nub pas dga' gzhas byed pa dang 'grig pa sogs ni/ 'jam mgon bla mas/ gang na thod dang skra gsar
dang / /gar dang rol mo'i sgra yod pa/ /de na mya ngan yod min pas/ /des na rol mo bsngags pa yin/ /zhes gsungs pa'i don lags/ de nas rgyal po dpon g.yog nas mjal phyag
dngos gzhi dang / phar legs so gnang rgyu tshes bcu bzhir mdzad rgyur de sngon ma bsgrigs kyang / sa skya'i g.yas g.yon mdun gsum na dar 'dzugs dang / chu mig rdzing kha
nas bu mo byi lo ma lo bdun lon pa gsum gyis rigs lnga dar dbyangs DA dril bum pa me long thogs nas khrus kyi stangs ka byas te chu 'khyer dgos bzhin la/ dkar po rnam gsum
gyi phyi rten thog nas byon pa'i 'jam chur grags pa 'di nas bum pa gang 'khyer ba de'ang mjal gong sleb pa dang / phan tshun legs so 'khyer mi rnams kyang gos rgyan gzabs
ma dang / lhag par phar gnang rgyu'i thog gang ci'i lo rgyus legs bshad kyi gsung

shog rgyas pa ljags rtsom ma de mgron gnyer rgyal tshing nas rim bsher gyis stobs par mdzad pas khong dpon g.yog rnams dgyes pa rab kyi rtser son/ de'i tshe gzim chung rtser
rgyal po yab sras la tshe dbang mdzad skabs char zim bur 'bab cing chos dung dkar po rgyang grags kyi mjal kha rten bshad bcas rje nyid nas stsal ba dang / gzhan yang byad
'grol sogs thugs 'dod kyi chos bka' dang / mchod 'bul thog lha chen khyams stod du gsol ston rgyas pa/ 'phel rgyas bzhugs 'tsher du'ang khrung bzhes sogs go babs dang
bstun pa'i bdag rkyen yang dag bka' drin che nas chu stod tshes gsum la rgyal po dpon g.yog 'thon pa sogs rten 'brel khyad par can de 'dra'ang ring por mi thogs par gdung
brgyud rin po che phebs pa'i la nye shin tu bzang bar ngos 'dzin mdzad/ zla nang der phun gling du phebs te mo lung bzhin brtse chen lha khang du rje nyid nas phur bzlog
shin tu rgyas pa nyin bzhi'i ring nam langs sa rub lta bur sgrub gnang gis lha chen steng nas nub tu 'phen par mdzad/ gro bzhin zla nang tsam la spyan ltas su/ pu trar
phrin 'chol dmigs phug mdzad tshe chu lug nang gdung brgyud rin po che 'byon par lung bstan pa dang dus mtshungs 'dar grong mkhan chen ngag dbang shes rab nas kyang dge 'phel
du gdung rabs myur 'byon gyi gsol 'debs nan tan mdzad pa'i mnal lam du/ 'jam dbyangs kyi bris sku zhig gi gras la byis pa chung ngu dar dang rin po ches brgyan pa zhig
kyang byung ba bzhin gdung brgyud phebs ngo shin tu che ba 'khrungs shing / gzhan yang gro bzhin nang rje nyid nas nang sor phrin 'chol zhag gcig ma dang / khrums zla'i
bcu bzhi nas bzung gta' gtor zur brgyad pa 'dzugs gnang dang chabs gcig phrin 'chol zhag gsum ma mdzad de rgyal zla'i bcu bzhi'i bar dus gtor chag med bzung nas

gtor ma spo bar mdzad de chu lug rta zla nas chu stod kyi bar la gtor 'dzugs mdzad pa'i dam bca' gnang zhing / de khongs su gdung brgyud nges par 'byon pa dang / de yang chu
lug nag zla'i tshes 'go rang la nges par 'byon pa'i phrin 'chol gnad bsnun mdzad pa'i dus gtor bzung ba gnang / mdos thog mtsho kha nas gu shrI rgyal brgyud jun wang bsod
nams bstan 'dzin yab sras/ btsun mo/ sku tsha/ 'khor rags bsdus bcas rgyal bstan spyi bye brag la mi phyed pa'i thugs dad brtan pos byon par gong ma bdag po chen pos wang
gi tshe lo stsal bas khyad par du che zhing / spyir yang rgyal rigs go sa mtho ba dang / yang sgos chos rgyal lugs zung mkhyen spyan yangs pa bcas sgo du ma nas bkur
bzos gang che mdzad cing / rgyal po nas kyang dngul bre chen nyer gsum gyis mtshon 'bul sbam mtho ba dang bcas zhabs brtan rdo rje'i re khA can gyi rten 'brel mdzad pa/ dus
mdos kyi zhabs tog nyin gang ma 'gan bzhes sogs ngo mtshar gyi mdzad pa dang / khong rang gi thugs bzhed rnams kyang ji lta ba bzhin bka' drin che bas dpon yab sras 'khor
bcas dgyes pa'i dpal la 'khod/ dus mdos kyi skabs nye 'gyangs gnas gzigs rnams dang 'thon phyag kyang stsal/ nyer dgur tshogs chen mor dpon nas dar 'gyed dang / de nyin
gnam gshis shin tu rtsub cing thal rlung nyin khyongs ma byung bar dpon thugs dad can gyi gsung 'phros su/ thal rlung des gtor ma'i gdong ma 'gags par g.yas g.yon du yol
nas 'gro ba de 'dra ngo mtshar chen po yin 'dug /ces bsngags brjod kyi me tog 'thor bar mdzad pa don la'ang de bzhin byung gsung ngo / /de dag gi don bsdu na/ phan bde'i
rtsa ba 'khon rigs 'dod 'jo'i dpal/ /myur bzhes thabs brgya'i 'phrul

mkhan kha lo pa/ /sprul pa'i ded dpon sngags 'chang rdo rje 'dzin/ /dbang lha'i dngos grub shes rab stong nyid 'jing / /zhugs tshe ya mtshan mthun pa'i rlung gi ltas/ /ci yang
g.yo ba'i mod du gru 'dzin rtser/ /gser khrir mnga' gsol mchod pa'i phreng bstar nas/ /dpal 'byor rgyal mtsho'i lto 'gro'i gtsug gi nor/ /rten 'brel dang bcas sa bcud
smin rjes su/ /phrin las lha yis dkar phyogs ba dan dang / /las mkhan mon bu dgyes 'dzum gsang lung grol/ /dregs ldan rgyal po'ang sa 'dir bskyod cing 'dud/ /ces kyang smras
so// // ! dgung grangs so lngar phebs pa chu lug rgyal po lo gsar nyin gong gi dpon la tshe dpag med lha dgu'i dbang dang / gsol sman/ mgul srung / rdo sku'i kha sarba
Ni khyad mtshar/ rje nyid kyi rgyun bzhes zhal dkar 'bras sil gyis gang ba sogs stsal nang sbyar bka' mchid tshang ma snyan du lhon nges dang / tshoms chen du bla bre
yol ba sogs gzabs mas mdzes shing / go babs dang bstun pa'i bzhugs stan sder kha sogs kyi thog legs bshad rigs lung gi bgro gleng bcas gra bgrig mdzad mthar dpon yab sras
'khor bcas kyis rje nyid la mgul dar sgron pa dang bstun skyabs 'jug gi rjes 'dzin zhu ba dang gang ci'i legs lam mtshams la lha mi ngo 'phrod lta bu'i 'phros yong tshul
zhus shing / rje rdo rje 'chang nas kyang lugs zung gi zhal ta mtha' 'doms bcas gnang bas khong thugs 'phreng nyams 'bral mi phod pa lta bu'i spyan chab dang thugs smon
yang dag mdzad pa dang mnyam du sras chung ngu des kyang sku mdun gyi gsol lcog brkos ma nas bzung ste smon lam mdzad pa sogs yab sras gnyis ka thugs tshims pa'i go 'phang
la 'god par mdzad do/ /de dus 'di phyogs kha tar da lo dpon khag stobs chen sras btsun mo bcas

shis par phebs shing mdos chen lo gsar bcas gzabs lugs 'di'i sad lo'u 'u cag la mdos chen gzabs spras byed rgyu yong zer ba'ang don la gnas/ de nas gtor spod sogs 'char 'phar
ci rigs mdzad mur tshoms dmar gnam yangs la 'grems rgyu'i bzang gos khra bsgrigs kyi nor bu'i do shal gsar bskrun gyi bka' 'doms dang / sku rim chen mo dang nye bar mnga'
ris 'phel rgyas gling gi grwa pa rnams la mjal phyag gnang ba'i nub mo 'od gsal du/ sa chen gyi sku zhal byang gzigs shin tu dgyes nyams can 'dzum zhing gsung 'byon la
khad lta bu zhig 'khrungs pa rjes su dgongs tshe zla ba phyi mar gdung brgyud rin po che zhal gzigs pa'i ltas dang / nag zla'i tshes brgyad rgyal phur 'dzoms pas rig byed
ma dang tshogs bdag nyin thang gsar bskrun dang / gdung rabs myur 'byon sku rim la gal che ba'i tshogs bdag bskang gso ljags bsgrigs nyams su blangs bde bar mdzad pa 'di'i
shom dbyangs rol dang bcas 'phags pa rin po che blo gros rgyal mtshan zhes rgya bod khams gsum dbang sdud de'i bzhugs khri padma can gyi steng nas gnang rgyu'i tho rengs
tshogs bdag yus pa lta bus glo bur du yum mchog nyid la sku khrag lta bu'i snyun thu mos ci mdzad gtol med du gyur kyang / rje rdo rje 'dzin nyid kyi thugs dam zab mo
dang / gsol sman/ rim gro sogs kyis myur dengs dang / de nyin mang sbyin gras su dam sel can gyi mi rgan zhig rgyab khur 'khyer bzhin du mjal phyag la byung bas des rkyen
byas sam dgongs pa'i thugs dogs bcas/ gang ltar gdung brgyud rin po che tshes brgyad rgyal phur nyin 'byon rgyur zhag gcig 'gyangs kyang dngos gzhi rten 'brel shin tu
legs pa ni sngar nas ma bsgrigs rang 'grig nor bu'i do shal 'dis thog drangs spyan

gzigs du ma dang / 'phags pa rin po che'i dbang ting dzhaikShim mar mchod bshams kyis tshogs bdag gi bskang ba thog ma de tshugs par mdzad pa'i spyan 'dren dang bstun kha'u
phyogs nas kha ba bu yug 'tshubs pa sogs lha 'go ba'i rtags dang bcas gsung bskang yongs rdzogs nyin khongs su grub par mdzad/ de dus yum yang snyun gzhi las grol bas yab
yum zhal rgyas te dmar po skor gsum gyi sku par 'debs gnang dang / tshes dgu dang bcur yang tshogs bdag bskang gso gnang mu'i dgu'i srod 'khor tsam nas bzung kha ba cung
zad 'bab mur sku gdung rin po che bltams ran pas/ rje rdo rje 'dzin nyid thugs lhag par spro ba'i ngang nas rgyal tshing sogs de skabs kyi zhabs phyi rnams la srung 'khor/
srid pa ho'i tsakli bcas 'dogs par mdzad pa dang / gang la gang dgos sngags dang rtsis sman nas bshad pa'i nyer mkho mtha' dag 'du mdzad cing / yum la'ang gang ci'i bka'
'doms lhus thengs zhib lhug stsal rjes rtsa ba'i bla ma dam pa dang dbyer med rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan dang / sangs rgyas sman bla/ rje btsun sgrol
ma rnams la thugs smon gsol 'debs rtse gcig tu mdzad kyin bzhugs pas sngar gyi kha ba char du gyur nas ches cher nyil ba dang chabs gcig sku gdung yid bzhin gyi nor bu rin
po che yum la gnod pa med par bde bar sku bltams pa'i gtam bzang snyan du lhon ma thag rje rdo rje 'dzin nyid dga' mgu yus pa'i rnam pa dang ldan bzhin du/ na bza'i khrod
nas dbu zhwa gang thebs shig bsnams pas kha gsar spus legs shig phyag tu son pa de bzhes/ de dus gnas bcur kha btags mang po skya nyog ge mchis pa'i khrod nas rje btsun
rin po che'i snang brnyan gsar bzhengs dang / lung bstan sgrol ma zung la snyan shal dang / yum sras la stsal rgyu'i kha btags bcas mdzod

rnying spus legs 'ba' zhig phyag thebs rnams bsnams nas byon pas/ sngon gyi bla ma gong ma rnams dang cha 'dra bar gsung 'byon la khad lta bur spyan gnyis rje nyid la dngas
gsal sgrib med du gzigs shugs che bar bzhugs pas/ rje nyid kyi thugs dgongs la sngar rje btsun sa skya pa'i bstan pa'i rtsa ba gdung rabs rin po che 'byon dka' ba de tsam
gyi thugs khur bzod par mdzad nas gang ci'i thad la 'on seng 'gyod med mdzad pa phyag thog tu khel ba 'di'ang bla ma dkon mchog gi thugs rje nyag gcig tu 'khums pas bslu
med rten 'brel gyi chos nyid la slar yang thugs spro ba'i ngang du dar cig 'byams par gyur/ de nas rten zung la snyan shal dang sras yum zhal rgyas la mgul dar/ 'bras dkar
gyi me tog nyil bzhin par phar phyin drug gi bkra shis kyi mnga' gsol yang bka' drin che/ de nub rje rdo rje 'dzin nyid ha cang thugs spro ches pas 'od gsal yer ba lta
bu zhig 'khrungs kyang sang nyin sku gzugs rgyun las kyang bde zhing thugs gsal la zhal bkod rnams 'khrungs bde ba sogs grub mtshan mngon sum du ston par mdzad nas nam
langs ma thag gzim chung rtser lha bsangs dang / rgyun gyi zhal 'don nyams bzhes sum cur nye ba rnams grub 'phral/ sku rten bi rU pa'i snang brnyan sdigs mdzub kab li can
khyad mtshar/ gsung rten rig gter rig gnas du ma 'dus pa'i yig cha/ lam zab dang bir bsrung phyi nang sogs sa skya pa'i yab chos duu ma 'dus pa'i dpe/ thugs rten lcags kyi
rdo rje rtse dgus thog drangs rten 'byung dngos skyes bzang dgu bcas stsal te phan bde 'byung ba'i sogs dge legs tshigs bcad kha shas bcas pa'i legs so dang / yum mchog
la'ang byas shes drin gzo dam pa'i rang bzhin can gyi gnang cha dang / zham 'bring pa rnams la'ang de bzhin bcas mdzad cing / chos bka'i thog mar rje btsun sa skya pa'i
yab

chos skyob pa 'chi med dbang po lha dgu'i bka' dbang gi sna bdun rdzas brgyad rnams gdung brgyud rin po che'i sku pang dang bzhugs gdan khar 'jog par mdzad pas de'i tshe gzhan
las 'jem chags pa zhig byung gsungs/ de nas gu ru drag dmar gyi dbang phul grub 'phral rje nyid kyi dbu sil bka' drin che ba'ang gong gi /gang na thod dang skra gsar
dang / /zhes sogs kyi lung dang 'byor/ de nas dbang khang phur mchod gtor gzabs bshams ngos snga mgyogs kyi gtang rag dang / rgyun ring bar nyin ltar sku'i rkyen sel mtha'
yas pa zhig mdzad par grags/ sku bltams nas zhag bcu zla bcu lo bcu rnams la sku rim gzab dgos mchis pa bzhin zhag bcu pa'i sku rim la/ chos gra nyi zla zung gi dge 'dun
rnams nas gzabs spros bcas/ tshe chog /gsung sgrogs/ mgon khang khag bzhir lha bsangs bskang gso bcas dang / rje nyid nas nang sor snga mgyogs btang rag dang / gzhan yang
gsang khog tu mchis pa'i rje btsun drung rnams dang mkhan phyag gnyer gsum sogs nas skabs babs kyi legs 'bul dang / gza' skar dge ba'i thog mtshan kyang dar dkar la mtshal
gyis dpal ldan chos skyong ngam dbang sdud snying por gsol ba ni rje sa chen gyi sprul gzhi de dang 'khrungs skabs dbang lha tshogs bdag gi bskang gso tshugs pas na
dbang sdud dang sa chen gyi mtshan mtha' snying por gsol ba bcas 'dri ba'i dbu tshugs pa dang tshogs dung gsung bskul ltabs 'grig kyang byung zhing / de nyin gsang yum sngon
ma'i sras mo dgung grangs lnga ma tshe 'dzin dpal bskyed bu 'khrid ces thugs rig grung po de rang gi thugs tshags nyer mkho nyung ngu'i khrod nas/ sder chung zhig gros
phyur por bkang steng dkar sngon chung ngu 'thus gang ba dang / mgron bu kha shas/ dngul gyi thur chung kha btags bcas gang

gi ming pho gdung brgyud rin po cher phul nas thugs mnyes pa'i rnam 'gyur ci yang mdzad pas rje nyid spyir yang sras mo der byams rtsis che ba dang / sgos su chung ngu des
rnam dpyod dod po de 'dra mdzad pas lhag par brtse skyong bcas de skabs kyi gro mgron mtshan byang rnams rten sgam du gzhug par mdzad/ zla mjug der khyad byang du gtang rag
gtor bsngo brgya tshar dang dus gtor chen mo lhan du gnang zhing / sa ga'i mgor bde mchog rje btsun rnam gsum nas legs skyes dang zla mjug sman chab la phebs skabs gnyer
bgres sogs nas da lo 'u cag 'di 'dra'i sku jus 'gro ba zhes sogs mi rgan bsam pa rdzogs tshul gyi 'phros zhu dang / de dus chos gra lho byang 'dus tshogs la bden tshig
bkra shis 'gyur med g.yung drung thugs 'dzin du stsal/ snron zla'i tshes dgur nyi ma me bzhi'i 'grub sbyor nyin lha mo gsol mchod mdzad rgyu'i shar mda' btang tsam la gnas
bcu'i rtse nas chos dung rin po che gsung bskul te/ mdud pa sogs kyis sdun bsus sgo rum rtser bzhugs khri 'dren chas/ byings la gdan thob dkar yol ja 'dren dngul tib bcas
lha bsangs grol nas mkhan phyag ban tshang sogs tshoms dmar du ja mgron thog mdzod 'dzin nas/ gdung brgyud rin po che zhal gzigs pa'i zhabs brtan 'dzugs rgyu/ legs 'bul
sogs kyi brda 'grims dang / de nas lha mchod grub nas mar phebs gdong ser khar rtse nas chos dung gsung bskul/ dar 'phyar/ dung chen/ cha zhabs khams drung bsam brling
du gzhas pa rnams nas bya khra ma'i byang gi gsing gshongs su bsu ba'i zhal bkod bcas sngon du btang nas/ lha khang chen mor g.yas bskor gyis shogs che bar tshoms dmar du
nor bu'i do shal

bkram pa dang so so'i gdan bkod bcas mchis par shar mar phebs te/ bzhugs khri padma can gyi steng nas legs skyes rnams thugs spro ba'i shogs rags dang bcas bzhes pas skya ser
kun shes pa 'ur zhing sing khrog khrog 'dzum nyams can rkyang pa rim bzhin byung / zhes gsungs/ de dus tshogs chen dbu byed bzod pas zhabs brtan bden tshig bskul/ slar
yang chos dung gsung bskul gyis tshoms dmar du zhabs brtan sku rim dang rje nyid nas sgo rum gtang rag zhag 'dun ma'i dbu tshugs tsam gyis nyin gung du grol bar gnang /
de skabs 'di ga'i lha mi'i sde tshang ma nas gtam snyan dar 'phyar gyi brdab shogs bo dong sogs gzhan rnams nas kyang bgyis pas dud chung sogs mdung dang mda' dar med pa
rnams dbyug pa rang bzhin gyi rtser dar ras gang 'byor 'phyar ba sogs kyi gnas tshul bya gshongs mkhan rnying nas snyan du phul/ rten 'brel des de nub nas bzung char drag
po yul phyogs kun tu babs pas ri klung gi rtsa 'bru rnams 'byor pa phun sum tshogs pas phal cher de kho nas dga' mgu yi rang du gyur cing / sang de nas bzung sgo rum du
gur lcam dral la gtor bsngo bskang ba brgya rtsa sogs mdzad skabs gong gi bya gshongs mkhan rnying nas/ bla ma lha khang du sku'i rnam 'gyur ha re ho re'i ngang nas legs
so phul bas gzhan las thugs la babs pa byung gsungs/ zhag shas nas khong la 'thon phyag skabs gong gi gnas tshul rnams rim bzhin gsung pas khong bzhugs gdan kha nas phrug
phrug gsig gsig gi rnam 'gyur mdzad par gleng / de nas mdung dar snyan shal spyan gzigs rnams dang bcas skyed lhas su chibs bskyod kyis zham 'bring ba re gnyis ma gtogs
mdzod 'dzin sogs tshang ma sa skyar mngags/ de lo thams cad la dga' nyams kyis rta zhon nas

brel por 'gro ba la dpe med mnyes 'gro ba zhig yod gsungs/ de nub 'phags pa phug tu gsung bskang bsdus tsam dang sang de nas dam tshig bskang gso dang / rje nyid nas skyed
lhas rtse dang sgrub sde ba rnams 'phral nas phyogs bzhi'i ri rtser bsangs/ de'i tshe sa skyar sras yum nas gnas tshul gyi gsung bris tshigs bcad ma phul ba'i bka' lan yang
tshigs bcad ngo mtshar can du mdzad de thugs dges pa'i ngang nas stsal/ de dus spyan ltas su/ dngul bum g.yu phra can sogs chos skyong dges pa'i mtshan ma mang tsam 'khrungs
kyang chos skyong bka' gnyan pa'i stabs de tsam las zin bris ma mdzad/ grol nyin lho'i spang steng du gtor 'bul sogs mdzad nas khang gsar mkhan chen bsod nams bzang
po'i phyag phreng mi thod ma rje nyid nas gur gyi yi ge bdun ma 'bru 'bum bzla gnang de'i rgyan mdo 'dzin bcu shad bcas brag sgo'i bug nang du 'bul gnang ni/ phyis shing
'brug lo khang gsar zhabs drung nas 'jam mgon sku mched la zhal pod dang mgon pod kha shas kyi lung stsal ba sogs ma 'ongs mngon mkhyen gyis rten 'brel bzang po bsgrigs
par mdzad rjes mdung dar gsum sngon 'gro'i glu gzhas gyis bsu ba bcas bsam brling du phebs/ de nub kyang mdzod 'dzin 'khor bcas sa skyar byon dus she mun 'thibs nas 'ga'
zhig lam du mgo 'khor ba'ang gad mo'i gnas su bgyid pa las ngal ba'i rnam pa gtan mi byed pa'ang byung gsungs/ bzhugs ring bsangs/ gangs mchod/ rab gnas/ dmag zor ma'i gtor
bsngo brgya rtsa/ bskang ba/ gsol kha/ mnga' gsol sogs bka' drin che zhing glu gzhas par ja mar sha chang kha btags sogs stsal/ snga dgongs zhal 'don gyi gseng la pu
tra'i mnga' gsol dang rtag gtor bca' bsgrigs 'phros

sa skyar phebs skabs kyi zhal bkod phyag bris rnams dang / grol nyin shar gyi spang steng du gtor 'bul mdzad rjes chibs bskyod de sgrol ma lha khang du mdung dar gsum sngon
'gro'i rgyal yum gnyer bgres sogs nas gzabs bzhes kyis chibs bsus/ rje nyid nas maNDal bzhi pa'i gsung chog grub 'phral lha chen bskor nas phebs skabs/ sos bskor ba dang
smron zla'i nyer brgyad ser 'du grol ba'i mi mang gyes thog 'ga' zhig 'khur po mgo steng khyer bzhin du gus 'dud dang bcas 'gro ba rten 'brel dge bar gzigs/ de nas nang
