so'i rtag gtor gzungs gzhug dang / gtor sgam nang gzhug rgyu'i las mgon bye brag gi drug ldan rten tshogs rnams la gzigs rtog dang / ma 'thus pa bzo rgyu'i bka' 'doms rnams
mdzad cing / sang de nas nang sor gtang rag thog rtags gtor bdud rtsir sgrub gnang dang lha sgrub kyi ljags bzlas grangs ni gtor sgam gsham yig na gsal ba bzhin dang /
gnam gang tho rengs puu tra chen po mi zhig la babs nas dar dkar gyi thod dang chu ba dkar po bzhes shing / phyag nas bkra shis kha btags 'dom 'khor ma zhig rje nyid la
phul ba dang bstun/ gsung las/ 'dre la drug ldan rten tshogs 'di 'dra sku drin che byung / zhes de ma thag sku sangs pa'i rnam pa byung yang don du pu tra chen po'i zhal
mngon sum du bstan cing / de nas rje nyid kyis sku rten pa yin rgyu'i mi de la 'ju bar mdzad de las mgon chen po zhes bos nas lung bstan yong re gnang mur mnal sad pas shin
tu phongs pa zhig 'khrungs pa'i tshul 'di ni/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse la mkha' spyod ma dang / a mes zhabs la mkha' 'gro ma zhig gis dbang gi brda mdzad pa sogs kyi
mur mnal sad pas thugs phongs pa dang mtshungs pas rje btsun gong ma 'khrul zad rnams kyi rnam thar sha dag go /de'i tshe thugs

shin tu spro bas yang bskyar gu ru rin po che'i bzhes snod mtshan ldan ka pA lar/ bdud rtsi ril bu khri stong brgya bcu rnams kyi rdog dang bsil bu phon ches bkangs shing /
gser zangs kyi tshe bum tshe rdzas kyis phyur ba dang / gzhan yang snod zangs kha shas su zas snas gang ba bcas chu stod tshes gcig snga dro rje nyid nas nang so'i bla mtshor
kab li'i bdud rtsi rnams phul nas/ kab li ma da na bzang pos bkangs/ tshe bum rtag gtor sgam nang dang zas sna mdun du bshams nas sgrub bzhin pa'i gtang rag mdzad/
gung tshigs la phebs dus mus gnyer dge phun gzabs 'chor gyis legs 'bul thog tsan dmar las grub pa'i tshe dpag med kyi sku che legs phul ba'ang rten 'brel dge bar gzigs te
sku gdung rin po cher stsal ba da lta'ang gzim chung rten gras la bzhugs/ de dus khal kha'i mi sna A yu She zer ba ngo g.yog gdong paNDi ta blo bzang sogs mtha' mi 'ga'i
thum bu rten chas gras tshe mdo dang nor rgyun ma'i mdo bod yig rgya nag par ma kha gsar phyag 'byor rnams kyang nang so'i rtag gtor sgam nang du bzhugs shing khal kha rnams
blo kha rdzogs pa'i mdzad sgo yang dag dang / de skabs tho rengs shig tu/ gzim chung 'dzam gling phun tshogs dpal 'bar gyi sgo lcog nang gi byang shar na/ stegs kyi
khar nang so'i zangs chen bkra shis 'od 'bar phyi nag cing snum pa nang zangs dmar kha gsar g.ya' dang bral bar shar gyi gyang ldebs de nas shing shol wa chu lta bu zhig
las chu dngas gsal zangs nang du 'bab pa'i sgra khrong khrong zhes snyan por 'byin mur mnal sad pas/ snyan khung na khrang khrang gi sgra de lhang nger mchis pa zhig 'khrungs
pa dang / yang nang so'i mgon khang mda'i g.yab der rgyal tshing snyan shal la phrin byang 'bri skabs rje nyid nas rang bzhin gyi gsung gleng du mgon khang de rgya dpangs
bskyed na legs tshul gsung pa dang

mnyam du de'i sa dpyad 'dra mo'i rnam pa mdzad pas gsol dpon bkras rgyan dang rgyal tshing zung nas bzo bab legs po yong ba'i snyan zhu bzhin/ ma 'ongs pa'i la nye de 'dra
yang bla ma dkon mchog gi rgyud bskul lta bu yin 'dra gsungs/ grol nyin gsung bskang mnga' gsol sogs kyi skabs rgyal yum nyid mchod mjal dang sbrags snyan shal phyi nang
gi mchod pa spyan gzigs na bza' mon gos sogs 'bul gnang dang / gtor 'bul dang chabs gcig sngar gyi ru mtshon chung ngu de'ang mgon khang steng lha spo gsar bskrun gyis thug
chog mnga' gsol sogs mdzad nas/ mgon khang du phebs te rtag gtor la brtan bzhugs/ thod pa nyi zla kha sbyor gyi bsrung dmigs bcas gtor sgam la sgo rgya mdzad nas rjes
chog bkra shis rgyas pa rnams bka' drin che ba dang / sngar gyi phrin 'chol 'dzugs gtor mdzes rgyan mda' dar dkar po kha tshar ma nyams pa de la tshe mdud kyis spras te tshogs
rdzas dang bcas sku gdung rin po cher stsal ba zhal byang can mgul srung gras su bzhugs/ sang nyin nas dngos grub gling du dpal chen yang dag gi phrin gzhung bdag bskyed/
gtor bsngo bskang ba spyi 'gro'i khog phub/ nor skyong yab yum la gsang ba snying rgyud nas gsungs pa'i bskang ba yig cha gzhan dang bsdebs bsgrigs lugs dang / dkar
bdud phur srung bstan ma bcu gnyis bcas la de skabs ljags bsgrigs kyi gsol kha mnga' gsol bcas zhag bdun mthar gtor 'bul bstan skyong can dang / de nas dus mchod gtang
rag thug 'dzugs sogs mdzad pa dang mnyam du dga' ldan smug chung la'ang de bzhin gzhan la bka' gsang gis 'doms shing / zla ba de'i gza' tshes dge bar tshang ma gzabs spros
bcas gsol thab lhor phebs thog rje rdo rje 'dzin nas drag dmar

sgom bzlas kyi lha'i nga rgyal brtan pos thog mar/ oM a ka ni sogs dang / gtsug 'bar/ rigs gsum mgon po/ de nas gur drag rnams kyi ljags sngags bzla bzhin par bum chu du ma
'thor bar mdzad pa dang / sangs rgyas byang sems sogs kyi sku zhi drag mang po rten sgam rnams dang bcas sku gdung rin po che phebs 'chams la gdan 'dren zhu mi mgron gnyer
rgyal tshing dang tshe bsam nas 'gan blangs lha chen rgyal sgo'i nang du phebs pa nas bzung rje nyid rgyal ba tshe mtha' yas kyi ngo bor bzhengs te/ tshe gzungs oM gsum
ma ljags bzlas mdzad mur mthong smon bla brang phun tshogs gling gi gzim spyil gsar pa rje nyid kyis gsar bskrun ngo mtshar dpal 'dren du phebs 'phral phar phyin drug gi
shis brjod byabs khrus sogs mdzad mur char chen po zhig babs pas rje nyid kyi thugs la rten 'brel rab la bsgrig mi dgos zer ba de 'di yin dgongs pa 'khrungs shing / gzim
chung rtser lha bsangs dang / de nas rnam 'joms sbyangs khrus tshe chog lo gtor gsar 'dzugs rnams mdzad cing / rig 'dzin pho brang dang lha chen rtser byang tshogs yong
nas lha bsangs bskang gso sogs zhal bkod bzhin dang / gnas de dag gi rtse nas nyin gang dar 'phyar dung 'bud gzhan yang kong gzhas bcas dang / rim gyis phur sgrub phrin
'chol sngon 'gro'i dngos gzhi'i mchod gtor rnams sngar bas bldabs 'phar dang / bcu bzhi bcu dgu nyer lnga sogs la dkyil 'khor zangs dra'i sgrom rtser gdugs/ rgyal mtshan/
ba dan sogs 'phyar zhing / nyer dgu'i nyin tshogs rdzas rgya cher bshams pa sogs mdzad pas deng sang phur sgrub gzabs res su grags pa'i rgyun 'di byung / phur sgrub skabs
gzhis byes nas zhabs brtan legs 'bul 'char 'phar mang

du bzhes/ khrums zla'i nang pho brang gzhi thog tu phebs skabs kyi bca' sgrig kyang gong bzhin la phebs mtshams brtse chen lha khang du gra sgrig mdzad de sa chen snang brnyan
rin po cher snyan shal mchod 'bul bcas gnang ba 'di ni 'jam mgon dbang gi mtshan can nyid kyis gtsug lag khang du phyags phebs pa'i sgo dang po dang / de nas gtang rag
sman chab sogs lugs 'gro bka' drin che nas khrums zla'i gza' tshes dge bar sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po'i gsung rab las mkhan ru 'dren dang bcas pa'i 'chams dpe dbang
por gnang nas rje nyid/ brgya dpon bkra shis 'od zer/ zur 'chad grub dbang dam pa rin chen rgyal mtshan rnams zhal rgyas te snga thog gi slob rgyun la dag ma dag gi dpyad
pa nan tan mdzad nas ru 'dren sde bzhi dang / pu tra 'chams pa dgu tshan bdun gyi 'go par bslab sbyangs dang / zla nang der dbu rtser lo rim la ched du dgongs pa'i mgon
po lcam dral gyi 'bur sku gsar bskrun gyi mgon po'i zhal khyim ni bdag nyid chen po'i 'chams sku sor bzhag lta bu dang / lha mo yang mgon po'i zhal khyim sor bzhag la zhal
rgyan dang rgya mtshon byed me ris med pa thun mong ma yin pa'i gzungs bcas bka' drin che zhing / gzhan yang de lo khyad 'phags 'phags pa'i thugs dam rten hor bzlog lcam
dral dang / tshoms bar mkhas btsun phyag bzo byang 'dul mgon po rnams gsar bskrun lta bur nyams gso mdzad de ring bsrel rnam bzhi spyi dang khyad par gyis phyur bar rje
rdo rje 'chang nyid kyis phyag nas dang / mdar mkhan po ngag dbang shes rab kyis mgon po'i thun mong ma yin pa'i rab gnas zhag bdun ma mdzad pa sogs zhib pa mgon khang
zung gi debs gsal bzhin dang / gzhan yang gdung brgyud rin po che gegs med du phebs pa'i gtang rag tu ched dmigs mdzod 'dzin pa shes rab phun tshogs la bka' 'doms kyis lha
chen zur

lcog lcags ri dang bcas pa'i spang bad span bad du bsgyur bar mdzad/ dbyug zla'i sa mchod chen mo'i bde kye gsang gsum la so so'i rab gnas 'bring po sbyor gnang gis bde mchog
rab gnas la rje btsun sgrol ma'i gser sku gsar bskrun ngo mtshar can 'di dang / sa chen gyi bris sku byin can gyis mtshon bris 'bur gyi sku du ma/ kye rdor la lam 'bras
bla brgyud bris ma sogs dang gsang 'dus la de'i bla brgyud bris thang sogs zhal dbye zhing mchod tshogs rgyas pa dang bcas bcu bzhi'i nyin sa bskor dang sbrags thog mar
tshoms dmar nas rgya dkar nag /mkha' spyod/ dngul gdung khyad 'phags steng 'og /tshoms bar sogs rim bzhin gzhi thog shar brgyud tshogs chen mo'i phyi mtha' nas khro khang
steng 'og /sa tshogs shar sgo nas bya khra ma'i shar brgyud lha chen sogs nas phyi bskor la rab gnas kyi me tog dang / grol nas 'chams kyi 'go pa rnams mdzod du bsgrigs
nas bka' tho bkram zhing zhal bkod mdzad/ sang nyin bco lngar gza' 'dzin la gzhan dag ni thugs rtog cher mdzad/ rje rdo rje 'dzin nyid ni/ gsang ba spyi rgyud las/ nyi ma
zla ba gzas zin dang / /ya mtshan che rtags byung ba dang / /cho 'phrul gyi ni zla ba la/ /sgrim ste dkyil 'khor bri bar bya/ /zhes dang / bdag cag gi ston pas sang bdud
rtsi brnyes rgyu'i do nub zla bar sgra gcan zhugs/ grags 'dzin mar rgyal po don grub kyi sras bltams pa'i mtshan sgra gcan 'dzin du grags pa rnams kyi rgyu mtshan des na
ya mtshan lhag par che bar dgongs pa bzhin don la grub pa 'di'o/ /zla mjug la dus mdos gzabs ma'i sku rim dmar chen gtor bzlog skabs kyang spyir rtags bzang zhing / lhag
par gtor bzlog grub nas 'chams sku gzhi thog tu byon gdong bzhugs gding

khyer ba'i a tsa ra des rkang g.yas kho na bteg ste shar rgyag rgyugs song bar khrom la dgod sgra chen po byung bas rten 'brel legs/ smin drug zla nang nas 'chams rgyugs rim
bzhes sogs 'char 'phar gyi mdzad sgo dang / dus mdos dkyus gzabs kyi dbye ba mchis pa'i bka' tho dang / phyag bzhes 'ga' zhig la skyon 'don bcas dang / mgo zla'i nang phur
khang du zhal 'bag zhwa phod ka khrab sogs chas rnams tshang mar rje nyid nas kye rdor rab gnas 'bring po mdzad rjes pho brang du phebs skabs bla brang zam pa'i g.yas
g.yon la a li chos rje'i khams pa nyi shu rtsa bgrangs shig 'khar rnga dar tshon sogs dngos po du ma khyer nas mchis pas bkra rtags shin tu legs pa'i bka' grol/ dus mdos
phrin 'chol rnams rim bzhin grol te nyer gsum nas tshugs skor sogs de skabs kyi phyag tho le tshan rnams gung bsgrigs te 'dir bkod na/ oM swa sti/ mdos chen gzabs spras
skabs tha skar zla mjug gi dmar chen gtor bzlog la tshoms chen du zhal thang spyan gzigs mdos chung lugs/ 'chams sku khyad 'phags 'phags mgon gnyis/ tshoms bar byang 'dul
mgon po grags blo lcam dral/ 'chams sku gdan 'dren dang gtor rgyag nyin gnyis kar khyad 'phags byang nas mi nag 'bag gnyis/ bzhugs gdan khyer mi a tsa ra gnyis/ gar g.ya'
lung gi phud dam pa/ 'phrang ba dang srang gzhug spos phor ba/ zil gnon pa dang lha dpon mdung pa/ dung chen pa/ rgya gling pa rgya gos bcas/ khrims gnon pa 'os 'tshams/
gtor bzlog ring gsol ja bzhes thug mdzod de bas nang bzhin/ zor 'phen nyin 'chams sku nas rgya gling pa'i bar gong bzhin dang / rnga rol la gos cham dang rol phod/ 'bag
pa lngar phod ka rdor gong sogs dang /

zor las pa lnga the ba'i sngags pa bco lnga/ dge slong / skyes pa/ bud med rnams kyi so so'i chas/ dngul tib pa/ gtor khur ba/ 'dren pa sogs nyer mkho gang dgos/ de dag la
bkye rgyu'i bdud rtsi ril bu dang kha ras gang dgos/ grol nyin 'chams sku phebs skyel gyi chas rnams gdan 'dren bzhin no/ /tha skar smin zla gang rung gi tshes 'gor g.yul
thang 'ong ba zhes dar 'dzugs la dar ras gang rung dkar po'i dar cog lag gsum ma ring ba/ de mtshungs dar shing lcang dkar shol po gang rung / 'dzugs mi drung 'khor skya
gras ming bkra shis pa zhig gis sngo nag min pa'i tshos mdog gang rung gi lding slog /mgo ras kong rna gser pad sogs gzabs chas gyon nas 'dzugs skabs phye mar kag shar gsum
dang thad bu gang / phud chang skor bsha' sdems nyis 'go bco brgyad/ mang ja 'phar ja re re/ skyes che chung bud med sogs mi skya nye skor 'chams pa rnams la'ang bzhes
dang chabs gcig gnyer dpon gyis tho 'grems/ dge slong sngags pa dgu tshan bdun dang / rnga rol gyi 'go pa rnams mdzod pa'i mdun bsgrigs te bkod khyab byed/ 'go pa rnams
kyis 'chams rgyugs pher byung na brgya dpon dang zur 'chad pa gnyis la sum shag rdor bcas/ dbu byed gnyis/ pu tra 'chams 'go bdun/ dge slong sngags pa bcas kyi 'go pa spyir
ja shag rdor bcas/ gong gsal spyir bdun tshan bcas gnang / mgo zla'i tshes gcig nas mgon khang khag bzhi'i phrin 'chol la nged rang mkhan chen 'byon na dang / brgya las/
ban tshang / bde gling dbu byed/ sku gnyer lto gzan/ drung ser skya rnams gzabs spros/ byings la 'chams rgyugs len skabs gzhi thog gzhol nub kyi shag steng nged rang
mdzod pa brgya dpon dbu byed gsum/ bde gling dbu byed zla bo ser skya bcas 'khod

nas blangs la/ nyin phyed nyin gang sogs yun la dpags pa'i ja gtong lugs dang / gnyer tshang nas 'chams pa dang rnga rol par nyin chas/ mi nag 'chams par chang / rgyugs pher
na mi bcu rer gsol ras 'bras bre re/ mgo zla'i nyer gcig chog bsgrigs la rnga rol gyi gral gong bzhin la mkhan po 'byon na dang / dung mkhan/ dung rgya rdzag dung rnams
kun ra'i shar gnyer tshad mda'i g.yab 'og dang / lha bris pa sogs kyi spos phor ba gnyis/ rkang gling cha/ ru 'dren las mkhan 'chams pa gang yod bcas nyi shar la 'dzom nas
thog mar nged rang dang gser skyems pa rnams kyis gser skyems kyi 'chams/ de nas dge slong sogs 'chams pa rnams gra tshang de bas bzhin 'thon la 'chams ja gsum gtong mtshams
rim bzhin bud med/ puu tra'i sum brdung / bdun brdung gnyis rdzogs mtshams rnams su gtong / 'chams pa ser skya tshang ma tshoms chen mda' phugs la gang bshom dang
/ rnga rol/ dung / rgya gling sogs la rang gnas su/ ru 'dren 'chams kyi mtshams gang 'os la gtong / gsum pa puu tra'i sum brdung rdzogs nas puu tra ba byings mthil du sgor/
nged rang rnga gral du yong / ru 'dren sogs la gong bzhin gtong / nyer gnyis bca' sgrig la tshoms chen gyi thog 'khor mar gos kyi bla bre/ gnam yangs la lda ldi/ gseng
g.yab la drag yol thung ngu/ gdung 'khor mar gos kyi lce le/ ka dar/ gyang ldebs 'khor mar gos yol/ sgo nang gi ka gdong gnyis la rkang bzhi 'bag cha tshang / ka ring dang
gung gral gyi ka thung gnyis rgyab gral lho byang gi ka ba rnams la go mtshon rnams bsgrig /nyer gsum 'chams sku gdan 'dren la khyad byang nas 'phags mgon lcam dral/ bsod
nams dbang phyug gi 'chams mgon

gsum/ tshom bar nas byar 'dul dang grags blo lcam dral/ khyad 'phags lho'i 'chams sku gsum/ mgon nub brgyad rnams dang / rol sil/ bar gos kyi chos gos snam sbyar/ rnga sar/
gos ber rnying ma gang 'khyed/ lha chen rnga khang gi gser rnga che gras/ phur sgrub kyi mdung dar dkar po gnyis/ mdung nag che chung cha/ lha mchod kyi dar khra bco brgyad/
dkar mo mgon khang gi zangs dung phun tshogs 'brug sgra/ gser dung 'dzam gling dbang sdud/ dngul dung dpal 'byor dar rgyas/ nged rang gi thog la bde gling pas phul ba'i
snyan grags/ nged rang gis gsar bskrun bsod nams nga ro/ ga ra g.yar lung gi gser skyems pa/ 'phrang srang gi spos phor ba ste/ mdung pa nas 'di bar rgya lu chas/ rdzag
dung ba bzhi zhwa gos sogs rgyun bzhin la/ gsar pa rgya zhwa rgya gos can gyi rgya gling pa bzhi/ nag rengs pa sogs rgyun bzhin/ ha shang lnga/ skya bo dpon rnams kyi
gral rim sogs grwa tshang debs bzhin/ mdung pa nas skya bo bar gyi do dam pa drung 'khor ser skya gang rung nas gral rim sogs grwa tshang mchod dpon dang gros bsdur thog
nas byed/ nyer bzhi mnyen chas las tshogs su khri dang / 'chams 'phyar/ gdan bkod rnams mgron gnyer gyi debs bzhin/ drung skya'i rigs dang skyes che chung / gser dung / dngul
dung / mdung dar dkar po gnyis rnams rgya lu chas/ rdzag dung dang rgya gling cha re chas gong bzhin/ drung 'khor ser mo ba dang 'chams pa rnams gzabs spros/ rnga rol
chos dung ba rnams gzabs spros kyi khar snam lcam/ bud med 'chams pa rnams gos dmar stod gos rgyan bcas/ drung ser gyi spos phor/ chos sde'i gdugs 'dzin pa/ lha bris spos
phor/ rkang gling / 'bob lcag /rgyug dmar ba sogs khrims gnon pa rgyun bzhin

bcas de nyin gyi tshogs pa grol nas gzhi thog rtse sogs nas chos dung gtang / thog mar mdung pa/ dung chen/ rdzag dung / lha bris spos phor/ rnga rol/ rgya gling / drung 'khor/
spos phor/ nged rang 'khor bcas/ mkhan chen yod na/ nged rang gi rjes la drung chen zung bcas gzhi thog nas chas te sa tshogs su mdung / dung / rgya gling / rdzag dung
rnams nub bstan/ nged rang 'khor bcas dang rnga rol rnams so so'i gdan la 'khod/ 'chams pa rnams kyi cha lugs/ 'chams tshul/ 'don pa/ rnga rol gyi rnam gzhag grwa tshang
debs bzhin/ khro khang du 'chams ja yag pa gsum mnyen chas gang yod dang / lho byang gi grwa khrol/ chos lhun rin sgang pa sogs mang ja rgyun rgyug ltas mor yod pa rnams
la ldangs par gtang / rung khang nas ja gnyis 'chams pa gang yod dad tshogs rnams la gtang / bud med sha skal gyi skabs su snga rting gnyis la bkras btags dang / gzhan
tshor gsar 'phel yag pa re/ 'chams grub nas gral rim gong bzhin gyis gzhi thog tu 'gro/ nyi shu bdun/ brgyad/ dgu gsum la thor dung sogs/ bdun brgyad kyi srod rdzag dung
/ nyer drug nyin mdos tshogs skabs dge slong sogs bzhugs min pa rnams la 'chams tho bshad kyin so so'i chas 'gyed/ gtor 'bul grub nas gong 'phros la so so'i 'chams chas
bkyed nas byings lha mthil dang / gser skyems/ pu tra/ rnga rol rnams kyi chas so sos tshom dmar du skyel/ nyer bdun la bud med kyi chas dang / gur nag /de'i mgo pa dang
gtso mo'i dam rdzas bco lnga/ gzhan tshor bcu gcig /sa 'dul grub 'phral gdan bkod sogs mgron debs bzhin la/ bud med kyi sa khri g.yang gzhi'i thum bcas khang dpon/ nyer brgyad
snga bar dar nag bcu gsum 'dzugs pa dang de mdun spos dud bcas kyi do dam drung

yig zla bo 'os mtshams/ bud med sha skal la rgyug tshe khrom nang phyogs bzhir sla nga sogs su sha chen cung zad bsres pa'i gu gul phon che ba dang / spos rengs bu dri bzang
gi dum bus dud pa shin tu gtos che ba sbyar/ 'chams dngos gzhi'i chas mdung dkar po nas skya bo pa'i bar 'chams sku gdan 'dren bzhin/ gser dam gsar brdung dang dngul gyi
phud phor bcu bzhi phud dam dang dngul gzhong 'brus gang ba khyer mi rgya lu chas/ dbyangs chags grub nas nged rang / gser skyems pa/ rnga rol/ spos phor/ rkang gling /
gdugs pa/ rdzag dung pa/ dge slong sogs 'chams 'thon nye phal cher chas zhugs grub pa dang sa tshogs nas chos dung thang bdun btang nas/ dung mkhan gzhi thog la yong ba
dang / 'chams la chas brda gzhi thog nas gser dung 'dzam gling dbang sdud byung bstun gong 'khod sngon 'gros pa rnams 'chams sku gdan 'dren bzhin gyi thog mar mgron gnyer
gzhon pas sna drangs te mdung pa rnams 'chams ra'i thig nang g.yas bskor la phyin nas gral mgo mjug shar sgo gnyis kyi mtshams su yong bar byas te/ yangs dog cha snyoms
grogs drung yig sogs 'phyar dar mdun yod rnams kyis byed/ zangs dung phun tshogs 'brug sgra'i g.yas su gser dung gzhi thog nas 'byor bstun bzhag /g.yon du dngul dung / gser
dung g.yas su rgya gling cha gcig dang bde gling snyan grags/ dngul dung g.yon du cha gcig dang zangs dung bsod nams nga ro/ dung pa cha lnga'i mtha' g.yas g.yon du rdzag
dung cha re bcas nub bstan du bsgrig /g.yang gzhi'i lag rtse gnyis thad a tsa ra'i spos phor ba kha lhor bstan/ 'don pa dang 'chams kyi go rim gra tshang debs bzhin/
'chams ja lnga'i gong 'og gnyis khro

khang nas yong ba 'di mang ja rgyun rgyug tshang ma la/ bar ma gnyis dang mjug ma rung byang nas gtang rgyu'i dang po bud med rdzogs mtshams gung sang / gnyis pa skyes chung
mtshams/ mi skyar gnyer khang nas chang / dur khrod bdag po grub nas gung sang / pu tra ba rnams kyi tshoms dmar nas 'chams chas gyon tshar ba dang / bskul bcas 'chams
rim bzhin 'thon/ gcig brdung grub nas spyi pa'i ja dang bdun tshan/ gsum pa rnga brdung rdzogs mtshams gung sang 'dus nas gtong zhing / skya bor chang gong 'dra/ bzhi pa
drug brdung dang bdun brdung gnyis song mtshams/ sngags pas log 'chams grub nas ja/ thams cad kyi log 'chams grub nas mdung sogs sngon 'gro'i nged rang dpon g.yog gong gi
gral rim bzhin 'gro/ nyer dgur dge slong sngags pa skyes che chung rnams nyer brgyad bzhin la/ skyes par rta go mdung dar 'go mi drug sogs gang 'khyed/ me mda' gang 'grig
/bu mo mda' dar can dge slong sngags pa sogs kyi grangs dang mnyam pa/ g.yag gzeng 'phar gnyis/ dar khra med pa ma gtogs gzhan tshang ma 'chams sku gdan 'dren bzhin/ sa
tshogs dang bya khra ma'i ja gnyis rnga rol 'chams pha ru 'dren g.yag gzeng mdung dud rdzag dung rgya gling ba sogs sa tshogs su gang yod la 'dren/ gtor bzlog grub nas skyes
che chung rkang thang gi dmag bcas bya khra mar bsdad/ gzhan tshang ma gzhi thog tu 'byor ba'i gral rim sogs gra tshang debs bzhin/ mgon po rnams kyi sku 'chams grub
nas phyag mdzod rab gsal nas dar brda btang la/ rgyab dmag tshang mas lha rgyal/ skyes che chung gis rbad shod grub pa dang rkang dmag dang rta ba rnams rgyun bzhin bsdad
la/ gzhung dang mi ser gyi rta rgyug la mgyogs dar/ de grub nas lha rgyal dang so sor gyes pa rgyun bzhin/

skyes che chung rnams la sa tshogs su chang ston/ dmag ston bzhugs gral/ bskang gso brgya tshar gyi spyan gzigs 'grems pa/ mnga' gsol mjug chog grub nas gtor 'bul gyi skabs
brgya tshar gyi spyan gzigs dang tshoms chen gyi drag chas rnams bsdus/ lda ldi'i shul du nor bu'i phreng ba gos drubs ma 'grems/ mgon po mnga' gsol rgyun bzhin la/ 'phyar
dar dkar po bcu gsum/ tshogs par gos lcam/ 'chams sku phebs skyel rol mo bar chos gos snam sbyar gos chen ma/ mdud pa nas skya bo pa'i bar 'chams sku gdan 'dren bzhin
dang / mgon khang khag bzhi'i gtor spod la gzabs spros rnams so/ /zhes rje rdo rje 'chang chen po de nyid kyi bka' yang dag pa'i de dus kyi zin bris rnams phal cher phyogs
bsdus 'di yang ma 'ongs par rim can du gzigs bde phyir 'dir bris pa yin lags/ de skabs nyer dgu'i nyin tshoms chen du tshogs 'gyed mdzod debs nang bzhin dang / 'phar bcas
kyang stsal to/ /bka' gnyan gyi 'chams 'di lta bu mdzad pa'i tshul la/ rje rdo rje 'chang chen po'i gsung las/ sngar gyi phyag srol la 'chams bka' gnyan 'di 'dra mdzad
srol 'dug par 'ga' zhig gi sems la/ spyir gsang sgrogs kyi nyes pa dang khyad par chos skyong gi 'khu ldog la 'dzem med rang yin 'dra snyam pa'i rtog pa 'byung mod/ spyir
shin tu bden yang lugs 'di la de 'dra'i dogs pa gtan nas mi dgos pa ni/ 'khon klu dbang nas shes rab tshul khrims yan gsang sngags rnying ma'i rig 'dzin snod bcud dag pa
rab 'byams su gzigs shing / dam can rgya mtsho bran du 'khol ba sha dag byon pa'i gdung dang / dkon mchog rgyal po nas gsang sngags gsar ma mdzad pa'i 'byung khungs kyang
bstan pa phyi dar gyi lo chen

rtsod bral grub pa'i sar bzhugs bla chen 'brog mi las rgyud sde'i nying khu dpal kye rdo rje'i bshad bka' gsan/ de'i man ngag 'dzin pa rnams kyi nang nas 'gran bral/ se ston
las man ngag yongs rdzogs bstan pa rin po che'i nyams len gsan te grub pa mchog gis mthon por byon pas yon tan tshad bzung med cing / spyir btang la'ang da lta'i bar du
sku spur ma nyams par bzhugs pas gdung brgyud ma nyams shing / klus gnod pa che rigs kyang mi 'byung ba sogs grub pa'i rtags mtshan yod pa de dang / yang sgos 'phags pa
rigs gsum mgon po'i rnam sprul rje sa chen yab sras dbon brgyud rim byon rnams zab don rdo rje theg pa'i mnga' bdag kho nar ma zad/ thog mar rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi phyag
nas ma rgyud sde rgya mtsho'i bstan srung thun mong ma yin pa gur gyi mgon po'i snang brnyan bse 'bag yid bzhin nor bu sku gsung thugs yon tan phrin las kyi rten/ man
ngag mkha' 'gro'i thugs bcud dang bcas pa zhal gzigs pa nas bzung mkhas grub dam can las 'khol sha dag byon pa'i rjes 'jug dbang gis smin cing / dus grangs kyi bsnyen pa
mthar phyin pa 'don pa lag len byang chub mang zhing / 'ga' zhig ni de'i khar gdams ngag yongs rdzogs thob cing / nyams 'khrid bskyangs pas bskyed rdzogs kyi go myong yang
yod pa rim can du byung bas na/ 'gro ba thams cad kye rdo rje'i rang bzhin du rnam par dag par lta ba sogs gsang sgrogs kyi nyes pa yong don med cing / bse mgon yid bzhin
nor bu lta bu'ang 'chams stabs kyi spyan 'dren mdzad pa nas bzung bka' gnyan gyi gar 'chams du mar mnga' brnyes pas 'di bzhin 'chams pa la nyes pa med pa'i gtan tshigs
yang dag yod pa bzhin mnyen chas dang dngos gzhi gtor bzlog rnams gzabs spros kyis mig gang

gi ltas mo lta bur 'chams dus gnam gshis shin tu 'jam zhing gra 'grig byung / 'on kyang 'chams ra dog cing do dam pa rnams kyis gtong ma mkhas pas khrom rnams 'dod pa rdzogs
pa rang ni ji 'dra byung yod dam bud med gcig mi nyog gis brdzis pa yang byung bas khrims pa tshos zhabs phyi go ma chod de rigs la slad nas kyang bsgrim dgos 'dug go /zhes
gsungs/ bskang gso brgya tshar grol nas sa tshogs su mi khrom rnams nub sgo nas yong shar sgor 'thon pa'i bka' 'doms bcas mi 'khrugs pa dang sgrib sel gyi gzungs ljags
bzlas dang / bdag gzhan brje ba'i byang chub kyi sems kyis gtong len dang / mdor na mthong thos dran reg thams cad la so so'i gnas skabs dang mthar thug gi don yid bzhin
du 'grub pa'i spyan dmigs dang chabs gcig phyag dbang stsal ba ste 'di lta bu'i thugs bskyed dang spyan dmigs ni rnam pa kun tu mnga' ba'ang 'dis mtshon nus pa bcas tshe
sems yo byad las skye ba mos pa smon lam sogs la dbang brnyes pas na skye dgu rnams kyi re 'bras yid bzhin du 'grub par gdon mi za'o/ /de dag gi don bsdu na/ dam ldan
gu shrI'i brgyud kyi mtsho nang du/ /lugs zung bsil zer phab tshe dad mos chab/ /jer cher 'phel ba'i rgyud ni 'dren byed nas/ /zegs tshe ya mtshan nor bu'i do shal 'khrungs/
/rigs lngas bsti gnas dbyigs 'dzin dga' ma'i ltor/ /mtshan gsum ti la ka yi ngo mtshar gzugs/ /sangs rgyas dbang bskur dus su smin pa'i gtam/ /snod bcud rna ba stong
gis nyan par lhags/ /gang tshe rdo rje 'dzin nyid bde stong dang / /bzhengs 'phral rten 'brel 'phrul brgya'i sgo 'phar 'bum/ /phye ba'i sgra ni ma bsgrags lhun grub grags/
/nor 'dzin bzhin snum 'byor rgyas mig gi'ang

blta/ /phrin las grub pa'i gtang rag kum bha nas/ /dge mtshan rab gsal brgyad ldan dag byed khrus/ /thabs shes myu gur bcas pa'i mi mthun dri/ /dbyings su skrod pa'i rgyun
bzang yang yang 'bab/ /sngon byon gong ma'i bzhed srol mdos gzabs zhes/ bka' gnyan 'chams kyis yid snang 'gyur rjes su/ /khor yug phyogs nas rgyug pa'i yid can kun/ /bdag
pas gces 'dzin byang chub sems kyis bskyangs/ /zhes kyang smras so// // ! dgung grangs so drug du phebs pa shing sprel rgyal zla'i tshes gcig lo gsar la 'phyar dar tshang
ma dkar po dang tshogs pas gos ber gyon pa sogs sngar srol med kyang khyad mtshar mdzad pa dang / tshoms chen gnam yangs la nor bu'i do shal thog mar 'grems gnang gi skabs
dang / bzhugs gral thog ngor gyi zhabs drung yas mas sde dge sku tshab rnams kyis thog drangs gzhis byes kyi sku mgron rnams tshogs dus sde dge nas gzungs gra lnga'i
sku sgros gtsang rnams phul/ de nas gtor spod rnams mdzad mur mnga' zhabs tshang ma dang gzhan yang 'ga' zhig nas bro gzhas sogs nyams dga'i rtsed 'jo yang phul/ nub gcig
rje rdo rje 'chang chen por tsha ba'i snyun thu mo zhig 'khrungs kyang sang de gar song cha med du dengs pa'i tshul mdzad/ zla ba de sku gdung rin po che zhal gzigs nas
bcu pa sku dogs tshul de yin pa bzhin rje nyid nas grub rgyal ma dang lcags sdong rta mgrin skyer sgang bla ma zhi khro lcags sdong lha mang rnams grangs mang stsal bas sku
gegs dbyings su yal/ rta zla'i tshes gcig nas dgung geg snga bsu'i mtshon phyi skyel bcas zhi ched sku tshe tshe chog lo gsum ma bcu tshigs rgyas pa'i sbyin sreg bcas
tshugs pa'i snga dro dam tshig phyag dril theg chen ma khyad mtshar de skyon can du gyur pas nyin gang thugs grang

stong nge byung gsungs/ lo gsum ring theg chen gan dril gzhan zhig gnang ba yang mi ring bar gas 'dzer du song ba dang / phyis kyi dam tshig phyag dril 'di ni 'jam mgon mthu
stobs dbang phyug gi phyag dril de yin gsung ba bzhin so bdun keg 'di gong gi gter ston gyi lung bzhin shin tu 'tshubs dus de yin gshis sngon 'tshubs des kyang sku gegs
rmeg med du gzhom par mdzad pa yin grang / dbo zla tsam nas sgrol sku gser ljang ma dang gra lnga'i lugs skur phyag nas brgya tshar dang / nag zla'i tshes 'go nas 'chams
dpe snang ba 'gyur thub dpang por bzung bar mdzad de rje rdo rje 'chang / brgya dpon/ zur 'chad pa grub dbang dang bcas zhal rgyas nas phur 'chams la zhus dag bka' drin
bskyangs te de nyid dang rje nyid kyi gsung rtsom kha shas gsung ngag skor sogs mang po zhig dus phyis bar la 'god par mdzad/ snron zla'i gza' tshes dge ba'i thog zhal dro
lha khang gis chog la phebs pas/ rdo skas ring mo'i 'gor dbang ldan bar tsho ba'i gnyer pa dpal ldan sgos skyes zer ba 'bul cha dang bcas byung ba ming bkra sogs gang sa
nas lam bkra legs pa dang / kho rang la'ang de sngon nas mi thod klad bcas rnyed pa sogs gtsug lag khang 'dir dge ba'i mtshan gsal bcas sa phyogs der 'bru'i char dang dpal
gyi zas mchog 'grims pa sogs sa chog spyi bye brag skabs sa khrod nas yungs kar mngon sum du 'thon pa sogs rnyed legs pa'ang byung gsungs/ rim gyis gtsug lag khang gsar
bskrun gyi dbu tshugs/ de'i bcu bzhi nas me phag nag zla'i bcu gnyis bar la rnying lugs 'khor lo 'bar ba spros bcas mdzad pa'i bzlas grangs chig 'bum chig khri drug stong
lnga brgya lnga bcu tham pa bzla bar mdzad/ de lo phur sgrub phrin 'chol gzabs ma dang dngos grub gling du rgyun bskang 'dzugs gnang gis chu stod zla nang

lhor spos nas lha chen khyams stod mda'i g.yab steng du rje nyid/ brgya dpon/ dbu byed gsum/ mchod dpon sogs nas 'chams rgyugs bzhes/ gro bzhin tsam nas yum mchog gi 'o 'dzin
g.yon snyun pa rim gyis je lod du gyur pa ljags chu dang / sman bla mched bdun klu dbang seng ge sgra sogs kyi rjes gnang grangs mang stsol bar mdzad/ phur sgrub thog
sgro lung pa chen po'i nye gnas dbang phyug rab brtan nas rje de'i dung chos khyad 'phags shig phul bas rje nyid nas de ma thag 'o 'di nga'i dung chos yin gsungs shing /
dbyug zla'i nang 'dzam gling phun tshogs dpal 'bar du da lta'i rten khri brkos ma bzo khyad can 'di gsar bskrun gyis sgrig par mdzad/ de skabs shig sde dge sman pa bla mas
'bul chen thog gser thig bug can zhig phul ba dang stabs mtshungs gong gi sgro lung pa'i dung chos la gser rdor/ gser dngul gyi gzungs thag mu tig sogs kyi spel bcas sgron
gnang gis tshe chog gnang ba bcas gser thig kyang de gras su 'grig pas legs par bka' stsal/ de lo'i dpyid dbyar ston sogs 'di khul la rims nad yod mur gdung brgyud rin
po cher yang beg ge bzhes pas mgul mi bde ba 'khrungs 'phral rje nyid nas ri khrod ma dang / ljags chu/ sku rim rnams nar mar gnang bas myur du snyun las grol bas rje rdo
rje 'dzin nyid thugs spro ba'i ngang nas sgo rum nang so sogs su phebs te/ sngar sku bltams dus gtang rag la phul ba'i lha mdung la dar yug ring mo re gsol bar mdzad nas
skyed lhas bsam brling gnyis la gtor spod gras su phyags legs par phebs/ mgo zla'i tshes drug gi tho rangs 'od gsal du/ si tu grongs pa'i rkyen byas sde dge blo gros rgyal
mtshan nyid shin tu mya ngan che nyams kyis nag mun ne ba zhig gi ka drung na zhal byang gzigs su bzhugs te si tus

bka' 'gyur rin po cher zhu dag mdzad pa sogs sde dger sku drin che tshul du ma gsungs shing / rta rkyang pa'ang brgyad cu tsam byin pa yin gsungs pa zhig 'khrungs so/ /de dag
gi don bsdu na/ gnam lo ljon rtse'i spre'u'i gar mkhan ma'i/ /gzigs mod gra lnga'i lha mo sa 'dir byon/ /'khon rigs rtsa ba tshugs pa'i yongs 'duu la/ /zhing 'di'i legs
bris gzhon nu spro gar 'bul/ /'khu ba'i tsha reg ting 'dzin g.yul ngor pham/ /'chi med ngor grub lta min sngon 'tshubs yal/ /bstan 'dabs gar 'chams byi dor byed bzhin du/
/zhal dro'i ror spyad keg sri rmeg med bcil/ /bcud ldan 'o 'dzin bskyangs dang sngon gyi gnas/ /rjes dran gsung gsang 'chi med 'dun sar grol/ /rgyal ba'i myu gur mi mthun
rlung gi beg /lo ma'i gos can lha mor bzhengs te bskrad/ /ces kyang smras so// // ! dgung grangs so bdun du phebs pa shing bya rta zla'i tshes gcig nas rnam sras bskang
bzla gang ma mdzad/ dbo zla nas mkhan chen chos bkra shis sogs la sa skya bka' 'bum gyi ljags lung yang tshugs shing rgyal yum zhabs 'bam gyis snyun par sman chab la phebs
pas ngo je gsal du song nas bcos rnams mdzad mur zhal dro'i 'jim sku rnams bzhengs brin nas rab gnas brgya tshar tshugs dus snga dro zhig sa skya'i nub phyogs su 'ja'
tshon ya mtshan can zhig shar bas rab gnas la dge ltas su gzigs/ de nas sde dge sman bla dkon mchog grags pa sogs la dbang bka' rjes gnang 'thon phyag sogs rim bzhin gnang
nas snron zla'i nang mdzod 'dzin dbus phebs shig dang bstun shab chu rags la zos skor gyi 'go zug /rab gnas grol nyin sbyin bdag bsgo bar sku gdung rin po che byon thog
rten gtso rnams kyi dbu thog gdugs dang sku mdun du mchod pa'i bye brag bla bre/

'phan/ mar me/ zhal zas/ rnga zlum/ 'khar rnga/ dung sogs gtsug lag khang gi nyer spyad rnams phyag tu bstar tsam re mdzad nas sku rnams kyi drung du phul te bzhugs khri la
phebs pa'i thog ma rang de 'grig bas rdzas brgyad mnga' gsol shugs 'byung du byung ba'ang sngar 'dra 'dra 'grig 'grig mdzad pa ma yin par rang bgrig de rigs rnam pa kun
tu mang du byung ba rnams ni yab sras yum bcas kyi ngo mtshar ba'i mdzad pa sha dag dang / de bstan grwa tshang nas kyang rab gnas gnang ba'i phyi bskor dang bstun sku rnams
gtsug lag khang du phebs rgyu'i zhal bkod kyis tshoms dmar du gzi ma 'od dang / zhal dror drung yig kun phun gyis do dam zhing gtsug lag khang gi rtse nas chos dung rin
po che gsung bskul te/ gzhi thog nang nas ltag sgo'i rdog skas bar btsun chung mchod rdzas can kha shas nas gdung rabs myur 'byon smon tshig brjod cing / rdo skas 'go
nas zhal dro'i bar byis pa lang tsho bcu drug lon pa kha shas nas mdung 'dzin pa dang / phye mar/ snod 'brus gang ba/ mchod rdzas sogs kyis sna drangs sku rnams rim bzhin
skya ser gzabs 'chor can nas spyan 'dren skabs rje rdo rje 'chang sras yum rnams rtse nas gzigs rtog gi tshe rje'i thugs la bstan pa'i rtsa ba gdung rabs rin po che 'byon
dka' ba de tsam byung yang ngal ba khyad bsad kyis thabs du mar 'bad pa'i 'bras bu mngon du gyur te da ni zhal gzigs/ zhal dro'i gtsug lag khang khyad par can 'di yang
rten 'brel bzang po dang bcas ha lam tshags su tshud pas thugs bde dgongs pa'i mur bde stong gi nyams khyad par can zhig de dus kyang 'khrungs byung zhes bka' stsal/ zhal
dror phebs skyes grub nas rab gnas zhabs bskor 'khor ba dus mtshungs dang / kun rar byis pa rnams kyis lha rgyal/ ser khang rtse nas chos dung rin po che gsung bskul mdzad
pa sogs thugs gra gang

'grig gnang nyin gnam gshis kyang bzang zhing / lhag par me tog gi char ni sngar dran ma myong ba lta bu 'bab pa 'dug ces skya ser mtha' dag nas gleng ba'ang don ldan bzhin
dang / mi ring bar gsol thab lhor phebs dang chabs gcig rgyal yum nyid sman chab skabs kyang sku gdung rin po che bde mu'i mtshan gzim thog 'gar/ bram ze tshangs pa tshangs
pa shes/ /zhes sogs mtshan brjod kyi tshig 'ga' gsung mur mnal ba dang / yum la sman chab des phan ngo cher gyur te rim gyis snyun las grol/ phur sgrub skabs mdzod 'dzin
yang 'byor zhing zhal dro'i skor tshang ma grub nas khrums zla rab ston gnang dus rje rdo rje 'chang ban tshang 'khor tshogs bcas gtsug lag khang 'og ma dang / mkhan
chen bsnyen song rnams steng du 'du bar mdzad de kye rdor rab gnas 'bring po bcas phyi bskor la me tog gi char nyil ba'i zhar la lha chen rung khang nyams gso khro chen gsar
blugs bcas la'ang shis brjod kyi me char phab ste/ chu kha ma nas drung gzhas kyis sdun bsus zhal dror rjes chog rnams dang / tshoms chen du dga' ston bzhugs gral gyi
tshe gsung bshad mtshams sbyor la rje btsun sa skya par gdung rabs rin po che dgos gal che tshul/ thog mar gnam kha'u pas dkon mchog rgyal po dang ma gcig zhang mo rten
'brel bsgrigs nas sa chen 'khrungs tshul/ sa chen la'ang sgyi chu ba'i zhal chems ser chas la rtsi 'jog mdzad mi dgos par gnam kha'u pa nyid kyi gsung bzhin gdung 'dzin gyi
go sar bzhugs nas ma 'ongs par phan pa'i lung bstan bdag nyid chen po bzang po dpal la rgya nag gong ma chen po dang sa skya'i dpon chen bu slob rnams kyis gsol ba btab
tshul/ sngags 'chang chen po dang a mes zhabs rab byung las slar gdung 'dzin mdzad tshul

sogs las 'phros te grags blo bas a mes zhabs la zhal ta nan tan gnang tshul bzhin deng dus rje rdo rje 'dzin nyid la'ang gnas tshul de ltar shar tshul/ gdung rabs rin po che
myur du phebs ched gong gi sgrub mchod brgya tshar rnams dang / grwa lnga lugs sku/ sgrol ma gser ljang ma/ rgyal yum nas dngul gyi sgrol dkar gsar bzhengs/ gzhan yang
'jim/ sku ldebs bris bcas bzhugs pa'i zhal dro lha khang rten brten par bcas pa'i rab gnas yin tshul sogs kyis 'doms par mdzad dus/ grags blo ba'i zhal ta lo rgyus rnams
gsan pas dbu byed bka' bcu pa spyan chab dbang med du nyil zhing / de nas legs skyes kyi bdog pa rnams bzhes nas bzo pa rnams la gnang sbyin gya nom pa'ang brims par mdzad/
dgun thog mdzod 'dzin bla brang mchog tu gtan tshigs zhu bar phebs pa dang / drung yig kun phun gdong sna ba'i kha mchu'i ngo len la 'thon/ rje nyid nas gong dkar 'or
sbug /rin rtse rdzong dpon/ sde dge a 'khro sogs kyi re skong dang / 'byung 'gyur sku gdung rin po che gegs med du phebs thub pa dang / sde dger rgyal sras 'byung ba sogs
kyi ched du mgon khang khag bzhir dpal gyi zhal zas 'dzugs gnang gis phrin 'chol gnad smin mdzad pa'i skabs so/ /de dag gi don bsdu na/ ngal bsos mchog gi dngos grub snang
brnyan du/ /shar 'phral dam ye dbyer med dge mtshan bdag /byin rlabs gzi 'bar nam mkha'i nor bu la/ /'gran zlar rtsom 'dod med khyer phung byed sgrub/ /rdo rje'i stan
la thog ma'i rten 'brel gnad/ /lhun grub chad med rgyal ba'i phrin las la/ /co 'dri min na rgyal sras dam pa ru/ /grub pa'i gtan tshigs gsal ba su yis 'gog /'phrog byed gdong
du thar pa'i gzhal med khang / /rgyud sde'i lha tshogs 'khrungs tshe zhal dro'i sgra/ /don dang ldan mod slar yang mchod yon gyi/ /myu gu gsar bu'i cho gar spro

dgas gzhol/ /zhes kyang smras so// // ! dgung grangs so brgyad du phebs pa me khyi rta zla'i bcu bzhi nyi ma rgyal 'dzom nyin gdung brgyud sku bltams zin pa dang ma 'gyangs
par bltams rgyu bcas kyi sku gegs sel phyir gdugs dkar nyer bdun ma'i dbang ras dkyil steng nas mdzad dus phan khang dbon nas byams sku'i rgyab yol gyi bzo gdan sar dbu
'don mthar phyin legs so'i gras la dngul gyi maNDal che legs shig phul ba lta gon nyin tshom bu bkod chog dang / bco lngar dbang gi dngos gzhi'i nyin me tog ser po kha gsar
'bul mi byung ba sogs rten 'brel gyi la nye shin tu shis/ bco brgyad dang bcu dgur gshed dmar ras dkyil thog nas sta dngos mdzad de sku gdung rin po che dgung grangs bzhin
pa dang yum sogs la dbang bskur mdzad pas gnas dang dbang rdzas sogs phal cher gdung brgyud rin po che'i mkhyen mtshor bzhugs pas rje nyid thugs dges/ sku chung ba ni
de dus yum gyi lhum na mchis pas rje nyid nas slob ma sta gon dang dngos gzhi thams cad la spyan dmigs yang dag mdzad pas bka' dbang de gsan pa'i go chod pa tsam yod gsungs/
de skabs yab rje rdo rje 'chang de nyid rje nyid kyi 'od gsal du yang yang dgyes nyams can du phebs te dbugs dbyung gzengs bstod kyang stsal zhing dus rtags dang bstun
bsam yas su rgyal po sku lnga dang yab skya bdun gyi rten mdos kyang 'dzugs par mdzad/ de nas 'char 'phar gyi bsten mkhas bgyi bas dus 'da' bzhin par sa ga'i tshes gnyis
gsum skabs ri bo che nas grub chen thang stong rgyal po'i rnam thar snga bsgrigs su grags pa par ma zhig phyag tu son pa ljags klog gi mu dang / tshes gsum nyin ban tshang
par rje nyid nas gsar btsugs mgon mdos dang dam tshig bskang ba'i phyag char sbyor 'jags kyi rdor dril theg chen 'dra cog dngos gtsang 'ga' zhig sgrig gnang de'i sang
shar ma skya tsam zla lag chu nang 'phrad pa bdud

rtsi sbyor ba'i thog sku gdung rin po che bltams ran pas gang ci'i bca' sgrig chu lug bzhin mdzad de bde bar bltams pas legs so bkra shis kyi mnga' gsol sogs gnang / nyi shar
thog gzim chung rtser rje nyid nas lha bsang mdzad rjes tshe dpag med kyi sku/ rnam rgyal sgrub thabs rjes gnang / dza bir/ sdom rig /rig gnas skor/ rdor dril sogs sku
gsung thugs yon tan phrin las kyi rten bdog pa'i dngos po dang bcas thugs dgyes bzhin du stsal te shis brjod kyi me tog dang / rim bzhin tshe dpag med kyi bka' dbang sogs
gnang / de nyin mdzod 'dzin nas zhal dro lha khang gi mchod kong gser ljang ma 'brus phyur te gzigs 'bul skabs da nangs yang gdung brgyud zhig 'khrungs tshul las 'phros
pa'i bka' gsang mang du grol zhing / de mtshams nas rje rdo rje 'chang nyid kyi dgongs par 'khrungs pa zhal sgo las byon pa ni 'di lta ste/ rang gi sems la'ang gdung sku
mched 'di dag 'khrungs rtags sogs gang sa nas shin tu legs shing / rang yang so bdun keg sri thu mo de las thar bas spyi sgos nas re ba mdzad cing / rang nas kyang lung
mo rtsis sogs la babs pa'i rim gro dang gzhan nas sgrub 'os kun 'bad pa bskyed khul la 'bras bu byung ba 'di bzhin spyir dkon mchog gi bden pa bslu med dang / bye brag yab
rje rdo rje 'chang de nyid kyis kho bo lta bu gnas skabs dus babs kyi gdul byar gzigs te rigs sras su rjes su bzung zhing lo chung ngu nas gong ma'i chos khri rin po cher
che 'don mnga' gsol thugs rjes gzigs te 'khur dbang med du 'khyer dgos la rang ni na phra lugs zung gang la'ang shes rgya med khar gti thom dang spra chal gnyis ka yod
pas zin re med cing / ma lags de nged rang la sku drin 'khor med yin yang go sa mthon po 'di 'drar zhal bkod mi thub cing / mdzod pa rgyal mtshan rin chen shes rab che bas
dpe 'dzin skyen zhing / dpe don 'brel ba brjod pa

gtsang ba'i gtam la rang dbang thob pa lta bu yin pas mi dbang chos rgyal sogs chen po rnams kyi dgongs par 'char ba de yang go sa chen po 'di'i bgyi ba rang thog tu babs pa
na 'o brgyal tsam yod dam ka bsam zhing / gnyer dpon bgres po/ drung yig kun sangs sogs drung ser rigs/ mgron gnyes sogs drung skya'i rigs/ mkhan chen sogs grwa tshang
rnams kyi khrod na'ang lugs gnyis ka nas mkhyen rlabs can rang yong dka' bas rgyu 'don spun 'don gyi bgyi bar yang 'ga' zhig mthun la 'ga' zhig mi mthun pa yang 'dug par
bcas 'dzin skyong nyag phra de skabs su gang sar thar rtse rdo rje 'chang de nyid kyis legs slob nyes bcos dngos brgyud kyi sgo nas bka' drin bskyangs shing / nged rang sger
gyi sgo gsum gyi bya bar gnas slob bzod pa bkra shis des yab rje rdo rje 'chang bzhugs skabs kyang bslab bya tshad med mdzad cing / rang la gdan sa'i 'khur babs pa nas
bzung nyin re bzhin yang skyon yon char 'bebs ltar bka' drin che bas de skabs su ni zhe bsun yong yang ring por ma thogs par mi gral du chud cing bla go chod tsam gyis
gdan sa bzung thub pa'ang de nyid kyi sku drin yin pas gang ltar rang gzhan rgyu rkyen de dag gis gdan sa chen por sku chag yong nye rang yin 'dug kyang / yab rje rdo rje
'chang chen po de nyid ni dus gsum sgrib med du gzigs pa'i rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas so so'i skye bo'i skur bsams bzhin rnam par sprul pa zhig tu gtan tshigs yang dag pa ni/
de yang sngags 'chang kun dga' bkra shis nas lcam zung gzhon nu nas bzhes kyang rigs sras zhal gzigs shin tu dka' tshul mdzad pas spyi sgos yi mug mun gling ngu 'khyams
skabs thugs rje'i rang gzugs nyi ma shar ba bzhin phebs te yab rje mchog las gsan pa rgya mtsho'i pha rol tu son/ gzhon nu nas gsan bzhes phul phyin bka' drin bskyangs
te dgung lo bdun par yab gshegs pas sku na phra mo sku rkyang ngang

la thug /ya nga'i dus tshod de 'dra'i skabs zhabs phyi rnams mgo ma 'tsho bar sngags 'chang kun dga' bkra shis kyi sku drin log 'jal byed mkhan tshos dbug shing gis yum sras
la thugs zos bde ba nyin gcig kyang med pa ltar gyur kyang log sgrub de dag gis nam yang mi brdzi bar bla ma gong ma'i phyag srol bzung bar mdzad cing / zhabs phyi'i thugs
bsun de las yol nas ma 'gyangs par jun gar pas bod yul la dpung 'jug mdzad dus bod kyi che gnyan phal cher skrag cing rtab rtab por gyur dus/ spyi 'gre bzhin 'dir yang
rgyal yum sogs bzod glags med pa'i thugs 'khol dang / mdzod pa phu gsum pa sogs sdings chen gyong nger gyi rigs nang du snying 'dar yang phyir snang med du sdod pas gzhan
phal cher gdung brgyud sku na phra skabs 'di tshos byed lugs kyi sa la hud ga 'dra zhig byas 'gro'am snyam rung re gnyis nas phag lab byed pa las zer ni ma nus/ nyen chen
de 'dra'i tshe'ang dpa' gdeng dang bcas bla ma mchod dpon sogs gzu bor gnas pa rnams la rang rer skyon mi 'byung ba'i gsung gis dbugs dbyung dang bcas bzhugs pas/ re
zhig nas dmag pa de gras kha shas gtsang la don spyod gzhan la yong zhor 'dir yang 'byor bar spyir kha 'khyams sna tshogs kyis brdab shogs dang / bye brag mi nyag dpon po
zer ba zhig gis dgos med du bsdigs pa thams cad blo gtor nas ci byar gyur pa'i mur dmag pa de rnams 'byor phyag zhu skabs rang bzhin sku mdun du 'ongs pa las dad gus kyi
par kab med kyang zhag shas nas 'thon phyag zhus dus/ gnang sbyin bkur gzos rnams kyang yar phul/ phyag 'tshal skyabs 'jug gi rjes 'dzin zhus shing / khong rang tsho'i dpon
por yang 'di ga'i gnas tshul bzo med zhu rgyu yin pa mdongs gsol du khas blangs pas 'dir yod rnams nyi zla sgra gcan las grol ba lta bu dang / yongs grags la'ang sa skyar
ci yang ma skyon zhes snyan grags don ldan deng sang mngon sum

du gyur pa dang / kho bo sogs gdung sras kha shas 'dul bya'i re skong du stsal ba las kho bo dang nu bo gzhon pa des re zhig cung zad phan pa'i rgyu mtshan gzigs nas ring 'tsho'i
bden tshig re'i dbugs dbyung mdzad par/ kho bo'i 'dir/ byams bstan ma shar bar du zhabs brtan pa'i/ /phrin las srung ma'i tshogs kyis bsgrub par mdzod/ /ces byams
bstan sogs ma 'ongs par 'byung rgyu yin pas nu bo de sngon la 'das nas ma 'ongs pa'i lci khag de khyod rang gcig steng du khel nas dar tsam zhig dka' mo yong yang phrin las
srung mar bcol yod pas hur thag thongs shig gsung rgyur 'dug kyang / ring 'tsho'i bden tshig yin pa'i lugs su mdzad nas gsung rigs de 'dra zhig mdzad pa sogs dus gsum
sgrib med du gzigs shing / gzhon dus nged rang rab byung nu bo de gdung 'dzin yin pa'i lugs su byas na chos 'chad sogs dga' rab byed rgyu yong ba dang / rtse gdong sogs rang
re'i lag 'byor der yang zla shas sdod dgos pa dang / dbang de'i sku thog la yang yang ngos 'gro byed dgos pas de skabs rab byung gi cha lugs kun gyi mig sngar mdzes shing
gdan sar yang gdung zhig bzhugs mkhan yod pas gdul bya rnams blo bag dro ba'i phyir ser skya'i rnam pa de ltar du 'gyur bar mdzad cing / phyis nas nu bo der sku tshe
dpag tu med pa nas lan chags pa'i snang tshul des sku tshe dang gdung brgyud gang sar bar gcod de bzhin yong ba bzlog tu med kyang / nu bo des gnas skabs 'khyug tsam zhig
tu khyed la phan thogs pas spun du bzhag pa yin no/ /zhes ston par mdzad 'dug pas/ skyabs gnas bslu med dkon mchog rnam gsum gyi/ /zhes sogs sku bstod shlo ka gcig po 'di
yang don la gnas pa'i sku bstod rang yin min gzigs pa zhu zhing / rgyu mtshan des na kho bos da lam gyi skye ba 'di la ngo skal du gyur pa rnams

sngo lo ma 'char tsam byung ba yang rnam 'dren dam pa de nyid nas dus tshod 'di tsam la kho bo'i dge ba'i las 'bras kyis spyir dal 'byor gyi lus dang / bye brag rje btsun sa
skya pa'i gdung du gyur nas ngo mtshar ba'i lag rjes la/ gdung spel thub pa 'dis mtshon kho bo rang dang 'dra ba'i dmu rgod 'ga' zhig spyi bye brag la 'byung ba'ang rigs
mthun gyi spyod pa des mgu bas gdan sa chen po 'dir phan re mdzad pa yin 'dug pas/ gdung sku mched 'khrungs rtags bzang zhing gang sa nas re byed rgyu yod pa 'di ni bla
ma dam pa de nyid kyi thugs rje dang / rang gi las kyis bdas pas rje de nyid kyi sras su rjes su bzung yang zhal gyi bdud rtsi nyung ngu las ma thob cing / nar ma son par
'khur 'khyer bas rang gis ni mi shes/ gzhan 'ga' zhig lhag bsam dag cing / la la rgyu 'bras la mi brtsiba'ang yod pa dang / kha cig rang gzhan gnyis ka'i 'phral phugs mi
shes kyang las kyi dbang gis 'khor du 'dus pas rang gzhan gyi spyod pa ma rungs pas sgyid lug pa dang / na tsha sems ngal bag med kyi spyod pa sogs snga phyi bar gsum gyi
bgyi ba rnams ni rang gi las yin pas bshags sdom byed mur rang dbang mi 'dus 'dug pas/ bla ma dam pa khyed kyis bdag skyid sdug legs nyes mtho dman ci byung yang thugs
rjes gzung du gsol/ rje de nyid kyi rnam thar dran zhing rang gzhan gdug rtsub can rnams la zhe log pa'i skyugs pa bskyil ma thub pa'ang kun blo kho rang la de 'dra zhig
las mi 'dug pas mthol lo bshags/ zhes bka' stsal pa lags/ de nas rim bzhin ril sgrub phrin 'chol sogs dang / gong gi rten 'brel rnams dang bstun dar dkar la mtshan gyi mnga'
gsol 'dri bar mdzad pa ni/ phan bde rgya mtsho'am e waM bzang por gsol ba'i rgyu mtshan sku mched gnyis byon pa dang / 'khrungs dus rdor dril

mang du bsgrigs par mdzad pas na e waM/ brtson 'grus bzang po'i mtshan mtha' bzang por gsol bar mdzad lags/ ril sgrub skabs bsam yas su gnang rgyu'i dbu 'ching / rgyal mtshan
jus dkar sogs bka' 'doms dang / de dus rje nyid dang rgyal sras gcung dam pa cung zad snyun tshul yang srung 'khor ljags sngags rim gro'i rigs nan cher mdzad ma thag yab
sras sku dkyil gsal bas ril sgrub gtang rag dang / chu lug nang bzhin lha mo gsol mchod gzabs shom legs 'bul rim gro rnams mdzad dus tshogs chen dbu byed bsod nams bstan
'dzin 'khod 'phral dang / snron zla'i tshes drug nas zla gcig ring mgon khang yod do cog tu bstan 'gro'i bde thabs la ched dmigs gsung bskang thog snyan shal 'dod gsol
can rnams bstar zhing / tshes drug la phun gling rtser gser zangs kyi rgyal mtshan zung gsar 'dzugs dang sbrags gzim chung steng thug gsum gnas spo'i thug 'dzugs gnang ba'ang
gong ma lcam dral/ nub ma zhal gtso 'khor/ shar ma las mkhan lngar bskyed chog gnang / de nas rje nyid kyis mgon khang bzhir gdung brgyud gegs med phebs pa'i gtang
rag thog 'dzugs gtor 'bul gnang gi skyed lhas su lho'i spang steng du gtor 'bul dus 'dzugs gtor dpal bshos de mgon khang du lus pas slar yang phrin 'chol rgyun 'thud na dge
mtshan 'khrungs/ bsam brling lho ri rdo gdugs 'di gcung dam pa'i bla ri dang sa 'dzin phun tshogs yang rtser mnga' gsol mdzad de slar yang skyed lhas su dam rdzas rgyan
ldan gyi gtor chen 'dzugs gnang gis gtor bsngo dang bskang ba brgya rtsa dang / de nas lha khang mkhan chen la lo gang gtor bsngo dang bskang ba brgya rtsa chag med mdzad
dgos 'doms par mdzad de phur sgrub phrin 'chol sogs dang /

lhor spo gnang gis phebs 'phral shis brjod sbyang khrus tshe chog lha bsang gtor spod sogs mdzad/ de nub rdo rje phug nas sras mo dpal lags 'jigs snang zhig gi rkyen gyis mtshan
langs byung ba ma 'gyangs par zhing brje ba'i ltas dang / zla nang der sras mo sku chos mdzad pa'i mtshan tshul khrims dpal rgyas dbang mor gsol/ phur sgrub skor chu
lug bzhin mdzad rjes gzhi thog pho brang du phebs/ gzhi nas me glang lo yan rje rdo rje 'chang nas sgrub mchod sogs la phebs rtag cing dbang bskur bgrang yas mdzad pa sogs
sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po dang 'jam mgon a mes zhabs kyi mdzad sgo sha dag las kyang brgal ba gnang zhing / de nas me khyi'i bar lo dgu tsam gyi ring phur sgrub
dus mdos gtor spod sogs gal che rigs ma gtogs phal cher la phebs ma thub kyang 'di nas bzung chos sde nyi zla rnam gnyis kyi bsgrigs la rtag par phebs pa'ang rje nyid kyi
tshogs gsog sgrib sbyong nyi skyel lta bu ma yin par thugs kyi mthil la 'di lta 'khrungs te/ sngon gyi bla ma gong ma phar cher sgrig rgyugs rang mdzad cing / khyad par
sngags 'chang yab sras dang a mes zhabs yab sras rnams nas tshogs 'don gsung bskul dang rol dpon sogs rtag por mdzad/ dbyar dgun gyi gzhis len gsung chos rnams la chag med
ltar phebs srol yod pa ni dam ba de dag gi rnam thar na gsal zhing / bye brag sngags 'chang chen po zhing brje kha mar zla ba sngon ma'i phur sgrub rol dpon mdzad/ a mes
zhabs dgung grangs re bgrangs tsam gyi gsung las/ tshogs 'gro mi thub pa'i lus 'di brjes na dga'/ zhes sogs kyi gnas tshul la dpags na thos bsam sgom pa 'chad rtsod rtsom
pa sogs mdzad pas sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa spyi byer 'phel rgyas 'byung gi /gzhan du sangs rgyas kyi

bstan pa ri rab khang khyim sogs snod kyi gzugs dang / mi la sogs pa bcud kyi gzugs ni min pas de bzhin du shes dgos pas na/ sngon gyi rje btsun gong ma bzhin du mkhas grub
grags pa can byung na mchog dang / gzhan du mkhas pa dang bstan pa'i bya ba rnams dang ya rabs bzang po'i ngang tshul ni gzhar yang mi bskyud pa sngar bas kyang lhag pa
sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa'i ched du sgrig rgyugs kyi 'khur 'di bzod par bya'o dgongs pa'i dam bca' thugs la bkod pa yin gsungs nas khrums zla'i gsang 'dus la phebs skabs shig
/dpal lags de glo bur du snyun bab lci ba gzigs pas 'phrod bzhes rim gro sogs yang dag mdzad kyang bzlog med kyis re zhig nas sku mi 'tsho bar mkhyen te/ so 'brang 'khor
lo sgron pa/ bdud rtsi stsol ba sogs mdzad de nyer bzhi'i tho rengs dag zhing du phebs 'phral rje nyid nas mi 'khrugs pa/ kun rig /sman bla sogs kyi gzungs sngags bsngo
smon gyi mtshams sbyor bcas dang / sras yum gyi sku'i rim gror bzlog pa'i rigs mang du mdzad rjes dgongs rdzogs rnams brgya dpon la bka' 'doms bcas rus chog spur sbyong
sAtstsha sogs dang / mchod 'bul bsnyen bkur rje nyid nas byang bu lam ston sogs mdzad cing / de'i tshe gcung dam pa 'khrungs pa'i dga' ston du yul chen ban tshang pas las
mkhan ru 'dren bcas kyi 'chams gzigs 'bul kha na yod kyang phugs kyi rten 'brel la dgongs te bkag med gnang / dbyug zla'i sa mchod sogs ston dgun sgrub mchod/ gtor bzlog
/dgun chos sogs tshang mar phebs mu'i smin zla'i tshes dgur lho phyogs kyis mtshon/ lung pa du mar sngar thugs dran mi gsal ba'i gangs chen po babs pa dang / gong ma'i
rnal 'byor ma'i dus tshoms chen 'gag tu gang nas 'ong med pa'i

'ug phrug byung ba'i ngan ltas bzlog ched sogs la thugs gzhol ba'i skabs so/ /de dag gi don bsdu na/ legs byas g.yab mos gnya' shing 'dzin ri nas/ /lha rigs snang byed rjes
su mched zla'i gzugs/ /bsnyegs la rnam 'dren nyi zla'i mtshan snyan ni/ /bskrun pa'i yab yum rgyal bstan spel ba'i bdag /phrin las zer phreng brdal ba'i zhal sgo las/ /dus
gsum lung bstan rdo rje'i mdud rgya dang / /mnyam du chas pa'i dge mtshan ci yang ni/ /sngon byon gong ma'i rnam thar ngang du g.yos/ /shes rab sgyu ma'i skyed mos tshal
'khrungs pa'i/ /padma gzhon nu yal yang rten 'brel gyi/ /zlos gar ra yig gnyis pas sgyur bzhin du/ /ngan ltas mun pa bsal ba'i snang ba 'bar/ /zhes kyang smras so// //
! dgung grangs so dgur phebs pa me phag rta zlar mgon nub gtor spod dang bstun thug rnams nyams gso dang 'dzugs chog ban tshang bcas nas mdzad cing / rgyud bla mchod sogs
la phebs rtag gi mur dbo zla gnyis brtsegs la gzhung sa'i sku rim bektse'i gtor bzlog dang 'char can phur bzlog la'ang phebs shing / zla ba 'di nas bzung ji srid bskal
pa'i bar sdom gsum tshes mchod gzhung skyor zla rer lan gsum re chag med kyi rgyun bzang 'di nyid gsar 'dzugs bka' drin che ste tshogs dbur byon/ nag zla'i nang kha skong
tshes mchod kyang sdom gsum dang 'dra bar gsar 'dzugs dang / de nas dam tshig bskang gsor phebs gong tsam du chos lung nas sku zhang rgyal po rnam lags/ sras yum sras mo
dpon g.yog byon pas sngar bzhin gang sar bdag rkyen yang dag dang / tshe dbang ston mo sogs zab rgyas su bstar ba mdzad pas khong dpon g.yog kyang dga' mgu yi rang ste slar
ldog /sa ga'i gsang 'dus mgon mdos snron zla'i lha mo mchod bde kye sgrub mchod sogs la phebs mu

dang / lhag par rje nyid nas sngar phan mus chen mchod 'bul la ma phebs kyang de lo nas bzung phebs te 'jam mgon a mes zhabs yab sras kyi sku thog bzhin chos spyod bar gdangs
sogs de bas bsgrigs kyis da lta'i nyin khyongs ma'i rgyun bzang 'di mdzad cing / chu ston sgrub mchod dang lo bcol sogs la'ang byon/ dus gtor chen mo dgung grangs nyer
gnyis nas bzung chag med mdzad kyang ban tshang pa dang lhan cig sgrub mchod gtor bzlog skabs ma gtogs mgon khang so sor ma gnang yang / de dus lha khang rtser phebs pa
nas bzung phal cher lhan du mdzad cing / gsol thab lhor mi phebs tsam la mdzod 'dzin shes rab phun tshogs nas gzhi thog lho'i shar nub mtho dma' mnyam na legs tshul snyan
sgron bzhin la nang so tshoms chen g.yab chen sogs la brling lta dgos pa'i bka' 'doms bcas phyag len du btab pa mthar phyin 'phral rje nyid ban tshang pa'i 'khor tshogs
bcas nas rgyal mtshan 'dzugs chog thug chog sogs yang dag stsal/ de lo nas bzung khrums zla'i rigs char yang tshogs phebs rtag po dang / de'i nyer bzhir stod la dwags rgyal
po mdzad pa mi legs pa'i sbir gtam gyi rkyen gyis/ la dwags rgyal blon la rgyu 'bras kyi bka' tshig sngon du gtong bar mdzad nas gna' bo'i chos rgyal gyi lugs bzhin bskyangs
na gang sar dge ba'i bka' 'doms dang / de lo spyan ltas shig tu/ rje rdo rje 'chang chen nyid bal yul na mchis par/ mchod rten byar rung kha shor gzi 'od 'bar zhing
byang phyogs na spyan gzigs kyi lha khang 'o brgyal ba zhig dang / bal po'i grong khyer kun mi nor zad pa 'dra ba mi thor re ba las med pa'i mur/ lho nub nas nyi ma shar
byung gleng zhing thams cad skyid nyams byed pa zhig 'khrungs pa ni kun gyis dgongs sla zhing / 'di la da dung spyan ltas dang dril bu phul ba sogs 'og

lo khams gang yin du gsal ba dang / gzhan yang 'char 'phar gyi thugs brel don yod rnams rim mdzad kyi skabs so/ /de dag gi don bsdu na/ bstan srung dbu 'phang bstod pa'i sgra
dbyangs kyis/ /sdom gsum rgyan phreng spud pa'i 'dus sde bos/ /shes rab lha mo'i gzhis mgron dga' mgu'i 'dzum/ /sras bcas rgyal ba mchod pa'i rgyun dang 'grogs/ /mthu
ldan rgya mtshor dus gtor bar med dang / /rgyal khab bla nar 'phags pa'i mtshan ma gzengs/ /drang srong r-i Shi'i dus ston gzigs mo las/ /rgyu 'bras don bstan chos rgyal
khrims lugs bsnyad/ /nai phal yi yul gru'i me long la/ /sngon gyi gnas dang lkog gyur gzugs brnyan ni/ /sgrib med gzigs pa'i khyab bdag bla ma rje/ /ye shes spyan ldan nyid
du bden par nges/ /zhes kyang smras so// // ! dgung grangs bzhi bcur phebs pa sa byi rta zla'i mjug tsam la mdzod 'dzin chu tshan la phebs/ dbo mgo nas rtsa 'chus sogs
mi bde ba'i mur/ de'i nyer gcig snga dro steng grib byung tshul gsan 'phral rje nyid nas khrus sna sogs brtse skyong dang mnyam du sman rim gro'i bka' 'doms rnams tshar
phyin mdzad nas rnal 'byor mar phebs/ gung sang sngon mar je lod mchis tshul gsan 'phral byas pa shes shing drin du gzo ba dam pa'i rnam thar gyis dza lung dpon slob gdan
'dren 'phral gnang bzhin nyer gnyis sa rub thog byon tsam la mdzod 'dzin gshegs nag zla'i 'gor kun rig sgrub mchod tshogs dbur phebs te gshegs por dgongs pa'i cho ga thugs
rus kyis gsung shugs dang bcas 'don par mdzad pas sku 'khrugs kyi rnam pas mgul cham bzhes tshul dang / de nas sngar gyi glo tshad 'phar nyams kyis zla phyed tsam mgul
glo thugs bsun can bzhes tshul yang dam tshig bskang gso'i skabs rim gyis snyun las grol/ de nas gnas bcur spyan gzigs

mchod gtor gzabs pa bcas tshogs bdag bskang ba zla gang ma'i thog /gzhung zhabs su mdzod gsar bsko yig zhu dus drung yig kun phun lha sar dos rta 'ul sngar bzhin 'khri med
zhu don gyi skabs dang / gdan sar 'byor phral sa ga'i nang gnas bcu lha khang du mdzod 'dzin khur bzhes kyi bka' 'doms dang / snron zlar rje rdo rje 'chang nas mdzod khang
du tshe dpag med lha dgu'i dbang bskur dang sbrags las zhwa lde khres gtong yong gtan tshig sogs de bas sgam/ gzhung zhabs bsko yig /dbang lha'i rjes gnang thog sku par
dang tsandan gyi phreng ba sogs gnang cha dang bcas las khungs su mnga' gsol te snga phyi bar gsum gyi bka' lung chu 'bab lta bur mtha' 'doms dang bcas stsal nas tshogs
bdag bskang gso dang / de nas lha mo mchod/ dbyar chos/ sgrub mchod sogs la thugs gzhol skabs nas mdzod 'dzin rgyal mtshan mthon por phebs nyin char drag po zhig gis bde
gling lcags ri'i shar phyogs chu chen 'grems pa kun mkhyen bzhugs khrir skyon med g.yas phyogs su 'bab pa rje nyid kyi dgongs par gzhan las ngo mtshar ba zhig 'khrungs tshul
ni phugs kyi rten 'brel zhig yin 'dra/ de'i sang mus chen thog mang ja bzhi'i rgyun 'dzugs dang / ba ri stag tshang ba'i gdung ba ri lotstsha ba'i dbon brgyud du 'khrul
nas bdag rkyen yang dag mdzad par grags shing mi ring bar mdzod 'dzin yang 'byor nas phur sgrub dang / rigs cha'i skabs tshoms chen lho brgyud nyen ches stabs zhig gso'i
gnas tshul shar zhing sman chab thog sku tshab rnams la zhib lta'i bka' stsal ltar/ lho skya gog po byin rlabs dang rdzu 'phrul kyis bzung ba lta bu min pa 'gyel zhig
mi yong ka med la slebs thog mgyogs rkyen spen bad spar ba'i lcid ma theg pas yin tshul phul ba bcas/ gang ltar nang so mgon khang zhig gso ran pas thugs rgyud bskul bar
gdon mi

za bas/ rje rdo rje 'chang chen gyi gsung las/ nged rang nas gzhon dus yab chos phal cher gnas gsar rdo rje 'chang dang brag rtsa rje las thob cing / yab rje rdo rje 'chang
sogs yongs 'dzin kha shas las yab chos 'ga' re dang gzhan thob rgya mi dman tsam dang / rang nas kyang kye rdor/ phur pa/ gur/ zhal sogs yi dam chos srung kha shas kyi dus
grangs kyi bsnyen pa yid ches song zhing / rgyun du'ang sgom bzlas mchod gtor bgyid mu dang na tshod kyang dar yol du slebs/ gdung sku mched gegs med du byon/ gdan sa'i
khur rgyun ring bas gang yang rgyus yod/ bod khams dus bde zhod 'jags rang yin pa bcas mkhar las bgyid dus skabs babs rang yin/ gong bshad 'od gsal la pu tras gnang ba
stsal ba'i dus thog de yin pa dgongs bzhin du re zhig tshoms chen lho skya las gzhan bka' ma stsal zhing / je zhig nas mdzod 'dzin pas nang so ma bsgul na phugs skyon chen
du 'gro tshul gsol bas de bzhin mdzad rgyu'i cha gzhir/ sku dang zangs chen gdan 'dren dka' zhing 'tshubs lhongs kyang byung dogs phal cher rtab rtab por gyur kyang rje
nyid kyi thugs rje kho nas skyon ye ma byung ste/ lha bzo ba zla 'od sogs la bka' 'doms bzhin sku'i sgron dar rnams gyen brdzes kyis bltas pas nyams tshod ha lam longs pas
gdan 'dren par thugs thag chod de rje nyid nas nang sor gsung bskang dang 'dzugs gtor rnams phul skabs dar phon gyen brdzes kyis zhabs gnyes phebs la khad dbu dud dud
mdzad pa lta bu'i tshul du gzigs pas/ zham 'bring pa tshos da lam ji gsung bzhin pu tra rang yang phebs pa la mnyis pa 'dra mo 'dug /ces zhus/ de nas rje nyid kyis smug chung
zhal 'bag dang a mes zhabs sogs kyis bzhes 'bag skur sgron pa'i phyag mtshan dar phon rnams bcas phal cher bsdu bar mdzad/

rtag gtor gyis mtshon gtor sgam rnams nang so'i thog nas tshoms chen du gdan 'dren dang / gtor sgam che ba spyan gzigs sogs rim bzhin bsdu ba'i bka' 'doms stsal rjes/ ban tshang
lha bris bsnyen song gnyis sogs kha ras lag bkru/ sngags 'chang chen po'i bdud rtsi ngo ma bzos rjes sku sa 'byar ma bsgul bas thog mar lcid che ba sogs rgyu mtshan
du mas dka' bar gyur dus mdzod 'dzin yang yang sku mdun du phebs te gang ci'i snyan 'bul dang / dar tsam zhig nas rje nyid gnas bcu nas 'dzam gling phun tshogs dpal 'bar
du zhabs g.yas kyi tshigs khrol bas 'theng bzhin du phebs 'phral mdzod 'dzin nas sgo bsgrigs steng du spyan 'dren thub cing zhabs g.yas la grum cung zad ma gtogs skyon med
kyi gnas tshul rnams phul bas shin tu dgyes te/ zangs 'khor che chung sna tshogs sogs chu snod gtsang ma thogs med 'du mdzad de mgon khang rgyab kyi nang de'i lho dang
thog la sgo phug steng du 'gro yul skas dang / mgon khang chen mo'i sgo glegs gnyis kyang phud chog gis sku dang zangs chen sogs bzhugs yul rnams lhus thengs mdzad rjes/
sang snga bar rje rdo rje 'dzin 'khor tshogs gang 'tshams dang bcas rnam 'joms rgyun sgrub gnang mu'i bum pa dang chu snod sogs la byug rdzas dri bzang byin phye sbyar ba/
de skor la gnang rgyu'i sngags 'chang chen po'i bdud rtsi ngo ma rnams sngon 'gro'i bka' 'doms mdzad nas/ rje nyid kyis rnam 'joms kyi gzungs bzla zhing bum chu 'thor
bzhin pas sna drangs te spyan 'dren skabs lcid med ltar bde bar yer gyis mgon khang chen mor phebs zhabs la nyams gso'i skabs/ rje nyid sku 'khor rags bsdus kyis nang so
nas 'phags pa rin po che'i phyag nas ma gur mgon lcam dral/ smug chung zhal 'bag sogs rim bzhin spyan

'dren dang / de nas yig brgya ljags bzlas su mdzad bzhin par zangs chen bla mtsho nas zangs shu gang chu tshags la 'dren par gnang / de nas gsol gzim gnyis kyis bcus te ban
tshang pas bkye skabs kyang nyog thams cad ras tshags su bzung zhing rdzogs dus med pa lta bu byung / zhes gsungs/ sngon sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal pos mgon khang de'i
shar nas zangs chen nub tu gdan drangs pa nas bzung rje rdo rje 'chang chen po nyid dgung grangs so dgu 'das bzhi bcu pa 'di'i bar du bsgul bskyod ye ma mdzad pas/ lo yun
ring po'i bar gyi bdud rtsi ril 'dam dang chu drag sogs myog gtsang rnams phyogs gcig tu bzlums par mdzad/ se mo'i ro sa bre gang gi tshod tsam la phal cher se ro rang
du ngos 'dzin dang / rje nyid kyi thugs la ni bla mtsho'i mtshan la khrag mtsho bkra shis 'od 'bar du zhu bas na/ rnam pa gdug can gyi khrag rgyun 'khyil ba la ngo bo ye
shes kyi bdud rtsi'i rgya mtsho dam can 'du ba'i chu klung chen por ngos 'dzin dgos pas na/ dgra bgegs kyi ro rang yin dgongs pa don ldan du 'khrungs/ chu phal cher dwangs
grub nas ban tshang pa brgyad gras zangs chen spyan 'dren gdong rje nyid nas gong bzhin bum chus sna 'dren gyis mgon khang chen mor spyan drangs te chus bkang / 'phags
pa dang sa lo'i thugs dam ma lcam dral/ pu tra/ smug chung / a mes zhabs kyis bzhes 'bag /bris sku phyag mtshan sogs byin rlabs che gras rnams gnas der bzhugs shing / gzhan
ma sku tshab rnams la bkas 'doms te gdan nas btu ba'i skabs mgon khang rnying ma de'i steng 'og bar gsum grum chen 'gro mi nus pa lta bu kun gyis gsal bar mthong zhing
/ gting rgyug khang thog gi khyams gdung spyi dang / khyad par pu tra'i bzhugs thad de'i gdung la nyen chen yod pa sogs dus gsum sgrib med gzigs pa'i nyams gso dus babs
dang / sang nyin zangs chen sogs

spyan 'dren gyi do nub 'chams khang gzhung sogs khad nye 'brel mtshungs su sdod mi phal cher gyi thog steng la ldir cham dang / snye drung rdo rgyal gyi nang du mi 'ong ba
lta bu'i shab shib mang po'i mur nang de'i ka drung nas langs pa 'dra ba'i mi dkar nag gnyis mthong ba dang / gzhi thog kun ngar yang thug chom sogs byung tshul gleng ba
bcas de ltar gnyan cing byin rlabs che ba'i skor rnams skyel bzhugs grub 'phral rje nyid nas rnam 'joms khrus/ rab gnas 'bring po/ mchod gtor gzabs 'dzugs kyis gtor bsngo
brgya rtsa bskang ba brgya rtsa sogs dang / zla re bzhin dus gtor chag med rnams bka' drin che nas chos grags pas rgyun bskang skabs zangs chen gyi ru long sgra 'byin pa'ang
byung zhing / de nas ang zug gi zhal bkod phal cher grub nas mdzod 'dzin gzhung phyag la byon/ de nas khyad 'phags lho'i thog dang / tshoms chen g.yab gsar thog mu mnyam
dang / a mes zhabs kyi zhal 'bag pu tra'i zhal brnyan la sku gzugs kyi zhal bkod dang sa mchod sogs mdzad mu dang / nang so mgon khang skor/ mnga' gsol g.yab kyi tshon
rtsi/ pu tra'i lder sku thun mong ma yin pa sogs myur du grub skabs rje rdo rje 'chang thugs dges pa'i gsung las/ bzo ba dang 'u la mi'i brtson 'grus las byung ba 'di
nged rang gi rdzu 'phrul yin zhes nyams ldan gyi gsung gleng dang / yang bsam yas ma bzhengs lhun grub kyang 'di 'dra ka yin yod gsungs shing / sku 'khor ba dang bcas bzhad
rgyangs dang / mnga' gsol g.yab dang pu tra'i lder skur phyag nas phul phyin grub nas smin zla'i gtor bzlog skabs mdzod 'dzin yang 'byor zhing / zangs chen dang sku gsar
rnying gi gzungs sgrig dang / rje nyid kyi phyag bstar gyis smug chung zhal 'bag nyams gso gzungs 'bul sogs gnang skabs lha mi'i dri bzang gis mtshon mi nus pa'i dri'i

khyad par dpag med 'thul zhing / phyag rogs gsol gzim gnyis nas mdzad pas nub gnyis kar khong zung la mon phrug gnyis mngon sum du 'ongs te gri khyer nas khyod gsod rgyu yin
zer ba dang / gcig la mon phrug gis rag dung rna rtsar 'bud pa sogs 'tshubs nyams dang 'jigs snang chen po byung ba sogs ni zhal 'bag bka' gnyan pa'i che bar 'khums/ mgo
zlar nang so'i mgon khang gsar par sbyong khrus dang / gur lha brgyad zhi ba'i sbyin sreg sogs rje nyid nas gnang ba'i sbyin sreg gi spyan 'dren mchod bstod sogs la 'brel
mtshungs rnga rol dbyangs sogs mdzad pas gzhan las babs chags pa byung bar gsungs shing me bkra'ang shis/ lha bzo zla 'od kyis zangs chen la nyams gso zhu rgyu'i thog
mar g.ya' rnams phyi bdar skabs zangs brdung gcig ma 'dra ba'i bzo khyad la kun ha las shing ngo mtshar du 'dzin/ de'i zhal bkod rnams grub nas yar lam mdo khams a li chos
rje'i sprul sku ngag dbang chos grags sogs dpon g.yog stobs chen nas dkar spyang rta sogs kyi 'bul chen dang bcas mjal phyag thog yar lam zos bde'i gnas tshul sngon 'gro'i
khong tsho'i yul grur sa lugs mdo sngags bstan pa dar ngo yod tshul gyis/ 'di nas bla ma gnang dgos zhus pa bzhin zhal gyis bzhes/ de'i tshe a mes zhabs kyi dgongs rdzogs
bde mchog tshugs mu bzhin dus chen tshes bcur bsu gnang dang / bcu gnyis gza' tshes dge bar nang so'i sku 'dra gsar rnying zangs chen sogs gdan 'dren dus/ lder sku rnying
pa shin tu yang zhing bla mtsho'ang de ma khad bkyed sla ba byung / zhes rgyus yod kun ha las las byed mur gleng ba dang / de nas kye rdo rje la brten pa'i rab tu gnas
pa'i me tog nyin gsum 'thor ba sbyin sreg bcas dang / rab ston nyin gos sku zhal 'byed sogs ngo mtshar

byin rlabs dang bcas pa'i bkod pas dus 'da' bar mdzad nas bcu bzhi'i sdom gsum grol 'phral a li chos rje can du phebs rgyu'i bla ma rnam gsum bsko bzhag dang / mi ring bar
a li chos rje dpon g.yog la 'thon phyag thog rnam kun don yod kyi bka'ang 'di ltar stsal te/ spyir chos 'jig rten gang byed kyang lugs legs dgos tshul/ khyad par chos lugs
grub mtha' gang byed kyang sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa dang mthun pa'i bshad sgrub byed dgos kyang / dus snyigs pas de bzhin dkon zhing / khyed rnams nas bstan pa spyi bye
brag la dar 'dod de bzhin rjes su yi rang gi gnas yin 'dug pas/ mdo sngags bstan pa spel ba'i bla ma 'phral bkod bgyis yod cing / 'dir 'byor thog kyang nang so'i nyams gso
grub nas rten rnams phebs pa dang 'grig pas rten 'brel legs shing / sprul sku rang yang lo gzhon nu la mkhyen sgo yangs pas mdo sngags thos bsam sgom pa sogs hur thag
mdzad pa dang / sbyin bdag rnams kyang dad zhen che ngo bcas gang sar legs lam che zhing / ma gir yang rnam dkar gyi bgyi ba yar ldan dgos lugs rnams bka' stsal pas/ sprul
sku ni bcos min dad gus kyis dbang med spyan chab nyil bzhin du/ gang ci'i mtshams la de bzhin dang gnas skabs kun tu skyabs 'jug gi rjes 'dzin zhu ba sogs dad shugs kyis
gdungs pa'i rnam 'gyur ci yang g.yo ba'i skabs so/ /de dag gi don bsdu na/ ngal bsos bang mdzod bdag po phan tshun gyi/ /yid mtsho byin rlabs rlabs phreng g.yo byed mkhan/
/dri bzhon dal bus bskyod la sbro dga'i bzhin/ /lbu dkar tshems phreng bstan te dgod pa bzhin/ /phal blor mi shong las mgon gzhal med khang / /'phags chen snying stobs
ldan pa'i ded dpon des/ /dam can snang brnyan nor bur dbang

thob ste/ /rten dang brten pa'i thang yangs 'di na bkra/ /shul ring mdo khams bstan pa'i yol go zhig /bstan 'dzin bcud kyis phongs tshe mdo sngags kyi/ /chu gter gsar bus phyur
dus dad mos kyis/ /rab myos rnam 'gyur stong ldan 'khun sgra 'byin/ /ces kyang smras so// // ! dgung grangs zhe gcig tu phebs pas glang rgyal zla'i tshes lngar bka'
khra rin po che'i dgongs don ltar/ mtha' dbus bde thabs ched bsam brling du gsung bskang rgyas pa dang / nyer bdun la nang sor gser zangs kyi rgyal mtshan zung dang srid
zhi dpal 'khyil du gser zangs kyi gambhIr/ rgyal mtshan/ maNDal sogs gzungs ldan du sgron par mdzad/ rta zla'i mjug sde dge nas 'bum rgyal a 'grub sogs 'byor bar/ sgo rum
bse mgon chen po'i mjal kha dang / dbo zla'i nang stod smad bla khang lam gtor gyi thog rten mjal sku tshab gzim 'od nas mdzad dus/ bse mgon chen po'i zhal gdong nang gi
gseng thag rnams dang ljags bcas zhal nas phyir phyung ste sku stod 'og tsam na phan tshun gzings shing brkyang pa'i tshul gyis shin tu 'jigs shing mchis pas/ de 'phral
rje rdo rje 'chang chen por snyan zhu mdzad pas/ dogs rtags rang ni gang yang ma byung / 'on kyang sgo rum du 'gro dgos gsungs phebs te gong gi gnas tshul bzhin gzigs pas/
rje nyid gsol gzim mchod gsum bcas nas phyag bsil zhal ras bdud rtsi gsol ba rnams mdzad rjes/ rje nyid nas zhal gdong nang du gseng thag rnams mdud bsdams dang / sku rgyab
gyang gzer la brtan par brtod gnang dang / ljags kyi gser thag hrul ba tshon si dmar sgrim sra 'thas kyis legs par bskrun dus gsung las/ sku byings kyang gog nyams che
rung re zhig gnang ba ma thob pas bcos ma nus/

zhes stsal zhing / 'on kyang kyog srong phyag g.yas g.yon la dar 'bol gyis sbyong stegs gang legs mdzad nas rdor gong / dar phon sogs sngar bzhin dang / sgom gtor lo gnang
dus su spo gnang de bsgul bskyod stabs gsar bskrun dang rnam 'joms khrus/ bla ma lha khang du khal kha gnyis dang gzhis rdzong mi sna bcas la mjal phyag /de nas gtor bsngo
brgya rtsa sogs mdzad do/ /snga sor yab rje ratna'i mtshan can gyis rje rdo rje 'dzin nyid la bse mgon la nyams gso zhig mdzad dgos yod 'gro stsal ba de mngon gyur du byung
gsung ba dang / gzhan yang sgo rum skor la gzigs snang ngo mtshar can mang po zhig 'khrungs tshul yang mchis/ de skor la mdzod 'dzin nas skyed ston dang rtsis pa sogs
la mo btab rim gro rnams tshar phyin mdzad/ gang ltar de sngon sde dger sku chag gis zhal ngo bstud mar gshegs pa sogs myang ngan gyi grib dang / sku tshab tshong dpon
yang dmag 'gro lan 'ga' zhig bgyis pa sogs grib rkyen du ngos 'dzin mdzad/ de tsam nas bzung gang gi a lce drung mchog gsum lags snyun gyi 'go zug ste/ nag zla'i dam tshig
bskang gso tsam la shin tu thu skabs bcas/ sa ga'i tshes bzhi 'khrungs bsangs grol nas rje nyid bde mchog tu phebs pas sku lus kyi rnam 'gyur 'gyur ba sogs gzigs pas/ nges
'byung lhag par 'khrungs pa dang bcas/ byab khrus la gtor ma yang yang bsngos nas gnod byed la brngan pa stsal te lan chags sbyong dmigs dang tshe dbang sogs mdzad rjes/
gshegs bzhugs gang byung yang phan 'gyur yang dag gi zhal bzhes stsal bas khong thugs dges pa'i gsung gleng yang phul/ rje nyid gzhi thog pho brang du byon 'phral tsam
nas bzung mgul glo bsun po de nyal gyi chag /mtshan gzim yang bde ba sogs kyi mur

zhag 'ga' khyol/ de nas yang je lod du song nas sa ga'i dge tshar bde mchog nas bsnyen bkur gzabs pa mdzad pa'i tho rangs sku zhi bar gshegs shing / dar tsam nas slar yang
phebs te gzim mal ma yin pa'i bzhugs stan zhig la rags tsam 'khod gnang gis/ sngon du rje rdo rje 'chang nas stsal ba'i byin phye dang / ring bsrel rgyu mtshan dang bcas
phul ba bzhes te bde bar gshegs/ de'i tshe rje nyid gsang 'dus tshogs dbur phebs skabs gsan 'phral gang ci'i bka' 'doms rnams dang / byang bu lam ston sogs kyis rjes su bzung
nas/ sku gdung rin po che zung la tshe chog dang sbrags tshe dbang yang stsal/ de skabs gzhung sa'i sku rim do dam par mes srong rjes drung yang mchis shing / nyer drug
nas mgon mdos bskul bar mdzad dus nang so'i ar brdung gi mu ste snye drung sogs la 'tshubs nyams kyis 'jigs snang ci yang byung ba dang / de nyin phyed yol tsam la btsun
ma sogs 'ul mi rnams bza' btung thog 'ga' zhig shar lho'i g.yab steng nas gzhan du 'gro 'dod kyis phor pa bza' btung gis gang bzhin du 'gro mur/ shar lho'i thad de yom
yom byed pa dang mnyam du glo bur rdib gzhom gyis shin tu yang zhing / snying rje la thugs thabs kyis dben pa zhig byung ba'i rkyen gyis thugs kyang 'khrugs gzhi shin tu
che ba'i bka' stsal dang / bka' lan/ thugs gso sogs so so nas dgongs dbyings dwangs pa'i rim pa rnams ci yang zhig phul mthar/ sa rdo'i khrod dang / de'i skyon gyis rkyen
lam du song ba rnams la thugs lhag par yang brtse bas rjes su 'dzin pa'i zhal bzhes dang bcas/ de rnams la byang buu lam ston 'phral gnang dang / de nas bzung nar mar
zhal 'don gyi skyabs 'og tu chud cing / thugs smon gyi mtshams sbyor dang / gzhan yang mang ja sogs dge rtsa rgya che/ nad pa rnams la

mthun 'gyur gyi rkyen sogs de dus su ma zad rnam pa kun tu ya nga ba dag gzigs tshe spyan chab g.yo ba tsam gyi snying rje'i kun slong dang bcas/ rlabs chen byang chub sems
dpa' chen po'i mdzad pa kho nas dus 'da' ba 'di dag ni/ ji skad du/ phan par bsam pa tsam gyis kyang / /sangs rgyas mchod las khyad 'phags na/ /sems can ma lus thams cad
kyi/ /bde don brtson pa smon ci dgos/ /zhes dang / bkur bar 'os pa legs khur zhing / /mgon med rnams la lhag par byams/ /byas la drin lan mi brjed pa/ /dam pa rnams kyi
mdzad spyod yin/ /zhes sogs gsungs pa ltar lags/ de nas sngon dus 'jam mgon a mes zhabs dang yab rje ratna'i mtshan can gyi sku thog sogs la dpa' bo dpa' mor rdor legs sogs
khog zhugs kyis ngan gtad 'don srol 'dug pa de bzhin gyi bka' gsang mdzod 'dzin sogs la grol nas/ bdun phrag gcig ring rje nyid sku tshe'i sgrub par bcad rgya mdzad pa
dang / 'jam mgon sku gdung bgres pa snron zla'i tshes mgor gsan sbyong gi thog ma gnang rgyu'i sku rim du/ 'jam dbyangs rtsod rgyal ma spyan 'dren gyis mchod shom rgyas
pa dang bcas/ 'jam 'don bskang bshags/ sku khrus sogs la thugs brtson dang / bde gling tshogs yongs 'phral nas gtsug lag khang byings la rab tu gnas pa zhag 'ga' stsal/ tshes
gsum nyin yon tan kun gzhi yi ge'i ma mo 'dzin chos bcas 'bul gnang gi sngon 'gror/ sku gsung thugs rten sogs kyis jeng drangs/ phan bde 'byung ba'i sogs bstan bstan
'dzin yun brtan sku tshe rgyas shing / gzhan don 'grub pa'i thugs smon dang / khyad par/ sgrub dang sun 'byin gsal ba'i nyi 'od kyis/ /zhes sogs kun mkhyen chen po'i tshad

ma'i lam rim nas byung ba dang / gzhung brgya 'chad pa'i lce bde blo gsal zhing / sogs nas/ yongs rdzogs bstan pa'i bdag por 'gyur bar shog /ces sa lo chen po'i rnam thar dkon
mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa nas byung ba de smon lam du bsgyur gnang dang / thub pa'i bstan pa rin chen gzhal med khang / /zhes sogs nas/ bstan bcos nyi ma'i snang
ba rgyas byed shog /ces sdom gsum rab dbye'i gsham nas byung ba de smon lam du bsgyur gnang sogs mkhas pa'i mdzad pa 'grub pa'i thugs smon rnams 'bras dkar gyi char nyil
bzhin du mdzad rjes/ glegs shing la gser bris kyi ka mad sum cu nas 'bul bar mdzad pas/ ka yi gi gu/ zhabs kyu/ 'greng bu/ nA ro rnams phul bas a yi bar la rigs 'gre nus
te mkhyen pa dang / gsung slob rnams kyang lan gnyis gsum la mkhyen pa sogs yab rje chos kyi rgyal po nyid thugs dges pa'i rtser son/ de'i tshe tshoms dmar du tshogs yongs
nas rab gnas kyis phyi bskor la me tog 'thor gnang dang chabs gcig sku gsung thugs rten 'ga' zhig spyan 'dren gras la 'jam dbyangs rtsod rgyal ma'ang phebs pas/ gsan sbyang
dbu tshugs pa dang stabs 'grig sku byin can gnas 'di'i phyi nang du byon pa ni/ gzhan las rten 'brel shis par mngon no gsungs/ gong gsal bzhin rta na gnas dpa' chen
yid ches gsang khog nas/ khog zhugs snga phyir bsam yas chos skyong gi ru dpon ga byang yin zer ba zhig gis gtad 'don nges 'drongs yod pas/ dus tshes che ge mor rdzas dang
yo byad che ge mo dgos tshul gleng ba dang bstun/ mgon po khro bcu dang / zhal gyi gtor bzlog nyer dgu'i dgongs 'phen te sa sros nas bzung pho brang gi phyogs bzhir uShNI
Sha'i sgom bzlas dang / drag po mdo bzhi klog pa sogs mdzad nas/ sku tshab zung sbrel dang bcas dpa' chen gyis gtad bton tshul ni/

lha 'dre'i rdzu 'phrul gyis thag ring na mnan pa byas pa'ang khog zhugs rang gi mdun du bkug rtsis bzhin phyogs der dong brus nang nas glang ra kha 'phur can zhig dang gnad
che ba de da dung lus song zer nas/ rtsod rus dong nang rum dus chu dkrugs pa'i skad lta bu lobs lobs zer zhing khrag kyang phran bu 'thon/ dar tsam zhig ci yang ma byung
bas klu bdud kho ded thongs shig zer mur g.yag ru kha 'phur can bton nas/ yi ge dang rdzas sogs phyung ba sku tshab nas klog rtsis byas pas/ ma byed zer zhing / bstan pa'i
bdag por 'di 'dra'i log sgrub rtsom pa zhes gleng nas thams cad gtubs te dong der dor nas/ lo gsum ring ci yang mi skyon/ de nas brtag dgos tshul zer ba sogs byung ba
bzhin dpa' chen la'ang bdag rkyen yang dag gis phyir mngags nas lung gsal gyi rim gro rnams tshar phyin mdzad do/ /chu stod zla nang a tsa ra spre'u khyer ba zhig gzhi thog
ltag sgor dar tsam bsdad nas thal gyis byung ba/ mgon po'i bskul rnams na ltas ngan du bshad pa bzhin de 'phral bzlog pa 'bum ther mdzad/ yang de lo'i lhums zhugs dus
ston nyin gzhi thog tu a tsa ra gnyis 'ongs nas/ sbrul 'jigs su rung ba/ bya sogs mig 'phrul 'ga' zhig bstan pa la mdzod 'dzin nas rje nyid la de bzhin gyi gnas tshul phul
bas/ de la skyon med/ sngar spre'u khyer ba la ni bzlog pa mdzad zin/ rgya gar pa mig 'phrul ston mkhan mang po 'byung skad 'dug pas ci yang mi skyon/ zhes bka' stsal/
phur sgrub skabs skar ma mjug ring zhig rgyal khams su shar/ gro bzhin tshes brgyad nas bla chen 'phags pa rin po che'i rnam thar thang ka ngo mtshar can 'di'i dbu tshugs/
khrums zla'i tshes gcig phur sgrub snga bar grol te nang so'i rtse nas chos dung rin po che gsung bskul

gyis kye rdo rje la brten pa'i rab gnas nyin gsum ma zhi rgyas kyi sbyin sreg sogs bka' drin che zhing / sbyin bdag bsgo bar sku gdung rin po che'i dbu g.yas zhal ngo rnams
dang phyag gnyer bcas te/ de'i tshe 'jam mgon gzhon nu'i phyag tu/ rje rdo rje 'chang nyid kyi thugs bskyed kyis bskrun pa'i sa le sbram gyi khams las grub pa'i bum pa cha/
phud dam/ phud phor/ 'dren chas cha tshang gsum sogs gser spyad mang du mchis pa'i nang nas/ gser gyi phud phor g.yu khra'i rtags brgyad can phye mar gyis phyur ba dang
/ rje btsun drung rnams kyis sna bdun/ sna lnga/ rdzas rtags sogs kyi tsakli/ yum mchog nas gser dam zhos gang ba/ phyag gnyer sogs tshang mas zhi drag gi mchod pa bag
dro ba bsnams nas rim bzhin phul te/ sbyin bdag bsgo ba/ bgegs skrod/ rdzas brgyad me long dUr bil dung sogs kyi snod pang tshad ma rje nyid kyi thugs rje las byung ba/
'bum thang mchod rdzas su bzhugs pa de rnams bcud so sos bkang ba rim bzhin bstar te rten drung du 'bul ba sogs phyag len rnam dag gi sgo nas mdzad cing / mchod bstod grub
nas phyi bskor la me tog gi char snyil bar yab rje ratna'i mtshan can gyi sku thog gi mchod phreng gcig dang / rje nyid kyi thugs bskyed kyis bskrun pa'i gnyis rnams gzhi
