thog nang la bsgrigs nang sor phun sum tshogs pa'i bkra shis sngon 'gro'i dril gsil/ rnga rol dung sogs kyi sgra sgrogs bzhin du nang so'i phyi bskor/ yang lam tshoms
chen du rab ston gyi bzhugs khri sogs bka' 'doms sngon grub la shis brjod kyi me tog dang / tshoms chen steng / srid zhi dpal 'khyil/ kun ra skyed 'phrang sogs nas rim pas
lha chen glo 'bur la 'phan nag zhal phye'i drung / sna lnga'i mchod shom rgyas pa'i mthar mchod phreng gis mdzes par bskor te/ skyabs sems nas bzung shis brjod mdzad rjes

mchod phreng sogs tshang ma 'phan nag sku rgyab nas lha chen nang gi zhal chen lho/ phur khang / khyams stod sku gsung thugs rten rnams kyi spyan snga brgyud/ lha khang byang
/ zhal chen byang sogs nas mthil bskor du phebs te/ mchod phreng gi sngon du kong gzhas pa bcas rim bzhin phyi bskor 'khor 'phral/ nang sor gsung bsngo'i thog mar rab
gnas kyi bshad pa dang / khyad par nang so'i rten gsar rnying gi lo rgyus bcas gang gi drin can rtsa ba'i bla ma dang / gong ma lnga/ sngags 'chang chen po/ /a mes zhabs
rnams gtso bor smos te mchod bsngo yang dag dang mjug chog rnams grub nas/ mgul la bkra shis pa'i lha reg gi spras shing / rdor dril rnam rgyal bum pa sogs bsnams nas tshoms
chen du rab ston la phebs thog zhal ngo sogs rim bzhin legs 'bul gyi skabs/ 'jam mgon gzhon nus phyag dbang thog ma gnang ba'i dus dang / rab ston nyin gong ma grol 'phral
sa rub tsam la kha skong sbyin sreg tshugs te srod chen la grol bar mdzad pa ste/ rab 'byams rgyal ba kun gyi drag po'i phrin las gcig bsdus dpal phrin las kyi mgon
po dam can mon bu pu tra chen po'i snang brnyan ring bsrel rnam bzhi spyi bye brag gi bdag nyid rab tu gnas pa thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa'i sgo nas ye shes sems
dpar sgrub par mdzad pa dang / bzhugs gnas nang so pu tra khang nyams gso gsar bzhengs drag po'i gzhal yas khang tshad dang mtshan nyin can du bskrun pa dang / gu ru rin
po che'i phyag bzo zhal 'bag dang / bla chen 'phags pa'i thugs dam ma gur dang / sa lo'i thugs dam puu tra'i sku sogs la nyams gso ngo mtshar can dang / khrag mtsho'i snod
zangs chen bkra shis 'od 'bar la nyams gso bzhugs yul bkod legs/ yi dam chos skyong

spyi dang bye brag las mkhan dbang po'i rnam drug rten dang gtor ma gsum la sogs pa rje btsun sa skya pa'i sde bstan pa gdung brgyud dang bcas pa'i 'thas su yang dag par mdzad
do/ /tshogs mang skabs nub gcig gzigs snang du/ bud med 'chor mo dang hrul mo mang po kun rang gzhas byed mu nas/ hrul mo rnams pho brang rtser rgyug shar byed pa zhig
'khrungs pa ni nad ngor ngos 'dzin mdzad cing / de dang skar ma ngan pa/ rong khog kha shas la nyi ma bdun dang gsum sogs mthong snang sna tshogs byung ba sogs bstan 'gro
spyi sger gyi rim gror ched du dgongs te/ gur mgon gtor ma'i las tshogs rje btsun gong ma'i phyag bzhes/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang dang / bdag chen rdo rje 'chang sogs
kyi gsung rab nas 'byung ba'i dmar chen gtor bzlog rgyas pa rje nyid nas bskul gnang gis sgrub skabs/ nub gcig zor las lnga'i mgyogs gtor dang bstun bsam brling phyogs nas
byung ba 'dra ba'i gtso zhig shar phyogs su mched/ nyer brgyad nyin kha ba 'tshubs pa dang bcas/ bal yul nas gorSha'i blon po sogs mi sna mang po dang / spang shing phun
tshogs sogs skyid grong pa re gnyis bcas 'byor phyag pu tra'i bstod bskul dang mnyam du byung bas mon bu dngos su 'ong ba lta bu'i thugs nyams 'khrungs/ gor rgyal nas gsung
bris rten bcas dang / mi sna rgan pa des rdo nag gi phor pa gu yus bkang ba sogs spyi sger nas 'bul ba dang / sku sang la mi sna lotstsha bcas la/ rgyal po'i sku khams
las 'phros pa'i gsung zhib gleng mdzad pas/ kho na re/ sngar nas bal yul rgyal khag mang pos rgyal ba yab sras sogs che gnyan du ma'i phyag mdzod dngul min gyis bkang
zhing / tshong 'dus rnams kyang ma rungs bar byas/ bal yul du'ang g.yul kho nas thugs bsun rang byung yang / da cha gorSha nas bal yul yongs rdzogs

dbang zhing / bod dang sngar nas lugs mthun rang yin pa bzhin/ slad nas kyang de bzhin bcas TaM gsar 'ja' 'u dngul tshad lhad med 'di bzhin 'don rgyur/ bod nas kyang gser thang
brgyad ma sogs dang / rgyal ba yab sras/ rgyal tshab dam pa/ bka'i dgung blon rnams bcas la rgyu mtshan zhu rgyu bcas/ 'di nas kyang char pa chu grogs dang / gzhan la'ang
bka' 'doms dgos tshul rgyal po'i bka' shog la'ang yod cing / ngag lam nas kyang zhu dgos bzhin bla ma khyod kyis phan 'gyur byed dgos zhes gleng bar/ rje rdo rje 'chang
gi gsung las/ phyag mdzod so so dang tshong 'dus sogs gang sar phan bzhed de bzhin rjes su yi rang / rang ni gdan sa go mtho ba las rgyal khams la bkod pa thub pa zhig
min yang / snyan 'bul zhu 'os tshang mar khyed rgyal blon gyis dgongs pa bzhin sne sbyor yang dag zhu/ sngar nas g.yul kho nas 'o brgyal byung 'dug pas/ da cha lung pa
des mtshon/ sems can rnams la byams skyong mdzad na don thams cad 'grub pas/ rgyal por de bzhin zhu grogs gyis/ zhes pa'i rdo rje'i tha tshig des khong rnams thal mo sbyar
zhing mgo dud pa bcas dga' mgu yi rang la 'khod cing / zur gsos sogs gnang cha yang dag mdzad/ nyer dgu'i nyin bskul dang bstun phyogs bzhir ru 'dren dang / las mgon/
gur lcam dral gyi 'chams sku byin can rnams 'chams par mdzad pas/ chu kha mar dus gsum rgyal ba'i drag bskul dus/ mkhas btsun chen po'i thugs dam ma khyer mis ma theg pas
nyen bslangs/ zor 'phen phyogs su zhal bub la khad kyi nyams dang / rlung phyogs kyang legs shing / bya khra mar mdun gyi shugs 'dren mtshon pa'i bu mo rnams nas zhing steng
du mda' dar drang por btsugs pas/ rje nyid kyi gsung

las/ mi 'gyur tshe yi ka ba tshugs rtags su 'dug gsungs/ smin zla sngon mar nang so mgon khang du/ rten mdos/ rtag gtor sogs 'dzugs gnang skabs/ mdos gzhung dam pas mdzad pa'i
mgon mdos rgyas pa dang / pu tra'i sger mdos/ bskang gso/ mdos kyi phyag tshad yi ge rnams gung bsgrigs/ shom dang 'don 'khrigs dbyangs rol bcas rje nyid nas zhag 'ga'
gnang bas ngo mtshar ba'i rtags kyang mang du 'khrungs shing / de mtshams nas rje rdo rje 'chang nyid kyi thugs bskyed rmad du byung bas/ gdan sa chen po 'dir rig gnas
kyi slob grwa 'dzugs bzhed ring mo zhig nas 'khrungs pa de nyid phyag tu son te/ mkhas dbang zhe chen drung yig 'byor zhing / chos grwa lho nas mi grangs bcu drug thog mar
slob grwar bkas mngags te 'phags chen mchog gi spyod par thugs gzhol ba'i skabs so/ /de dag gi don bsdu na/ ye shes mgon por mnga' brnyes cho ga'i tshe/ /mched zla'i rje
btsun skyengs te dbyings su gshegs/ /glo bur rkyen ngan lhags pa'i gzhis mgron rnams/ /thugs rjes sbyangs so 'gyod pas ci'i phyir gdungs/ /'jam mgon gzhon nu'i mkhyen pa'i
me long la/ /ltar snang chos kyi ma mo 'bad med 'khrungs/ /ngan gtad nus pa'i g.ya' bral thang yangs su/ /ngo mtshar rten brten snang la rang bzhin med/ /rdzas sngags
ting 'dzin g.yul du nad bdag dpung / /bcom nas bal rgyal rdo rje'i tshig gis bskyangs/ /tshe yi ka ba tshugs pa'i la nye'i mgur/ /rig gnas rgya mtsho rgyas pa'i ngogs su
grol/ /ces kyang smras so// // ! dgung grangs zhe gnyis su phebs pa lcags stag dbo zla'i nang / sog yul ha la shan nas dwags po sprul sku 'byor bar/ sdom gsum rab dbye'i
ljags lung zhig stsal zhing / nag zla'i nang mdzod 'dzin par bka' gsang 'di ltar grol te/ 'dzam

gling bstan pa'i bdag po sa skya pa zhes rje sa chen gyi sku thog nas bzung / deng sang gi bar du rang gis bsgrags pa ma yin par/ rgya bod mkhas grub dang gzur gnas kun gyis
rang bzhin brjod du gsungs pa de/ skye dgu phal cher la rlung ltar grags pa 'di la/ ngo mtshar gyi gtso bo spyi ring nas bzung gdung rabs rin po che zam ma chad par byon
zhing / gzhan yang gnas mchog 'di na 'phags bod kyi sku rten ngo mtshar can dang / bshad sgrub dar zhing rgyas pa 'di yang ngo mtshar gyi gnas yin mod/ de rnams kyi nang
nas zhing 'di'i skye 'gro phal cher gyis rtogs sla ba ni/ bla chen 'phags pa rin po che blo gros rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i thugs bskyed dang phrin las kyis sprul pa'i
lha khang chen mo 'di la/ 'dzam gling 'di nas lho phyogs shrIdhA nya ka Ta ka'i grong khyer dang / byang sham bha la'i rigs ldan pho brang 'gran zlar mchis na ma gtogs
kun gyis spyod yul du rdzu 'phrul gyi bkod pa 'di bas lhag pa med snyam pa dang / dag pa'i gzigs ngor bde ba can gyi zhing khams kyang de bzhin bcas/ sa skya pa'i bstan dgra
gdug can rnams kyis kyang 'di la cha shas tsam las rgol ma nus pas bskal pa'i bar du'ang rje btsun sa skya pa'i phyag tu gnas thub pa 'di la/ 'phags pa rin po che'i zhabs
rjes pa rang gzhan kun gyi lus srog longs spyod thams cad zhabs tog tu 'bungs dgos nges bzhin/ de nas bzung gdung rabs dpon rabs sbyin bdag bcas kyis sprul pa'i gandho
la 'di gces par skyong bar mdzad 'dug pa dang / khyad par sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal pos rten brten par bcas la zhabs tog bla med mdzad cing / nged rang gi thog la'ang
phyi nang gi spen pad nyams gso gsar bzhengs dang / sku gsung gi rten khyad mtshar grangs mang mchis kyang / thugs rten ngo mtshar can ma mchis pas 'dzam gling 'od

gsal 'di nyid gsar bskrun bcas bgyis shing / ma 'ongs pa na'ang tshul de lta bu bsgrub dgos so/ /zhes ston pa mtshon byed du da lam gtsug lag khang gi rtser skal ldan thams
cad bgrod pa'i skas ring ngo mtshar can kun gyi blor mi shong ba lta bu dang / snyan grags 'bum du ldir zhing mdo sngags chos kyi sgra dbyangs gnas mchog 'di nas stong gsum
kun la khyab par mtshon phyir rnga bo che gsar bskrun sogs bka' 'doms tshar phyin du stsal 'phral/ gza' tshes dge ba nas dbu tshugs te rim gyis 'grub nyer/ chos tshigs
mar ngo sngon 'gro'i don chos pa rnams dka' spyad sngon la btang nas lung rtogs yon tan phyi nas 'phel ba mtshon phyir/ snron zla'i nyer gsum la skas 'dzugs dang / 'jig
rten pa rnams yar ngo sngon 'gro'i don bde skyid 'phel yang 'khor ba'i chos las ma 'das so/ /zhes pas na 'dir bde skyid 'phel ba mtshon phyir chu stod tshes bzhir dge tsha
shol nas zhal dro mdzad dgos kyi bka' bzhin rdo skas gsum dang / shing skas san zhe gcig /sngar yod sgo them the ba'i zhe lnga mchis pa ste/ de lta'i skas ring ngo mtshar
can de thag pa dang rgyug bzo'i 'phrul sogs kyis 'dzugs skabs kyang rje nyid kyi thugs bskyed kho nas rgyun ring ma 'gor bar dka' tshegs dang bral te gzengs kyis 'bad
med lhun gyis grub cing / tshes gsum srod char thog mar dri bzhon gyis rdul gcags/ zim char gyis sa gzhi snum por byas/ 'brug skad snyan par bsgrags pa sogs sngon 'phags
chen de nyid kyis chu mig chos 'khor gyi rnam thar las byung ba de slar yang shar ba'i ngo mtshar dang / tshes bzhir gsol thab spo gnang dang chabs gcig rje rdo rje 'chang
gi dbu g.yas zhal ngo rnams dang / chos gra rnam gnyis/ drung 'khor lto gzan shar nub kyi mi sde/ zhe drung sogs kha 'thor ba rags bsdus bcas gangs nyi shar tsam la gang
'khod tshang ma gzabs

bzhes kyis rim 'dus dang bcas/ skas zhabs su chos dung rin po che rje nyid kyi phyag tu bzhes/ 'jam mgon sku mched la tshe dpag med dang bkra shis rdzas rtags kyi tsakli phul/
zhal ngo gzhan rnams nas phyag cha gang 'os/ mkhan pos thub dbang gi sku/ phyag gnyer nas 'dod 'jo mtshon phyir bum pa nyer lnga'i rdzas kyis bkang ba kha rgyan mgul
'ching can/ drung 'khor nas phyag cha gang 'os/ chos grwa byang pas rdor dril bum pa sogs/ lho pas bka' bstan glegs bam/ gzhan byings nas rang rang gi blos dpyad kyi lag
cha bcas/ chos dung rin po che'i gsung gis thams cad bskul bar mdzad nas/ rje rdo rje 'chang nyid thog mar phebs pa'i sngon tsam la/ bye'u chung ngu zhig gyen 'gro'i tshul
gyis byung ba ni/ gtsug lag khang chen po'i srung mas bsu ba mdzad pa'i brda dang / de'i tshe rje nyid kyis 'phags pa rin po che'i gsung tshe dpag med kyi bkra shis shlo
ka bcu dang / gtsug tor dri med dkyil chog nas byung ba'i/ rmi ngan 'jig dang / zhes pa nas/ nor dang bkra shis rnam par 'phel/ /zhes pa'i bar shlo ka so bzhi/ rje nyid
kyi gsung dpal sa skya pa'i chos srid la dge legs 'byung ba'i shlo ka gcig ste skas san gyi grangs dang mthun par mdzad mur gyen phebs kyang dgos pa 'di lta bu dang ldan
pa ste/ tshe dpag med kyi bkra shis ni/ steng phyogs 'jig rten gyi khams yon tan dpag tu med pa la bsngags pa yin pas gyen phebs la nges par gnad du che ba dang / dri med
nas 'byung ba'i bkra shis ni/ gzhung de nyid las/ lam 'jug dus dang nor dang 'bru rnams sdud pa dang / /nangs par dus sam yang na zhi ba'i las byed dang / /dga' ston kun
nas 'jug dang dgos pa sgrub pa na/ /ming tshig 'di dag mi yis rab tu sgrim ste nyon/ /zhes gsungs pas/ lam 'jug ni skas ring la gyen

phebs dang / nor sogs sdud pa ni de'i tshe legs gso'i dngos po rnam sras kyi bang mdzod kha bye ba lta bu dang / nangs par ni chu stod tshes bzhi gangs nyi shar dus de dang
/ zhi ba'i las ni/ 'brel thogs kyis mtshon sems can thams cad kyi sdug bsngal zhi ba'i thugs bskyed de bzhin dang / dga' ston ni/ mdo sngags kyi gzhung du ma 'don pa dang
lhan cig bsnyen bkur dang / skye bo rnams so so'i 'dod yon gyis tshims par mdzad mthar glu gar sogs rgya cher gnang ba dang / dgos pa ni/ bstan 'gro spyi bye brag gi chos
srid yar 'gro'i rten 'brel tsam du ma zad/ rje rdo rje 'chang yab sras dpon brgyud dang bcas la 'brel thogs thams cad srid zhi'i rtse mor 'khrid pa sogs te/ skas 'go'i
sgo nang du rje nyid khri'u shing la chos dung rin po che bsnams bzhin par bzhugs te/ yar 'gro tshang mar phyag dbang rdzogs nas/ rtser lha bsangs skabs bya rog snum bag
can gsum 'ongs te dbus ma'i mchu yas mas mar gyis dkar por byas te/ gsum ga rje'i zhal dkyil la blta bzhin du skad snyan sgrogs par byed do/ /de dus zhal ngo byings rnams
theg chen pho brang du bzhugs shing / bka' ram nas thig g.yab shar gyi byang du tshe chog /bsgrigs pa yan gyis de'i lhor 'dul lung sde bzhi/ 'bum sde lnga sogs gsung sgrogs/
btsun chung rin sgang rnams nas chos spyod/ byings rnams mkhar thog khud yangs su bsdad/ dga' ston gyi spro zas sogs stsal te rim gyis lha khang byang gi skas la btang
/ de nas theg chen pho brang du phyag nas dang / mdzod nag gtor spod/ phyi dro sde yangs su kong gzhas sogs legs lam dpag med mdzad pa de'i tshe lha chen steng gi rten
grags che ba rnams dang / chos dung rin po che sogs la snyan shal 'dod gsol can re 'bul bar mdzad/ de'i sang dge tsha

dang de mtshams nas mdzod 'dzin bla brang mchog tu gtan tshigs zhu bar phebs pas mgo 'dren bdag rkyen gyi brtse 'dzin yang dag gnang / de nas zhal dro'i lhums zhugs dus ston
gyi tho rengs mnal lam du/ phun gling dbang khang nub byang gi ka ba 'gyur nas gzim chung yongs rdzogs la skyon yong la khad mchis pas/ rje nyid kyi sku gzan sne mos ka
ba de brdungs shing bgegs skrod dang / phun sum tshogs pa'i shis brjod mdzad song bas/ mi zhig nas da skyon yong ba med zer mur mnal sad/ de skabs mdzod 'dzin par yar lam
rta dre'u'i gdong 'ur gyis 'ga' zhig gi rkang lag la skyon pa sogs 'tshubs nyams de dag zhi ba'i bka' 'doms dang / phur sgrub skabs gang gi rnga bo che gsar bzhengs la
shing rtsi/ nang gzungs/ rnga lpags/ dbyug gu/ khri/ bzhugs yul sogs phal cher grub ste gsung bskul gyi thog ma 'dar grang mkhan chen ngag dbang gis mdzad/ de lo bsam yas
chos skyong gi lung bstan du spre'u'i mgo tog gi rgyal mtshan sogs dgos gsungs pa bzhin stsal/ khrums zla'i sgrub mchod thog stod sgar dpon shag byang erkhe thA ji 'bul
chen dang bcas 'byor bas gang ci'i gsung gleng zhib cha dang / byabs khrus bcas stsal/ dbyug zla'i chog mang bde kye gsang gsum thog rab tu gnas pa sbyor gnang gis gong gi
'phags pa rin po che'i rnam thar zhal thang gsar bskrun ngo mtshar can dang / gdung rabs rin po che'i zhal thang gsar bskrun/ gzhan yang phur khang du gsar bzhengs mang
po/ lha khang byang du 'jam rdor bla brgyud bris rnying dang / grub brgya khams thang sogs zhal phye nas cho ga rnams chu lug lo bzhin mdzad dus/ sta gon nyin khang gsar
dpon bgres gzhon la 'thon phyag thog rje nyid kyi mgul la mdzod rnying khyad mtshar sgron pa dang /

lcang skya rdo rje 'chang nas gsung shog rten spam mtho bcas chibs zam brgyud phebs pa sogs rten 'brel legs shing / de dus khyams stod dkar po rnam gsum/ a mes zhabs rnams
kyi 'dra skur sa zhu/ na bza' bcas 'bul bar gnang / sa bskor nyin tho rangs snga mor rje nyid nas sgo rngar phyag nas dus/ gsar bzhengs 'phags pa rin po che dang / bdag nyid
chen por rgyu dbang zhal ngo nang brgyud dang / g.yu ring nas bdag nyid chen po'i bar dang / de nas dus mchod gdung rabs kyis bskor ba dang / tshe dpag med rnams gser
thang / bka' 'gyur gser bris/ gsar ma'i mdo bskal bzang / rje nyid nas rnam rgyal stong mchod mdzad dus kyi mchod rten sogs sku gsung thugs rten/ rab gnas kyi chas/ rgyal
chen bzhi dang stag 'dzin bsgo ba'i mchod gtor/ sna lnga'i mchod pa grangs mang rnams sa yul dog po der yangs khrol dang bcas rdzu 'phrul gyi bkod pa 'gyed nas/ cho ga
dngos kye rdo rje la sbyar ba'i rab gnas 'bring po'i lugs la/ sgo rnga 'od dpag med du bskyed de rgyal chen rnams la rdo rje phur pa'i rgyal chen tho 'dzugs la gzhi mdzad
sgos chos ma 'dres par sbyor gnang dang / stag 'dzin gtor bsngo sbags sgrub skabs gur lcam dral las mched pa'i gnod sbyin yab yum las/ puu tra ming sring spro ba'i pu tra
dang lhan cig bskyed de mchod gtor bstod phrin gyis/ gtsug lag khang / dge 'dun sde/ sgo rnga sogs srung skyong gi gnyer dam dang sbyin bdag bsgo bar sras yum rnams phebs
thog drung ser skyas legs so bcas shar mda' btang tsam la grol cing / chog mang bde mchog rab gnas kyi sbyin bdag bsgo bar yang gong bzhin sras yum dang / kye rdor gsang
'dus gnyis la sbyin bdag phyag gnyer

nas mdzad de/ lha chen steng 'og sogs nas rim brgyud phyi bskor la me char nyil dus/ nam mkha' sprin gyis gang zhing rlung yang ldang ba bcas cung zad 'tshubs nyams dang /
'jam mgon gcung rin po che sku rgyab tu gdan 'dren gyis mnal thog /brdal la sgang bzhugs khrir phebs tshe thugs spro nyams kyis mnal sad pa ni/ mdo sde rnams las/ de bde
bar gnyid kyis log cing / bde bar sad par 'gyur ro/ /zhes gsungs pa bzhin dang / phyi bskor 'khor nas rje nyid kyis mchod bsngo rgyas pa dang / bstan bstan 'dzin spyi bye
brag snod bcud bcas la gnas skabs mthar thug gi bsngo smon bkra shis kyis mtha' brgyan pa bcas stsal nyin nyi ma'ang gzhan las ring ba byung zhing / de'i tshe rje rdo rje
'dzin chen pos 'dzin par mdzad ces gleng bar gyur to/ /de sngon gzhi thog rtser sku yon khang gsar bskrun mdzad par dbyug zla'i nyer gsum nas bdun phrag gcig phur sgrub
rdul dkyil steng nas nyin gang ma mdzad skabs/ gnya' nang sho dpon ji'i sang kha sha kha'i sras dpon g.yog lcags sogs dngos po mang po'i 'bul cha dang bcas 'byor zhing /
ji'i sang la byang chog kyang gnang / smin zla'i tshes gcig la rtse thab bar thab bcas nyams gso grub pa'i rtser lha bsangs/ thab gong 'og tu khrus/ mdo klog pa rnams ban
tshang dbu byed zung la bkas mngags/ de nas byin rlabs kyi gzi 'od 'bar bar mdzad pa'i sku yon khang du 'jam mgon gzhon nur gyur pa sku mched sa zhu bzhes te thog mar zhal
dro'i rten 'brel tshar du dngar ba dang bcas phebs skabs/ snga dro kha ba nyil ba dang nyi 'od gsal ba gnyis ka byung ba ni phugs kyi dge mtshan ngo mtshar can dang /
gnas der phur pa'i zhi ba'i sreg blugs kyang mdzad rjes rje nyid nas gsol thab yas mas su rab gnas/ rnam 'joms/ tshogs bdag gsung

bskang bcas dang / sku yon khang du rten mchod rgyun bzhugs steng dmigs bsal 'jam dbyangs rtsod rgyal ma/ bla ma gong ma'i rgya dpe glegs bam/ rnam rgyal mchod rten/ sgrol
ma gtsug lag khang steng ma'i tshe dpag lha dgu'i rten gtso sangs rgyas tshe dpag med sogs mchod tshogs dang bcas par tshes brgyad nyin rab gnas mdzad rjes/ sku yon khang
du thugs gnyer dbu tshugs thog zhal dro'i rten 'byung rdzas kyis thog drangs/ 'jam mgon gzhon nu rnam gnyis/ sku yon pa bcas la rje nyid nas mgul dar sogs stsal rjes sgo
rum du phebs te/ lha bsangs gur lcam dral la gtor bsngo brgya tshar/ bskang gso/ phrin 'chol/ thos bsam sgom gsum dang / 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum dar ba'i 'dod gsol smin grub
rnams dang / sku yon khang du skyabs sems bla ma yi dam gyi sku bstod sngon 'gro'i/ sdom gsum rab dbye rtsa 'don/ bsngo smon shis brjod sogs zhal dro'i ched du thugs
bskyed kun bzang smon lam gyi rjes 'gro mdzad/ de sngon tsam nas bla brang rtse shod dbus phebs skabs sku tshab cig legs skyes 'bul bar mngags/ tshes dgu'i nyin skyed lhas
me 'bar gyi mgon khang gi g.yas g.yon ri nas shag mcher nyil ba dang / de sngon snron dang gro bzhin nang la'ang zhal gyi cho 'phrul sna tshogs byung ba rnams zhi phyir/
rje rdo rje 'dzin nyid chibs bskyod kyis skyed lhas lho ri'i spang steng du lha bsangs phyag nas bcas dang / mgon khang du gtor bsngo bskang ba so so nas brgya tshar sogs
spyi bye'i bstan pa thugs kyi dpal ber dam du bzung ba'i rlabs chen rgyal sras mchog gi mdzad pas zhag 'ga' zhig 'das rjes su/ skyed lhas lho ri de na rje nyid gtor 'bul
mdzad kyin yod dgongs par/ mgon khang mdun gyi ri gsham de nas/ gzugs mi mthong ba'i DA ma ru skad sbom po brgya tsam zhig bsgrigs nas

dkrol ba zil chen zhig 'khrungs/ mgo zla'i nang khal kha dge slong 'tsho byed chu nad can zhig sku'i gam du bcar bar sman bla'i mdo lung sogs mdzad cing / khong rang gi lung
par dge lugs chos dang gtsug lag khang sogs gsar 'dzugs bgyis par bzhugs rgyu'i rten dang / dgon ming sogs zhus 'bras thub dbang gnas bcu'i zhal thang / sman bla'i mdo/
dung dkar sogs stsal te dgon ming theg chen dbang rgyal gling du 'dogs par mdzad cing / dge slong gi lus kyang bde bar gyur te mi phyed pa'i dad pa la bkod/ zla ba de nas
badzra kI la ya'i sgrub mchod skabs kyi zhal 'bag gsar bskrun du mar rab gnas kyi me tog brgya tshar stsal te byin rlabs kyi gzi 'od 'bar bar mdzad pa'i skabs so/ /de dag
gi don bsdu na/ 'phags chen phrin las dag pa'i zhing khams rtser/ /'gro kun 'dren pa'i 'od kyi them skas dang / /ma rig gnyid slong chos kyi dundu bhiH /mig ldan spyad
bya las gzhan rdzu 'phrul ci/ /lkog 'gyur rjen ston 'od gsal lam yangs su/ /gdon bgegs skrod pa'i dam bca' mnyel ba med/ /khams gsum dbang sdud ngo mtshar mdzad pa'i cha/
/chu zla'i rol rtsed zin pa'i cho gas brel/ /'jam mgon gzhon nu bsten mkhas spyil por drangs/ /gnyan mgon gdod ma'i rang zhal lhug par gzigs/ /mtha' 'gro'i re ba'i yol
go bcud kyis phyung / /lnga bcu rtsa gcig srung ma'i byin mthu bsgrubs/ /zhes kyang smras so// // ! dgung grangs zhe gsum du phebs pa lcags yos rgyal zla'i mjug tsam gyi
gzigs snang du/ rje nyid bal yul du phebs par sngar bas bag dro zhing / /mchod rten bya rung kha shor shin tu 'drongs la/ /gdugs chos 'khor rnams gser shog gis 'phral byugs
lta bu'i dbyibs can zhig gzigs mur/ mi 'ga'

zhig nas 'di la khyed rang dril bu zhig phul na thams cad la phan thogs yang zer ba zhig 'khrungs pa bzhin/ rje nyid kyi gsung las/ bden min ci ltar yang / phan du re nas dril
bu gsung bskul rlung g.yab/ zhal byang smon lam bde skyid dpal ster bcas ngo mtshar du phul ba yin gsung ba de'i sbyar byang du/ ces ma 'ongs lung byang rnams las/ lnga
brgya tha ma'i dus 'dir bal bod mi rtag sgyu ma'i snang tshul ston par gsungs pa'i dus der sleb pa lta bu'i gangs ri'i ljongs 'dir mchod yon du ma zhig la 'pho 'gyur rim
can byung ba dang / nged rang dran nas rang lo bcu bzhi lon pa nas bzung bzhi bcu zhe skor lon pa'i bar/ bal yul du dus 'khrugs che chung sna tshogs rgyun ma chad cing
/ mthar rgya gar sogs yul gru gzhan la'ang brdab gzings langs pa lta bu shar skabs bstan 'gro'i bde skyid brtas phyir phul ba yin gsungs pa'i skabs su/ ngo mtshar gyi rnam
thar 'di lta gleng ste/ de'i tshe gnya' nang sho pa zung gi yi ge las/ 'di nas bang mi bal yul la 'gro skabs yo mo'i chu sogs 'bab pa'i chu chen zhig la/ rang phyogs kyi
gru shing gzhong lta bu zhig rgyag dgos 'dug pas gru de rdo la thug pa lta bu'i rkyen gyis chag nas bang mi gru mkhan sogs chur shor 'dug rung / skyabs mgon khyed rang
gi thugs rjes chu chung ba zhig tu bang mi gru mkhan gru chag sogs dang / de gnas gnang ba'i dril bu bka' tham sogs la skyon med byung 'dug lags/ dril bu mchod rten chen
po'i shar phyogs chos 'khor bcu gsum gyi gsham du bzhugs pas gsung sogs 'gran bral du 'dug tshul bris nas phul ba bzhin/ rje rgyal sras mchog gi thugs bskyed smon lam gyi
dbang gis phyi rol 'byung ba'i rkyen gyis kyang brdzi bar mi nus pa de ltar lags so/ /zla mjug blo bur du paN chen

thams cad mkhyen pa gtsang la chibs bsgyur gyi gleng ba dang / chibs zam brgyud lha sar khams nas 'brum bu'i nad dogs kyis thugs bsun pas/ bstan 'gro'i bde thabs gang la ci
'tshams zhu dgos/ rgyal tshab dam pa/ bka'i dgung blon lhan rgyas bcas nas stsal ba bzhin/ de 'phral ljags chu/ srung skud/ sku khrus sogs 'bul gnang dang chabs gcig gang
ci'i snyan 'bul tshang ma mchod yon bstan lar dgongs pa'i thugs bsam che bskyed mdzad pas 'phral du nad thag chod pa sogs rgyal khams kun tu rje nyid kyi thugs rje las
byung ba'i rnam thar sgrogs pa la gcig tu gzhol bar gyur to/ /de nas rta zla'i nang gi gtor spod le tshan nyin gcig la bka' drin che ste/ zhag lnga'i ring rje rdo rje 'chang
nas bskul mkhan dang rdo rje slob dpon gnyis char 'gan bzhes kyis/ bde gling tshogs yongs nas ri khrod ma'i bum chog rgyas pa tshoms chen du mdzad pa la/ 'phags pa rin
po che'i rnam thar thang sku gsar bzhengs zhal phye zhing mchod gtor sogs rgyas pa dang / khyad par nye skor mi phyugs tshang ma'i bza' btung lhag ma nad bdag gtor rdzas
su bsdu gnang thog /cho ga smin grub mdzad de/ nad bdag dkar dmar la dga' ba'i gtor rdzongs dus/ gong gi rdzas rnams gtor ma dang chabs gcig ting 'dzin sngags rgyas bsngo
gnang gis/ de dus kyi nad bdag grwa rgan lus stod smad rma shus gang ba zhig dang bud med 'o zom khyer ba gnyis rje nyid kyis dngos su gzigs te/ bka' las nad rims dang
byang 'brog khrod la phyugs kha mi gtsang ba 'di nyid kyi cho 'phrul yin 'dug pas da skyon yong ba med gsung ba dang bcas/ 'dzam bu'i gling 'di'i phyi rol bde ba can gyi
zhing gi shar tsam du/ ri lung khang bzang zas nor so so'i 'dod pa bzhin dgos dgu 'byung ba zhig tu brdzangs gnang gi spyan dmigs brtan po dang / nyin re bzhin lha chen
rtse

nas phyogs bzhir sbyong khrus mdzad pas/ yul ngan gyis dpon slob kun 'dar bun grang 'bur can du gyur kyang / bdag pas gzhan gces byang chub sems dpa'i rnam thar gyi ngang nas
thugs rus mdzad cing rje nyid kyi thugs bskyed kyis ri khrod ma'i thog ri bya sder ma sogs phyi bskor thang 'ga' zhig kyang snga phyir gnang / de nas bzung rgyal khams
su 'go nad mi 'byung ba'i thabs mu sbrel du mdzad gras dbo zla'i nang 'dod khams dbang mo rje khol gyi mdos chog bstan 'gro spyi sger gyi rim gror ched dmigs dang / nag
zla'i nang sa skyar mi brtsis shig byung skabs rje rdo rje 'chang yab sras la mgul cham zhig kyang bzhes/ snron zla'i mdo sde lha mchod thog bsam yas chos skyong gi lung
yin tshul gyis/ rab grwa zhwa ser du bsgyur dgos kyi 'go zug la rje rdo rje 'chang nas mdo rgyud dgongs 'grel dang bcas pa'i lung dang sbyar te rang rang gi lugs bzhin gyis
bstan par phan slebs che ba'i mtha' 'doms mang du stsal yang ldog par ma gyur cig /chu stod zla nang zhig 'od gsal gyi ngang du gnas gsar rdo rje 'chang de nyid yang yang
phebs nas/ zhi drag gi bka' 'doms du ma mdzad mu las thugs dgyes nyams kyis chos 'phro rnams bstud mar ma tshang med pa gnang ba zhig 'khrungs pas/ sngar ma gsan pa'i
chos bka' zab khyad can mang po zhig de dus 'od gsal du gsan cing smin zla'i nang rje nyid nas khrus sngags kyi chu dang / rdzas srung sogs nye skor kun la bkye gnang dang
bstun/ bsang rgyas pa/ ri khrod ma'i bum chog bcas mdzad nas phyogs bzhir sbyong khrus/ srung ma spyi dang lha mo rje khol la phrin 'chol bcas nyin gsum sngon 'gro'i zla
ba kha shas de bzhin nar mar mdzad/ mgo zla'i nang gser khar 'brum dogs kyi gleng je gsal gyis gzhis rtse sogs su'ang 'o brgyal gyi gnas dang / lam sdems

kyang shin tu dam pa bcas/ de'i tshe 'brum srung dang yor srung spyan bsal 'chang ba tsam gyis nus pa 'thon pa da lta'i bar du'ang lhag ma yod pa 'di rnams gnang zhing / der
ma zad rgyun gyi zhal 'don nar ma'i rigs dang / sgrub mchod/ rgyud dang rgya bod kyi gzhung sbyor mdzad pa/ bskang ba/ gtor bzlog sogs mdor na sku tshe de'i mdzad sgo thams
cad bstan 'gro spyi sgos kyi gnas skabs de dang de'i 'gal rkyen bar chad zhi zhing / 'phral yun re smon rje btsun sa skya pa'i gong ma spyi dang / khyad par sngags 'chang
chos kyi rgyal po dang 'jam mgon a mes zhabs sogs kyi dgongs bzhed ji bzhin 'grub pa'i thugs 'dun dang phyag bzhes kho na mdzad pa ni/ gnas skabs de dang de'i dpyad
khra rnams la gsal ba 'dus tshogs kyi snyan du ston pa rnams so/ /de dag gi don bsdu na/ dag snang rnam bkra nang gi ma ku rar/ /phyi rol ring po'i nai pa la yi yul/ /chos
sku'i rten bcas 'khrungs tshe ghanTI'i sgras/ /ya mtshan ltas bzang phyogs kyi rna bar grags/ /'dzam gling yul grur 'phyan pa'i mi ngas khyu/ /rdzas sngags ting 'dzin
dpung gis pha mthar dbyung / /rang rang grub mthas rgyal bstan spel ba'i dril/ /mdo rgyud lung gis bsgrags tshe spobs pa bdar/ /rigs brgya'i bdag po dam pa'i chu gter zhal/
/gzigs 'phral lus min hub gcig gis gsol ba'i/ /sngon med drin can bla ma dzahnuH /zhi bsil zhal skyugs 'jo phyir sa 'dir byon/ /ces kyang smras so// // ! dgung grangs
zhe bzhir phebs pa chu 'brug rgyal zla nas rta zla'i bar la rje rdo rje 'chang nyid nas rnam pa kun tu bstan 'gro'i don nar mar bka' drin che gras/ rgyal khams kun tu nad
gdon mu ge'i nyer 'tshe zhi phyir/ mgon khang rnams su tshes thogs dang / gzhan yang snga lo dang de lo gnyis la ljongs 'dir

nad yams kyis mnar ba rnams myur du zhi phyir rim gro spyi bye brag sku dngos dang bkas 'doms pa bcas nas mdzad mur/ dbo zla'i bcu bzhi nas nag zla'i bcu bzhi bar/ rgya gar
shes bsangs/ bstan gsol/ dgra lha/ sde brgyad cha snyoms bcas dang / de nas ri khrod ma'i bum chog /phyogs bzhir sbyong khrus re mos/ /gsol 'debs spyi bye brag /barNa sha
ba ri'i mdo/ /lo ma gyon ma dang / nad thams cad rab tu zhi bar byed pa'i gzungs/ rims nad/ mig nad/ 'brum nad/ zhang 'brum/ ma zhu ba/ sdug bsngal thams cad rab tu zhi
ba rnams dang / rims dang srog chags kyis mi tshugs pa/ dug zhi ba/ mdangs phyir mi 'phrog pa/ bdud thams cad skrag par byed pa/ rma 'byor ba/ me'i zug rngu rab tu zhi ba/
bad mkhris kSha ya skran rnams zhi ba/ bar gcod rnam sbyong / re manta dang mgon po'i rta gzungs/ dzam bha la'i lugs gzungs/ dbugs chen mo rnams nyin re bzhin ljags klog
mthar/ sgrol bzlog /gtsug tor rnam rgyal bstod pa gzungs 'dod gsol bkra shis rnams dang / de nas lha mo rje khol gyi mdos bskang la bdag bskyed phur chung bcas bcu bzhi'i
nyin grwa grangs nyi shu skor gyis glud rdzong rnams dang / ma mo spyi gtor rje khol gyi bskang gtor/ mdos bcas bsam brling du spyan drangs shing / de'i tshe dbang khang
du mdos sgrig rgyu'i snga dro bud med dpal mo zer ba zhig gis dkar yol che legs zung dang chung ba gcig bcas 'bras dkar gyis phyur po bkang ste phul ba dang / mdos tshugs
pa'i zhag shas nas gdan sa dan khrod kyi bu mo 'ga' zhig rtse dga'i do rang rdo 'jim la bcos pa'i lus rgyan 'chor mor bgyis te lhan 'tshogs kyis gtsug lag khang gi 'gag
dang sde gseb rnams su rgyu ba sogs/ ma mo mkha' 'gro'i cho 'phrul 'khor nyams ci yang byung zhing / sa khams

mi gtsang ba'i gleng gsan 'phral nas mdos 'di gnang bzhed thun min du 'khrungs kyang / 'char 'phar rnam kun don yod kyi thugs brel spyi dang / bye brag rje rdo rje 'chang nyid
kyis rje btsun sa skya pa'i sde bstan pa gdung brgyud dang bcas pa'i 'thas su/ sprul pa'i lha khang chen mo gcig pur yang shar nub byang gsum la spen bad gsar sgron/
lhor kha gso/ mtha' bskor lcags ri lcogs bcas kyi spang bad spen bad du bsgyur ba dang / thugs rten khyad mtshar 'dzam gling 'od gsal gsar bskrun/ sngon med pa'i thar pa'i
khang bzang gi rtser bgrod pa'i skas ring rmad byung rdzu 'phrul gyi bkod pa 'di nyid dang / 'gro kun ma rig pa'i gnyid las slong pa'i chos kyi dundu bhiH rje btsun 'jam
pa'i dbyangs kyi snang brnyan byin rlabs kyi gzi brgya 'bar ba/ rje nyid kyi rtsa ba'i bla ma dam pa yab rje rdo rje 'chang dang 'jam mgon gnas gsar pa chen po'i snang
brnyan sogs mtha' yas pa zhig sprul pa'i dri gtsang khang 'di nyid na bzhugs pa dang / de dang nye bar dpal brtse ba chen po'i snang brnyan byin rlabs phul du byung ba/ khams
gsum chos kyi rgyal po 'phags pa rin po che bltams khar yum gyi dbu sngas su bzhugs shing / phyis 'jam mgon bsod nams dbang phyug gi sku thog gdan sar spyan drangs pa
gsung 'byon ma bzhugs pa'i rten gzhal yas khang dang / brten pa lha'i dbu thog tu gser zangs kyi rgya phibs nang rten dang bcas pa mi ring bar gnang rgyu sogs mdor na sprul
pa'i dri gtsang khang 'di nyid gcig pu'i sa phyogs su yang grags che ba de snyed cig mchis na/ ngo mtshar ba'i phyag rjes gzhan dag ni so skye'i blo'i ra ba las brgal
zhing / cung zad zin pa rnams lo khams so sor gsal ba bcas/ dus mdos gzabs ma'i skabs su mkho ba'i zhal 'bag gsar bzhengs la phyag nas brgya

tshar zla gsum ma sogs kyi thugs brel gyis 'gyangs pa dang / gzhung sa mchog nas kyang gzhis rtses mtshon bod khams bde thabs su mngags pa'i rim gro rnams dang dod lhus blangs
gang la gang 'tshams ye shes gzigs pas dpyad nas mdzad cing / gang na'ang grol nas zhag gsum pa'i tho rengs 'od gsal du/ mi pho mo mang pos sku nyid la dad 'dun lhag
par che ba dang / bud med gcig 'chor gnyis 'chor bdun brgyad cig 'ongs nas pad bskor sogs lus kyi rnam 'gyur dod nyams dang / skad sbom phra snyoms shing bzang bas/ tshe
dbang zhu la phebs zhes glu blangs te khrom lta bu zhig la brda gtong ba'i ltas 'khrungs pa ni/ spyir rgyal khams nad dogs myur du zhi ba dang / lhag par yul gru 'di nyid
du bde 'jags 'byung ba dang / yang sgos rje rdo rje 'chang nyid kyi sku 'phrang 'tshubs ma zhi ba'i rtags su gor ma chag go /de lta'i skabs rgyal khams su rje nyid kyi ljags
chu rims srung sogs kyis phal cher la khyab cing / gong gsal gyi thugs bskyed de dag bcas nyid kyi sku drin gyis bskyangs so zhes pa'i sgra sgrogs pas brel ba bzhin
don la'ang gnas so/ /sa zla'i mjug bas si tA la sbo shog thu'i gsung mngags zhib cha bcas/ bla ma sangs rgyas don grub dpon g.yog 'byor pa rje nyid ril sgrub bcad rgya dang
'grig pas zhag 'ga' sgugs thog nas/ rten 'brel rab la bsgrig mi dgos par 'grig pa ni/ snron zla'i tshes gnyis la 'jam mgon khams gsum dbang sdud nyid kye rdo rje'i rgyud
'don la thog mar phebs dus bla ma dpon g.yog la 'byor phyag thog khong tshos/ mgul la bkra shis pa'i lha dar phul ba dang / tshes gsum nyin sprul pa'i lha khang chen mor
zab pa'i yang rtse bla ma'i rnal 'byor nyams bzhes pa mdo sngags tshogs yongs kyi dbur rje yab sras byon thog /

dam tshig 'gyur med pas se phyag rdor skyabs kyi gsung shog rten gya nom pas thog drangs/ maNDal gyis gtsos dngul bre chen mang po'i 'bul chen mdzad pa sogs dge legs rten 'brel
bzang po rab 'byams rgyal ba'i zhing khams su'ang khyab cing grub par gyur to/ /de nas chu stod dge tsha dang / bco lngar zhal dro lha khang du rje nyid kyis debs bsgrigs
bzhin bstan don rgya cher mdzad pa ni rnam pa kun tu'o/ /gro bzhin phur bsgrub nyer gcig mus chen mchod bsngor dpal 'khor lo bde mchog gi rnam sprul yin pa'i bsngags
brjod mdzad pas/ de'i tho rengs kyi 'od gsal du/ rje nyid khyad 'phags lho'i mgon khang na bzhugs mur/ dar tsam nas sras yum gnyis kyang phebs byung ba la/ rje nyid nas
rten bshad gnang rgyu yin dgongs par rten khri'i steng na bde mchog lhan skyes kyi sku yum phag mo'ang sngon mos 'khyud pa 'jim sku khru gang tsam zhig gi bzhugs gdan nyi
dkyil de la/ gser yig dbu chen gyis/ ka lingga'i tshogs dpon gyis phul sa skyar gdung byon yong / gegs chag le tshan gsum mchis pa'i gnyis mnyel tshul dang / gsum pa shar
lho'i dmar grib la 'dzem zer ba zhig bris 'dug pa dang / rten khri gzhan zhig na kha che paN chen gyi thugs dam ma bde mchog lhan skyes gser zangs kyi sku mkhyid gang
tsam zhig bcas gzigs snang du 'khrungs pa 'di la/ rje rdo rje 'chang gi bka' las/ ka lingga 'di bde mchog gsung 'khor gyi gras lus kyi kha nang mnye ma'i khams sbyong byed
dang / phyi shar lho'i rtsibs na rab tu bzang po dang shyA ma de ba bzhugs pa de yin pas brda tshig gang yin ni dbye dka' gsung ba 'di la gnad khyad par ba zhig yod snyam
yang re zhig btang snyoms su bzhag /de'i tshe 'jam mgon dbang

sdud snying po nyid phur sgrub tshogs phebs thog ma'i skabs dang / khrum zla'i tshes gsum la lha chen nas sangs rgyas don grub chos khrims mdzad gong gsung brtag zhus pa'i
tho rengs 'od gsal du/ rje nyid lho byang dge 'dun rnams dang lhan du bzhugs thog sku sang zhig mdzad par mkhan rin po che nas/ sngar yang lha khang bla brang du thub sku
khyad can zhig 'byor zhing / da dung 'byor rgyu zhig gzhan nas gdan sar zhus tshod 'dug kyang lan ma gnang bas ma 'byor gsungs pa la/ rje nyid kyi dgongs par yang / sngar
nas thub sku zhig ser phreng sogs kyis drangs pa yin/ da dung 'byor tshe de bzhin bgyid dgongs mur/ thub sku de 'bul mi yin rgyu'i mus phyogs nas dge slong bud med kyi
chas can zhig 'dug par/ bka' las/ spyir dge slong gi skya chas dang / bye brag bud med kyi chas 'di 'dra glang dar ma'i dge slong yin 'dra gsungs pas/ nged la dgos gal zhig
byung nas byas pa yin zer bar/ 'don pa ci shes dri ba mdzad lan/ ma Ni las mi shes zer bas brdzun yin dgongs nas/ khyed rang mtshan brjod/ bzang spyod/ ltung bshags rnams
spyir 'don pa dang / bye brag rang res lugs la gong ma lnga bstod med na mi rung bas thon gsungs pas/ rtsod pa bgyid rtsis kyis gong ma lnga ci yin zer/ dkar po rnam
gsum dang chos rje khu dbon yin gsungs pas mgo gug gug byed mur 'od gsal 'byams pa zhig 'khrungs pas/ bka' las/ da lta'i mkhan po dang / slad nas 'byon 'gyur zhig kyang khyad
mtshar yong ngor/ gdan sa rang nas 'grig min byung dogs bcas ma 'ongs lung bstan 'dra zhing / bud med gyi chas bgyis pa gab tshig bzang ngan dbye dka' gsungs/ yang tshes
bdun gyi tho rangs sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal pos byas 'gyur nas gsung chen po'i sgo nas gsung mgur zhig mdzad byung ba la de'i gsung lan/

rje rdo rje 'chang nyid kyis sa skya nas 'bul gnang gis phar gsan tshur gsan shin tu gsal bar 'khrungs kyang tshig don ji bzhin ma nges/ zhes gsungs pa 'di dag ni/ nye ring
kun la snyoms pa tshangs pa'i dbyangs/ /zhes gsung gi gsang bar mnga' brnyes pa'i brda'o/ /sngon sngags 'chang nyid la sa lotstsha ba 'od gsal du byon nas lung bstan phul
du byung ba stsal ba bzhin/ rje nyid la'ang sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po zhal gzigs kyi bka' gsang rmad du byung ba grol ba ni gor ma chag kyang / de dus su ma zad/
dus gnas dang bstun par mdzad de gnad che ba 'ga' zhig gi tshe rnam pa kun tu ma nges pa'i zol mdzad cing / gzhan du mnyel ba mi mnga' ba'i ngang tshul bzang po rje nyid
la mnga' ba ni ma bcos lhun grub bo/ /tshes brgyad nas phun gling dbang khang du sras yum rnams la/ kye rdo rje'i rgyu dbang rdul dkyil steng nas dang / aShta'i bzlas lung
bcas rgyas par stsal ba de ni gong sa gcung rin po cher gong gsal gyi lhums zhugs thog go chod par zhal gyis bzhes pa'i dbang de dang / sku bltams nas 'di nyid smin byed
kyi thog ma rang yin par nges la/ de dang mu sbrel zhu dpon ngag dbang dge legs dang / mkhas dbang zhe drung slob grwa dge rgan bcas la'ang stsal zhing / rigs cha/ rtsa
rgyud/ sdom gsum rnam gnyis bcas kyi tshogs dbu dang / chos lhun mkhan gsar la mnga' gsol sbyong khrus/ 'jam mgon sku mched/ rje btsun drung zung / rgyal yum bcas la kun
rig dbang rdul dkyil steng nas dang / bsnyen thabs kyi ljags lung bcas stsal/ bkra shis zla ba de'i nang lha chen khyams stod gser khri rin po che gsar bskrun mdzad rgyu'i
bka' 'doms bzhin/ mdzod 'dzin nas lha bzo zla 'od sogs la bkas mngags te ha lam gyi tsag par zla ba de'i tshes dge bar spyan bdar dus/

zhal dkar 'bras sil gyis gtams pa phul ba dang stabs 'grig byung bas la nye bzang ba'i sgo dang po dang / dbyug zla'i nang lha bzo zla 'od nas ngor thar rtser gur/ zhal/ lha
mo stag zhon rnams dang / rje dpal ldan chos skyong gi dgongs rdzogs rten rnams bskrun par bkas mngags shing / gzungs 'dod gsol sogs cha rkyen bcas legs par gdams/ de nas
zhu dbon dang sde dge'i hor 'dra bcas la spyan gzigs gtso 'khor gsum gyi rjes gnang dang / lung phon che ba bcas stsal zhing / mkhas dbang zhe drung la 'thon phyag thog
rig gnas skor las 'phros pa'i bka' stsal zhing / rgyas mdzad pas khong dgyes dgur son cing gnang cha'ang gya nom pa stob par mdzad/ smin zla'i nang rje nyid dang zham 'bring
pa chen po gzim 'od bcas nas/ sdom gsum kha skong bdud rtsi nying khu/ gdung rabs gsol 'debs zhal skong bcas dang / phun tshogs dge legs ma/ gtor ma brgya rtsa/ dkar
cha bzhi/ de dag gi gsal byed bcas ljags zhus dag par mdzad de chos sbyin mi zad par du bskrun pa'i bka' 'doms dang / tshes bcu dgur mdo pha sgar dang chu 'bum bla ma gnyis
kyi 'bul bzhes la tshogs dbur phebs shing / 'dis mtshon snga phyi kun tu 'bul bzhes tshogs phebs mdzad pa mang ngo / /de dag gi don bsdu na/ las ngan smin pa'i nad gdon
mu ge'i gzugs/ /rmeg med nus mthu'i rdo rje'i thog ser gyis/ /tshar bcad rjes 'dzin dam pa'i snying stobs phul/ /phyogs bcu'i rgyal ba'i thugs rje las kyang brgal/ /gnyis
med rgyud rgyal 'jing du 'jam pa'i dpal/ /gzhon nu'i ded dpon zhugs la rten 'brel gyi/ /las dbang mthun rlung mtha' yul nas g.yos te/ /dag snang lung bstan nor bu'i
khyu tshogs rnyed/ /dpag tshad phyogs nas phan tshun 'dod 'jo'i dpal/ /bsam 'phel

dbang rgyal thar pa'i ba gam rtser/ /mchod cing zab rgyas chos char g.yar lam du/ /mi zad par gyi 'phrul 'khor bla med bskor/ /zhes kyang smras so// // ! dgung grangs zhe lngar
phebs pa chu sprul lor sku 'phrang shin tu 'tshubs pa yod thog /bod lo gsar ba nas bzung lo gang phyir phebs spangs te/ sku tshe'i cho ga tshugs 'phral zhig tu/ ze'u
lha khang 'dra mo zhig nas tshe dpag med kyi sku che chung sna tshogs shig rnyed pa 'khrungs pa dang mnyam du/ 'jam mgon dbang gi mtshan can gang la'ang gtsug tor rnam rgyal
gyi sku zhig dang / yang rgyal zla'i nang zhig sku par mang po zhig gi khrod nas tshe dpag med kyi sku par gsal ba rnams rnyed pa 'khrungs pa ni/ sku tshe'i 'phrang
las grol nas bstan 'gro'i dpal mgon du yun ring 'tsho zhing gzhes pa'i brdar nem nur dang bral/ yang dbo zla'i tshes gcig tho rangs gangs ri chen po'i khrod nas/ 'bras dkar
khal du ma zhig rnyed pa gnang mur/ lho rong gi lam yin dgongs pa zhig shar ba ni/ de dus bstan gsol gnang mu yin pa bzhin jo bo lha ri'i cho 'phrul zhig yin 'dra gsungs/
de nas bzung rgyun ring bar ljongs 'dis mtshon 'dzam gling snod bcud spyi dang / bye brag bstan 'dzin skyes chen dam pa rnams zhabs pad brtan phyir bstan srung rgya mtshor
phrin 'chol dang / de dag dbang dang gzi 'bar du bskyed de lha bsangs/ bstan gsol/ 'go lha/ dgra lha/ sde brgyad cha snyoms bcas chag med mdzad skabs shig /rgyal tshab
mchog nas mgon khang rnams su phrin gsol snyan shal sogs stsal ba bzhin rje nyid kyis thugs smon dang bcas ji bzhin bka' yis 'doms/ yang tshes gnyis kyi tho rengs chos
lhun dbu byed byams pa yin snyam pa zhig nas/ byams pa mched lnga'i ya gyal chos lhun byams sku'i lo rgyus

rje rdo rje 'chang la zhu mur/ rab gnas dus byams pa dge slong rnam pas lhung bzed chus gang ba bsnams pa zhig thim zer ba dang / shog dril lo rgyus kyi yi ge yod pa zhig na/
de dus mar pa mi la zhal gzigs/ brgyud pa'i rtsa ba sa ra ha/ te lo pa rnams kyang gzigs shing / /khyad par 'gro mgon 'chi bdag gi 'jigs pa las thar zer ba zhig 'khrungs
pa ni/ zhe lnga'i sku 'phrang 'tshubs ma las grol zhing / sku zhi bar thim dus kyi lung bstan zhib gsal du gor ma chag /de lo rgyal tshab de mo rin po che ngag dbang 'jam
dpal bde legs rgya mtshos/ zan yangs mi 'gyur lhun gyis grub pa'i gandho la chen por zhig gsos kyis mtshon/ spyi sgos bstan 'gro'i bde thabs la ched du dgongs pa'i rim
gro'i thebs su dngos 'byor gya nom pa stsal ba bzhin/ chos dung rin po che gsung bskul gyis mtshon/ mdzad sgo kun gang 'tshams ye shes gzigs pas gnad smin gnang / sa zla'i
nang dgongs nyul zhig rje nyid thugs dam la bzhugs mur/ rgyu mtshan med par sku shin tu nyog nyams kyis thugs snang nub pa lta bu 'khrungs 'phral/ gzhung zhabs nas bsam
yas sku rten skor gyi chibs zam 'byor bas/ dam sel sbyong thabs sogs rim gro rnams gab sbas med par stsal/ snron zla'i mdo sde lha mchod thog sku rten phrin las sam/ skal
ldan 'os shar su zhig la zhal gzigs kyang dam bsgrag phrin 'chol sogs mdzad dgos kyi gsung mchid rgyal tshab mchog tu zhib lhongs dang / rje nyid nas kyang gzhi thog
rtser lha bsangs rgyas pa stsal rgyu'i tho rangs/ thugs nyams dang 'od gsal 'dres pa'i mur/ ban de gzugs bzang gzi brjid can zhig kha btags thogs nas gleng mo byed la khad
yal ba zhig 'khrungs pa ni/ dam ldan pu tra dmar

po nyid kyis phrin las g.yel ba med pa'i brda dang / chu stod tshes bcu nas nyin gsum ring snod bcud spyi dang / bye brag 'dzam gling / yang sgos bod/ nying sgos dpal sa skya'i
gdan sa ma lag kun gyi bcud 'phel phyir/ phywa phrin nor bu'i mchog rgyal sde dge zhu chen rin po che'i gsung rab bzhin rje nyid kyis gnad nyin kho nar/ sde dge nas
gsung shog 'phral rdzong 'byor rten/ gser srang lnga/ dngul bre chen/ gos yug sogs dang / khyad par rdor dril/ DA ma ru/ ting shags/ bodhi tsitta'i phreng ba sogs kyi zhar
la/ gzhan yang gser dngul dar gos sogs mang tsam bcas tshang ma phywa rten gras su phyag rtags 'byar ba dang / bcu gcig chad pa'i bcu gsum nyin phywa sgo dbye ba'i skabs/
'jam mgon sku mched yum mchog bcas la phyA rdzas bstar zhing / zhal 'don gyi tshe rgyu mtshan med par rje nyid kyi snyan khung du chos dung dkar po rgyang grags kyi gsung
rgyun ma chad par gsan cing / phywa 'gugs grub nas gong gi sde dge'i rten rnams rgya bkrol nas dmar po skor gsum gyi sngags bzla bar mdzad de/ rdo dril DA' ru'i gsung
bskul zhing / phreng ba ni byang dar dmar pos gril nas 'dug pa rten 'brel shin tu legs par stsal/ bco lnga'i tho rengs/ khyad 'phags bla ma lha khang gi ring bsrel las ring
bsrel gyis char babs 'khrungs pa dang / bco brgyad tho rengs nang g.yab 'khor gos yol can na mi mang po bdud rtsi ril bu sgril bar/ nyi ma zhud la khad shar pas/ de nyin
'brug chos 'khor bsod nams pho brang gi nang rten rnams la ring bsrel gtso gyur gyis gzungs gzhug dgos tshul gsung ba bzhin/ de lta'i lo rgyus dang bcas stsol bar mdzad
pa'ang ring min nas 'brug phyogs su me skyon gyis rten mang po dmigs med du song ba sogs

dus gsum sgrib med du gzigs pa zer ba de 'di 'dra'i rigs la gsung ngam snyam/ gzhan yang zla nang der sa ngor sde gsum gyi sku gegs sel phyir chos srung rgya mtshor phrin 'chol
la thugs gzhol ba dang / gong gi gser khri rin po che'i shing brkos yongs rdzogs grub nas/ sngon thub pa'i dbang pos chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba'i dus chen gyi zla ba'i
nyer drug sngon mas nang 'phrad thog /rje nyid kyi dbu skyes kyi phon po gsar bar bskrun skabs/ rdor brag padma phrin las kyi rnam thar kha ba ljags klog mur tshogs kyi
'khor lo'i dga' ston la longs spyad do gsung ba dang mdzod 'dzin nas spyad bdar phul ba dus 'grig cing / 'o 'thud kyang bzhes mu dang / glo bur char zim wa chu 'thon tsam
nyil nas/ /de 'phral nyi 'od gsal ba sogs rten 'brel dge ba'i mtshan ma gnyis pa dang / lo de'i gro bzhin phur sgrub rje rdo rje 'chang nyid dang / 'jam mgon dbang gi
mtshan can 'di nyid/ da lta'i mkhan rin po che sbyin pa bkra shis dang gsum zhal rgyas te/ gnas bcu lha khang du phur cha sogs khyad byang nas bzhes te mdzad/ rgyun gyi phur
cha rnams la nyams gso rtsi gsol yang legs par gnang / ma 'gyangs par a li chos rje dpon g.yog rnams 'byor zhing / gdan sa nas phebs mi bla ma nas gsung brtag zhu rgyu'i
tho rengs 'od gsal du/ a li chos rje'i bla ma rnams la rje nyid nas dung zhig gnang rgyu yin dgongs te/ dung dngul gshog la skyon cung zad yod pa zhig gzhi thog pho brang
gi rtse nas rje nyid kyis 'bud par mdzad pas/ de'i skad kyis sa skya'i lung pa thams cad gang ba dang / kun dga' sangs rgyas kyi yin zer ba'i mchod me shin tu gsal ba
zhig mchis par/ gzhan gyis gnod pa byed 'dug pas rje nyid nas legs par bcos gnang gis slar gsal po yong ba yod dgongs pa 'khrungs pa'i 'bras bu'ang da gzod mngon du

gyur cing / dbyug zla'i tshes bcur a li bla ma sbyin bdag ngo g.yog rnams la gsung gsang 'di ltar grol te/ a li chos rje sbyin bdag bcas rnams rang gzhan gnas skabs mthar thug
phan bder bsam ste/ sde snod bshad grwa bzang po'i rgyun rje btsun sa skya pa'i bzhed pa dang mthun par 'dzugs 'dun gyis 'di nas bla ma dgos tshul byung ba bzhin gyi
re 'bras don smin spyi sgos bstan pa rin po cher bya ba lhag par yang byas pa 'di ni/ rang cag rnams kyis rnyed pa'i mchog legs par rnyed pa sogs/ sngon gyi rgyal blon lo
paN byang sems rnams dang / rje btsun sa skya pa'i gong ma'i bzhed srol dang mthun pa'i legs byas ngo mtshar rgya mtsho yin 'dug pas/ bla slob sbyin bdag kun la rjes su
yi rang zhing / gong ma bdag po chen po/ skyabs mgon rgyal ba yab sras kyi mtshan don la phan nges kyi bya ba yin 'dug pas dga' spro rgya cher mdzod/ ces gsung gis dbugs
dbyung bar mdzad do/ /smin zla'i nyer lngar lha chen gser khri rin po che gsar bskrun gyi zhal dro mgo zla'i tshes bzhir yin tshul gyi brda 'grems mdzad rgyu'i snga dro/
rgyal tshab mchog nas bsam yas sku rten pa 'phral rdzongs gnang ba'i snga dron gyi gsung shog /dngul gyi maNDal/ sa snying srang / lha gos sogs gser khri rin po cher dge
ba'i la nyi gsum par 'khums/ mgo zla'i tshes bzhi'i shar mda' btang tsam la rje rdo rje 'chang nyid kyi thugs bskyed phrin las kyis/ gcig tu na lha chen sprul pa'i gandho
la chen po mdzes pa'i rgyan gcig gser khri rin po che gsar bkod bsgrig rgyu'i do dam du mdzod 'dzin par bkas mdags pa bzhin legs par bsgrigs 'phral/ dung mkhan gyis chos
dung rin po che gsung bskur dang bstun/ lha khang chen mo'i gser gyi rgyal mtshan rnams la nyi ma shar ba'i

'od zer 'phro ba dang mnyam du/ gang na thod dang skra gsar dang / /gar dang rol mo'i sgra yod pa/ /zhes dga' ston gyi ngang tshul bzang po dang ldan pa'i kong gzhas pa rnams
kyis sngun bsus/ a li dpon g.yog /spu nag bla gnyer/ stod tshong dar rgyas sogs 'bul sdud pa rnams dang / phye mar gyis bkang ba'i dngul gzhong gsum khyer mi/ rgya gling
pa/ mgron gnyer/ spos phor pa/ sbyong chas/ gtor theb gsum du mtheb kyu kha phyir bstan sum cu brtsegs steng gyen bstan sum sgrom/ gcig la lhag gcig bcas brgya tshar/
snod 'brus bkang steng rigs lnga'i rtse phran dar dpyangs bcas gsum bkod mthar/ dngul grub bkra shis rdzas brgyad/ rgyal srid sna bdun/ tsakli tshar re thogs pa'i phan tshang
gsum/ dngul bum rdzas ldan mgul ching kha rgyan can thogs pa yang gsum/ mdo sngags rig gnas dang bcas pa'i dpe tshan gnad bsdus khyer mi gsum/ dam pa gong ma'i phyag
cha dril smyon du grags pa che chung / klu dbang gi phyag dril/ thod DAM/ 'thor nas/ ka pA la bdud rtsi ting shags bcas yod pa'i phan tshang gsum/ snam sbyar phrag par gzar
zhing lhung bzed spyi blugs thogs pa gcig /gsol dpon/ spos sna ba/ yum mchog sogs zhal ngo byings phyag 'degs bcas dang / de nas skyabs mchog 'jig rten gyi sgron me nges
don gyi rdo rje 'dzin nyid sku 'khor rnams dang bcas/ bcom ldan 'das nyan thos kyi dge 'dun dang bcas pa chos 'khor la 'du ba bzhin cha lugs dang spyod lam bzang zhing
dul ba'i sgo nas phebs shing / sprul pa'i gandho la chen po'i khyams stod du sbyong khrus/ bgegs skrod sogs dang / de nas rje rdo rje 'dzin nyid kyis/ oM na mo bhrUM a
yurdznyAn hrIHa ro lika hU~M hrIH zhes ma 'ongs srid mtha'i bar du 'byon 'gyur

dang bcas pa'i gdung brgyud rin po che gser khri 'dir mnga' gsol ji snyed kyi sku tshe bde ldan mgon po'i ngo bor byin gyis rlabs te/ 'bru dkar gyi char nyil bzhin par rtag
brtan gzhom bral gyi khri 'phangs su/ skyabs mchog yab sras rnam gsum sku gsung thugs lham me/ lhang nge / lhan ner bzhugs grub pa dang dbu mdzad che bas/ 'phags pa dkon
mchog gsum la phyag 'tshal lo/ /zhes pa nas/ mjug bkra shis kyi bar rim bzhin bskul zhing / spyi sgos nas mang ja bsnyen bkur 'bul cha sogs gzabs pa'i thog /dngos 'bul dngul
thog tu phab pa bsdoms dngul srang lnga stong sum brgya dang bzhi/ zho phyed bdun du longs pa bcas mdor na/ de nyin srid zhi'i dpal 'byor yod dgu cog sprul pa'i mchod
sdong chen po'i gser khri rin po che ngo mtshar gsar du bzhad pa'i drung du/ ma 'ongs srid mtha'i bar gyi rten 'brel gyi legs lam bzang po dang bcas 'phos pas/ bde skyid
rdzogs ldan gzhon nu'i dga' ston la longs spyod pa'i skabs so/ /de dag gi don bsdu na/ sku tshe'i ka ba tshugs pa'i gzhal med khang / /bstan dang de 'dzi dar ba'i dkyil
'khor ngom/ /mkhan slob chos gsum phrin las gandho la/ /dge mtshan bzhad pa'i blang dor g.yang du khug /sangs rgyas rnam sprul dgra bcom gnas brtan che/ /ngal 'tsho'i gnas
su dpal chen he ru kas/ /chos kyi dung gi sgra chen bsgrags pa'i mgron/ /don mthun gsung gsang rna ba stong gis nyan/ /a ho sngon med bcu gsum rdo rje'i sa'i/ /khri 'phangs
mthon por zhabs zung bkod do zhes/ /dkar phyogs lha srung dgyes pa'i mtshan ma 'bum/ /lhun grub rgyun mi chad pa'i drin can rje/ /zhes kyang smras so// // ! dgung grangs
zhe drug du phebs pa

shing rta lo 'gro mgon bstan pa sangs rgyas dang / /rje nyid kyi zham 'bring pa chen po bsod nams 'od zer gnyis 'das pas/ so so'i rjes sgrub gu ru rin po che dang 'jam dbyangs
sogs kyi zhal bkod sogs 'char 'phar gyi bstan mkhas mdzad sgo rnams la thugs gzhol ba'i mur/ gro bzhin tshes lnga'i tho rengs 'od gsal du/ sde dge mkhan chen shar chen
zhabs drung 'khor bcas la phag mo zhal gnyis ma'i byin rlabs phul zhing / de'i sku snang la rang bzhin med pa zil chen zhig gzigs pa'i mod du dar gcig mnyam gzhag la 'byams
par gyur/ de nas gzhan yang chos bka' 'dra 'bul rgyu yin dgongs pa zhig 'khrungs so/ /zla nang der 'brug sde srid rnying pa bsod lhun bod la bros te rgyal rtser mchis
dus/ dam pa'i rang bzhin 'gog med kyi gzigs pas gnang cha gya nom pa stsal bas/ khong pa shin tu mgu zhing slad nas zhabs 'gyur yang dag zhu rgyu'i tha tshig phul zhing
/ 'di 'dra'i rigs kyi thugs bskyed gzhan yang mang du mchis pa'ang 'dis mtshon nus so/ /khrums zla'i tshes gsum tho rengs zhal dkar ngag dbang lags rig 'dzin pho brang na
thugs dam gnang mur/ mnal du song ba'i rmang lam du/ rje rdo rje 'dzin nyid 'grul la phebs zer rgya gling btang byung ba'i mod gzigs pas/ rje rdo rje 'chang nyid ma gzigs
par thugs skyo lhang byung mur/ de ma thag rje nyid kyi gsung las/ bstan ma khyod ni mya ngan ma byed cig /nga ni da dung 'bum tsam 'tsho bar 'gyur/ /gsung ba zhig gsan
cing / /dbyug zla'i bcu bzhi sa chen yab sras gnyis ka'i dus chen dngos dang / gzhan yang tshes mchod bzung ba sogs kyi dbang du byas na/ chos rje sa paN/ rong ston thams
cad mkhyen pa/ sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po rnams kyi'ang dus chen nyin/

gdan sa chen po'i dri gtsang khang rnams su sna lnga'i stong mchod/ lha chen 'dus tshogs su bsnyen bkur gya nom pa'i thog rgyal bstan rin po che spyi bye brag dar brtan gyi
thugs smon dang chabs gcig /sngon du mdo smad sa skyong blo gros rgyal mtshan yab sras la chos sbyin mi zad par gyi 'phrul 'khor bkas dbang bskur ba bzhin phyag thog tu
son te/ phur pa bla ma'i 'bul skyel gdong / bod kyi rdo rje gdan dpal ldan sa skyar phebs pa bzhin/ de nyin rig gter gsal byed/ phar phyin bka' 'grel/ sdom gsum kha skong
/ bdud rtsi nying khu sogs kyi bar phud 'dus tshogs su stsal/ mgo zla'i nyer drug chad pa'i nyer lnga gza' tshes dge bar rje rdo rje 'dzin nyid kyi thugs bskyed rlabs po
ches dpal sa skyar dpal ldan chos kyi grags pas mdzad pa'i rgyas pa'i bstan bcos tshad ma rnam 'grel gzhung skyor tshes mchod thog mar tshugs skabs/ ma bsgrigs rang 'grig
gi ngo mtshar du/ /or du su dza sag pas se tA las tshe chen tsho thur bkra shis tshe ring gi gsung bris rten gos dar dngul sogs spam mtho ba dang / de sras thA ji mgon
po rdo rje byon pas dngul gyi maNDal/ dngul bre chen mang ba/ zhang po me rin bde mchog gis kyang de bzhin bcas 'byor pa sogs gzhung skyor gyi la nye bzang zhing / de nyid
rje rdo rje 'chang yab sras nas gnas bcu lha khang rten drung mchod tshogs gzabs pa'i dbus su gong gi maNDal sne 'dogs bcas bshams nas/ rnam 'grel gzhung skyor thugs bsam
rnam dag gis bskrun pa 'di/ rgyal ba bu ram shing pa'i bstan pa'i gsal byed dam par gyur nas/ skye dgu kun la 'phral yun phan bde rgya cher 'byung ba zhig bla ma yi dam
sangs rgyas byang sems rnams la gsol 'debs dang thugs smon 'phags pa kun tu bzang po'i rjes

su 'gro ba stsal zhing / gzhan yang sku tshe de nyid du rnam 'grel tshogs dbur phebs bzhed thun mong ma yin pa'i sgo nas/ gzhung yang ha lam thugs kyi bang mdzod du zhugs par
gyur kyang nag phyogs mthu bdo ba'i dbang gis phyag tu son par ma gyur to/ /de dag gi don bsdu na/ byas shes drin gzo'i mkhyen rab dwangs pa'i mkhar/ /rig stong gling
bus bsus pa'i chu 'dzin las/ /chos sbyin rgyas pa'i bstan bcos tshad ma'i gzhung / /ji srid rgyun mi chad pa'i char zim nyil/ /zhes kyang smras so// // ! dgung grangs zhe
bdun du phebs pa shing lug rgyal zla nas bzung / 'jam mgon sku mched la zab rgyas chos bka' rgya cher gnang rgyu'i tho rengs 'od gsal du/ gser chos glegs bam ngo mtshar
can bka' 'gyur gras yin dgongs pa zhig /dge 'dun gyi sde'i dbus na bzhugs pa'i phyed tsam na shog rtags shig 'dug pas/ 'di yan sngar phul zin/ 'di nas da 'bul dgos yod dgongs
pa zhig 'khrungs pa ni/ da gzod brtags tshe lkog gyur rjen gsal lag mthil du skyu ru ra bzhag pa bzhin du go /'das lo'i 'phros dang de lo gsar 'phral rnams su gzhung
zhabs nas chibs zam yang yang gis rgyal tshab mchog sku cung zad ltem pa'i rim gro spyi dang / bye brag bskang phrin gnad smin sogs mdzad cing / de nas rim bzhin zhi ba
lhar phyag dpe phon chen dgos tshul/ bsam yas mkhan po sogs kyi skor bse 'bag 'dra ba zhes thog mtha' bar gsum/ gur gar sogs ji gsung gi thugs brel rnams dang / dbo zla'i
bcu bzhi'i tho rengs/ sku rim chen mo'i zor las pa rin chen yar 'phel gyis/ mchod zhing bya khra ma'i lam dang mnyam pa'i ltas ngan sems can ring mo zhig dum bur gtubs pa
dang / yang mi zhig gi'aphros las/ rin chen yar 'phel nas sa

skya par rbod gtong byed mi de bsad tshar bas khrag sku gnyer khang du 'thung na dmar dri yong 'dug pas/ mgon khang du khrag rdza chung gang 'thungs pa yin zer/ kha dmar dri
chil le slebs byung zer ba zhig 'khrungs par/ bka' las/ 'di ni nges par bsad rtags tshad ldan rang yin 'dra bas/ dam can pu tra nyid kyis gnod byed zhig bsgral lam snyam/
zhes gsungs/ nag zla'i nang sde dger bzang ngan blang dor gyi lhas ched du bzung gnang gi tho rengs/ gsang 'dus mi bskyod pa'i rdul dkyil gzabs bris thog nas gzhan zhig
la dbang bskur mdzad rgyu yin dgongs pa dang / gzhan nas dkyil 'khor de drung du tshe brtan gyis mtshon/ 'brel thogs la bsngo ba zhu dgos zer ba zhig 'khrungs pas/ bka'
las/ dkyil 'khor gzabs bris de ni dge ba'i mtshan ma dang / bsngo ba zhu dgos zer ba cung zad 'tshubs nyams bcas rim gros khyor na skyon cher med/ de las gzhan du gyur na
de bzhin 'byung ngo yin 'dra/ zhes gsungs te/ gtsug lag khang rnams su mchod 'bul rgya che thugs smon gyi mtshams sbyor dang bcas pa/ sbyin sreg spel tshig la sde bzhi
dge bcu 'dzom pa'i snod bcud gtso phal la sngon las 'phral rkyen las gyur pa'i byur dang skal ba ngan pa bkra mi shis pa'i nad gdon nyer 'tshe thams cad shAntiM ku ru swA
hA/ zhes sbyor bar mdzad/ tshes brgyad kyi nyin sde dge rgyal sras dam pas mtshon gang ci'i legs spel rten 'brel sgo brgya dbye phyir/ sku gsung thugs rten gyis mtshon dngos
'bul gya nom pa dang / dus gsum phyi nang gsang ba'i bka' tshig gsung shog tu 'khod pa dang / sku tshab ngag lam nas kyang 'bul rgyu bcas/ mgron dpal ched mngags kyis
mdo smad phyogs la 'thon/ gzhan

yang de lo phyi lo sogs la sde dge'i chos srid dar brtan 'byung phyir/ lha bsangs/ sme brtsegs/ de'i grib glud/ brgya bzhi/ phywa phrin/ tshogs bdag /kye rdor las bzhi'i sbyin
sreg /mgon khang rnams su bskang phrin/ phur bzlog /drug cu pa/ mchod 'bul/ gsung sgrogs sogs nar mar mdzad cing / gzhan yang sa ngor sde gsum gyi sku rim du bdun phrag
gcig ring / kye rdor bdag mdun gtor bsngo bskang ba bcas gnad smin du mdzad pa'i tshe/ tho rengs shig /sdig pa rwa can khru gang tsam zhig rje nyid nas bsgral bas/ de'i
khog na glo snying nang cha thams cad dmar myog ge gzigs shing / shi ba'i ro de'i rwa dang rkang lag rnams kyis nyid kyi zhabs phyi zhig la 'thams nyams 'khrungs shing
/ / ! yang mgon mdos shig mdzad pa'i tshe 'od gsal du/ si tu karma chos 'byung dpon g.yog dang mjal bas/ rje nyid ni grub mtha' ris med kyi mkhas grub la dad pa dag snang
rgyun du bcos min bsgoms pa'i bag chags kyis/ gsung gleng sna tshogs dang / khyad par rig gnas skor gsan yul sogs dri ba mdzad pa'i lan gsung skabs/ khong gsung 'gag sku
drang por bzhugs mi thub pa'i mur shangs g.yas nas khrag dmar nyor gyis byung bar/ khong gi zhabs phyi rnams kha skyengs nyams dang / gzhan zhig nas 'di dam sel rtags yin
'dug zer bar/ rje nyid nas de ma thag khong la phan re'i oM e ho shud dhe sogs 'don par mdzad pa 'khrungs pas/ bla ma 'di la gzhis byes kun kha gtong ba de bden pa e yin/
zhes gsungs pa sogs dngos su lta ci/ mnal lam gyi tshul du'ang rje des byang chub kyi sems dang 'bral bar ma mdzad lags/ de nas chu stod nyer drug la/ gong mi khyi tsam
la rje nyid kyis bstan lar gcig tu dgongs te/

gnyal gyi rdo mon pa thang gi mgon khang na 'phags pa klu sgrub kyi phyag bzo ma gur mgon gyi 'chams sku sumbha nag por grags pa mal los rgya gar nas gdan drangs zer ba de
yod min rgyal tshab de mo gong mar rtsad gcod gnang dgos zhu don bzhin dang bzhes kyis/ gri gu rdzong dpon mer mo nas la rtsad gcod zhib dgos bka' stsal ltar/ des kyang shin
tu zhib bris gnas tshul zhabs pad du phul ba ngo ma gdan sar stsal ba las/ sngar yod dus zhing bskor re la gdan 'dren zhu srol gyis/ skabs shig nyin mos rub pa sogs 'tshubs
'gyur chen po byung skad dang / de nas mgon khang rdib gzhom gyis/ sa 'og tu shor nas ma 'thon/ zhes dran pa lung pa de na rgan mo zhig las gzhan med tshul der yod
rnams kyis smras pas/ slar khungs rdol min la gan rgya 'jog nus sam dris pas nus zer nas bzhag song zer ba phul yang / phyis su khungs rdol te 'chams sku gsang sngags dga'
tshal du phyag 'byor gyis/ 'dra bzhes gnyis pa sa skyar shing lug chu stod zla nang gsang sngags dga' tshal gyi lha bzo ba zhi ba bzang po'i gdong stsal bzhin/ brtse chen
na lha khang du gdan 'dren nyer brgyad la gnang ba'i nyer dgu'i tho rengs/ zur 'chad grub dbang rje drung lags nas rje nyid la/ mang thos klu sgrub rgya mtsho'i gsung
'bum nang gi mgon po'i rjes gnang de gnang dgos zhu bar/ de 'dra zhig yod dgongs dbang khang du gnang song bas/ mngon rtogs ni dkyus ma dang / sngon 'gro'i gsung bshad la
'phags pa klu sgrub kyis rgyud las btus nas 'di mdzad/ man ngag rnams rje rdo rje 'chang dang mgon po dngos la gsan/ de nas bram ze mchog sred nas brgyud rje btsun sa skya
par bka' babs/ spyir mgon po 'di la rjes gnang dang dbang bka' kha shas yod pa las/ 'di gur mgon khro bcu'i gtso bo de'i rjes gnang yin

gsung ba zhig 'khrungs pas/ thugs la sngar rjes gnang de 'dra gsan pa dang mdzad pa ni ma dran/ klu sgrub bka' 'bum na'ang yod med ma shes/ gang ltar 'chams sku gsang phebs
'di'i cho 'phrul zhig ni nges par yin 'dug pas/ bzang ngan dpyod dka' mo zhig 'dra zhes gsungs/ klu sgrub bka' 'bum na mgon po'i rjes gnang gi zin bris shig ni mchis lags
so/ /de lo gro bzhin phur sgrub la 'jam mgon e waM bzang po 'di nyid thog mar phebs rgyu dang / sri gnon ljags bsgrigs ma'ang thog mar gnam gang nyin mdzad rgyu bcas/ gdan
sa'i rtsis pa rnams dang skye re ba sogs nas de'i bco lngar zla 'dzin dang / de nas gnam gang la'ang nyi 'dzin yod par thag bcad kyang gtan ma byung ba ni/ sngon dus
rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan dang / 'dul 'dzin kha che paN chen gyi lo rgyus ltar/ rje nyid kyis thog ma'i rten 'brel de dag la gnod par dogs nas nang gi gnad
kyi rgyu ba 'gog par mdzad pa ni gor ma chag cing / de lta bu'i sri gnon de ban tshang bas mdzad pa'i rgyu mtshan yang / sngar 'brug lo 'jam mgon dbang sdud snying po
'di nyid phur sgrub la thog mar phebs skabs/ drug pa'i mjug nas bdun pa'i 'go zhag shas par kun rdzob ltar snang dang bstun rje rdo rje 'chang nyid glo bur thor pa 'dra ba
zhig gis snyun tshul bzhes pas/ de lta'i sri ngan bzlog phyir mdzad pas rten 'brel yang legs te/ sri gnon las sbyor dngos mdzad dus mi gzabs 'chor can glo bur der lhags
shing / 'byung ba rim brtsegs rnams kyang rdo rje slob dpon des rnam 'gyur 'thon pos gzhan las rngams zil che ba dang mnan grub ma thag /lho phyogs nas 'brug skad snyan
pa tshar gcig bsgrags shing / sgrub khang du 'byon skabs rgyal sgo nas btsun chung zhig me tog kha gsar spar gang thogs te khyams stod

phyogs la shar gyis song ba dang / zim char gyis sa gzhi brlan pa sogs mtshan ma bzang la zhal dro ba zhig mchis pas/ slan chad kyang dgongs par 'khyil dgos pa'i gras dang
/ phur sgrub gegs med du grub nas khrums zla'i nang tsha rong ba'i sras gzhon nu lo bcur byon pa sman lha phun tshogs pas/ rgyud bzhi rgyug 'bul gyi shog grangs sum brgyar
nye ba rje nyid nas bzhes pa bcas/ dus phyis mkhyen rab kyi dper 'os pa lta bu dang / bsam brling gtang rag gi zhar la mchod zhing gsar pa bde legs dpal 'phel la shis brjod
me tog gi char snyil nas phebs rjes su/ chags lug rnams yong ba dang / rdo gcal na'ang ngor klu sdings dpon gnyer nas tshe thar du phul ba'i lugs rnams kyang mchis bas/
rje dges pa'i gsung las/ g.yang dkar phyi nas yong ba dang nang na'ang slebs pa bcas lo legs yod/ zhes gsungs/ de nas kha'ur sman chab la phebs pa'i yar lam skyed lhas
gsung bskang thog /ngor pa bsam pa phyin ci log 'chang ba 'ga' zhig gis yi ger bkod pa'i tshig gnad ngan pa rnar nyan mi 'os pa zer mkhan de'i bsam pa bzang por skye ba'i
phrin 'chol mdzad/ smin zla'i nang ching wang gi mi sna bod pa em ji sog por song ba sogs dang / sde dge nas dkar lu dpon g.yog dang / a mdo ba mang tsam bcas la gang
'tshams bdag rkyen dang / mgo zla'i nang mtsho sngon dza sag dga' ldan erkhe dA ching la'ang tshe dbang sogs lugs zung gis skyong bar mdzad cing / de lo tshe chog ji song
bsdoms par mdzad pas tshe chog ngo grangs chig stong bzhi brgya dang gcig /gzungs ring sum 'bum/ drug stong / chig brgya nga gsum/ snying po nye snying so so nas bzhi 'bum/
lnga khri/ nyis stong / nyis brgya zhe gnyis/ rigs lnga'i sngags bzhi khri nyis

stong bcu gcig /las sngags chig 'bum/ drug khri/ brgyad stong / chig brgya go gcig bcas 'brug sbrul rta lug gi khongs song bar gyur to/ /de dag gi don bsdu na/ rin dang warNa'i
brdas bstan 'byung gyur gtam/ /bod dang bod chen bdag po'i re 'bras rdzogs/ /'od gsal ngang du 'chol sngags byams snying gi /mtshon chas mi dge'i sems can bsgral zhes
sgrogs/ /thabs dang shes rab e waM zung 'jug sgo /rten 'brel bzang po'i gnad kyi lag pa yis/ /phye ba'i grogs su 'tsho byed gzhon nu yang / /phyi nang gsang ba'i g.yang
dkar drangs te lhags/ /las ngan mun par 'khyams pa'i bsam ngan sdig /me 'bar khrod du sbyangs nas ring po'i mgron/ /lugs zung snang bas ngoms mdzad drin can rje/ /'od mtha'
yas pa'i dpal 'byor bdag de'o/ /zhes kyang smras so// // ! dgung grangs zhe brgyad du phebs pa me sprel rgyal zla'i tshes lngar lcang skya rdo rje 'chang gi sku mdun
pa mdung nag zhabs drung 'byor rgyu'i tho rengs/ rje rdo rje 'chang nyid dbang khang na gnas gsar rdo rje 'chang la bka' chos zhu mur/ mangga la ku Ta'i sgra sgrub dang bcas
gsung bshad rgyas po zhig mdzad pa 'khrungs pas/ de'i don ni bkra shis brtsegs pa zhes bya ba yin no/ /chos drug pa she 'grub sbyor nyin gzim chung gtor spod skabs/ gong
gi rigs sras dam pa 'jam mgon gzhon nur gyur pa nas/ da nangs bka' bzhi thugs su chub pas da dpe 'dzin ji 'dra yong bka' stsal bar bskul bas/ thugs rje che/ da ltar rang
gsal zhig 'bul dgos gsungs shing / thugs la glo bur du spre'u lo'i dbyar chos la gsung bshad gnang / de nas gser 'phyang mchu zla'i nang gzhan yang

yong 'dra dgongs pa'i thugs spro dang bcas/ gtsug tor rnam rgyal gyi sgom bzlas grub ma thag lha'i nga rgyal brtan pos yab sras yum bcas nas gzabs bzhes dang bcas/ sku gsung
thugs rten/ bzang dgu 'dzom pa'i spro zas/ mgul dar sogs stobs par sku yon khang du phebs lam 'char can dang 'gyed grabs bsham skya 'khyil dang / rtser lha bsangs grol
ba'i lha rgyal/ mdung dar khra rog ge yod pa sogs rten 'brel bzang po dang bcas rgyal sras lam bzang stsal te thugs 'dzin gnang shig par shis brjod kyi me tog dang bcas phul/
de'i tshe mdzod 'dzin la gong gi gnas tshul rnams dang / lhag par bstan don gal che'i skor phyag bris thog nas gnang ba'i bka' grol/ mdung nag zhabs drung dge bshes
bcos med nas maNDal gos dar sogs dngos po bzang dgu du ma dang / lhag par lcang skya rdo rje 'chang nas gsung shog gnang rten bzang pos sba ba'i gsung tshig tu/ thub bstan
gsal bar byed pa'i sgron me dpal ldan sa skya paNDi ta zhes snyan par grags pa gang de'i zhabs drung du/ zhes dang / bkra shis kyis mtshan pa'i dus kyi char yang / 'gro
ba yongs kyi dpal rmad du byung ba gzugs sku'i dkyil 'khor dwangs shing / mdzad khyab bzang po 'gran bral gyi ring nas/ zhes sogs kyi tshig sgra sogs che 'don mdzad rgyu'i
thog ma'i dge ltas dang / zhabs drung der ngor lugs rig byed thun mong ma yin pa'i rjes gnang dang sbyin sreg yig lung / ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub dang / rje nyid
kyi ljags rtsom rig byed ma'i sgrub thabs rjes gnang lung / byin rten sogs re ba'i yol gong bkang zhing / de'i zhabs gras bu mo lo bcu gcig ma de bro 'tshal bar rje nyid
nas bka' bsgo stsal

'phral nad las grol bas/ khong rnams dad gus che ba las kyang lhag par che bar gyur te/ sngon gyi mkhas pas/ chos dam tshig gtsang na dngos grub myur/ /zhes 'brel tshad don
ldan de nyid kyi byin rlabs kun la 'jug kyang / dad pa med pa'i mi rnams la/ /dkar po'i chos rnams mi skye ste/ /sa bon me yis tshig pa la/ /myu gu sngon po ji bzhin no/
/de dang dus mtshungs no min han thon dar rgyas kyis mchod gnas zha lu pa'ang 'byor/ /rta zla'i tshes bzhi nas/ bka' 'gyur rin po che gsung sgrogs/ tshe chog /mgon khang
bzhir bskang phrin/ sgrol mar sgrol 'don/ dbu rtser 'jam 'don rnams rje btsun sa skya pa'i gdung rabs rin po che rnams zhabs pad srid mthar brtan cing bzhed don 'bad med
'grub pa'i ched so sor 'dod gsol bcas gnang ba'i sbyar byang du/ kho bo lo bcu bdun tsam nas bzung / bka' 'gyur rin po che yang yang gsung sgrogs zhu yin yod/ gsung pa bzhin/
rje nyid kyi spyil khang nas lo ltar bka' drin che ba'i rgyun bzang mi nub par mchis so/ /dbo zla nas rje rdo rje 'chang nyid kyi rlabs chen thugs bskyed nar ma'i gras/
chos khri rin po che mkhas pa zil gnon nyams gso gsar bskrun lta bu kun gyi mig gi bdud rtsir gsal ba 'di nyid/ rgya cher mdzad rgyu'i bka' gsang gis mtshon/ gang ci'i
bab yul 'di dang 'di lta bu gyis shig pa'i gsung bris bzhin/ mdzod 'dzin 'go bzo 'ul mi bcas nas dang blangs kyis rim bzhin mdzad skabs dgung gsar 'bul mi'ang 'byor gdong
nas/ 'jam dpal rdo rje no min han dpon 'bangs stobs chen rta zla'i nang zhabs pad du 'byor zhing / paN chen thams cad mkhyen

gzigs chen por mjal phyag zhar la/ 'dir yang nag zla'i mjug tsam la 'byor ba 'dra/ zhes snyan du gsol/ nag zla'i 'gor sman chab la phebs thog ma mo'i ltag gi khang brtsegs
mchod rten gog po de phal cher gshegs gsol gyis mi ring bar gsar bzhengs mdzad rgyur/ sngar gyi bzhugs yul dpa' log gis bkrol bas brling cha ma byung dogs/ skyed lhas me
'bar gyi mgon khang du brtag sgrig mdzad pas spor rung ba 'thon pa bzhin/ zla nang der byang chub mchod rten tshad ldan 'di nyid/ bod khams spyi dang bye brag bzang po'i
yul gru 'di'i snod bcud legs tshogs spel phyir/ gsar bzhengs ring bsrel rnams bzhis phyur por gtams shing / phan yon byin rlabs kyi khyad par yang / gzhung las sangs rgyas
bye ba 'bum phrag dgu bcu rtsa dgu sogs sangs rgyas tshad med pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' brgyad/ gnod sbyin gyi sde dpon brgyad/ gsang ba'i bdag po/ /rgyal chen bzhi/
tshangs pa/ dbang phyug /sred med bu rnams kyis mchod rten de chos skur byin gyis rlob cing / ring bsrel dang ldan par mdzad nas/ mchod pa dang bsnyen bkur mdzad pas yid
bzhin gyi nor bu rin po che dang / rin po che bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong du ma las byas pa dang 'dra ba'i dge ba'i rtsa ba rgya che bas/ tshe ring nad med bgegs kyis
mi tshugs/ mthong ngam/ de'i dril bu'i sgra thos sam/ mchod rten de'i mtshan thos pa tsam gyis kyang rigs drug gi sdug bsngal zhi zhing / mngon mtho dang nges legs 'grub
par gsungs pa'i phan yon de rnams dang ldan pa yin lags/ sa ga zla nang ngor mkhan chen khang gsar ngag

dbang chos skyong bzang po sde dger phebs rgyu la/ kye rdor rgyu lam/ lam zab phyi ma/ bla ma rin 'byung / rnam sme byabs khrus bcas/ bla ma zhi khro/ rig byed rjes gnang thun
mong ma yin pa/ tshogs bdag khyad par ba/ 'dod rgyal thun mong ba rjes gnang lung bcas/ rje nyid kyi ljags bsgrigs skor/ rig byed ma'i rjes gnang dang de'i gsal byed/
rig byed sngon mo dang mgon po'i char 'bebs/ grib glud/ sha brgya zan brgya/ gtad hrul zangs gling yig rnying gsal byed bcas jag ching de bzhin/ sri gnon rnams kyi ljags
lung dang / phur pa bla gsar sde dger 'thon rgyu'i thugs brel/ ril sgrub rnams mdzad mu'i nyer brgyad nyin drung yig rgyal tshed dus las yol 'phral zur 'chad grub dbang
dam pa nas 'pho ba mdzad pas/ spyi gtsug nas rnam shes 'thon pa'i rtags nges gsal dang / rje nyid kyis byang chog dang rjes bsgrub rnams bka' gsang gis 'doms par mdzad cing
/ de nas sngar nas rgyun ring gnad mu'i tshe chog /rnam rgyal/ zhal dkar po tshe 'phel rjes gnang sogs dang / bskang gso brgya tshar skabs gong gi khal kha rnams 'byor
rgyu'i gra bsgrig gi bka' 'doms kyang stsal/ snron zla'i tshes gcig la chos khri chen mo rags tsam grub pa'i rab gnas chig sgrub rje nyid nas stsal ba'i tshe phyag gnyer
'go bzo sogs la gnang cha dang / dbyar chos spyi pa gzhis len thog /'jam dpal rdo rje no min han/ rgya dpon zung rnams nas 'tshams zhu dang / sang nyin rgyud 'don grub 'phral
gdan thob/ sder thob sogs go rim ma 'chol bar/ 'jam dpal rdo rje no min ha na/ bas se/ khe pe gung sras ngag rdor/ thu she thu khal kha'i mi sna/ rtse mgron chos dar/
sne shan

shag byang sras/ bla brang mchog gi sku tshab/ ched mkhan cung po/ bla ma me le'i ngo tshab sogs dpon g.yog gtos chen tsho gcig /rgya dpan sbyar kho chi/ sbi chal chi/ spo
shog thu/ thang si zung bcas tsho gcig rnams la mjal phyag rgyas par stsal/ de nyin 'jam dpal rdo rjes bskang rdzas gzabs bshams kyis sgo rum du gsung bskang la ban tshang
bcu bzhi byon thog /spyan 'dren skabs khong la rten mjal dang / gzhis len chen mo rgyas shom gras la bla chen 'phags pa'i rnam thar thang ka gsar bzhengs zhal phye zhing
de'i tshe khong rnams la phebs phyag dang / 'jam dpal rdo rje sogs sku drag nyi shu skor la gnyan sgrol rjes gnang dang sgrub thabs las tshogs kyi ljags lung / bka' bsgo
bcas tshoms dmar du stsal/ bas se/ khe pe gung / shag byang / bla brang sku tshab sogs bcu skor la 'byung 'dul rjes gnang lung bcas bka' bsgo sogs e waM du stsal te/ tshes
lngar khong dpon g.yog byings phebs shing / thu she thu'i mi sna zung dang shag byang sogs zhag 'ga' bzhugs/ de'i gangs nyi shar tsam la chos dung rin po che gsung bskul
gyis tshang ma gzabs bzhes bcas/ gsung chos la phebs te chos khrir rje nyid dang / bshad gral 'gor 'jam mgon gsung bshad kyi dga' ston stsol ba po/ /'chams khang lho
'gram nas zhal ngo byings rnams dang / ru thog rgyal po/ /phyag gnyer drung 'khor sogs/ mdun gyi sa stegs rtsa bar dbus su klu sdings zhabs drung / g.yas phyogs la lha chen
dang chos lhun mkhan po zung / brgya dpon/ g.yon nas chos las pa zung / zur 'chad/ ban tshang pa bcas lhor bstan

dang me lcags 'gugs/ 'jam mgon gsung bshad pa'i sku mdun g.yon ngos su sku yon pa/ de nas tshogs bral rnams la chos sde lho byang / chos lhun pa sogs dang / brgya dpon g.yas
nas bla rigs bya chu ba rnams/ gzhan yang khal kha thu she ye thu rgyal po'i mi sna e rte ne jo bo'i dge bskos blo bzang chos grub pi lig thu dang / mi sna gzhan ye shes
rab rgyas/ lo tstsha ba bcas dang / sngon gyi bu chen gras bdag chen shar pa kun dga' ye shes lhun grub/ sde dge sku tshab mtshon byed phur pa bla gsar/ glo bo rgyal khab
nas byon pa mtshon byed gnas bskor ba/ dbus phyogs nas gong dkar gnas bskor ba/ khams phyogs nas bde gling grwa rgyun dang gser can grwa bskor ba/ mnga' ris nas byung
ba mtshon phyir stag mkhar gnyer rnying / lho phyogs nas byung ba mtshon pa'i grwa rgyun gnyis/ byang phyogs nas byung ba mtshon pa'i mus pa rgyugs 'bul ba sogs/ gtsang phyogs
nas gzhi grwa/ chos lhun/ skyed tshal/ bya gshongs pa bcas 'dus pa'i thog mar/ bstan srung yus pa lta bus bser bu phran bu ldang zhing / 'jam mgon mchog nas gsung bshad
tshugs pa dang gnam gshis kyang 'jam la/ grol khar chos char nyil ba sogs kyi dge mtshan dang ldan bzhin par/ nyin dang por gsang phu ba'i skor cha'i gras la rig gter/
sdom gsum/ so thar skabs dang / gnyis pa bzhi pa'i skor cha'i gras la mngon rtogs rgyan dang / sdom gsum sems bskyed skabs dang / gsum par ngam ring ba'i skor cha'i gras
la sdom gsum skabs gsum par gsung bshad mdzad cing / de lta bu'i rgyun yang sngon sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po'i sku thog la 'jam

dbyangs sku mched kyis gsung bshad gnang ba nas bzung / 'di lo'i bar gdung brgyud gsung bshad gnang mkhan ma byung bas rje rdo rje 'chang chen po yab sras nas de lta'i rgyun
bzang nub dogs thugs bskyed rmad du byung ba gnang ba'i tshe/ spyi sgos nas bsnyen bkur legs skyes mi zad nam mkha'i mdzod sgo phye ba lta bu dang / khyad par gong gi khal
kha nas zhabs brtan legs skyes dang bcas 'dus tshogs su 'gyed kyang bstabs/ spyi sgyur thog legs so'i mgul dar sgron pa sogs legs lam phul byung gi mdzad pa rnams grub
nas/ ril sgrub gtang rag /lha mo mchod bcas dang / tshes bcur gur drag rgyas pa dang sbrags rdor brag rig 'dzin chen po'i dgongs rdzogs dang / de nas gong gi khal kha lotstsha
bcas la/ gur lha bcu gnyis ma'i dbang dang / theg chen rin po che dang rdzogs pas de'i sgrub dkyil/ thub pa dgongs gsal rnams kyi ljags lung stsal rjes/ zur 'chad
grub dbang la bka' 'doms bzhin khal kha de dag la/ kye rdor rgyu lam/ mkha' spyod ma/ lha brgyad thun mong ba dang lha bcu gnyis thun mong ma yin pa/ dud sol ma/ pu tra/
dmar po skor gsum/ sengge sgra/ khro bcu/ dur bdag rnams kyi rjes gnang yig lung bcas dang / seng sgra'i ngag bsrung 'grol/ mgon pod me 'bar ma'i thun mong ma yin pa bdun
spangs pa'i tshang ma/ kye rdor sgrub dkyil/ brag rdzong ma/ gtor bsngo chen mo rnams kyi lung yang stsol bar mdzad do/ /tshes bcu bzhir 'jam mgon dbang sdud snying po
nyid sdom gsum gzhung 'don la thog mar phebs thog /khal kha de dag gis dngul gyi maNDal dang / bstan pa rgyas pa'i thugs smon zhu rten dngul bre chen

rnams phul ba sogs 'phral phugs kyi la nye'ang bzang / de nas khal kha'i rdo rje thu she ye thu rgyal po tshe brtan rdo rje/ sras tshe ring ye shes rdo rje/ thA ji mi 'gyur
rdo rje/ dpon mo 'od zer skyid sras mo no yon khu ru/ mchod gnas e rten ne jo bo'i dge bskos bla ma dge bdun bcas nas dpal ldan sa skya pa'i sbyin bdag mdzad rgyu'i dgongs
gtad can de dag nas dngos 'bul nam mkha' mdzod sgo dbye ba lta bu'i gsung lan du 'di ltar grol te/ khal kha'i thu she ye thu rgyal po tshe brtan rdo rje zhes sngon dus
chos rje khu dbon gyi bstan pa'i sbyin bdag go dan dang se chen rgyal brgyud phyis sog yul g.yon ru'i dpon khag gras su byon pa'i nang nas/ da lam khal kha'i rdo rje sogs
nas/ e rte ne jo bo dge bskos chen mor gsung ngag sogs chos bka' du ma bcas dgos tshul gnang ba de bzhin tshang ma 'bul shin tu spro yang / chos bka' de dag rgya che zhing
/ lag len grangs mang po zla ba tsam gyi ring la 'grub dka' bas/ da lam rten 'brel sarga dang po nged rang nas gur mgon lha bcu gnyis ma'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor
du dbang bskur ba dang / lung kha shas/ zur 'chad nas chos bka' ma nyung tsam dang bcas/ dpal kye rdo rje'i bshad rgyud thun mong ma yin pa mkha' 'gro ma rdo rje gur gyi
le'u bco lnga pa nas gsal bar bstan cing / 'grel byed kyang sangs rgyas gnyis pa klu sgrub kyis Arya de ba la gnang / de nas rnal 'byor dbang phyug birWa pa/ shar phyogs
nag po pa/ bram ze mchog sred nas rim bzhin brgyud pa'i chos skor sku gsung thugs kyi rten dang bcas pa rgya gar nas lo chen rin chen bzang pos spyan drangs pa'i dpal rdo
rje nag po chen po rten dang bcas pa 'di nyid kyi bka' gung thang mal lor babs/ de nyid kyis sa skya pa chen por stsol bar mdzad pa'i mal gyi

gdan sa la sngon dus gung thang na la rtse'i gnas gsar zer ba de na mal lo'i thugs dam ma yin zhes/ gtsang nyang phyogs kyi dgon pa glang pa gser gling gi grwa pa byams pa
ye shes kyis/ gung thang gnas bskor 'gugs nas shing rta chu stod nang dpal sa skyar 'byor dus nged la byin pa des dge bskos la gur gyi dbang bskur dus/ sku'i rjes gnang gi
rten bgyis te rten 'brel khyad khal kha'i thu she ye thu rgyal po tshe brtan rdo rjer mchod rten du phul ba yin pas/ shin tu gces pa'i sgo nas mchod gtor la brtson zhing
/ dam tshig bsrung bsdom gyis thugs tshags mdzad pas ji ltar smon pa'i bzhed don thams cad 'grub par 'gyur ro/ /gsung pa dang / gzhan yang sangs rgyas kyi 'phel gdung /
bdud rtsi'i sku par/ byin sne gsar rnying sogs mang ba/ srung ba dang phyag dpe phon che ba bcas legs par stsal to/ /de lo rje rdo rje 'chang yab sras rnam gsum zhal rgyas
nas phur bsnyen bdun phrag gcig sbyin sregs bcas gsung gnang / de mtshams nas chos khri rten brten pa bcas kyang ha lam tshags su tshud skabs dang / snron zla'i nyer drug
nyin 'chams sku dregs pa zil gnon lcam dral ngo mtshar can 'di gnyis gsar bskrun mdzad rgyu'i bka' gsang lha bzo tshul khrims bkra shis la grol nas nyer dgur/ sku rgyu
byin sne khyad par can rnams dang / ras gos nag sogs la byin rlabs gnang skabs glo bur du/ a tsa ra bzhi dga' nyams dang bcas 'byor ba'i nang tshan/ bhe ta ghe ri zer ba
zhig gis rje nyid la rakSha'i phreng ba phul ba sogs la nye shin tu bzang ba'i dbu tshugs shing / de rnams la yang gser gyis mtshon mkho dgu gya nom

pa stsal/ de tsam la gzhung zhabs rin po cher/ gser ljang brdung gi kum bha 'di zung dang / dngul gyi maNDal che legs/ rdzas brgyad sna bdun rnams 'dod 'jo dpal rgyas su brtse
