skyong zhus don rim gyis smin cing 'jam mgon sku mched me bya rta zlar chos khri 'khor lo gsum ldan du che 'don bka' drin che rgyur nges pa'i brda 'grems zhu srol bzhin/
gzhung zhabs rin po cher snyan sgron dang chu stod yar tshes nas dbu rtse rnying mar de'i bris mgon dang / gsar bzhengs 'bur sku'i drung gtor 'dzugs kyis bskang phrin
chag med dang bcas 'chams sku'i las gra tshugs/ de nas 'char 'phar gyi thugs brel rnams la gzhol ba'i mur smin zla'i bcu drug nas/ sa tshogs jo dar chen mor nyams gso'i
zhal bkod ngo mtshar can 'di nyid mdzad nas/ gting du bum gter dgu sogs dang / steng gi rgyal mtshan la rnam bzhi'i ring bsrel gyis phyur por gtams pa la/ mgo zla'i tshes
gcig nam gzir la rgya dkar nag steng nas rje rdo rje 'dzin ban tshang pa'i 'khor tshogs bcas nas jo dar rgyal mtshan 'dzugs cho ga phyag len rnam dag gis bsgrubs pa de lta
bu'i jo dar der/ sngon dus bla chen khams gsum dbang sdud 'phags chen blo gros rgyal mtshan la/ gong ma se chen go pa las/ gos dar lnga khri dgu stong phul ba'i phud mtshon
phyir/ gos jus dkar po dar lcog dang / dar mtshon sna lnga'i yug chen srid na ring ba dpal sa skyar dus mdos gzabs ma dang / gdung brgyud khri phebs skabs legs par
'phyar rgyu'i logs la 'dod gsol can du mdzad do/ /de nas sa tshogs khri chen mdun du gur chen bsam grub pho brang phub pa'i nang gi gdung la nor bu'i dra phyed/ 'khor mor
'phags pa'i rnam thar thang ka /khri khang byang skyar gdung rabs thang ka /rje btsun sa skya pa'i

gdung rabs srid mtha'i bar chad med 'byon pa'i rten 'brel gyi ched du/ dus mchod nas bdag nyid chen po bzang po dpal mchod phreng sogs sngon 'gro'i sgo nas gdan drangs/ gzhan
yang bka' bstan/ sa skya bka' 'bum/ dbang khang nas bde gshegs mchod rten brgyad/ tshe bum bcu gcig sogs dang / mtha' bskor du sna lnga'i mchod tshogs dang bcas bcom ldan
'das snying po kye rdo rje'i rab gnas sgrub zhag lnga'i grol nyin sbyin bdag bsgo bar zhal ngo rnams dang / phyag gnyer sogs phebs shing / cha zhabs khams drung nas gzhas
bcas phyi bskor la me tog 'thor bar mdzad tshul yang / chos khri skor/ de nas 'chams khang steng brgyud ka bzhi/ ka drug /'phel rgyas steng 'og /tshong dpon shag /khro
khang steng 'og sogs gsar bzo rnams dang / rim gyis mdzo mo sgang sogs nas par bskor rgyal po sgang brgyud dpal 'byor rab rgyas/ bzo khang gsar pa/ de nas lha chen 'phen
nag la mchod 'bul sogs rgyun bzhin phyi bskor grub nas/ gsung bsngo/ dga' ston rgya che ba dang / sbyin sreg sogs mdzad/ de'i sang nas rgyun gyi sgrub mchod dang bcu dgu
nas nyer gnyis bar 'chams rgyugs dang / rgyal yum mchog nas rgyal gsung bka' 'gyur rin po che zhal dbye ba/ nyer gsum nas phur bzlog /'jigs byed/ zhal gyi gtor bzlog rnams
tshugs pa'i skabs so/ /de dag gi don bsdu na/ rigs kyi bdag po zhal gzigs ma dros klung / /'jam mgon gzhon nu 'khor lo gsum ldan dang / /bzang po'i yul dang chos kyi
sbyin yul te/ /rnam bzhi'i lam nas 'bab pa'i ngo mtshar la/ /mgron gyi zol du lhags pa'i che dgu kun/ /gsung gsang brgyad ldan zhi bsil dag byed ni/ /'khor ba'i tsha gdung
sel ba'i khrus mchog

tu/ /sngon byung gtam gyis bsus nas sbyin min nam/ /srid gsum dregs pa'i yang rje'i ngo mtshar gzugs/ /rten dang brten par byin rlabs spro bsdu'i char/ /bstan srid bla nar
'phags pa'i dge mtshan bcas/ /legs lam rmad byung dar ba'i dus su smin/ /zhes kyang smras so// // ! dgung grangs zhe dgur phebs pa me bya rgyal zla'i tshes gcig tho rengs
rtser lha bsangs dang bstun mdzo ra'i nang gsar steng nas/ gong gi jus dkar dar chen sna lnga'i sgron bcas gzim drung gis do dam pa sangs dud shin tu che ba dang bcas yang
'then/ de nas rgyal mtshan 'dzugs chog gong bzhin grub nas rgyal po lo gsar gyi dga' ston dang / rje nyid kyis dmar po skor gsum gtor slod/ dge sdings ma Ni bas gzigs
'bul thog dga' ston gyi yan lag tu bro 'khrab gras gzhan dag byung na'ang khri phebs grub nas 'khrab chog pa'i bka' 'doms dang / lhag par ri bo che nas sngon dus gzigs 'bul
zhu mu zhig yin na'ang / bar skabs su rkyen 'ga' zhig gis ma byung ba de bzhin phyis su yang yang zhu ba 'di dag kyang rje nyid kyi thugs rjer 'khums shing / lo sngon
ma dang de lo gnyis char la rgyab ri dpon po rir mtshan ngan bstud mar byung ba rnams zhi phyir/ rin chen sgang gi ltag tu 'od zer can ma'i sbyin sregs sogs bzlog thabs mang
du mdzad/ tshes gnyis la nang so'i rtag gtor zhal 'byed la phebs dus gtor sgam chen mo bkod legs 'gro yul bkas 'doms/ tshes gsum la dbu rtser 'chams sku dregs pa zil
gnon lcam dral dam ye dbyer med du byin rlabs dang mthu stobs kyi bdag por mnga' gsol mdzad/ de nas sa skya pa'i gdung brgyud rin po che rnams khri 'don gnang skabs dus phyis/
rim bzhin je rgyas su song gras dus mdos

gzabs ma rgyal zlar 'gyangs pa'i tshes 'gor gtor spod dang sgrags/ sgo rum/ nang so/ /'dud 'dul phug /skyed lhas/ bsam brling rnams su ru mtshon gsar bzhengs re dang / bdud
'dul phug min pa'i mgon khang bzhi la lha mdung gsar pa re 'bul ba bcas/ dus mdos phrin 'chol dang chabs gcig thug chog re mdzad pa 'jam mgon bsod nams dbang phyug gi sku
thog tsam nas bzung chag med byung ba bzhin/ gtor spod dang sbrags gong gi mgon khang rnams su thug chog dang / de nas phur khang thub chen sku mdun du dus mdos gzabs ma'i
'chams chas rnams go rim bzhin legs par bshams nas rje nyid kyis phyag nas dang / 'chams skur ban tshang pa'i 'khor tshogs dang bcas mgon po'i rab gnas smin rgyas mdzad
pa'i tshe rje nyid kyi gzigs snang la/ 'chams mgon gnyis kyi zhal gnyer zhing spyan 'khyug pa sogs ye shes sems dpa' byon rtags gsal por 'khrungs/ nyer gcig la kun rar
chog sgrig /nyer gnyis la mdos gzabs bca' sgrig /nyer gsum la 'chams sku gdan 'dren gzabs ma rnams debs nang bzhin dang / de lo dbu rtse nas lcam dral gdan 'dren bcas/ nyer
bzhir mnyen chas 'di snga sor lha khang rdo gcal du mdzad kyang rje nyid kyis debs chen dus tshogs su dgos tshul bzhin mdzad cing nye lngar rgyun bzhin/ nyer drug nyer
bdun la lha chen shar nub gtor 'bul/ sa 'dul/ nyer brgyad la 'chams dngos/ nyer dgur gtor rgyag /gnam gang la bskang gso brgya tshar sogs gzabs spros skor rje rdo rje 'chang
nyid kyis debs bsgrigs snga sor chu lug lor mdzad pa bzhin la/ 'chams ja nyung skyon gyis de lo nas bzung mnyen chas dang / sku 'chams dngos gnyis char la 'chams ja
brgyad re spor

gnang dang / skol snod kyi khro chen la dkar g.ya' byugs pa sogs thugs bskyed bla na med pa dang gnam gzhag zhal bkod kyi rim pa'ang rgya cher mdzad do/ /rta zla'i bcu gcig
nas khri phebs dngos gzhi nyin gsum ma mdzad pa'i tshe/ thog mar nam langs la chos khri steng gi lha khang 'chi med yang rtser rje rdo rje 'chang nas rang bzhin 'byung ba'i
gtsug tor rnam rgyal gyi sta gon sgrub par phebs/ sngar srol la nyin gnyis yab phebs srol ma mchis rung / de lo nyin gnyis sgrig gras ma mdzad pa ma gtogs rje nyid phebs
shing / de yang bzhugs khri'i dbus su bka' chos kyi dga' ston stsol pa po ngag dbang kun dga' dpal ldan chos skyong bkra shis grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po 'di
nyid dang / g.yon du ngag dbang kun dga' phan bde rgya mtsho theg mchog bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po 'di nyid dang / rig dang dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho'i khyab bdag
drug pa rdo rje 'chang chen po de nyid ni/ nyin dang po gnyis rab gsal shar lho'i 'gugs nang du khri chen la nub gzigs su bzhugs/ de nas byang la zhal ngo / /mkhan phyag
gnyer/ gzhung zhabs rin po che'i sku tshab sogs gsol ja dang 'bul chen 'gro yul ma gtogs sku drag ji snyed pas phyur zhing / bzhugs khri'i g.yas rdo skas 'gor sku yon pa/
de skabs 'dren chas thob pa rnams la rang rang gi 'dren chas 'bul mi dang / de min sku drag rnams la 'dren pas zhal dkar rag stegs bcas thob mi thob kyi rnam gzhag dang
ldan par mdzad/ mthil rdo gcal la sngar phan byang gral 'go mdzad nas zhal shar nub la gzigs srol yang / de lo nas bzung byang gzigs kho nar mdzad dgos la bsgrigs can rnams
ni bka' chos chos spyod sogs dang bstun/ de phyin rang rang blo dang bstun chog pa'i bka'

'doms dang / nyin gnyis rje nyid kyang sgrig gras min pas/ nam langs la nang so sogs brgyud gong gi rnam rgyal sgrub mchod ji 'gro dang / bka' chos ran pa dang bstun gsang
sgo nas phebs/ bka' chos dang 'bul bzhes rnams grub nas rje nyid kyis sgrub mchod 'phro dang / 'jam mgon sku mched gzhi thog tu phebs/ bka' dbang ran pa dang phebs brda bcas
'chi med yang rtser byon/ nyin gsum par sgrig gras mdzad pa de bas nang bzhin bzhugs khri'i g.yas su phebs shing / bka' chos stsol ba pos/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i gsung
rab dri ma med pa la phyag 'tshal lo/ /gsung pa dang / mdo klag pa sogs/ maNDal gyi tshe sngags 'chang bla ma thams cad mkhyen pa rgyal sras sems dpa'i dbang phyug dam pa'i
drung du/ theg pa chen po'i dam pa'i chos zab mo zhu ba'i yon du sogs dang / gdung brgyud las sngar dbang gsan phyin/ dus gsum sangs rgyas thams cad 'dus pa'i ngo bo
sogs/ lugs 'di ni zhu 'bul phyag btso brgyad kyi tshe'ang dbang ma thob pa'i tshogs dpon la/ ma tshang ba med pa 'di nyid bshes gnyen dam pa khyed la tshogs kyi rdo rje slob
dpon zhu ba'i yon du/ zhes sogs dang / dbang thob nas dus gsum sangs rgyas sogs gsungs dgos pa'i rgyu mtshan bzhin mdzad bka' chos gnang nas chos spyod gtong ring 'bul
ba rnams gral gyi sku rgyab dang / g.yon sku mdun rnams bskor/ rdo skas shar ma brgyud bzhugs khri'i g.yon nas sku mdun du sleb pa dang / mdzod 'dzin bzhugs khri'i lho
nub tu bzhengs te 'bul tho gsher nas gsang sgo la drangs/ de nas 'phro rnams la gzhol bar mdzad/ nyin gsum pa bkra shis mnga' gsol gyi tshe/ gzhi thog tu mkhan phyag gnyer
brgya las ban tshang / bde gling dbu chos/ tshogs chen dbu chos/ gling dpon

bcu drug /yul slob gnyis/ rtse gdong slob dbu ban tshang bcas byon nas/ mkhan chen gyis sku rten/ brgya dpon nas gsung rten/ las chen pas thugs rten dang phrin las rten/ phyag
gnyer la yon tan rten gser bum re re/ ban tshang rim bzhin rol sil rnga/ chos dung rin po che/ rdor dril/ sna bdun/ rdzas brgyad/ bzhugs stan rdo rje rgya gram rnams
phyag khyer gyis phebs gong tshogs pa byings bzhugs tshar ba mdzad/ 'jam mgon sku mched chos khrir bzhugs pa'i sku mdun yab rje rdo rje 'chang nyid bzhengs mthar/ g.yas g.yon
la phyag khyer ba rnams bsgrigs nas/ dbu byed che bas bskul la/ sangs rgyas chos tshogs shur ma gsum nas bzung / khrus gsol/ sku phyis bar de dus kyi zin bris bzhin
mdzad/ de nas sku rten yab kyi phyag tu bsnams te/ rgyal srid sna bdun gyi gdangs dang bcas pas/ tshogs gnyis mthar phyin mtshan mchog so gnyis dang / /rab mdzes dpe byad
bzang po brgyad cus spras/ /sprul pa'i 'od zer dpag med 'phro ba can/ /longs spyod rdzogs sku chen por dbang bskur ro/ /oM badzra kA ya siddhi a bhiShinytsA mi/ gsung rten
bsnams te/ nye ring kun la snyoms pa tshangs pa'i dbyangs/ /thar lam ston pa lha yi rnga bo che/ /skye med 'gag pa med pa brag cha'i gsung / /yan lag drug cu'i dbyangs
kyis dbang bskur ro/ /oM badzra wAka siddhi a bhiShinytsA mi/ thugs rten bsnams te/ chos nyid dag pa gnyis ldan mngon du gyur/ /chos can ji snyed dbye ba so sor gzigs/ /chos
rnams rnam kun mngon rdzogs byang chub pa'i/ /sgrib bral rnam dag thugs kyis dbang bskur ro/ /oM badzra tsItta siddhi a bhiShinytsA mi/ yon tan rten gser bum cha bsnams
te/ stobs nyid rdo rje mi 'jigs sengge bzhin/ /ma 'dres mkha' dag thub bstan chu zla ltar/ /bral dang rnam par smin pa'i 'bras bu yi/ /

yon tan drug cu bzhi yis dbang bskur ro/ /oM gu Na siddhi a bhi ShinytsA mi/ rgyal srid sna bdun tshe chog bzhin/ /rdzas brgyad bsang sbyangs byin rlabs 'bul tshig rab gnas

ma'i gzhung lugs grub mtha' phyi nang gnyis kas zhal gyi bzhes pa las/ nang pa'i gzhung lugs rgyal ba'i bstan pa rin po che dag par bsgrub pa'i ched/ dgra bcom pa chos skyob
la sogs pas 'phags yul du rig gzhung rnams dag spel bar mdzad mod/ de dag las kyang ches khyad par du 'phags pa ni/ dpal ldan chos kyi grags pas rgyas pa'i bstan bcos
tshad ma rnam 'grel zhes/ tshad ma'i bstan bcos rnams kyi nang nas mchog tu gyur pa 'di nyid/ sngon gyi lotstsha ba chen po rnams kyis ljongs 'dir bsgyur zhing / bshad pa'i
rgyun bzhugs pa ltar yongs rdzogs bstan pa'i mnga' bdag rje btsun sa skya pa chen po kun dga' snying pos/ dpal me dig pa dang / mes lhang 'tsher ba sogs las tshad ma
gsan pa dang / rje btsun rtse mos phya pa chos kyi sengge sogs la gsan cing / de bas kyang phul du gyur pa 'jam mgon sa skya paNDi tas/ rgya bod snga rabs pa dag gi log rtog
rnams lung rig gis bsun phyung nas/ chos kyi grags pa'i dgongs pa 'khrul med du skyong bar mdzad pa sogs sa skya pa'i yab chos gras rang yin pas na/ ring mo'i dus nas
rje rdo rje 'chang chen po nyid kyi dgongs bzhed thun mong yin par gdung brgyud rnams dang / 'dir bzhugs tshad ma pa rnams la gzhung skyor zhig byung na ci mi rung dgongs
pa dam pa'i thugs bskyed mngon du gyur to/ /de lo'i phur sgrub la rje nyid nas rje btsun sa skya pa'i bstan pa rin po che'i zhabs tog tu gos bzang dgu las bsgrun pa'i phod
ka /rdor gong / gos bem/ ral phod sogs bgrangs yas rnams thog mar bzhes te 'chams par mdzad do/ /de dag gi don bsdu na/ dbang lung man ngag 'khrid kyi chu gter cher/
longs su spyod pa'i 'khon rigs dzahnuH legs bshad zhal skyugs tshad

ma'i dga' ston mkhan/ /ngo mtshar lhun grub mtshan ma chal chil 'jo/ /zhes kyang smras so// // ! dgung grangs nga gcig tu phebs pa sa phag rgyal zla'i sked tsam nas gro bzhin
zla sked tsam par rje rdo rje 'chang chen po yab sras rnam gsum zhal rgyas nas phun gling bzhugs g.yab tu/ bcom ldan 'das snying po kye rdo rje'i gzhi bsnyen ngo mtshar
gyi mtshan ma bzang po dang bcas mdzad skabs rje rdo rje 'chang nas brtse chen lha khang du zhabs bskor yongs bsdoms nyi khri chig stong bzhi brgya tham pa dang / phyag
'bul sum stong nyis brgya bcu tham pa gnang dus dang / phun gling dbang khang du bzhugs dus bcas brtse chen snying po'i snang brnyan dang rje btsun rin po che'i snang brnyan
zung nyin re bzhin zhal gzigs tshul mi 'dra ba'i gzigs snang mang po zhig dang lhag par rje btsun rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug dpal ldan birWa pa nyid mngon gsum du byon
nas rje nyid la dges nyams kyis bzhugs pa la rje nyid kyi thugs rnam par mi rtog pa'i ye shes kyi ngo bo de nyid rje btsun rnal 'byor dbang phyug gi thugs kar 'pho la
khad pa'i tshe/ sku 'khris kyi 'jam mgon gzhon nu'i zhal dkyil skya khrom gyis gzigs pas/ gsung ngag slob bshad sogs gdams pa rgya mtsho da ka 'bul dgos dgongs thugs rje'i
lcags kyus nam yang ma bskyud nas/ re zhig dag snang de 'gag par mdzad pa zhig rje nyid la 'khrungs shing / 'di ni kye rdor gzhi bsnyen thang gsum pa'i skabs so/ /khrums
zla'i tshes bdun nas bzung / gang gi rigs sras dam pa 'jam mgon rnams dang gnas gsar rdo rje 'chang gi mchog sprul/ 'phan yul bco brgyad pa gzim 'og sprul sku rnams la/
tshe dpag med dze tA ri'i dbang / tshe dpag med dkar po/ sgrol dkar/ dbyangs can dkar mo'i rjes gnang lung bcas tshar lugs dkar lha gsum/ mi g.yo ba dkar sngon/ sman bla/
klu dbang lha lnga/ gnas brtan bcu drug /'jam dbyangs dmar ser/ gang blo ma/ 'jam dkar ma ti lugs/ 'jam dkar gser gdugs can/ smra seng / 'od zer can/ rnam rgyal/ gtsug
'bar/ gza' yum/

bka' gdams lha bzhi/ rnam 'joms/ utsarya/ gtum po/ sme dud/ ljang nag /sme nag /bcu gcig zhal gtso 'khor lnga/ de gtso rkyang / sgrol dkar 'od zer drug sbrags/ don zhags lha
lnga/ gnyan sgrol/ rta mgrin lcags ral/ shwa na bzhi bskor/ jo lugs dbyug thog can/ ri khrod ma/ dzam ser nag gnyis/ dzam dkar/ nor rgyun ma/ 'byung 'dul me dbang dang
bcas pa'i rjes gnang bcas las/ bcu gcig zhal gtso 'khor lnga dang / shwa na bzhi bskor/ ri khrod ma/ nor rgyun ma rnams ma gtogs lung bcas/ sgrub thabs brgya rtsa'i rjes
gnang lung bcas/ grub chen brgyad cu'i rjes gnang / rnam thar/ rdo glu/ bstod pa/ tshogs 'khor rnams kyi lung bcas/ rdo rje phur pa'i stod las dbang / drag dmar nyang lugs
kyi dbang / rdo rje phreng ba'i dbang nyin bco brgyad ma'i lugs rnams stsal ba sogs rkang grangs tsam dang yig cha ni 'dir ma spros so/ /lung gi skor la/ gdung rabs chen
mo dang / de'i zhal skong drug pa'i lo rgyus de bzhin dang bar/ e waM chos ldan gyi chos spyod glegs bam dang po nas birWa pa'i sku bstod gnyis dang gong ma lnga bstod/
sde par sa skya bka' 'bum pod ka kha gnyis yongs rdzogs rje nyid kyis gsan yig bzhin/ bu ston chos 'byung / rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi rnam thar mdzad pa 'khrul med spyod
pa'i gter/ rdo rje gzhon nu'i mngon rtogs rgyas pa klags pas don grub/ dkyil chog blo dman rtogs sla/ gtor chog phrin las myur mgyogs kyi pho nya rnams dang / rje nyid
kyi ljags bsgrigs skor la/ tshar lugs bla ma gtso bsdus la phyag 'tshal/ rdo rje phur pa'i mngon rtogs bsdus pa zhal skong can/ drag dmar gyi phrin gzhung phyag len mdzes
rgyan/ sa skya pa'i gdung brgyud rnams dang ban tshang pa'i zhal 'don gtso bsdus/ zhabs brtan bden tshig rnams dang / sdom gsum brgyud 'debs rnams stsol bar mdzad cing
/ de'i

tshe mchog sprul rin po cher bka' gsang lhug grol gyis 'jam mgon sa skya paNDi ta'i nang rten thub chen 'dzam gling g.yas bzhag gi drung du lha chen mkhan rabs nyer lnga pa
byams pa chos bkra shis sogs dge 'dun grangs tshang ba'i dbus su bsnyen par rdzogs pa dge slong gi dngos po yang dag par bzhes pa dang / ring min chu stag lor yang nyid
kyi bka' bzhin/ rje btsun 'chi med bstan pa'i nyi mas kyang rab byung de drung du bzhes so/ /de mtshams nas brtse chen lha gang steng gi rgya phebs gsar sgron mdzad pa'i
nang rten/ 'phags mchog kha sarpa Ni/ 'jam dbyangs/ phyag rdor/ so 'brang / ri khrod ma rnams sman 'dam las bskrun pa'i nang gzungs ringabasrel rnam bzhis phyur por mdzad
de/ rgyal bstan spyi dang bye brag rje btsun sa skya pa'i bstan pa de 'dzin dang bcas pa'i phyi nang gsang gsum gyi 'gal rkyen zhi zhing / yul phyogs 'di ltos bcas kyi mi
nor phyugs gsum la nad gdon god rigs chag che nyam nga thams cad dang / sad ser btsa' mu ge'i gnod pa thams cad las bsrung ba'i thugs smon 'dod gsol dang bcas bskrun par
mdzad nas/ sa mchod thog brtse chen lha khang du phur sgrub dang sbrags phur pa'i rab gnas kyi me tog 'thor bar mdzad/ ston chab skabs ma mor chab bdugs gnang zhing / de
nas smin zla'i bcu gcig nyin phyug po dbu rtse'i ne'u gsing du shar gzigs/ ri bya sder mar lho gzigs/ phyag 'tshal sgang mchod rten du nub gzigs/ gar zhing gsar du byang
gzigs bcas lho byang cha snyoms te/ byang pas lha bsangs rgyas pa sngon 'gro'i sme brtsegs/ de'i grib glud/ brgya bzhi rnams mdzad pa'i glud rnams phyogs bzhir brdzangs
par gnang / lho pas/ gtor ma brgya rtsa/ 'byung bzhi/ cha gsum/ so 'brang / tog gzungs/ gtsug lag mdo bzhi rnams klog 'don/ gnas brtan phyag mchod/ bsam myur ma/ sgrol bzlog
rnams smin

rgyas/ mgon khang mtshan thogs/ bon gyi phya 'gugs/ sgrol ma dang gser 'od mtshan 'don/ rnam rgyal stong mchod sogs rim gro rgya cher sngon 'gro'i dmar phyogs dga' ba gnyis
pa'i srod kyi cha mkha' 'gro 'dul ba'i dus kyi tshe gsang khog tu da lta'i bdag mo 'di nyid phebs shing mtshan gyi mnga' gsol yang rje nyid kyis stsal lo/ /zla ba de nang
bstan dgra gdug pa can sku gnyer du rdzu ba tsha bo dang bcas nas las ngan ji snyed cig bsags pa la brten drug cu pa'i gtor bzlog gcig kyang gnang / mgo zla'i dgun chos
thog rje nyid kyi bka' bzhin 'jam mgon dbang sdud snying po'i zhal snga nas dbu ma thugs mtshor zhugs pa'i gsung bshad kyi dga' ston yang lhug par stsal to/ /de dag gi don
bsdu na/ dus grangs mtshan ma'i bsam gtan spyil po'i ngogs/ /phyi nang gsang ba gdod ma'i lhag pa lha'i/ /rang zhal rjen par gzigs pa'i drin can rje/ /bdag med lha mo'i
bdag las gzhan na 'khrul/ /snang stong sgyu ma lta bu'i thabs mkhas kyis/ /las can dag pa'i 'khor rnams phyag rgya che'i/ /khang bzang rtse mor 'khrid pa'i blang dor la/
/sna tshogs rgyu 'bras chos sbyin mdzub mo'i 'phrul/ /de lta'i gzhal yas steng du rten brten pa'i/ byi dor gtsang ma'i pho nyas bkug pa'i mgron/ /mtshan gsum rigs kyi thig
le'i 'byung khungs shig /theg chen dbu ma chen po'i lam nas byon/ /ces kyang smras so// // ! dgung grangs nga gnyis su byon pa lcags byi rgyal zla'i nyer dgur zur 'chad
grub dbang dam par bka' 'doms bzhin/ sngon dus bdag chen rdo rje 'chang bla brang shar na bzhugs skabs shig /gdan sa 'dir rgya 'dre mang po zhig lhags nas sgar rgyab/
gdugs nyi 'og tu slebs pa tsam byas nas gdan sar g.yon bskor byas dus/ 'khrugs pa sogs mi mthun pa yong 'dug pa de/ drag po sngags rgod kyi spyan dmigs kyis tshar bcad pa'i
lo rgyus mchis pa bzhin/

de dus kyang rgya 'dre'i 'phrul gyis rta nad sogs sna tshogs mchis pa rnams/ ma her bzhon pa'i rgya 'dre'i glud gzugs brdzangs chog gis sa mtshams sgrol bar mdzad do/ /chu
bya rta zla'i tshes gcig nas bzung rje rdo rje 'chang nyid nas rgyun gyi phyag tsha mang nyung ji ltar rigs pa nyin ltar 'debs par mdzad pa dang / skabs 'gar bshol ba bcas
mtha' ma lcags byi rgyal zla'i tshes bdun bar la gnang ba yongs bsdoms brgyad khri drug stong zhe lnga bka' drin bskyangs so/ /de lo gsar 'phral khams phyogs kyi sbyor
ngan la brten g.yul gshom la nye dus/ nyes med sems can du ma'i srog skyob kyi ched du/ ngan sbyor de dag rang zhir 'gyur ba'i phrin 'chol dang thugs bskyed rgya gang che
mdzad pas 'bras bu mngon gyur de bzhin dang / de mtshams nas rje nyid la sngar gyi glo tshad dang zhabs 'bam gyi snyun gzhi lhan 'doms lta bu'i tshul bzhes dang / dbus phebs
la'ang nye ba bcas/ rta zla'i tshes gcig nyin gong gi gsang rgya'ang grol zhing gang ci'i dga' ston legs 'bul rim bstar dang tshes gsum nyin chos sde lhor tshe chog
/maNDal bzhi chog /gtor ma/ 'byung bzhi/ cha gsum/ sAtstsha/ bka' 'gyur rin po che gsung sgrogs/ thub dbang byams 'jam dbyangs kyi sku bstod/ gnas brtan phyag mchod/ bsam
myur ma/ rnam rgyal bstod pa/ gzungs ring tshar gsum/ 'dod gsol/ ri khrod ma/ sna tshogs yum gzungs phreng 'khor/ sgrol ma/ mdo tshar gsum sngon 'gro'i bzlog pa dgu tshar/
tshe gzungs nyer gcig /bsngo smon rnams dang / 'grul phebs ban tshang pa rnams nas gzungs gso dang sri gnon thun gnyis/ 'dir bzhugs ban tshang bsnyen song rnams nas phur
bzlog mgon po drug cu pa/ 'jigs byed drug cu pa rnams mdzad cing / tshes drug nas mgon khang khag bzhir phrin 'chol dus skyed bsam gnyis la snyun gzhi'i

stabs rje nyid ma phebs/ tshes dgu'i nyin sdo ra dpon slob rnams la gang ci'i zhib gsung grol ba dang chabs gcig sras mo stsal ba'i legs gso'i bdog pa gya nom pa'ang bstar
bar mdzad de/ tshes bcu gcig nyin rje rdo rje 'chang yab sras rnam gsum/ rje btsun drung 'chi med bstan pa'i nyi ma/ bdag mo 'chi med dpal 'byor bzang mo sogs zhal ngo rnams
dang / sku zhang chos lung pa dang 'gro mgon pa rnam gnyis mdzod 'dzin gyi dbus dpon g.yog skabs su bab pa rnams dang bcas dbus phyogs su chibs bskyod kyi sgo dod pa'i
lo rgyus rgyas pa ni gzhan du shes par bya zhing / 'dir rags tsam smos na/ bla brang zam sne nas ki sgra dar g.yab dang / lha chen lcags ri'i steng nas ki sgra zhwa g.yab
skyel chang ba rnams nas ki sgra rnams la chibs kha bsgyur tsam mdzad/ srom rdzing khar ja zhus/ gra ma lung du gsol tsha/ ga ra bkra shis dar rgyas kyi drag yur bzhugs/
sang nyin tho rengs zhong pa la rtser lha bsang rgyas pa'i skabs kha ba cung zad 'tshubs shing / dpon slob kun grang ngar 'dar zhum can dang / lhag par rje nyid snyun
tshul de ltar lags na'ang bdag gzhan brje ba'i byang sems kho nas dus 'da' bar mdzad pa ni rje de'i khyad par gyi chos so/ /de nas dgon rgyas dang tsha rong du byon 'phral
dkar spro'i dga' ston la longs spyad nas/ byang ri'i lha khang gnas gzigs thog skye dgu mtha' yas pa zhig gi gtsug tu phyag gser gyi 'khor lo ngal bso mdzad pa nas bzung
yul gru mtha' las su skye bo mtha' yas par byin gyis rlob pa'i tshe rje nyid kyi bsod nams kyi mthus sems can thams cad sdig spong dge la gnas pa byang chub sems dpa'i
thugs smon dang bcas spyan phyed btsum gyis spyan chab 'khrugs bzhin du 'khor ba par nges 'byung gting nas 'khrungs pa'i mdzad pa ni/ kun dang thun mong du bdag gis kyang
rtogs pa de ltar lags/ der ma

zad sems can ngag dig can dang / mig rna ba/ sna sogs nad can/ rma shu 'thor sogs kyis gtses pa rnams gzigs tshe/ nad pa de drag gzhan che chung ji ltar yang kun la btang snyoms
chen po'i sgo nas khyod rang dbang po sogs na ba de dang de ston cig gsungs te ljags sngags mdzad pa'i tshe/ de'i gnas der zhal mchus reg kyang srid zhi mnyam gzigs
kyi brdar gtsang rme'i thugs rtog ye mi gnang bar/ kho la phan na nga la rtog pa med/ ces yang yang gsungs/ dbul po ngan ngon can dag gzigs tshe nga khri mthon por zas gos
gya nom par longs spyod pa 'di ltar na/ kho snying rje gsungs nas zas gos kyis tshims par mdzad pa sogs 'phags chen byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa bla na med pas rnam
kun 'da' bar mdzad pa kun gyi spyod yul du gyur pa las gzhan pa'i gzhan don rjes chags kyi mdzad pa bem por ston rgyu ci zhig dgos/ gang ltar rje nyid kyi bka' bzhin 'jam
mgon sku mched dang rje btsun drung bcas nas tsha rong pa'i gnas khang steng 'og la me tog gi char phab/ de nas lhun rtse mkhan pos chibs bsus te lhun rtser phebs 'phral
'dus tshogs nas zhabs brtan thog mkhan rin po ches mdo rgyud kyi lung dang 'brel ba'i zhal bzhes zhus pa nas bzung / dgon sde phal cher du de bzhin bcas/ maNDal gyis gtsos
pa'i dngos 'bul gya nom pa dgyes bzhes kyis/ gnas gzigs dang / rgya mdud du bzhugs/ de nas gnas sa la sgang pa'i 'khris su bzhugs pa'i tshe gzhis rdzong khang brag dang
sna dkar ba gnyis nas phebs bsu gra sgrig yang dag dang / gangs can gnas gzigs dus lha mo'i bla mtsho yin zer ba'i rdzing klong der mtsho rdzas zhus don phran bu'ang gnang
zhing / khong tshos dkar spro dngos 'bul sogs legs lam yang dag dang / gsol dpon chen mo'i sku tshab pa dge slong de'i dbu gtsug cung zad 'phar ba zhig yod pas/ rje nyid
nas dge slong gtsug tor can/ zhes thugs mnyes

nyams dang bcas lcags rir skye dgu mang por phyag dbang blo kha rdzogs par stsal nas/ ha cang mi ring ba'i sar ngor khag gi dpon g.yog rnams nas chibs bsus snar thang du phebs
te spyi sger gyi re skong dang / sang snga char zhal ngo gzhan rnams nas snar thang gnas gzigs mdzad rjes phebs te/ bla brang bkra shis lhun po dang nye ba'i sa nas rtse
drung lung pa shar pa dang / la mo chu skor ba sogs brgyad tsam zhig dang / kha che tshong dpon yul lha pa sogs nas chibs bsus/ pho brang gi sku mdun du phyag 'bul mdzad
de gzhis rtses bzhugs sgar thog chibs bsu bas mtshon/ spyi sger nas mjal phyag mang ba dang / skye bo khri khrag du ma longs par dmangs phyag gis mtshon/ gar phebs kyi
sar tal mar mdzad pa dang / so sos chibs bsu skyel/ gsol ston dngos 'bul sogs dang / mchog gsum rten gyi drung du mchod 'bul snyan shal/ spyi bye'i bstan pa thugs bcangs
kyis bstan de 'dzin bcas rgyas pa'i thugs smon/ rab tu gnas pa'i me tog 'thor gnang / dge 'dun bsnyen bkur/ ngan slong sbyin gtong sogs ni brjod kyis mi lang bas mang bas
'jigs te rgyas par ma spros shing / rje nyid kyi bka' las/ da lo spyi sgos nas sngar dang mi 'dra ba'i bdag rkyen tshang mas mdzad byung / zhes gsungs/ de skabs thams
cad mkhyen gzigs chen po ni rgya nag tu chibs sgyur gyi dus dang / sku tshab lde phyung pa nas mtshams zhu dang / bla brang gzhung nas zur gsos gyi bdag rkyen sngar lam las
mi 'gong bar stsal/ gser can du spyi sger re skong rnams mdzad rjes/ phebs gru bde mur rtse gdong pa'i thab bsu dang bcas sle phu pa'i steng khang du bzhugs tshe'ang /
gtsang mda' pad kyis mtshon spyi sger mang por byin rlabs kyi zil dngar phab/ de nas rtse gdong du zhag bcu gnyis skabs chos sde dang rin sgad dge 'dun/ rtse sprul

dpon g.yog /thob rgyal gru tshang pa/ ri gdong pa sogs la phur dbang stod las dang / smad las mda' pad sku ngo zung la tshe dbang / smyung gnas pa rnams la ma Ni'i bzlas lung
/ rtse ban sogs la gur drag /g.yul sa shar du skya ser mang por khrom dbang / zhal ngo gzhan rnams kyis gye re rnam rtse sogs gnas gzigs mdzad/ de'i tshe rje nyid ches
cher snyun tshul gyis gzhan gyis gdan 'dren dgos pa'i skabs de ltar na/ mdzod 'dzin sogs nas rang re'i gdan sa 'dir sku khams rim dngas par bzhugs na legs tshul sogs phyi
nang gsang ba'i gsung mchid du ma snyan du phul bas/ bka' las/ rang re gdan sa nas 'thon skabs kho bo da lam nad bab lci mo 'di ltar mchis rung / gdung sku mched kyi dbu
'don la nges par 'gro ba'i dam bca' de bzhin dang / mchog gsum la mchod cing bsnyen bkur/ gnas khyad par can rnams bskor zhing de dag gi me btsa' gso ba/ tha na mu to ba
sprang po yan gyi sems can la phan sems dang bcas/ nyin mtshan g.yel med mgo la me shor ba lta bu'i brtson 'grus 'di kho bo rang gi dam bca' yin pas/ da dung dus las yol
med byed pas/ khyed rang tsho sems las mi dgos/ rim dwangs yong zhes gsungs nas snyun tshul gyi ngal ba khyad du bsad de nyin mtshan g.yel med lta bur 'gro don kho nar/
brtson 'grus kyi phar phyin rdzogs pa'i thabs chos rgyal nor bu bzang po'i rnam thar la 'gran bzod pa ni rje de nyid la rnam pa kun tu mnga' 'o/ /de nas bzung phebs 'phyang
la rtag par phebs te snum rir bzhugs/ /nya mor gsol tsha dang se shing khar bzhugs/ sne bzhir gsol tsha dang zhang pa brag gdong du bzhugs dus 'bras skyed 'dus spyi nas
zhabs brtan gsol 'debs kyis mtshon/ spyi sger la mjal phyag bkag med du mdzad pa ni de skabs rnam pa kun tu'o/ /zhal ngo byings rnams

'bras skyed la'ang phebs/ de nas rin spungs su rdzong dpon sogs la tshe dbang lcags sdong ma dang / rta mgrin skyer sgang rjes gnang dang / rong byams chen du lam 'bras mgon
rkyang dang 'byung 'dul gyi rjes gnang / de nas mkhar tshor bzhugs/ sang nyin ngur smrig dang nye bar sa chen dang yum gyi phyag rjes pha bong la mchis par khrus gsol rab
gnas dus rje nyid kyis nam mkhar gzigs pas brtse ba chen po mngon gsum du byon byung gsungs/ ngur smrig g.yon 'gram gyi pha bong la sa chen gyis sku 'brum bzhes dus byung
ba'i sku rjes la'ang khrus gsol dang / ram par bzhugs/ sang sku 'bum du gsol tsha dang bsil du bzhugs/ de nas dpal de dang phan la rtsa/ sang nyin snga mor phebs nas
gam pa la rtser lha bsang rgyas pa dang / byang thang du bzhugs/ de'i sang phebs gru 'thon stag khu spe dang / de nas spos te skyed tshal du zhag 'ga' bzhugs shing khrom
dbang / gnas bcu'i rjes gnang sogs chos bka' dang spyi sger re skong mtha' yas pa zhig stsal zhing / der rje nyid kyi sku la dwangs bskyed bzhes pa'i 'go zug cing / gzim
chung der brtson 'grus mthar phyin yang rtse zhes pa'i sgo yig kyang thugs dges pa'i dbyings nas mdzad par dpags na brtson 'grus kyi phar phyin gnas der rdzogs tshul bstan
pa gdon mi za'o/ /de nas stag khur khrom dbang / chu shur gsol tshe'i thog thar pa gling pa sogs spyi sger mang po'i re skong dang / gsal byed rdor gling du bzhugs thog
sne shan pa dang dpal ldan bkra shis gdang / gong sa mchog nas mnyes spro le tshan gsum/ mtsham dar legs pa gsum/ khri chen bka' shag bcas nas kyang lha'i reg bya dkon mchog
gi grangs ldan re bcas thog mar dge ba'i gzigs bskyangs dang / de nas shel grong gsar gling nas gsol ston dang gnam du gsol tsha'i thog /yar klungs mchog sprul rin po

che dang zhal rgyas/ snye thang brag sna 'phags sder klong rdol bla ma sogs la rnam rgyal gyi rjes gnang dang / khrom dbang / bkra shis sgang du bzhugs nas sang nyin stod lung
mdar gsol tsha/ gsol tshigs sgang du dbu gur thabs su bcas sngon 'gro'i rtse mgron byings ba sogs rtse drung bcu skor/ khri chen mchog nas spos 'dzin pa sogs dang / bka'
shag nas gnyer tshang pa rdo rje sogs skya gras kyang gong mtshungs tsam nas chibs bsu lcang can du dbo zla'i nyer bzhir phebs pa nas/ lha sar zla ba phyed gnyis bzhugs/
gung dpon g.yog sde dge lcam zung sogs la sgrol dkar rjes gnang / rtse mgron bka' bcu lung rig /mchod dpon mkhan po/ /bka' mgron bya tshang ba sogs sger mjal grangs mang
dang / de nas rje nyid stod lung sman chab tu tshes nyer dgur byon 'phral rnam 'joms khrus bcas sngon 'gro'i chab zhugs mdzad ma thag nas sku khams rim dwangs yar zla'i
rjes 'gror mdzad/ chab zhag bdun gyi ring la nyin ltar sengge sgra/ chab klu/ lha bsangs rnams gnas des mtshon snod bcud kun la legs tshogs spel bar gnang nas/ dgon chu
bzang du grub rgyal ma dang / bla ma zhi khro/ phyag rdor gtum po'i rjes gnang bcas dang / sdings dkar khrom dbang rnam sras ser chen/ lam 'bras kyi mgon rkyang / phyag
rdor gos sngon can rnams so so'i re skong du stsal nas/ dngos grub sdings su rab gnas lha bsangs/ khrom dbang rnams dang / khong tshos bal po a su'i thod pa sogs byin rten
grangs mang zhig gzigs phul/ de nas rang re'i zhal ngo rnams dang / rtse shod kyi mgron gnyer sogs nas chibs bsus lcang can du phebs/ tshes bcur 'byor phyag dang / bcu
gnyis la mjal phyag dngos gzhi dang gong sa mchog nas tshe bka' dang khri chen nas phyag rdor 'khor chen yang gsan cing / gru 'dzin du phebs skabs de ring rgan bus

rta rtsal ngom rgyu yin pas ltos shig gsungs nas/ rdo skas ring mo de na yar chibs pa'i rmig pas rdo la 'thabs pa'i me stag 'phro bzhin pa dang bcas phebs skabs chibs pas rdo
la rmig rjes bzhag pa sogs ngo mtshar mang du gleng / sa ga'i tshes gcig la phebs phyag /de dag gi bar skabs su gser gdung gsar rnying gi drung du mchod 'bul dang / mchod
spyad ngo mtshar can yang sbyor 'jags gnang / gzhan yang phyi nang gi rten ji snyed par phyag mchod bsnyen bkur thugs smon gyi mtshams sbyor/ gong sa mchog gi bka' bzhin
jo bo rin po che'i sku mdun kye rdo rje la brten pa'i rab gnas rgyas pa sbyin sreg bcas dang / lha sa bla brang / ra mo che/ klu'i pho brang rnams su sengge sgra/ chab
klu/ bstan rgyas gling du kye rdo rje la brten pa'i rab gnas sgrub zhag gsum par phyi bskor du me tog 'thor gnang / sems dpa' rin po ches zhus ngor mkha' spyod ma'i byin
rlabs kyi tshe bdud rtsir ba~M yig rang byon du 'khrungs/ sde dge'i lcam zung sogs la lcags sdong ma'i tshe dbang / grwa tshang la grub rgyal tshe dbang ljags lung phon
chen/ lcang lo can du phur pa'i zhi ba'i sbyin sreg /mkha' spyod ma'i byin rlabs/ tshe dbang / tshogs bdag dang / phyag rdor dregs pa kun 'dul/ so 'brang rjes gnang / skye
bo khri phrag du mar khrom dbang / gzhan yang gzhis sde rme ru sogs su'ang khrom dbang thog che btsan phal cher nang dbang gras su bzhugs/ phur lcog dang sems dpa' sprul
sku/ rje drung a khu lags/ sku bcar mkhan po/ bka'i dgung blon chu mig /dza sag /dga' bzhi gung gi sras/ drung yig zung / mchod dpon/ mgron gnyer byings ltag /rtsa gnyer/
chibs dpon/ mda' dpon g.yu thog /sgrum rje/ khri chen gsol dpon sogs kyis mtshon

che phra spyi sger nas mjal phyag legs skyes sogs ni bgrang ba las 'das shing / khong 'ga' zhig la rnal 'byor ma'i byin rlabs dang / bde mchog nag po pa'i dbang / rig byed
ma'i rjes gnang / tshe dbang sogs kyis thugs 'dod kyi re ba skong bar mdzad/ bka' blon thon pas gdan 'dren dus rgya am pas thong si mngags te mtshams zhu sogs kyang bstar/
gzhan yang zhu ba po sna tshogs kyi ngor/ khro bcu/ sgrol dkar/ sgrol ljang ljags lung sogs dang / che gnyan de rnams kyis thog drangs rnam pa kun tu chos kyi gnad go ba
rnams la chos kyi de nyid/ las byed sne mo ba rnams la las byed de dang mthun pa'i gtam/ tshong pa rnams la tshong sogs gang la gang 'dul gyi thabs lam bzang pos bstan
'gro'i bde skyid spel gnang dang / bka' rtsom gnang ba/ thugs dam 'od gsal du 'khrungs pa/ phyi nang gsang ba'i lung / grub pa'i sa la zhugs pa'i rtags sogs mtha' yas so/
/sa ga'i tshes dgur lha sa nas chibs kha sgyur te/ yer par gnas gzigs bco brgyad tsam yod skad nas phal cher la zhabs bskyod/ de'i tshe dril bu phug par klu dbang bsrungs
pa'i sku gsar bskrun mdzad rgyu'i bka' grol/ de nas 'brom stod du gsung bskang smin rgyas bcas bzhugs/ nang pa mgar grong pa'i thog kha dang glang thang du yang lha bsangs/
khrom dbang / phyi skor la me tog /na lendrar bzhugs zhag drug dang phur dbang tshar gsum/ drag po sgrol dbang/ lam dbang / rnam bir rjes gnang / kye rdor rnam bshad
gsang sngags mdzes rgyan dang / ljags bsgrigs 'od zer dri med ljags lung / gzim 'og tu kye rdor rab gnas sgrub gnang gis/ phyi skor la me char nyil zhing / der 'jam dbyangs
dmar ser rjes gnang dang / sdom gsum rab dbye'i ljags lung / gzim 'og tu sme nag rjes gnang dang rong ston gyi gsung 'ga' zhig gi ljags lung / dpal ldan rtser

gsung bskang rgyas pa sogs bstan 'gro'i mdzad sgo rnams zin nas chibs bsgyur gyi nyin bco brgyad du gnang sbyin byin rten sogs mang po dang kye rdor rnam bshad/ rab brtan ma'i
zhal 'bag zho phye las sbrus pa'i gsol ba rnams gnang nas 'di gsum sku gsung thugs rten gyis slar 'dir nged rang thengs gcig sleb yong ngo / /zhes bka' stsal nas phebs
te lhun grub rdzong mdun du bzhugs shing / rdzong rtser rgyal khams bde thabs la ched du dgongs pa'i lha bsangs bcas mdzad nas/ shar sum mdor bzhugs/ chag la'i rtser yang
gong bzhin lha bsangs thog rje nyid la gzigs snang ngo mtshar can yang 'khrungs/ stag lung du grub rgyal tshe dbang zhig stsal nas gnas gzigs dang phun mdor bzhugs/ sang
nyin ko bar 'thon byang ra sgreng dang nye bar gsang ye'i pho brang du thab bsu dang bcas/ ra sgreng du phebs te jo bo rjes rgya gar nas gdan drangs pa'i 'jam pa'i rdo
rje'i sku drung du de'i sgrub mchod rgyas pa/ gnas ngo mtshar can de'i shug khrod nas phyi bskor la me char phab ste skye dgu de dag gi gtsug tu phyag gser gyi 'khor lo
ngal bsos te bzhugs sgar du phebs/ de'i sang gsang ye'i pho brang du mkha' spyod ma'i sgrub mchod/ ra sgreng gi gnas tshang yin khul bcom mda' dang / ko bar 'thon a dkar
sum mdo dang / 'bar tshag /nyi ma tshal/ ki ra thang rnams su bzhugs zhag re dang / gter sgrom chu tshan zhag lnga chab bdugs bcas phebs 'phral rnam 'joms dang / nyin ltar
lha bsangs rgyas pa/ chab klu/ tshe chog rnams dang / snron zla'i tshes gcig la lha mo gsol mchod kyi gsung bskang yang der mdzad nas/ phebs lam 'bri gung mthil gnas gzigs
dang grog sna zangs khar bzhugs/ de nas 'bri gung spro khang yang ri sgar du bzhugs/ de nas klong chen rab 'byams pa'i gdan sa zhwa lha khang du gza' dang dam can par
gtor bsngo bcas mdzad

nas/ dbu ru bka' tshal du bzhugs te/ klu mal dro gzi byin gyi pho brang mdun du ma 'ongs par skye 'gro rnams klu gza' rgyal gsum gyis 'joms par gsung yod pa'i lo rgyus stsol
ba dang bcas/ sengge sgra/ chab klu bcas smin rgyas bstan 'gro'i bde thabs su gnang nas phyed dkar du phebs te/ 'dus tshogs la rnam sras ser chen dang 'jam dbyangs dmar
ser rjes gnang stsal nas/ rim gyis mal dro gong dkar gyi rdor legs mgon khang sogs mjal zhing rgya ma sgrub rnying du bzhugs te/ zhabs brtan bskang ba sogs kyi lung dang
/ tshe dbang sogs stsal zhing / khri khar du tshe chog /kun rig /rnam 'joms byabs khrus bcas dang / de nas la mor bzhugs nas ko bar 'thon/ lo sems dpa' rin po ches chibs
bsus te lo dgon du zhag drug bzhugs/ gur drag /gshed dmar dbang / dkar bdud rjes gnang / bskang ba'i ljags lung sogs stsal/ phan tshun nas 'chams gzigs dang / kye rdor zhi
ba'i sbyin sreg /phyi bskor la rab tu gnas pa sogs mdzad nas gtsang thog tu bzhugs/ sang nyin ri bo dge ldan gnas gzigs thog sme brtsegs kyi khrus dang / grwa dmangs la
phyag dbang / rje rin po che chos dbyings su mnal sa yin zer ba'i mdar spyi sger gyi mjal phyag sogs grub ste tshal bde chen du bzhugs/ de nas tshal gung thang du khrom
dbang dang bla ma zhi khro'i dbang / 'bum mo cher phyag nas bcas dang / bde chen gnas gzigs rnams grub nas chang tshul du bzhugs/ tshes nyi shu'i nam phyed tsam la chibs
bsgyur te dgod kha la'i rtser nam langs phebs 'phral/ lha bsang rgyas pa stsal nas sngas 'gor bzhugs/ sang nyin g.ya' ma lung gnas gzigs dang bcas bsam yas su zhag bcu bdun
bzhugs ring mgon khang dang / lcog gnyis su rtag par gsung bskang dang / spyi sger

nas mjal phyag /'chams gzigs/ ljags lung / chos skyong sku phebs/ bka' rtsom dang gsung brtag /bsam yas dang 'chims phu'i gnas gzigs mtha' dag /rab tu gnas pa'i me tog 'bul
ba/ de dag gi snga phyi bar gsum du zhal bkod che phra rnams dang / srod dang tho rengs mtshan gung sogs su phur dbang cha drug /bde mchog lU nag gi dbang cha drug re/ grwa
sum brgya skor la rta mgrin yang gsang gi dbang / rjes gnang sogs ni bgrang ba las 'das shing / mchims phuu gnas gzigs skabs rje nyid la klu 'dul phug tu 'tsho rgyal
gyi zhal gzigs te lung bstan zhig byung gsung ba las/ 'di byung bka' ma grol/ lcog tu phyi nang gsang ba'i rten 'dzugs kyi tshe rje nyid kyi 'od gsal du/ chos skyong chen
po byon nas yon tan gyi rten de la lhag par dgyes nyams kyis 'di phye mar gyis bkang dgos gsung ba bzhin dang sdig khrab la bzo skyong yang mdzad pa sogs gnas der bstan
'gro'i legs spel rnams rim grub kyis/ brag kha rdzong mdun bzhugs sgar du bco brgyad sku mched/ bsam yas mkhan po sogs la lam dbang / lam zab phyi nang / bir bsrung phyi
nang sogs dang / 'on khri smon mgon khang du gsung bskang dang rab gnas/ de nas rgyal sras rin po ches chibs bsus 'on chos sdings su zhag bzhi bzhugs/ rgyal sras sogs la
rnal 'byor ma'i byin rlabs dang / sku rkyang la rig byed ma ngor lugs thun mong ma yin pa'i rjes gnang / zhal bsnyen dus bcas dang / tshur yang 'jam dbyangs chos skor gyi
byin rlabs dang / las gshin phyi nang gsang gsum zhu bar mdzad/ gnas der rab gnas rgyas pa'i thog phyi bskor la phyag nas/ rmor chen rin po che'i bzhugs gnas rgod tshang
du gsung bskang bla mchod/ lha bsangs/ sme brtsegs dang de'i grib glud/ sha brgya zan brgya/ brgya bzhi rnams bod khams

bde ba'i thugs bskyed can du ban tshang pa'i 'khor tshogs bcas kyis mdzad nas phebs lam du khrom dbang dang / brag kha rdzong mdun du bzhugs/ de nas rtse thang 'bras gling
du lha bsangs/ khro bcu'i rjes gnang tshar gsum/ ljags lung phon chen khrom dbang bcas dang / dga' ldan bkra shis chos 'khor dang lnga mchod la'ang phebs/ bsam gtan gling
gi kye rdor ba spu ma sogs gzigs te khra 'brug tu sengge sgra/ chab klu/ kye rdor rab gnas zhi ba'i sbyin sreg bcas dang / yum bu bla mkhar du mchod 'bul sogs mdzad nas/
bkra shis chos sder zhag bcu gnyis bzhugs shing / kye rdor/ bde mchog /gsang 'dus/ phur pa/ mgon po rnams kyi rab gnas/ mgon po'i zhi ba'i sbyin sreg bcas dang / kye rdor
dang kun rig dbang cha bzhi re/ mgon khang chen mor dus gtor/ sgrol dkar/ rnam rgyal/ rnam 'joms/ 'byung 'dul/ sengge sgra/ sme nag /sgrol ma nyer gcig rnams kyi rjes gnang
dang / lung mtha' yas pa/ rnam sras khang du rnam sras kyi bskang ba/ sku brnyan rnams la na bza' gsar sgron dang / 'on rgod tshang du gnang rgyu'i sku rnams phebs skyel
ba bkas 'doms pa sogs/ bsten mkhas kyi mdzad sgo rnams grub nas shel brag tu gur drag dang / gnam gang gi dus gtor mdzad rjes btsan thang du lha bsangs rgyas pa dang
/ de nas bye tshogs su lha bsangs rgyas pa/ lcog tu gsung bskang / chos skyong sku phebs thog zhal ngo so sor sku sprul pa mchog gi lung bstan dang / der kye rdor rgyu dbang
cha bzhi/ sgrol ma nyer gcig gi rjes gnang / rab gnas/ ljags lung sogs rgya cher stsal nas smin gling mkhan rin po ches chibs bsus/ smin gling du bdun phrag gcig bzhugs/
mkhan rin po cher dgongs 'dus sogs dbang byin rlabs lung phon mi chung tsam gsan cing / phar yang bla ma zhi khro'i tshe dbang

sogs stsal/ der tshes bcu'i thog 'dus tshogs kyi dbur phebs/ 'chams gzigs gnas gzigs sogs grub nas/ bye tshogs su byon te 'gro don rgya cher mdzad/ de nas gra thang du rdo
rje phur pa'i sbyin sregs rgyas pa dang / gsang 'dus dang kun rig gi dbang cha kha shas/ mkha' spyod ma'i byin rlabs/ phyag rdor khang brtsegs dang zhang blon gyi rjes gnang
/ sgar chen rin po che'i gdan sa dpal rab tu gsung bskang gsol 'debs sogs dang nyams gso gsar bskrun gyi bka' 'doms/ byams gling du kye rdor rab gnas/ gzhan yang ljags
lung phon chen khrom dbang sogs stsal nas gdung phud chos 'khor du kye rdor dbang cha drug dang / de'i rab gnas zhi ba'i sbyin sreg bcas/ mgon khang gtor spod/ gnas bcu/
phyag rdor u tsarya/ bcu gcig zhal/ gang blo ma/ gur drag dang khrom dbang sogs re skong rnams kyis dus 'das rjes/ ra ba smad du bde mchog nag po pa dang / kun rig dbang
cha bzhi/ lcog tu lha bsang rgyas pa/ 'byung 'dul/ spyan gzigs gtso 'khor gsum/ ri khrod ma/ sgrol dkar/ dzam ser nag rnams kyi rjes gnang / chu 'gram du kye rdor rab gnas
thog chu rags mgo mjug la me char nyil ba/ dus gtor khrom dbang sogs dang / de nas rnam rab tu lha bsang rgyas pa/ kun rig dbang cha lnga/ sgrol ma nyer gcig gi rjes
gnang tshar lnga dang / spyan gzigs/ sgrol dkar rjes gnang / kye rdor rab gnas sbyin sreg /rgyal po rnam gsum sku phebs/ sngar gyi gtor rnying spo gnang dang lcog tu gsar
'dzugs shig kyang gnang / khrom dbang sogs dang / rngog bsod nams bstan 'dzin gyi gdung rten/ dud sol ma bcas gnas gzigs dus dud sol ma'i sgos kyi gtor chog kyang gnang
zhing / de nas jo phug gnas gzigs dang gong dkar rdo rje gdan du zhag nyer gcig

bzhugs ring yang / nyin mtshan khor mo yug tu bstan 'gro'i legs spel 'ba' zhig gis dus 'da' bar mdzad pa las/ gtso che ba rnams smos na/ skya ser mang por dbu ma lugs kyi sems
bskyed/ rta mgrin yang gsang / khrom dbang rnams dang / phur dbang rab gnas thog phyi skor la me tog nyil ba/ gzhan yang yongs 'dzin dam pa rnams la chos gsan pa/ 'ga'
zhig la bla ma rin 'byung / tshar gsum khug pa/ lam sbas bshad/ mkha' spyod ma'i byin rlabs dang / de'i 'khrid/ dmar po skor gsum gyi be'u bum lung / de'i rjes gnang sogs
rjes gnang grangs mang / ljags lung yang de bzhin/ bshad sgrub gling / sku gnyer grwa tshang / bde chen chos 'khor rnams la'ang zhabs kyis bcags pa/ bstan srung rgya mtshor
rgyal bstan rin po che spyi bye brag rgyas pa'i phrin las 'chol ba/ mdor na ya mtha' bla ma dge ba'i bshes gnyen nas ma mtha' sprang po'i bar gyi re 'dod skong ba'i
dam bca' las g.yel ba nam yang rje dam pa der mi mnga' zhing / de'i tshe sne shan pa dpal ldan bkra shis la byin rten grangs mang / bdog pa'i dngos po gya nom pa bcas stsal
nas rang gnas su mngags/ de nas ta ra phur bzhugs dus bshad sgrub gling sku rten par sku phebs thog da bzod mngon du gyur pa'i lung bstan yang stsal/ sang nyin ta phul
rtser snod bcud spyi bye'i bde thabs la ched du dgongs pa'i lha bsangs dang bzhugs tshong khang da mar/ de'i sang nam phyed tsam la phebs lam shin tu rtsub par nam 'og
tu byon pas/ rgyus yod rnams kyi gleng mor rgyun du ni mi rengs yang mi thar ba lta bur mchis/ da lam dpon g.yog kun nam phyed she mun gyi dus su bde bar phebs pa las gzhan
pa'i rdzu 'phrul lhag tu mi dgos 'dra/ zhes sgrogs par gyur pa'ang don gnas kyi tshig yin lags/ de nas sga 'dra chu tshan dang nye bar rje nyid phebs

'phyang thog 'od gsal du 'khrungs skabs 'di ltar gsungs te/ khrums zla'i nyer bdun la mgyogs 'phyang thog 'don pa byed mur shul lam bgrod pas gnyid gzir re ba zhig byung bar/
rmi lam du byang phyogs nas btsun ma 'dra mo zhig gis/ sga 'dra'i gzhi bdag bsdad med pas res shig la shog gsung pa'i yi ge bri rogs mdzod/ zer bar/ nub phyogs nas bud
med dar yol dpral g.yu can kha shin tu che ba gdangs pa zhig thal mo sbyar nas mgo gug gug byed pa shar bas/ khyed rang gzhi bdag su 'dra zhig yin na'ang / sga 'dra chu
tshan dang nged la las 'brel yod pa zhig ni cis kyang yin 'dug rtags/ lo kha shas nas tshoms dkyil na chu tshan yod pa zhig bdugs pa rmi ltas shar ba mngon sum myong ba yin
'dug /ces gsungs shing / de'i ka ba lho ma bdag 'dzin mdzad/ cha bzhag lnga dang der yang lha bsangs rgyas pa dang / rjes gnang kha shas bsam mkhan sogs la stsal nas zangs
khrod du bzhugs/ de nas ri bo brag tu bzhugs dus khrom dbang dang / sang nyin snga bar dga' ldan ri khrod dang gling rdzong sogs brgyud/ stag lung du phur pa'i sbyin
sreg /dkar bdud rjes gnang tshar bzhi/ zhal bsnyen dus dang / tshe sgrub kha rag par gnang 'phral khong mig gsal du song ba sogs byin rlabs zhugs rtags gsal bar byung /
gzhan yang kye rdor rab gnas/ lha brgyad dang zangs gri can gyi rjes gnang tshar kha shas/ gying lnga gza' gdong dang tshe'i rdzong chung sogs chos bka' rgya cher stsal zhing
/ rdzong lha dbang rab brtan gling dang / gsang sngags chos 'khor gling sogs la'ang zhabs kyis bcags nas/ bsam sdings su phebs lam thog dus mchod bla brang pa'i gdung
rabs la gsol 'debs thugs la glo bur du shar ba dang / bsam sdings su phebs 'phral rje btsun sku zhabs kyi dpe khrod nas pod gcig bzhes pa gdung rabs chen mo phyag thebs
bcas ma 'ongs pa'i la nye'i rten

'brel gang yin mngon du 'gyur ro gsungs nas dus mchod bla brang gdung rabs sger la gsol 'debs kyang bka' rtsom dang / der lha bsangs/ rdo rje phag mor tshe dpag lha dgu dang
byings la khrom dbang / gzhan yang phag mor lha brgyad dang zhal bsnyen dus rjes gnang dang / tshur yang chos bka' phran bu gsan/ de nas sna dkar rtse'i mgon khang du gsung
bskang dang / mi sde spyis zhus gtor 'dzugs kyang gnang nas srin lag tu bzhugs/ sang nyin kha ro lar lha bsangs dang gnod sbyin rnam gnyis gsol mchod bcas mdzad cing
ra lung chu mdo'i rgya mon khar bzhugs nas ra lung gnas gzigs dang sne bzhir phebs/ au rgyan yang zab gling du kye rdor rab gnas dang / khong dpon g.yog la phag mo skor
gsum gyi byin rlabs rjes gnang dang / 'dod rgyal rjes gnang yang stsal zhing / tshur yang chos bka' phran bu gsan/ de nas rgyal rtse gur par lha bsangs/ rta mgrin yang gsang
/ phur dbang grangs mang / khrom dbang / rjes gnang dang lung phon chen/ rdzong rtser lha bsangs/ brtse chen mgon khang du gsung bskang / 'chams gzigs gnas gzigs sogs
spyi bye'i mdzad sgo rnams grub nas/ brtse chen gnas gzigs dang / 'brong rtser lha bsangs/ byad 'grol/ sengge gdon 'grol/ 'jam dbyangs dmar ser dang / lha chen srog gtad/
chab klu/ gur drag dang tshe dbang / khrom dbang / rab gnas sogs re skong rnams tshar phyin nas gnas gsar rgyal khang brgyud/ 'bras khud du sme brtsegs kyi khrus gnang
nas skyid sbug tu phebs te phyag nas dang / sang nyin nas skyin mkhar chab bdugs zhag lnga/ de nas bar tshor lha bsangs/ ku ru kulle lha lnga'i dbang / khrom dbang / mngon
dga' gnas gzigs dang / rab gnas/ 'byung 'dul rjes gnang sogs mdzad nas/ bde ba can du kye rdor rgyu dbang tshar bzhi/ khrom dbang rjes gnang sogs

mang du mdzad cing / lhas sdings su rab gnas/ zhi ba'i sbyin sreg /khrom dbang / lha brgyad rjes gnang sogs gnang ste pa nam rdzong brgyud/ dga' sdong dgon par bzhugs te gnas
gzigs khrom dbang / lha bsangs sogs gnang / de nas yul lha ba'i nang du zhabs kyis bcags nas/ pad tshal du rab gnas/ lha bsangs/ byad 'grol sogs mang du mdzad de zha lur
byon/ gling bskor la me char nyil ba tshogs yongs la dbu ma lugs kyi sems bskyed/ 'jam dbyangs dmar ser dang rnam sras mdung dmar can gyi rjes gnang / lung sogs phon chen
dang / gnas gzigs sogs don yod kyi mdzad sgo rnams tshar phyin nas/ ri sbug brgyud/ la rtser lha bsangs bcas ngor du bdun phrag gcig bzhugs ring gsang ba'i mgon khang
du gsung bskang / tshogs yongs la dbu ma lugs kyi sems bskyed/ tshe dpag med sprul sku/ sman bla/ gnas bcu sogs kyi rjes gnang dang / sdom gsum kha skong dang ngor gdan
rabs ljags lung / khrom dbang rnams dang / klu sdings su tshe dpag med sprul sku/ sgrol dkar/ rnam rgyal rjes gnang bcas dang / khang gsar du bla ma zhi khro/ thar rtser
rab gnas bla mchod sogs mtha' yas pa'i mdzad sgo rnams tshar phyin nas/ sred rgod du bzhugs te/ klu sdings sku gshegs kyi dgongs rdzogs mkha' spyod ma'i sgrub mchod mdzad
pa nas bzung zhe dgu nam rdzogs bar du bka' drin che/ de nas dge sdings su khrom dbang / rab gnas/ lha bsangs/ Da Dir yang khrom dbang ma gtogs de bzhin/ de nas dmigs su
sbyin sreg rab gnas/ mtha' bskor du me char nyil ba sogs dang / gra tshang par byad 'grol/ tshe dbang / gnas khang la phyag nas/ lha bsangs bcas mdzad nas bya gshongs su
byon te/ dbang lung rjes gnang gnas

gzigs/ rnam sras la gsung bskang / skye bo khri phrag du mar khrom dbang sogs rnam kun don yod kyi mdzad sgo rnams grub nas/ smin zla'i tshes lngar ram se lung du bzhugs/ tshes
drug la phu chen la rtser lha bsangs dang / de nas khams yul du gur dkar bsam grub pho brang nang / chibs bsu ba las chen pa zung gis thog drangs phyed gnyis brgya brgal
tsam la byin rlabs kyi zil dngar phab/ de nas a krol la rtser lha bsangs rgyas pa dang bcas rim phebs kyis/ chu kha ma'i steng du 'chams mgon rnams la snyan shal sgron
par mdzad de/ ser phreng dang gzhas sogs kyis sngun bsus/ gzhi thog pho brang du bde bar phebs te dga' ston gyi dpal la longs spyod par mdzad do/ /de'i sang tshoms chen
du legs ston rmad du byung bas dus 'das shing / de nas nyin bzhi mgon khang rnams la gtang rag dang / rtser lha bsangs rgyas pa dang bcas gzim chung mgon khang zung gi
gtor 'bul/ de nas rgyal dbang mchog tu 'bul rgyu'i zhal gyi 'khor lo dang chabs gcig 'jam mgon sku mched la'ang 'khor lo re stsol bar mdzad/ mgo zla'i tshes bzhi la mkhan
rin po che gsar pa khri phebs gnang rgyu'i gsum gyi tho rengs 'od gsal du/ mkhan gsar sbyin pa bkra shis dang gzhi thog rtser mjal bas/ rje'i gsung las/ 'o da lam mkhan
gsar la bu chung bgres pas legs so gyis gsungs 'di gnang byung gsung ba dang / nyid kyi sku hrag nas me long zhig gnang bar/ mkhan gsar nas 'di la tshigs bcad zhig rtsom
rogs zhu gsung bar/ rje rdo rje 'chang nas/ bde gshegs bstan pa'i lha lam rab yangs par/ /lung rtogs tsha zer rgyas pa'i dpal yon las/ /shes bya'i 'dab rgya 'dzum pa'i ze'u
'bru'i bcud/ /blo gsal bung ba'i sbrang rtsi dam par shog /gsung ba 'dra mo zhig 'thon song bas ma 'ongs pa'i rten 'brel zhig ni cis kyang yin 'dug /ces gsungs/ zla ba
de nang nas 'jam

mgon dpal ldan chos skyong 'di nyid lha mchog rdo rje gzhon nu'i ljags bsnyen la bzhugs pa'i skabs so/ /de dag gi don bsdu na/ dam pa chos kyi chol kha'i snod dang bcud/ /yangs
pa'i klong du kun bzang thugs bskyed kyi/ /chu 'dzin 'khrigs so dge mtshan gsang ba yi/ /byin rlabs zim char mi nyil gdeng ci zhig /chos kun bslu med rten 'brel che
ba yis/ /rang rang bde skyid sa bon smin pa'i 'bras/ /nyams dga'i glu gar 'khrol ba'i gzigs mo ru/ /ston gyi dpal mo'i lang tsho ngoms bzhin rgyud/ /mchog dman bar gsum mos
gus bang mdzod du/ /'brel tshad don ldan dpyid kyis phyur ro kye/ /'phags chen snying stobs brtson 'grus gces pa'i nor/ /bdag bzung nor bzang thugs bskyed las kyang brgal/
/gang zhig zhabs zung bskyod pas nor 'dzin steng / /bde skyid snum po'i me tog dgod byed na/ /rlabs chen spyod pa'i zer phreng g.yos pa'i mod/ /legs spel bstan 'gro'i
'dab stong cis mi grol/ /slar yang rigs lnga'i pho brang dga' ba'i tshal/ /ngo mtshar g.yur du za ba'i cho ga ni/ /lhun grub phrin las tshad med bla ma rje/ /rgyal kun
mkhyen brtse nus pa'i rang gzugs can/ /zhes kyang smras so// // ! dgung grangs nga gsum du byon pa lcags glang rgyal zla'i nang / rtsod dus 'gro ba rgyal sras gzhan gyis
'dul zhing du ma 'tshal ba'i mgon med yal bor rnams la lhag par brtse ba chen pos rjes su bzung ste/ dpag dka'i thugs bskyed smon lam bzhin thugs brtson chen pos myur du
mngon par mdzad pa bdag cag gi ston pa mnyam med shAkya'i rgyal po dang / rgyal sras thu bo dpal phyag na rdo rje/ rgyal ba'i nye gnas 'phags pa kun dga' bo/ bsil ljongs
mgon gcig padma 'byung gnas/ lo chen 'jig rten mig gyur bai ro tsa na/ grub rigs kun gyi gtsug rgyan rje btsun rin po che/ shes bya kun gzigs sa skya paNDi ta/ sngags 'chang
bdud kyi stobs

'phrog ngag dbang kun dga' rin chen/ de nyid slar yang rang rigs las grub pa'i brtul zhugs 'chang zhing / mnga' ris gtsang dbus khams sog mon 'brog kun la thugs rje che zhing
/ lhag par yar rgyab dpon sa'i gzhis ka dpal 'byor rab brtan char gtogs bcas gdul zhing du gzigs nas phyogs der gdan phab ste bstan 'gro'i don chen du mas rjes su bzung
mthar/ gzugs sku 'od gsal chos dbyings su bsdu bar mdzad pa'i rnam thar yang gdan sa der mdzad pa dpal sa skya pa chen po sgar chen mthu stobs dbang phyug rnams kyi snang
brnyan byin rlabs kyi gzi 'od 'bar ba gsar bskrun mchod tshogs dang bcas te/ sa phyogs de'i bde skyid la ched du dgongs pa'i thugs bskyed dang chabs gcig zangs ri gung
bkra shis rnam rgyal la phebs skabs bsu ba sogs legs lam gyi bka' 'doms dang bcas dpal rab tu stsal/ rta zla'i tshes gcig la bsam yas mi 'gyur lhun gyis grub pa'i lha lcog
tu rje nyid kyis gsar bskrun gnod sbyin tsi'u dmar po'i spu gsob la zhugs rang bzhes dang / dbo zla'i mjug nyi ma rgas nye zhig la'ang gang nas 'ongs cha med pa'i me phung
skad chen zhig 'thon nub dang byang phyogs su song ba'i sbir gtam mang du gleng ba sogs byung zhing / de'i nyi shur lha rdzong dgon gsar lu spe nor bu chos lung zhes/
sngon g.yag mi pham chos kyi bla ma'i dgon gnas gog po zhig la lhas rdzong pas nyams gso chos sde bcas btsugs shing / 'bru'i sngags 'chang bsod nams chos 'phel gdan 'dren
gyis chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba dang / yang yang zhabs kyis bcags pa sogs kyi gnas de nyid na grwa rgyun dang / grwa sdod 'os gzhan ma mchis pas/ de nyid kyis sngar rgyun
bzhin dgon par 'khra bzung bgyis pa legs sam/ da tsam dgon pa bsdus shing rten mchod rnams sa skyar drangs te sbyor 'jags dang / dge rgyun rnams mo dgon rin chen sgar
du sbyar na ji ltar legs/

zhes bstan srung rgya mtshor brtag zhu mdzad pas bsdus na legs pa stsal ba bzhin du mdzad pa dang / gzhan yang 'brong rtse nas zhus pa'i klu nor gyi bum pa'ang mang du bsgrubs
gnang gis stsal zhing / de nas 'jam mgon zhal rnam pa gnyis kyis gtsos zhal ngo bzhi dang / yar klungs mchog sprul rin po che/ ngor bla brang khag gi zhabs drung rnams/
bco brgyad sku mched sogs sa lugs bstan 'dzin drag bsdus rnams gtsor smos gzhis byes nas don gnyer can mang du 'dus pa'i tshogs la/ zab rgyas chos kyi 'khor lo rgya cher
bskor ba'i sngon du/ rje rdo rje 'chang yab sras rnams nas bstan srung rgya mtshor phrin 'chol yang dag dang bcas nyi ma me bzhi'i 'grub sbyor nas dbu bzung / 'chi med
rnga sgra/ dri med rnam gnyis/ rigs gsum spyi/ mi 'khrugs pa/ gza' yum/ a ra pa tsa na lha lnga rnams kyi dbang dang / lung la sde dge'i par phud gong 'phros ga pa nas dbu
tshugs par mtshams su gang 'gro/ jo bo'i chos 'byung brgya rtsa/ rin spungs skor gsum/ bka' gdams skor/ dri med lha lnga'i chog khrigs rin chen bsam 'phel/ dri med cho
ga'i lag len khrigs chags ma/ dri med rnam gnyis cho ga zung 'brel/ 'od zer dri med dkyil chog lhan thabs dbang chog bcas mun sel nyin snang / de'i dkyil chog gi kha skong
/ dbang chog bdud rtsi'i chu rgyun/ de'i gzungs las gsungs pa'i mchod rten srog shing 'dzugs chog /mchod rten bzheng tshul/ thig rtsa/ srog shing brtan chog sogs chos
char bar med du bskor ba'i thog /nag zla'i nang lcang can gung nor bu phun tshogs nas pha drug kha rtar rnam rgyal sku 'bum gsar bzheng mdzad rgyu'i phyag len pa de dus kyi
dbu byed che sar/ sangs rgyas kyi 'phel gdung dbang po'i grangs ldan gyis mtshon ring bsrel rnam bzhi'i gzungs/ 'dod gsol sogs gang ci'i

bka' 'doms kyis brgyan te pha drug tu mngags/ gung 'di pas khong ming zhus dus bu 'byung bar thag gcod mdzad pa bzhin byung ba'i mdzad pa ngo mtshar ba yang yod cing / de nas
lha chen mkhan po chos bkra shis kyi dgongs rdzogs thub dbang gnas brtan bcu drug sbyin bdag hwa shang rgyal chen bzhi dang bcas par 'dod gsol zhus don bzhin kha'u'i sman
chab nas stsal/ rim gyis dam ye dbyer med kyi cho ga bsgrubs te/ shab sgo lnga'i ya gyal Da zhes thabs dang Di zhes shes rab mtshon pa'i dgon gnas su bzhugs su gsol ba'i
bka' grol/ de mtshams nas rje rdo rje 'chang chen po de nyid ni rgyal sras byang sems chen po'i rnam thar lhur bzhes g.yel med nas/ snga sor bud med sems ma dpa' mo zer
ba zhig gis bdag 'chi bdag gi zhags pas zin pa'i tshe nyid kyi thugs rjes zungs shig pa'i gsol btab bzhin/ de nyid lnga lam du song ba'i g.yu byur spos shel lha gos dri
med sogs 'byor bas/ de 'phral lha rdzas la dmigs yul gyis mtshon lnga lam pa kun dal 'byor gyi rten dang mjal ba'i 'dod gsol dang bcas rje btsun sgrol mar phul te thugs
smon sogs 'di 'dra'i rigs snga phyi kun tu mang du 'byung ba'ang 'dis mtshon par bya'o/ /de'i tshe lha chen phun tshogs gling du gzim chung smon grub thar rtse sogs dang
khams pa shag sogs ar zug skabs yin pas/ de gras la phu gsum nas btsun ma gzhon nu zhig mchis par/ tshes bcu dgu'i nyin dregs byed zhig gis brlams tshul gyis cal col mang
du gleng ba'i dus/ thugs bskyed bla na med pas gong ma'i byin sna khrus chur sbyar ba dang / zas gos sogs gnang zhing / ci yin gyi rgyu mtshan dang bcas gsung shog zhig
stsal yang nges gsal ni ma byung / sa ga'i tshes gcig nas bzung gong 'khod kyi zhal slob sogs skal ldan bcu phrag lnga lhag tsam la/ rje btsun sa

skya pa'i yab chos bla na med pa gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa zab mo slob bshad kyi dga' ston stsol bar mdzad pa la rje nyid kyi gsan yig nang bzhin gyi
nyams khrid/ bla ma rgya bod nas bzung nyid kyi dbu bla'i bar gyi rnam thar pod dmar ser nag gsum/ lam skor phyi ma brgyad sogs cha lag dang bcas tshang ma/ nyer gsum nyin
sems bskyed chen mo/ de nas ril sgrub skabs ljags bsnyen dang / snron zla nas 'phro 'thud kyis/ bdag chen/ sngags 'chang / ngag dbang chos grags/ klu sgrub rgya mtsho/
a mes zhabs sogs kyi gsung ngag skor rnams dang / bar mtshams su gzungs gra lnga sogs dbang chen 'ga' zhig /rje nyid kyi ljags bsgrigs de'i dbang chog yang dbang chog bde
dga' rgya mtsho dang lhan thabs bcas kyi lung dang / 'ga' zhig la 'dod 'jo'i bum bzang nang gi rta mgrin/ drag mthing dregs 'dul/ bstan ma rnams lung bcas dang / tshe dbang
mda' 'phel sogs stsal to/ /gsung ngag gi tshe gro bzhin bcu bzhi'i tho rengs rje nyid la ngor chen rdo rje 'chang gi zhal gzigs te zhal slob ka bzhi gdung brgyad sogs
'byung bar lung bstan dang bcas dbugs dbyung gzengs bstod mdzad pa dang / rje nyid kyi gsung las kyang / tshar chen yab sras gnyis da lta dpon slob 'di khrod na yod/ ces
lung bstan pa dang / bdag med lha mo bco lnga'i tshe nang mchod 'khol zh-iing phyogs brgyar lud nas lag mi tshugs pa ltar tsha dbal dang bcas kun gyi mthun snang du mdzad
pa dang / bir bsrung phyi nang gnang ba'i tshe gdan sa'i rtsis bzung / skye re ba/ khang gsar mchod dpon sogs rtsis pa rnams mthun grub kyis nyi 'dzin yong bar thag bcad
sgo yig kyang sbyar zhing / don la'ang byed grub mthun par ri mos gtan la phebs pa'i tshe/ rje nyid grub mtshan

'jog bzhed gyi gsung las/ de ring nyi 'dzin yong bar thag chod de bzhin la/ rgan bu rnal 'byor dbang phyug tu langs rgyu yin pas khyed rang kun/ nyi 'dzin rtsis pa'i sgo yig
dang bcas pa la bltad mo ltos shig gsung ba dang mnyam du nyi 'dzin mi mngon dbyings su byin gyis brlabs pa sogs sa lam mthon por byon pa'i rtags 'ga' zhig 'di dus ston
par mdzad/ chu stod zla nang gong sa rgyal ba'i dbang po gang nas zhing 'dis mtshon/ mtha' dbus bstan 'gro'i srid zhi'i dpal 'byor la/ bka' lung yid bzhin nor bu'i shing
rta ci dgar bsgyur te/ grub gnyis 'dod dgu'i dga' ston gyi bskal bzang shar ba'i skabs su/ zhabs pad srid mthar brtan pa'i rten 'byung legs skyes/ sku gsung thugs yon tan
phrin las kyi rten rnams sngon 'gro'i sgo nas bzang dgu'i dngos 'byor rnams bstar ba dang / de sngon nas 'jam mgon sku mched la mi 'gyur phyag rtags kyi las tham che chung
re rje nyid nas gsar bskrun mdzad pa'i/ dam phud 'di ga'i rten ji snyed pa dang / de skabs rgyal dbang mchog sogs la'ang 'bul bar mdzad pa bcas mdzod 'dzin par bka' gsang
gis gdams nas/ 'dir phebs skabs gang ci'i gsung shog legs lam dge ba skyes bzang gis sba bas mtshon/ rin po che khams brgyad kyi dzhaikShiM las grub pa'i mkha' spyod
rdo rje btsun mo'i snang brnyan che chung gsum rje rdo rje 'chang yab sras zhal rnam pa gsum la dgyes stsal dang mnyam du/ rje nyid la phan khang dbon sogs nas nA ro mkha'
spyod kyi 'khrid sogs gser chos bcu gsum gsol btab bzhin gnang ba'i 'go zug dang stabs 'grig bcas rten 'brel gyi gnad khyad par can du 'grig cing / gzhan yang chu stod

can rnams la mchod pa bsnyen bkur/ dngos 'bul sogs yang dag mdzad cing / khong rnams kyang lugs zung gi bdag rkyen bzang pos rjes su bzung ba dang / lhag par tshe dbang rigs
mi 'dra ba kha shas dang / gdugs dkar nyer bdun ma dang / grwa lnga'i dbang tshan sogs brtse bas bskyangs mu dang / gong sa rgyal dbang mchog dgung keg snga bsur byon pa'i
sku gegs sel phyir/ gzim spyil dkar po'i bse mgon yid bzhin nor bu'i sku drung du/ 'jam mgon zhal rnam pa gnyis/ rje btsun drung ban tshang pa'i 'khor tshogs bcas nas
rje nyid kyi bka' bzhin gsungs bskang smin rgyas dang / zhag gsum ring 'dus tshogs su sde dge sa dbang la cung zad 'tshubs nyams 'khrungs pa sel phyir sku rim rgya che gnad
smin du 'doms par mdzad/ ring min nas rgyal dbang mchog gi thugs bzhed bzhin gnod sbyin tsi'u dmar po'i sku gsob gzungs rab gnas sogs cho ga rnam dag gis bskrun pa/ sku
tshab ched mngags kyi phul bas dgyes bzhes yang dag par mdzad ces thos lags/ de nas dmar po skor gsum gyi rjes gnang thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa/ dmar mo skor gsum/
