ldem dang 'grogs/ /

zhes kyang smras so// // ! dgung grangs nga bzhir byon pa chu stag /lcags byi dbyug zla lhag pa'i dbang du btang na gong bsam yas su zhugs rang 'bar dang zla dus mtshungs par/
ljongs 'dir bstan pa snga dar chos rgyal khri srong lde'u btsan gyi sku ring la/ bla mchod mkhan slob dam pa zhal rnam pa gnyis nas dpal bsam yas rgyal po'i dgongs pa
bzhin bstan 'gro'i dpal du gsar bskrun gnang rjes bka' srung klu ma dros pa la zhus pas ma gnang bar/ ma mo dang rgyal po rgya yul bkra shis khri sgo'i dong ka'i gtsug lag
khang nas ma mo dang / li yul lcang ra smug po nas rgyal po bkug pa'i ma mo khyung lung mar grags pa 'di ni/ sngon yab bdud rgyal mthong rtags dang / yum dmu bzhin mi
sdug la bu mo bzhi dang / ming po gcig 'khrungs pa'i a lce gnam sman dkar mo'am rdo rje rab brtan ma sogs mtshan gyi rnam grangs mang po dang / de 'og 'brog chen 'khor 'dul
sogs mtshan gyi rnam grangs can/ de 'og grom pa rgyang gi srung ma rgyang ma sogs mtshan gyi rnam grangs can/ de 'og lha mo 'di nyid ni dong ka'i gtsug lag khang gi 'phan
ring nag po la gnas pa slob dpon rin po che'i rdzu 'phrul gyi rten bcas bod du bkug te/ rgyal po dpe dkar dang lcam dral du mdzad nas bsam yas kyi srung mar bskos/ re
zhig nas zhang zhung rgyal po li man gyis/ mnga' ris stod du khyung lung dngul dkar gyi gtsug lag khang bzhengs pa'i srung mar slob dpon shIntaM garbha'i rdzu 'phrul gyis
bsam yas nas bdud mo gnas pa'i 'phan ring bkug /ming pos bsam yas su log byon/ lha mo rten la chags nas khyung lung du bzhugs pas khyung lung mar grags pa byang sems zla
rgyal gyis dmu rdzing du 'phan bcas spyan drangs pa 'dra ba'i 'phan byin can de yin nges na/ 'phan des mtshon dmu rdzing mgon khang rten brten par bcas la dge byed rgyal

zla'i nang rgyu mtshan med par zhugs bzhes kyis dmigs med du song bas/ bod gangs can la dus rtag shin tu gsal ba yin pa bzhin/ rje rdo rje 'chang chen po nyid kyi thugs la
bzod blag dang bral bas rgyal dbang rtse shod bla brang zhabs pad bcas su snyan sgron te/ rten brten pa bcas gsal bskrun rta zla'i brgyad tshul la tshar phyin mdzad de/ gos
nag lha mor bsgrubs pa bka' bsgo dam bzhag gi yi ge can/ rta mgrin yang gsang dang lha mo'i snang brnyan/ rnga rol sil snyan gos lhwam sogs dang / rgyun bskang gtong mi
bzhi gra rnams legs par 'doms so/ /rta zla dbo zla sogs la gzhungs mchog dang / bla brang zhabs pad sogs nas dmu rdzing skor sogs legs nyes kyi blang dor 'byed pa'i bka'
tshig gsal por phebs dgos rnams la'ang / gtso bo rgyal mchog lnga pa chen po'i lung bstan rgya chen dang / gter chen bdud 'dul gling pa'i lung bstan skor/ gter bdag gling
pa'i dag snang chu zla'i rol rtsed/ rdor brag rig 'dzin chen po'i dag snang skor sogs la zhib dpyod mdzad dgos nyi shar sgron 'degs kyi dpe'i sgo nas phul ba dang chabs
gcig /bka' bstan rnying ma rgyud 'bum tshar lnga bcuu nga lngar nyung mtha' byas pa gsung sgrogs sogs gnang ba ni/ rje nyid dgongs pa gzhan don du gtad pa'i lung gsal de
dus ka phebs shing / gzhan yang dmu rdzing du brgyad grwas bskang ba gnad smin gyi bka' dang / rje rdo rje 'chang yab sras sogs nas bskang phrin sogs dgongs dpyad kyis/
bstan 'gro'i bde thabs la ched du gzhol dgos kyi bka' rnams dang bzhes nas/ rgyal dbang yab sras kyi sku rim gtsor smros bse mgon yid bzhin nor bu'i sku drung du/ rje rdo
rje 'chang yab sras nas nyin re bzhin bskang phrin rgyun ring bar gnang skabs thams cad mkhyen gzigs chen po re zhig dag zhing du phebs pa gsan phral/ mchog gi sprul sku
rin po che myur phebs phrin 'chol zhu ba dang sbrags/ gangs can chos 'phel sogs na 'dzugs

bkod zhus pa'i gdung shugs gsol 'debs 'di yang / snga dro zhig thugs skyo lhang lhang gi ngang nas skad cig la mdzad/ de'i tshe bla brang zhabs pad mchog tu spyi sger rgyal
bstan rin po cher sri zhu dang / de 'dzin dam pa rnams kyi zhabs brtan sku rim du ched dgongs kyis/ snar thang bka' bstan rin po cher bar sangs nyams gso zhu dag sogs snyan
zhu bzhin/ 'phags chen dam pa'i rnam thar phan tshun 'gran pa lta bu'i sgo nas dang bzhes bka' drin che ba'i 'go brtsams/ gzhan yang gong sa yas phyin sde dge sa dbang
rnams nas/ mchod yon bstan lar dgongs pa'i bka' gsang ba'i skor snga phyi kun tu mang du mchis kyang 'dir de tsam dang / nag zla'i nyi shu skor la/ zur 'chad grub dbang
la sku khrus sogs 'bul bar khro khang du phyags phebs/ de nas se dkar rigs kyi thig le 'dar sde srid blo gsal tshe dpal dbang phyug ltos bcas la/ rnam pa kun tu thugs rje'i
rjes 'dzin g.yel med bka' drin che mu nas sa ga'i nyar/ tshar chen rin po che'i snang brnyan mi tshad ma sman 'jim las bskrun pa ring bsrel rnam bzhis phyur por btams
te byin rlabs kyi mtshan ma can dang / glo bo rgyal po dbang rgyal rdo rjes legs ldan ma zhi drag gi sku dang / sa bcud 'phel ba'i bum gter brgya rtsa byin rlabs kyi mtshan
mas phyug pa rnams thugs brtse ba chen pos stsal bas/ rgyal po dgyes pa'i rtser son te/ sA lu 'bras dkar khal mang po dang / gzig bcas phul ba'i gzig ni bsam yas chos
skyong la 'bul bar mdzad do/ /snron zla'i tshes gcig nas bzung gsang sngags bde chen gling gi grwa gras lhas brten pad rdor ba'i chos dpal 'byor/ ko chag rdzong pa ba dge
'dun dpal bzang / bar sdings bcu dpon pa'i kun dga' chos bzang / rgya mdud zhu ba'i dpal ldan yar 'phel/ bar sdings dpon ne ba'i blo gros chos 'phel/ sa skya don bkras
kyi rgyal mtshan rin chen/ khams dar mdo ba bsam gtan rin chen

rnams kyis gsol btab bzhin sprul pa'i lha khang chen mo'i thub chen dar bzhes ma'i drung du/ gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i gdams ngag zab mo tshogs bshad
'chad thang lnga pa'i zhal slob kyi gtso bo/ /gang gi rigs sras dam pa 'jam mgon e waM bzang pos gtso mdzad/ yar klungs mchog sprul sogs sa lugs bstan 'dzin drag bsdus
rnams dang / chos sde nyi zla rnam gnyis phal mo che/ thub bstan pa/ gser can pa/ 'bras yul skyed tshal ba/ chos lhun pa sogs kha shas/ rnam rgyal ser khang pa grwa gcig
sogs khyon bsdoms 'dus pa sum brgya dang brgyad la stsol bar mdzad skabs/ chos dung rin po che shar skya tsam la gsung bskul dang / skabs 'gar snga phyi bcas/ de skabs su
mkho ba'i zin bris shig kyang de dus kyi dbu byed che sar brtse skyong mdzad cing / phur sgrub skabs khyams smad lhor skal ldan rnams rjes su bzung bar gyur to/ /gzhan yang
snron zla'i nang gling tshang bla gsar gdong / sngon du sde dge sa dbang dgung lo bcu drug lon phyin khab bzhes skor bka' 'doms bzhin/ chu yos ston ra tha las ma 'gyangs
par dgos pa'i bka' gsang dang / bkra shis chos sde'i chog dkyil rnams par du bskrun rgyu'i gzhi mo rnams bcas legs par gdams so/ /bstan 'dzin de gras nas rje nyid kyi
bka' bzhin bco brgyad sku mched nas sgrub mchod kha shas dang / rtsa rgyud brtag gnyis/ phur sgrub sogs la gdan sa'i 'dus pa rgya mtsho'i dbus su phebs shing / khrums zla'i
yar tshes nas/ chos zhu ba rnams la dpal gshin rje gshed dmar po'i smin grol nyams 'khrid dang bcas cha tshang / sgrol dkar tshe 'khrid/ gsang 'dus lugs gsum gyi dbang
/ kun mkhyen rin po che'i bka' 'bum dang / dmar po skor gsum gyi be'u bum ljags lung 'phro can/ bskang ba'i skor rnams bcas dang / gzhan yang chos sde lho byang sogs chos
zhu ba ji snyed

par/ 'jigs byed bcu gsum mar lugs thun mong ma yin pa'i dbang grangs mang / sgrub thabs brgya rgyam/ grub chen brgyad cu/ snar thang brgya rtsa/ nyi sbas dang jo lugs sgrol
ma nyer gcig /mgon po'i dbang chen lnga dang de'i rjes gnang zab mo'i rigs rnams dang / phyi 'khrid 'phro can rnams gtso bor smos/ chos kyi 'khor lo nyin mtshan khor mo
yug tu ngal med bdag gzhan brje ba'i thugs bskyed kyi dam bca' g.yel med nas/ bskor bar mdzad pa 'di gcig pu'i sku drin yang bskal pa rgya mtshor khyer mtha' mchis min shes
ldan gzur gnas dag gis dgongs 'tshal lo/ /de ltar na rje 'di snyigs dus kyi rgyal ba gnyis pa 'jam dbyangs mi'i zol can mngon sum yin pa'i gtan tshigs kyang kun dang mthun
grub tu 'di lta ste/ nyin mtshan bar med du chos 'khor ji snyed bskor ba'i tshe'ang / gzhan dag ni yun ring du dpe sbyong sngon 'gro'i sgo nas chos 'chad la 'jug kyang
/ rje 'di ni gsung ngag slob bshad kyis mtshon dbang khrid rjes gnang kun/ dpe 'di dang 'di lta bu'i thog nas yin no zhes 'doms pa mtshon byed dpe spyan lam du phab tsam
las gzigs yul ye mi dgos shing / phyag len rnam dag gi rgyun ma nyams pa gsung lam kho na nas shar mar gsung rgyun phyag len bcas 'di dang 'di lta bu yin no/ /zhes 'doms
pa dang mnyam du stsol bar mdzad pa'ang deng sang gi skye bo kun la rlung ltar grags pa 'di'o/ /dbyug zla bkra shis zla gang bla brang zhabs pad mchog gi bka' bzhin/ sgo
rum ye shes mgon po'i sku drung du/ gang gi rgyal tshab dam pa 'jam mgon zhal rnam pa gnyis rgyun thebs dang / bco brgyad sku mched nas bzung dge 'dun res bskor gyi brgyad
gras bskang phrin gnad smin zhu dgos bka' gsang gi 'doms nas grol 'phral rtags bzang ngan rnams kyang gab sbas dang

bral bar phul zhing / /de'i tshe gan rdzong du mi dge ba'i mtshan ma sogs la blang dor gsol ba bzhin/ sngon gyi lo rgyus las 'phros pa'i spang blang dang / rdo sku khyad mtshar
can gdan sar gdan drangs nas nyams gso rab gnas kyi mnga' gsol dang bcas slar gan pa rang du bla ma bsnyen song nas spyan 'dren mdzad/ zla ba de nang nas rje nyid kyi
thugs bskyed bla na med pa'i gras su gyur pa bya khra ma'i shar brgyud/ ma thang rten brten par bcas gsar bskrun gyi las 'go brtsams te/ mi ring bar ma skor rnams la rab
tu gnas pa'i me char dang / de'i bcu dgu'i nyin zur 'chad grub dbang bde bar gshegs/ de nas drug cu pa'i zor 'dzin sngon 'gro'i ljags bsnyen zla gang mar thugs gzhol te/
zor 'phen sogs lugs 'gro gnad smin du bka' drin bskyangs shing / mgo zla'i nang pas se phyag rdor skyabs kyi bsngo 'bul ba sog po rnams la lugs zung bdag rkyen yang dag
dang sbrags lcang skya rdo rje 'chang nas gsung bris rten ldan gyi bka' lan dus gsum gnas tshul las 'phros pa'i bka' gsang rmad du byung ba'ang legs par gdams shing / zla
mjug nas lha mchog rdo rje gzhon nu'i ljags bsnyen zla gsum mar thugs gzhol ba'i skabs so/ /de dag gi don bsdu na/ ye shes byin za 'bar ba'i 'od snang gis/ /blang dor spu
ris phyed pa'i brda zhig bsnyad/ /ma 'dres gzigs la gangs can skyabs gnas kun/ /phan tshun bzang ngan shan 'byed drang thig 'debs/ /smin grol gdams pa'i nor bu thob pa'i
'dzum/ /skal ldan gdul bya mang po yang yang dgod/ /dregs ldan rgyal po pe dkar 'dod pa'i snod/ /don ldan re bas phyur mkhas drin can rje/ /mchod zhing mtha' la 'gro drug
sgrol ba'i rten/ /grub pa'i snyan grags thos tshe mtha' sogs g.yos/ /zhi bas mi dul zhing bcu'i bstan dgra kun/ /drag pos tshar bcad rjes 'dzin sgrub la gzhol/ /

zhes kyang smras so// // ! dgung grangs nga lngar byon pa chu yos rgyal zla'i tshes gnyis la gnya' nang go thang pas/ bal yul gyi gnas tshul las 'phros pa'i gsung brtag gis
sa bon 'byor rgyu'i tho rengs 'od gsal du/ bud med rgan mo lus chas 'chor can zhig gis srang dbar zhig tu byis pa chung ngu zhig bzhag nas/ phar logs thang ka zhig bskyod
mo rang gzhan zhig la dbang yod byed la 'gro rgyu'i khul la/ btsun ma zhig dang 'phrad pas/ btsun ma de rgan mo der 'dzem nas song ba dang / byis pa thal phyur ba gsum
nas khyi phrug skyes byung tshad rdo brdung btang nas gsod rgyu yin/ zer ba zhig 'khrungs pas/ bal yul la lho nub nas nyi ma shar ba snga mo nas 'khrungs pa'i lo rgyus dang
bcas zhib gsal du stsal zhing / zla mjug zham 'bring ba rnams la bka' 'doms kyis gnas bcu'i rten ji snyed pa rnams la rje btsun sa skya pa'i gdung rabs myur 'byon gyi
ched du dgongs/ rngul sprugs dang sbrags na bza' gsar sgron dang / rta zla'i nyar mchod 'bul rgya chen/ dge 'dun bsnyen bkur/ ngan slong sbyin gtong / brgyad stong pa dang
kye rdor sgrub mchod/ dri med bshags rgyud mtshan 'don rnams dang / khyad par nyam thag phongs pa'i 'gro ba rnams thugs rje'i spyan ras kyis ma bor nas/ ngan slong sbyin
gtong ni snga phyi kun tu grangs med rnams bka' gsang gis 'doms shing / zla ba der 'jam mgon dbang gi mtshan can nyid tshe mtha' yas pa'i ljags bsnyen zla gang ma'i skabs
dang / rje rdo rje 'chang nyid la ltar snang tsam du zhabs 'bam dang chab bsags sogs mtha' ma'i snyung gzhi'i 'go zug pa nas bzung / rim gyis sku khams je zhan dus spyi
sgos mtha' dag nas zhabs brtan sku rim rgya che rgyun khyongs mdzad dang mdzad mu'i/ zla sked tsam nas rje nyid kyi bka' bzhin sAtstsha 'bum ther gdab pa bde mchog tu zhabs

brtan mchod rten gyi nang gzungs su 'bul gnang dang / de'i tshe lha chen pa sogs dge 'dun 'ga' zhig la tshe lha gsum gyi bsnyen sgrub/ gzhan yang gsung sgrogs/ gtor ma sogs
bka' stsal rnams tshar phyin gnad smin du bsgrubs pa dang / dbus kyi chos skyong khag gi lung gsal rim gro dang / mo rtsis kyi spang blang spyi dang / phyi rten sku 'bum
dang / rig 'dzin pho brang / brtse chen lha khang bcas kyi rgya skar steng du bya rog gi tshang bsags pas g.yas ru byang gi spyi mtsho skya mo'i mtsho sgo yang skya bo kha
gdangs la zhugs pa/ gnod sbyin rtsi'u dmar po'i lung du/ bsod nams kyi zhing sa dam pa de/ /'od nub phyogs su 'phro bar mi 'gyur ram/ /zhes gsungs pa dang / bsam yas su
bla ma dam pa'i bla shing sdong po chen po la zhugs rang bzhes dang / mo lung du rgyal po gdan nas bskyod pa zhes bya bas bla ma bzang por dogs tshul/ gling gi mun nag
g.yogs mo rtse ma 'thon pa sogs rje nyid dgongs pa gzhan don du gtad pa'i snga ltas shar ba'i zhabs brtan sku rim dmigs bsal rnams la 'bad 'bungs ngos/ dbo zla'i zla mjug
sku rim chen mor yang ma phebs na ji ltar lags/ zhes snyan zhu mdzad pa'i phyir phebs su/ spyir lhag pa lha'i ljags bsnyen yang dag don ldan snyun gzhi thu mo de lta bur
ji snyam du yang mi sems par sku srog phongs med du mdzad pa'i 'bras bu mthar phyin pa dang / yang sgos rje btsun sa skya pa'i gdung rabs phyis 'byung 'di bzhin mdzad mkhan
rnams la sri ngan gyis mi brdzi ba'i phyir/ da lam cis kyang phebs dgos gsungs te/ phur bzlog gi tshogs dbu rdo rje slob dpon gnang skabs kyang ngo mtshar rdzu 'phrul
gyi mdzad pa 'di ltar mthong ste snyun gzhi de lta bu la ni/ 'jig rten na skye bo phal mo che drag gzhan ji snyed pa dag rnga rol me nyi sogs spang bya dang / zas spyod
sogs 'phrod bsten 'dzol med

bgyis kyang ngal ba 'bras med du song ba mang zhing / rje rdo rje 'chang chen pos de dag rnams la blang bya lta bur mdzad pas gnas skabs de'i tshe ci yang ma skyon khar cung
zad bder song ba'i tshul gyis gtor bzlog mthar phyin du gnang ba 'di ni/ grub pa mchog gi sa la bzhugs pa'i mdzad pa 'di lta bu'o zhes skye dgu kun la 'doms par mdzad pa
dang chabs gcig chos kyi phyir du sku srog phongs med de tsam du ma zad rnam pa kun tu bzhi mdo'i rtsa bzhin 'dor bar mdzad nas/ skad cig tsam yang dal bar mi bzhugs pa'i
brtson 'grus kyi phar phyin rdzogs pa'i thabs zab mo las nam yang g.yel ba med pas/ gdul bya mtha' dag la brtson 'grus kyi lcag gis bskul ba 'di las gzhan du ma dmigs
lags/ ljags bsnyen gyi skabs dge mi dge'i mtshan ma mang du 'khrungs pa ni gor ma chag kyang / rje rdo rje 'dzin chen po de ni/ 'jam mgon bla mas/ chu phran rtag tu ku co
che/ /rgya mtshos ca co ga la sgrog /ces gsungs pa ltar gnas skabs dus skabs dang bstun par mdzad nas gzhan dag la cher bka' mi stsal zhing / nyid kyi gsung las kyang /
kho bo'i gsang gtam logs su 'chad par spro ba'i gsung mu bzhin snga phyi kun gyi gsang 'os 'ga' zhig /rje nyid las gzhan du cher ma grags sam snyam zhing / 'on kyang ljags
bsnyen de'i skabs shig mi dkar po zhig gzigs skar nas 'ongs te rje nyid la mtho mtshams byed nyams 'di ni snga mo zhig nas resaX meX phungaX duX sprulaX/ res mi gzugs su
byas te 'ong skad thos pa de'i cho 'phrul zhig yin 'dra zhing me phung du byung ba'i tshe gzhan thabs gang gis kyang kho mi 'gro zhing rje nyid nas rtag chad mtha' bral
dbu ma chen po'i dbyings su mnyam par bzhag 'phral me phung de gzigs skar la song ba zhig snga mo nas byung ba dang / yang dngos nyams dang 'od

gsal 'dres pa lta bu'i ngang du rje nyid kyi gzim mal drung mtho mtshams byed mi ban gzugs can zhig byung ba la/ de ma thag rdo rje rnam par 'joms pa'i thugs rgyal gyis sna
tshogs rdo rje gnod byed de'i mgo bor bsnun par mdzad pas/ kho dus chos su gyur pa zhig 'khrungs pa ni rje btsun sa skya pa'i bstan srid la gnod cing 'tshe bar byed pa'i
rgyal 'gong zhig mo brtag sogs su 'byung ba de bsgral bar mdzad pa ni the tshom dang bral/ gang ltar phur bzlog sbyin sreg zhag bdun ma bcas thugs brtson che bskyed ngal
ba khyad bsad 'phags chen byang sems chen po'i rnam thar ngo mtshar rgya mtsho'i sgo nas/ gegs med mthar phyin du mdzad de/ gzim chung gzhi lam 'bras dus smin grol dpal
'bar du gsung bskang smin rgyas thog /tshogs kyi 'khor lo'i dga' ston rgya chen po la rol par gnang zhing / mgul la bkra shis pa'i lha'i reg bya khyad mtshar can dag gis
spras nas/ gzim chung der mchis pa'i 'phral gyi nye mkhor thugs tshags mdzad pa rnams kyang so sor ngo sprod sogs mdzad de/ sku'i 'phrod bzhes la lhing chags gnad bsnun mdzad
rgyu'i dgongs rtse mngon du gtod par gnang ste/ nag zla'i tshes gcig nas tshoms dmar mkha' spyod du phyags legs par phebs/ 'phrod gzhes rnams dang / spyi sgos nas zhabs
pad yun brtan gyi bgyi ba mtha' dag 'bad pa chen pos zhus kyang / sems can las ngan spyod pa la/ /sangs rgyas kyis kyang ci byar yod/ /ces gsungs pa bzhin/ las ngan dus
su bdo ba'i sems can gyi spyod pa ma rungs pa rnams la rje rdo rje 'chang nyid kyang thugs khrel nas dgongs pa gzhan du gtad pa la mngon du phyogs te/ res ni sku khams
kyang bstar chags dang / res ni je zhan bcas sku byug /gsol sman/ gsol zas/ sku rim rnams 'thud ma shor bar bka' drin che skabs rnams su'ang / skal ldan rnams la rjes gnang
zab mo'i

rigs sum cu kha yar/ dud sol ma'i be'u bum gyi ljags lung sogs dang / khyad par zhal ngo rnams kyi dbu g.yas phyag gnyer sogs drag bsdus ji snyed par bzhugs khri padma can
gyi steng nas rnam sras ser chen gyi rjes gnang gzabs ma'i thog nas stsal ba'i tshe/ so sor 'byung 'gyur hur bskyed mdzad dgos kyi bka'ang grol ba dgongs gsal ltar dang /
gzhan yang ston smad kyi bla tshong khag ji snyed par bka' slob snga rabs kyang zhib rgyas 'byung 'gyur dang bcas dang / spyi sger dad can rnams la mjal phyag /zhags 'chags/
bka' rtsom/ gsung bris/ rnam sras bskang phrin/ sku rim gyi ljags bkod/ gnod sbyin 'khor lo mang po'i sgrub pa/ rje nyid kyi 'dra sku rin po che byes log bzhis brtan
zhes rje nyid nas mtshan gsol zhing / dar gling grub dbang la ma stsal bar 'jam mgon mchog la stsal ba de'i rten 'brel gyis rjes su mang mkhar nas sa skyar byon thub pa'i
yin snyam kho bo sems pa sogs la phyag nas rgyas pa/ las bzhi'i sbyin sreg phyag rdor gtum mo'i dug dbyung rgyun ring bar/ ring mo'i dus nas rje nyid kyi thugs dgongs thun
mong ma yin pa gro bzhin badzra kI la ya'i sgrub mchod thogs 'grems par mdzad rgyu'i nor phreng phye phur sogs gos bzang dgu las grub pa'i/ mchod rdzas 'di rnams bkas
'doms shing spyan lam du'ang gzigs su gsol ba/ sde dge gnyer chen mgon tsher lugs zung gi bdag rkyen yang dag pa'i thog /rgyal sras mchog la khab bzhes skor sogs phyi nang
gsang ba'i bka' stsal du ma dang / chos lhun grwa pa zhig la dregs byed rdo rje shugs ldan rtsal glo bur khog brlams kyis de ga'i gtor bzlog 'phen dgos kyi lung bzhin
ljags bsgrigs thog de bzhin mdzad pa sogs/ snyun babs lci mo de lta'i gnas skabs su'ang / ngo mtshar dang bcas bsten mkhas kyi mdzad pas dus 'das rjes/

ma 'ongs mngon sum du gzigs te/ tshoms dmar mkha' spyod sogs bkod legs kyi bka' 'doms ni/ spur bzhu'i gnas dang / pho brang la zhig gso'i skabs sku chas 'jog par dgos so/ /zhes
gsungs rgyur gor ma chag /de nas kha'u sman chab la phebs 'phyang thog sku bskyod kyi tshe kun rar drag bsdus rnams nas rje nyid la mjal dar bstar ba'i tshe'ang bka'
gsang so sor grol mur/ lha bris dbu byed la/ kho bo'i 'dra sku 'dra mang du bzheng dgos yong bas ngos kyi gdong la yang dag ltos shig /ces bka' stsal/ kha 'ur dga' bo chu
tshan chab bdugs skabs kyang sku khams res 'jog kho na dang / thog steng du snga dro lha bsangs/ sengge sgra/ chab klu bcas rgyal khams lo rim la ched du dgongs te rtag
par gnang / snron zla'i lha mo mchod kyang rdo chu'i steng du ji bzhin gnang rgyu'i tho rengs/ sku khams shin tu nyog pa de'i tshe/ dpal ldan lha mo nyid kyi dngos su zhal
bstan nas lung bstan mang du stsal mthar/ gzims lugs de ltar ma mdzad par/ krong gis dbu mnyel sku rgyab gtad de gzims nam gul glo chung ba yong / zhes kyang gsung ba
dang / de nas nyin gcig sa skyar bzhugs tshe'ang gzhi thog ser khang steng du lo rim la ched du dgongs pa'i lha bsangs sengge sgra/ chab klu sogs thams cad kyang 'phags chen
byang chub sems dpa' bdag bas gzhan gces kyi rnam thar lhur bzhes kho nas dus 'da' bar mdzad pa ni deng sang kun gyi thugs gsal ltar dang / de'i sang nas mang mkhar sman
chab la phebs lam sgrol ma lha khang la gnas gzigs dang / g.yas bskor gyis/ zhal mjal phyag dbang sogs bkag med phebs 'phyang thog nas stsol bzhin par shel phreng la
brgyud rgan mo kha dron zhes par bzhugs nyin de ni/ sa skya'i thad nas lho nub phyogs su 'ja' dkar po shing sdong chen po lo 'dab rgyas pa lta bu zhig dang / me tog gi char

nyil ba sogs kun gyi mig gi bdud rtsir byung ba dang / gzhan yang lha kha ma sogs kyis/ dpa' bo mkha' 'gros gdan 'dren mdzad kyin 'dug zer ba sogs byung zhing / de'i sang thub
bstan dge 'phel dar gling sogs nas ser phreng gis sngon bsus te/ dge 'phel du gsol tsha'i thog zhabs tog rgya cher bsgrubs shing / rim gyis chab gdugs skabs kyang sku
khams thog mar res 'jog dang / de nas je zhan bcas/ gnas der yang gdul bya spyi bye brag gi skal ba dang 'tshams pa'i mdzad pa ni sus kyang bzlog med du bka' drin bskyangs
shing / lhag par yul phyogs des mtshon rgyal khams bde skyid la phan pa'i lha bsangs/ seng ge sgra/ chab klu sogs nyin re bzhin rtag par mdzad pas de lo yul phyogs der
lo legs pa dang / phyi lo chu bzang ba sogs rgyal ba'i mdzad pa nyi shar spar mos mi khebs pa'i dpe bzhin kun gyis gleng pa 'di bzhin dang seng ge sgra sogs gnang ba'i tshe
nyin re bzhin sbrul mang po sku'i gam du 'ong ba dang / rtsig pa'i seng nas sbrul chung ngu mang po rje nyid kyi phyogs su mgo bteg nas 'dug ste slar gsung chog grol
nas gar song med pa ltar nyin ltar gyur ba'ang der yod kun la rgyus yod cing de dus bla brang zhabs pad/ shel rdzong / lha rtse rdzong / mang mkhar khul gyi drag zhan mtha'
yas pa sogs nas kyang chab gsos kyi legs skyes tshar du dngar ba dang / zhabs pad yun brtan gyi gsol 'debs zhus shing / dza lung mthu stobs dpal 'byor nas kyang dug dbyung
dang tshe dbang chag med du phul/ seng dbar rnams la gang gi rigs sras dam pa 'jam mgon gong ma rin po che nas gro bzhin badzra kI la ya'i sgrub mchod skabs/ legs bshad
kyi bdud rtsi stsol bar mdzad rgyu'i sngon 'gro'i mtshams sbyor ljags rtsom du mdzad pa 'di ni/ rtogs brjod rin po

che 'di'i phyi mo lta bur shar ba dang / ljags rtsom gyi phyi ma rang yin lags/ de nas phebs te thub bstan dge 'phel du bzhugs nas/ rje btsun rin po che'i snang brnyan lung
bstan sku 'dra rin po che'i drung / de'i bla ma'i rnal 'byor dang sbrags rje btsun sa skya pa'i gdung rabs rin po che srid mtha'i bar du byon nas bstan 'gro'i mgon po mchog
tu 'gyur ba'i thugs bskyed rgyal sras kun tu bzang po'i ngang tshul can du mdzad pa dang mnyam du/ sku de sku pang du gdan 'dren skabs rje nyid la ring bsrel gnyis tsam
byon zhing / mgon khang rten rnams dang tshar chen rin po che'i snang brnyan sogs la'ang gong gi mtshams sbyor de bzhin dang / tshogs bdag kyang mdzad cing / de'i nub
mo ni sku khams ches cher nyog cing / tho rengs kyi char gsung lhang lhang gi mur rje btsun rin po che phebs byung bzhugs stan things gsung ba dang / yang skabs 'gar rje
btsun rin po che gdan 'dren zhus shig gsung ba dang / skabs 'gar dza lung pa sku mdun du myur du gdan 'dren zhus gsung pa sogs 'khrungs snang mtha' yas pa'i mur 'byams/ de
nas gzhi bdag sho dmar bar gsol mchod dang bcas sngar gyi rgan mo kha dron du bzhugs/ de'i sang 'phrang phur bzhugs dus rlung chen po ldang ba sogs 'tshubs nyams kyang
'ga' zhig byung zhing / de nyin gza' skar yang 'jam pa bcas rje nyid kyi rtogs brjod rin po che dbu tshugs tsam zin bris phran bu zhig mdzad pa ni/ 'di dang 'di lta bu dgos
so zhes 'doms par mdzad pa yin grang / de'i sang snron zla sngon ma'i nyer drug nyin lhun grub ldengs su zhal ngo rnams dang / chos zhu ba sku drag rnams bcas nas chibs
bsus/ mnga' zhabs kyis gzhas/ ser phreng sogs legs lam bzang po dang bcas gdan sa chen po'i gzhi thog pho brang du phebs skabs/ khyad 'phags byang gi them skas la 'chel
bzhugs yun ring tsam mdzad nas/ skye dgu kun zhal dkyil la longs spyod du 'jug

par mdzad de gzhi thog pho brang du phyags legs par phebs nas/ sku ngo tshang ma zhal rgyas thog gang ci'i phyi nang gsang ba dus gsum gyi gnas tshul dang bcas ji bzhin gsung
ba dang / phyag gnyer gsol gzim mchod sogs gzhan ma rnams la'ang gnang cha gya nom pa dang bcas so sor snga phyi bar gyi gsung gleng ji bzhin mdzad de/ dus gtor sogs la
thugs gzhol ba'i skabs so/ /smras pa/ skyabs kun 'dus pa'i nor bu'i za ma tog /phyi rol 'dod 'jo'i dpal du shor dogs kyang / /mi dman bsod nams ldan pa'i ded dpon gyi/
/lag tu son pas cung zad yid dbang bde/ /'on kyang snyigs dus sems can dbul po'i lag /ji ltar brkyangs kyang bsam 'phel mi 'byung dang / /byung yang yun du mi gnas gna' bo'i
gtam/ /bden par nye ba'i dus shig shar min nam/ /ji bzhin dpyad tshe snang tshul thams cad kyang / /gzhan don nye ba'i gong ma'i rnam thar dang / /mthun pas thabs brgya'i
'phrul la kun gus kyang / /ngan spyod khrel bas dgongs pa mngon du phyogs/ /zhes kyang smras so// // ! rtsa ba'i sa bcad lnga pa zhing 'di'i gdul bya re zhig rdzogs
nas mthar sku zhi ba mchog gi dbyings su thim ste dgongs pa zab mo rdzogs thabs rnams mdzad tshul ni/ de nas snron zla phyi ma'i tshes gcig gi bar du thugs dam nyams bzhes
rnams chag med dang spyi sgos nas zhabs pad yun brtan gyi gsol 'debs/ gsung bris/ zhal bkod sogs kyi skabs su'ang gdul bya'i blo sna 'khrid pa'i phyir du rje rdo rje 'chang
chen po nyid kyi sku la skyon mi yong ba'i gsung 'ba' zhig snga phyi kun tu byon pa dang / khyad par gzim chung skor gyi rten rnams sku mdun du spyan drangs/ re re nas
phyag bzhes kyi sngon byon dang rje nyid kyi phyag babs rnams so sor ngo sbrod dang / bla ma gong ma'i rten sgam rnams kyang zhal phye nas so sor 'di dang 'di zhes bya
ba'i ngo sprod sogs mdzad mu'i srod tho rengs kyi cha 'ga'

zhig gsung dar dir gyi ngang du/ sa skyar phebs dus na bza' gzabs ma dang bcas phebs dgos gsung ba dang / nged kyis sa zhu kha gsar sum brtsegs su bzhes yod gsung ba dang /
rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan zhes yang yang gsung ba dang / rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan byon nas dbang bskur mdzad kyin 'dug gsung mur thugs
zag med kyi bde bar 'byams pa sogs ni dngos su mthong thos su gyur lags/ tshes gcig gi nyin rje rdo rje 'chang chen po nyid kyi dbu bla rnams la mchod bshams rgyas pa dang
/ dbu sngas kyi gsol lcog steng du yab rje rdo rje 'chang bsod nams rin chen gyi byin rten 'ga' zhig dang / khyad 'phags nas ma skyes dgra'i gdung skal sangs rgyas kyi
'phel gdung sogs spyan 'dren mdzad/ tshes gnyis kyi tho rengs kyi char sngar mu bzhin bzhes thug zhus pa yang gsol bar ma gnang nas/ 'o da thugs dam lam dus kyi nyams bzhes
la 'jug go gsungs nas/ lam dus rgyas pa gnang ste mi bskyod pa chu dbang gi snying ga yan chad gang / shes rab ye shes kyi dbang thob/ ces yang yang bskyar zlos kyi tshul
du thugs bde nyams dang bcas gsung mur/ rgyun ring 'das rjes rje btsun gong ma'i byin phye dang / sangs rgyas kyi 'phel gdung sogs bzhes te/ rtag 'dzin can rnams chos
la bskul ba dang / le lo can rnams brtson 'grus la bskul ba'i phyir nyi dros kyi dus su gzugs sku 'od gsal chos dbyings su bsdu ba'i tshul bstan par gyur to/ /smras pa/
kye ma skyabs gcig drin chen rdo rje 'chang / /bde nas bde ba mkha' 'gro'i dar lam la/ /gshegs pa'i tshul 'di dngos sam rmi lam ci/ /dngos su gyur na gdul bya'i lhag ma
kun/ /bye phrug thang la 'khyams pa'i rnam thar shar/ /rmi lam yin na chos kun de ltar du/ /snang stong ma zhen ma 'gags mgon khyod kyi/ /gsung gis gdams pa'i nges shes da
ni go /grangs med bskal pa'i sngon du byang chen gyi/ /sa la 'dzegs kyang

gang 'dul sku mchog tu/ /rgyal ba'i phrin las shar ba'i mgon po khyod/ /rang nyid zhi bde'i sa la phebs min nam/ /snyigs ma'i ngan spyod dug mtshos bslad pa yi/ /bzang por
'khrul pa'i 'gro la skyengs gyur nas/ /bde bar byon na mgon pos ma nongs te/ /slar yang gdung shugs gsol 'debs rjes 'dzin mdzod/ /mtha' med 'khor ba'i sa gzhi khyon yangs
por/ /zin med mi dge'i sa bon btab btab nas/ /ngal med stsol ba nor ba'i sems can la/ /dmigs med thugs rjes gzigs shig drin can rje/ /dung dung sems pa 'gul ba'i dran shes
kyi/ /lhang lhang smre sngags cho nge'i dar dir dbyangs/ /hrig hrig mig gi bung ba chus brnangs nas/ /had had 'dre zhing ldog la thugs rjes gzigs/ /yang yang 'khor ba
lu gu rgyud nyid du/ /mang mang 'khyams pa'i ma rgan sems can kun/ /bde bde thar par bkri ba'i mgon po ru/ /myur myur sprul pa'i gar mdzod drin can rje/ /zhes kyang smras
so/ /de ltar bdag sogs lha dang bcas pa'i 'gro ba yongs kyi skyabs mgon sku drin nam mkha'i mtha' dang mnyam pa de nyid kyis dgung grangs lnga bcu rtsa lnga'i snron zla
phyi ma'i tshes gcig gi bar du/ bstan pa dang 'gro ba'i don rlabs po che kun gyis 'gran zla dang bral bar mdzad nas/ mdzes byed chu mo yos kyi lo'i spre'u'i zla ba nyis brtsegs
kyi phyi ma'i yar ngo'i bzang po dang por res gza' mig dmar/ zla skar nabs so la babs pa'i nyi dros sbrul gyi 'go zin tsam la ngo mtshar gyi ltas dang chabs gcig gdul
bya rtag 'dzin can rnams chos la bskul zhing / le lo can rnams brtson 'grus la 'god pa'i phyir dang / snyigs dus kyi spyod ngan la khrel ba dang yang bcas gzugs sku chos
kyi dbyings su bsdu tshul bstan pa'i mod nyid la/ nam

mkha' g.ya' dag pa'i khrod du 'ja' dkar po me tog rgyas pa'i dbyibs can dang / me tog gi char mang po rgyun ring babs shing / thugs dam zab mo'i nyams bzhes gsal 'debs sogs
mdzad sgo rnams kyang ji bzhin 'jam mgon gong ma mchog gi bka' 'doms kyis mdzad nas/ yar ngo'i dga' ba gsum pa'i nam langs bar la sku spur la skyon gyi rnam pa ye ma bzhes
pa'i ngo mtshar dang bka' drin lhan cig tu che ba dang / nam langs nas dri bzang gi phye mas byugs pa'i sku spur zangs nang du spyan drangs pa de mchod phreng / spos bsu
sogs dang bcas tshoms dmar mchod rdzas mang po'i dbus su gdan 'dren gyis/ chos sde rnam gnyis/ drung skya ser/ rin sgang / chos lhun pa sogs nas sku spur yid bzhin gyi
nor bu rin po cher byin rlabs sogs zhu bar mdzad rjes/ mkhan rin po che/ dbu byed rnam gsum/ grwa tshang mchod dpon bcas nas kye rdo rje'i dus mtha'i cho ga smin rgyas kyi
thog nas byin zar bzhu sbyong mdzad 'phral/ zhugs rang bzhes lta bu'i ngo mtshar gyi tshe'ang nam mkhar 'ja' dang me tog gi char sogs ni kun gyi mig lam du gsal zhing
de nyid sku gdung bzhu sbyangs zin 'phral nas bzung klu rnams kyang zim char rtag por 'bebs par byed/ de nas dgung zhag nam rdzogs par 'jam mgon zhal rnam pa gnyis nas 'khor
lo bde mchog nag po lugs rdul dkyil gyi steng nas bdun phrag re'i mtshams su dkyil 'khor gshigs gsol dang bcas zhal phye bar mdzad/ bde mchog tu a Ni drung dang btsun
mo kun skyid lags nas kyang dgongs rdzogs sgrub mchod dang / rje btsun drung 'chi med bstan pa'i nyi ma nas mkha' spyod rdo rje btsun mo'i sgrub mchod kyang de bzhin/ gzhan
yang 'dus tshogs rnams res bskor gyis/ kun rig /kye rdor/ gsang 'dus/ 'jigs byed ro langs brgyad bskor/

bdag med ma/ phur pa/ gur drag sogs thugs dgongs zab mo rdzogs thabs spyi dang bye brag thams cad 'jam mgon gong ma mchog gi bka' gsang gis 'doms par mdzad cing / gzhan yang
yar klungs mchog sprul rin po che dpon g.yog nas bdun gsum ring kye rdor dang / bco brgyad sku mched nas kun rig sogs dgongs pa zab mo rdzogs thabs rgya che rgyun khyongs
su mdzad skabs spyi sger nas mchod 'bul bsnyen bkur gzabs mas dus 'das shing / dgung zhag them nyin kyang rtse shod nas mchod pa bsnyen bkur bla na med pa sogs mdzad skabs
su'ang nam mkha' dngas shing / 'ja' 'od 'khyil ba dang / me tog gi char ni rtag par khor mo yug dang lo ltar dus dran gyi thog tu'ang 'bab par byed do/ /bdun phrag gnyis
kyi ring chos sde lho byang / chos lhun/ rin sgang / sngags drug sogs nas bla mchod/ smon lam/ gsol 'debs le tshan rnams la rtag 'grus dang / mang ja brgya mchod/ stong
mchod/ snyan shal sogs ni grangs mang stsal zhing / dbus gtsang mngar ris lho phyogs dang bcas pa'i grub mtha' ris med dgon bzhi brgya brgal tsam la mang ja/ bsngo rten/
spyi 'byed dngul srang brgya dang lnga bcu ri ba nas gnyis gsum ri ba'i bar du 'dus pa mang nyung dang bstun pa dang / ngor gong mus bkra shis chos sde sogs rang lugs
kyi dgon chen 'ga' zhig tu dmigs bsal gyi dgongs rdzogs sgrub mchod dgos cha yon sogs bzang por bstabs shing / gzhan yang rgyal dbang rin po cher gtsos ldan gyi tshan bcu
gnyis/ khri chen la de bzhin brgyad/ bstan rgyas gling du mchog sprul rin po cher bzhi/ bka' shag lhan du de bzhin/ phur lcog /lo sems dpa'/ 'on rgyal sras/ sle lung /
smin gling / dngos grub sdings/ dza lung pa/ bsam sding sa rje btsun sogs la re re/ bla brang mchog tu thams cad

mkhyen gzigs rin po cher drug /phyag mdzod du bzhi sogs gshegs rdzong che phra'ang mang du stob par gnang / de rnams kyis gtsos gzhis phyes mtha' dag nas dngos po bzang dgu
mtha' yas pa'i gdung 'bul kyang phul/ gdung rus rnams gzim chung du spyan drangs te rgyun ring bar 'jam mgon zhal rnam gnyis rje btsun drung sogs nas gsol 'debs bla mchod
sogs mdzad/ de nas gdung rus rnams las rang byon sogs yod pa 'ga' zhig ma gtogs tshang ma btul nas sAtstsha 'bum brgal tsam dang / bla ma yi dam sangs rgyas byang sems
chos srung nor lha dang bcas pa'i sku par grangs mang 'debs par mdzad skabs/ dngul srang chig stong chig brgya re bdun zho drug /gser srang brgyad cu gya brgyad dang zho
phyed brgyad sogs las grub pa'i dngul gdung rin po che phra rgyan gyis spras pa dang / 'dra sku rin po che gsar bskrun ring bsrel rnam bzhi spyi dang bye brag de dus kyi
tho gsal bzhin gyi sa phyur te/ 'jam mgon gong ma zhal rnam pa gnyis kyi dbus/ mkhan rin po che sogs ban tshang 'dus tshogs bcas nas rab tu gnas pa'i me tog gis byin rlabs
kyi gzi brgya 'bar bar mdzad/ de nas thang ston/ 'jigs byed bcu gsum ma'i sgrub mchod dang rab dbye kha skong rnam 'grel gzhung sbyong ser 'du bcas dus dran thog rgyun
'dzugs/ rje rdo rje 'chang de nyid kyi dgongs bzhed bzhin lha chen sprul pa'i khyams stong du rgyal ba tshe mtha' yas pa'i snang brnyan dngul rdo tshad brgya rtsar nye ba
las grub pa ngo mtshar can 'di nyid kyi gzungs phra rgyan sogs de dus kyi zin bris bzhin dang bcas/ rab tu gnas pa'i me char gyis byin mthu can du grub pa sogs 'di rnams
gtso bor smos/ dgongs pa zab mo chos dbyings de bzhin nyid du rdzogs pa'i thabs mtha' yas pa zhig /'jam mgon gong ma zhal rnam pa gnyis phrin las kyi kha lo sgyur ba po
bcas nas yang dag par 'bad med lhun gyis grub pa'i dge mtshan can du

'doms par mdzad pa bzhin/ rgyal bstan rin po che spyi dang / bye brag brtse chen snying po'i lung rtogs kyi bstan pa rin po che yar zla ltar 'phel zhing / bstan 'dzin gyi skyes
chen dam pa rnams sku tshe bde ldan mgon po'i rang bzhin du grub ste 'gro rnams bde skyid rdzogs ldan gzhon nu'i dga' ston la longs spyod par 'gyur ro/ /de dag gis ni
rigs dang dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho'i khyab bdag /snyigs ma'i dus kyi rgyal ba gnyis pa 'jam mgon mkhas grub dbang po/ /dpal sa skya pa chen po sngags 'chang bla ma thams
cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang kun dga' blo gros sangs rgyas bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i thun mong ba phyi'i rtogs pa brjod pa sgro skur kun bral drang gtam las 'bras
khungs thub ngo mtshar 'phrul gyi rol rtsed sde bzhi'i 'byung gnas zhes bya ba blo chung bdag gis gang zin phul zin to/ /yang smras pa/ kwa ye mig stong ldan pa nye dbang
gtsug gis 'dud cing bsnyen na mgon khyod zhabs pad spyi bor mi mchod ci/ /tshangs sras dgyes pa'i gsung rol 'khrol te tambu'i rgyud du chos kun 'jo na bstod bsngags me
tog cis mi 'thor/ /rang byung 'od kyi mdzes ma la chags gdong bzhi sprul na drin can bla ma'i zhal dkyil mjal ba'ang bskal bzang mchog /gtsug na zla bas de nyid thod kyi
rgyan du spud de legs par skyong na dam pa'i rtogs brjod su mi 'dzin/ /de phyir gang gi mdzad phrin rgya mtsho che/ /blta 'dod don mthun skye bo mchis so cog /thar lam
gru chen 'jug ngogs 'dir zhugs dang / /byin rlabs yon tan nor bu'ang ngang gis rnyed/ /mthong thos dran reg rjes 'dzin lcags kyu yis/ /dam du bzung ba'i nges tshig don ldan
du/ /mgon po khyod kyi che ba'i yon tan te/ /des na byin rlabs stsol ba'ang dngos po'i gshis/ /kye ho dgos 'dod

rin chen 'byung ba'i gter/ /blo chung ded dpon byis pa'i ngang tshul bdag /brgal 'dod 'bras bu gyi nar 'khums na yang / /lhag bsam mthun pa'i rlung dang lhan cig 'grogs/ /de
slad yongs rdzogs rin chen ma lon yang / /rmad byung ngo mtshar bsam 'phel dbang gi rgyal/ /mgon po thugs rje'i bdag nyid klu dbang gis/ /sa steng 'dod dgu 'jo ba'i dpal
du stsal/ /rgyu des chos kun rten 'brel grub pa'i phyir/ /bka' 'bangs byis blo'i phongs pa nyer sel nas/ /lce dbang don yod bden tshigs gsar ba'i skyes/ /'di ko kun bzang
mchod pa'i sprin bzhin 'bul/ /kun dang thun min gsang ba dag snang skor/ /mgon de'i thugs ka'i yang mdzod dmar po las/ /phal cher brjod tshig yig lam ma byon gshis/ /bdag
yid smra bsam brjod med ngang du lus/ /drang thig rgyal kun dpang bzhugs dge mtshan las/ /sgro skur rdzun phugs rdib pa'i kun slong bral/ /ya mtshan ngo mtshar che'am
chung yang rung / /yin lugs blo chung gang zin de ga yin/ /skyes sbyangs phra rag rngul las ches dman pa/ /bdag blo glang chen smyon pa'i dran dbang gis/ /dam pa'i rtogs
brjod smra spobs mi ldan yang / /rgyal ba'i thugs rjes sems med bem po'ang g.yo/ /de phyir gang gi gsang gsum dran pa dang / /skyabs gcig 'khon ston nyi zla'i bka' lung
gi /zer phreng snying gi ze'u 'brur 'phos ma thag /legs bshad sbrang rtsi'i bcud 'di zegs par gyur/ /de lta na yang thog med 'khor ba'i 'dam/ /ma spangs skye rga na 'chi'i
tshal gnas pas/ /las nyon lang tsho bdo ba'i bzhin ras kyi/ /me tog dgod kyang ltar snang skyon mchis na/ /dus gsum mi dge'i las 'bras do ra nas/ /chas dang lhan cig lhag
bsam dge ba'i lag /

ring du brkyangs te mchog gsum spyan snga ru/ /mthol bshags rten du 'bul gyis dag par mdzod/ /chad lhag 'gal zlos mu cor smra ba'i skyon/ /ci mchis thog med sdig dang lhan
bshags nas/ /gang gi mdzad phrin dri bsung mngar po'i rgyun/ /yid gnyis spangs te phyogs brgyar bsku bar shog /tshe rabs bgrangs yas ngal ba khyad bsad cing / /gtan 'dun
sgrub pa'i dam bca' snying bkod nas/ /brtson 'grus dang 'grogs 'bras bu sgrub pa bas/ /don yod stong lhag las 'di grub pas bde/ /gang gi gsung gi gdams pas rgyud brlan zhing
/ /rnam kun thugs rjes 'tsho ba'i dbugs dbyung gis/ /gnang ba thob dang lhan cig bla ma dang / /mgon po dbyer med mthong ba'ang skal ba bzang / /dam pa mchog dang dbyer
med 'khon ston rje'i/ /byin rlabs snying gi chu mtshor nyer sim ste/ /rtogs brjod rin chen sde bzhi'i yur lam nas/ /drangs pa'i rgyun 'di skye dgu'i dad mchor rol/ /lhag
bsam g.yas su 'khyil ba'i shang kha yis/ log smra 'dzin khri'i rgyu ba nyer bcom nas/ /ris med rgyal bstan chos 'khor bskor ba'i sgras/ /sa steng khyab cing de 'dzin sku
tshe brtan/ /khyad par rigs lnga rdo rje 'chang chen bcas/ /bsti ba'i gnas 'dir rigs gsum sprul pa'i gar/ /nam yang mi nub dpag bsam shing chen gyi/ /'dod 'jo'i rjes 'gror
mdzod cig drin can rje/ /skyabs gcig 'khon ston nyi zla'i 'od snang gis/ /'dzam gling gzhi chen khyon la nyer dkrigs te/ /mdzad phrin sku tshe rgyas pa'i dpal yon gyi/
/dge legs phyur por lud pa'i bkra shis shog /'di nyid skyong zhing dges pa'i mtshan ma yis/ /bdag yid 'phrogs so bla ma rdo rje gur/ /nam yang 'bral med thugs rje'i gur
khang du/ /rjes 'dzin

nyer 'tshes dben pa'i bkra shis shog /ces dam pa gang gi zhal snga nas kyi rtogs pa brjod pa sgro skur kun bral drang gtam yid ches las 'bras khungs thub ngo mtshar 'phrul
gyi rol rtsed sde bzhi'i 'byung gnas zhes bya ba 'di ni/ rje mkhas grub dbang po gang gi gsung 'bum pusta kar longs dang ma longs pa'i shog dril zin bris rnams dang / khyad
par rje nyid dgung grangs sum cu skor gyi mdzad pa'i zin bris/ rje btsun sa skya pa'i gdung rabs rin po che'i zhal skong las byung ba'i 'jam mgon mthu stobs dbang phyug
gi rnam thar dang / rje gnas gsar pa chen po'i rnam thar ljags rtsom ma rnams la gtsor brten/ khungs ldan rnams la zhib 'jug yang dag bgyis nas rang bzo'i sgro skur bab
col gyi rigs spangs te phan tshun lhu sgrig tshig sdeb rgyas bshad don bsdu bcas go rim ma 'chol ba'i lugs su gnad bsdus lta bur/ gang gi thugs rje dang 'jam mgon gong ma
bdag po chen po'i bka'i phrin las pa dang bcas pa'i bka' stsal gser gyi cod pan spyi bor bcings te/ lhag bsam dag pas zhus shing / da dung 'dir med du mi rung ba'i ngo
mtshar 'dra yod tshe mkhas grub blo ldan rnams nas bsnon par zhu zhing / rang nyid nas kyang de bzhin zhu rtsis dang / gzhan dgos gal che rigs ma gtogs gong smos bzhin rje
de'i mdzad pa mtha' dag pa smra ba ni/ sa chen po la gnas pa'i byang chub sems dpa' chen po rnams kyang ngal bar 'gyur bas na/ 'di nyid rtsom skabs kun la rgyus yod pas
de dus ngo mtshar 'di 'dra'ang yod pas ma chad pa gyis shig mi zer bzhin du blo ngan byis blo'i ngang tshul can dag nas 'di tsam rtsom pa pos lus so zhes mdzub rtser khur
'os kyang min pa bcas rje rdo rje 'chang de nyid kyi dgongs pa bzhin/ sku lhums zhugs nas bzung nar mar nag 'gros lta

bu'i tshul du zhus shing / gzhan mdzad pa phan tshun phyogs bsdoms kyis lhu bsgrigs bgyis tshe gzhan las ches cher ngo mtshar ba'i rnam thar dper 'os pa lta bu zhig yod 'dug
na'ang / da lam rje de'i dgongs pa las gzhan du gyur ba ma zhus shing / nyung 'dus ngo mtshar can zhig slar zhu 'dod yod lags/ blo gros can rnams kyis mgo mjug tshang ba
zhib mo'i blos rtog dpyod mdzad pas ngo mtshar che chung dgongs pa dwangs par yod cing / gzhan du gzu lums can dag gis shog bu kha shas bklags te smra ba por gshe ba'i
tshul gyis/ rje dam pa'i rnam thar la smod pa'ang dus dang gnas skabs kyi dbang gis mi 'ong pa'i nges pa med cing / snyan ngag mkhan dag ni don bsdu 'dir zhib dpyod kyis
mdzad pa mdo tsam rtogs nus shing / gang na'ang rje rdo rje 'chang chen po de nyid kyi gsang gsum dran pa dang / 'jam mgon gong ma bdag po chen po zhal rnam gnyis bka'i phrin
las pa dang bcas pa'i gsung gis gnang ba stsal ma thag nas 'go brtsams te khro mo shing 'brug lo'i/ rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyis chos 'khor bskor ba'i dus chen chu stod
zla ba'i yar tshes bcu gcig /rje rdo rje 'chang nyid kyi 'khrungs tshes su'ang gyur pa lhag pa lha mtshams kyi 'grub sbyor nyin dbus gtsang ru bzhi las ru lag gi sa'i
cha/ bod kyi rdo rje gdan dpal sa skya'i sprul pa'i gandho la chen po'i nye 'dabs rje btsun brtse chen snying po'i snang brnyan byin rlabs kyi gzi 'od 'bar ba'i sku drung
du rje de nyid kyi bka' 'bangs kyi tha shal rmongs rtul gyi na ba kun bkras kyis rdzogs par bgyis pa'i dge bas/ rgyal bstan rin po che spyi dang bye brag mi nyams dbyar
mtsho ltar rgyas pa dang / de 'dzin gyi skyes chen dam

pa spyi dang bye brag 'jam mgon gong ma rin po che zhal rnam gnyis 'byon 'gyur dang bcas pa'i sku tshe mdzad phrin dpag bsam gyi shing chen ltar rgyas nas/ ma gyur 'gro ba
kun bde skyid rdzogs ldan gsar pa'i dga' ston la longs spyod pa'i rgyur gyur cig/ // ! swa sti/ zab zhi sbros bral lhun grub gdod ma'i dbyings/ /rig gdangs snying rje'i rgya
yis yongs 'khyud pas/ /gzugs sku'i sgyu 'phrul drwa ba 'byams klas su/ /spro bar mdzad pa bde gshegs yongs kyi chos/ 1 /de las rgyal kun ji lta ji snyed kyi/ /ye shes
me long gzhon nu'i rdzu bag can/ /kai lA sha ri'i skye dgu bsrung slad du/ /he ru ka yi brtul zhugs la rol ba/ 2 /gdod nas ma rig dang 'khon ye shes kyi/ /stobs bcu'i dpung
gis bdud bzhi'i g.yul pham pas/ /ngaXg dbaXng kunaX dgaX'i blo grosaX saXngs rgyasaX kyi/ /legs gsung bstanaX paX'i rgyalaX mtshaXn 'dzin mkhas de/ 3 /rigs gsum rgyal
ba'i mkhyen brtse nus pa'i cha/ /yon tan phung por 'char ba'i 'phrul ji snyed/ /dri bral du kU la yi gos gcig gis/ /bcings pa'i sgyu 'phrul rmad byung gcam bu min/ 4 /gsang
gsum sgyu ma'i rol pa thun mong dang / /thun mong ma yin dag dang ma dag pa'i/ /gdul bya'i yul la ji ltar mtshams pa'i gar/ /bsgyur tshul sgra dang rtog pa'i rjes 'gro
ba/ 5 /ming tshig yi ge'i gzugs su shar bas kyang / /thos dang bsam pa'i dge mtshan srid gsum na/ /skal bar che ba'i rtog brjod a mr-i ta/ /kunaX dgaX' bkraX shis mkhyen
mtsho bsrubs las so/ 6 /gang de brtse chen ring lugs chu shel dbang / /dad stobs 'byor pa'i ral pas gus mchod pa/ /

sde bzhi dge bcu'i rgyal khab gangs ri'i bdag /sras lcam yum dang btsun mor bcas pa yis/ 7 /dad pas kun nas bslangs pa'i lhag bsam gyis/ /phyi mo gcig las du ma 'byung ba'i
'phrul/ /sbyor dngos rjes gsum dag pa'i 'du byed kyis/ /mthun rkyen ma tshang med pas legs par bsgrubs/ 8 /dge ba des mtshon dus gsum bdag gzhan gyi/ /bya byed dang 'brel
dge tshogs gcig bsdoms te/ /'gro kun rnam mkhyen sku bzhi'i go 'phang mchog /'thob rgyur yongs bsngo rnam par dag gyur cig 9 /gnas skabs su yang tshe dpal 'byor pa sogs/
/srid zhi'i dpal kun ma tshang med pas 'byor/ /bar chad bgegs dgra nang 'khrugs mi mthun phyogs/ /ma lus ming gi lhag ma nyid gyur cig 10 /dam pa'i rnam par thar la rjes
slob cing / /dam pa mchog rnams mnyes pa'i spyod la 'grus/ /dam pa mchog gis rjes bzung rnam grol nas/ /dam pa'i thugs dang ro gcig dbyer med shog/ 11 sarba mangga laM
siddhintu// //dge'o/ / #/ /skyabs kun 'dus zhal rnam 'dren srid zhi'i mgon/ /bka' drin mnyam med kun dga' blo gros kyi/ /ngo mtshar rnam thar gsol 'debs legs byas kyi/ /gtam
bzang byin rlabs bdud rtsi'i zil dngar bzhugs// // ! bod skad du/ mkha' khyab chos sku dbyings kyi pho brang nas rig pa rang mdangs kyi gsal snang rdzogs pa nges pa lnga
ldan gyi thugs rje rtog med lhun grub gang 'dul gyi rol pa shar ba ngag dbang kun dga' blo gros sangs rgyas bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i rnam thar gsol 'debs
legs byas gtam bzang byin rlabs bdud rtsi'i zil dngar zhes bya ba/ skyabs gnas kun 'dus grub gnyis stsol

ba'i zhabs kyi padmor phyag 'tshal lo/ /dpag yas rgyal kun mkhyen pa'i chu gter las/ /brtse ba'i thugs bskyed bstan 'gror 'dod pa dgu/ /'jo la nus mthu grub pa'i bsam 'phel
dbang / /kun dga' blo gros zhabs la gsol ba 'debs/ /nges par rdo rje snyems bdag ngang tshul las/ /g.yos min mi chad lhun grub phrin las kyis/ /'jam mgon dpa' bo nas bzung
sgro lung par/ /sna tshogs sprul pa'i zlos gar sgyur la 'dud/ /slar yang mtshan mchog gsum ldan gdung rigs su/ /sa spre'u snron zla'i yar tshes lhums zhugs nas/ /sa bya
dbo zla'i yar ngo dga' gsum la/ /bstan 'gro'i mgon du phebs la gsol ba 'debs/ /de tshe nyid kyi yon tan mthu nus kyis/ /skyed byed yum gyis lkog gyur mkhyen pa sogs/ /dngos
nyams 'od gsal gzigs snang ngo mtshar gyis/ /dus kun 'da' bar mdzad la gsol ba 'debs/ /bltams tshe gzim spyil btsun mor 'ja' 'od dang / /me char nyil dang 'obs nang
'jam dbyangs kyi/ /me tog gsar 'khrungs dang bcas phebs 'phral nas/ /thugs dran mtha' dag gsal la gsol ba 'debs/ /gzhon nur gyur kyang phal spyod mi mnga' zhing / /gsung
gsang dang por 'jam dbyangs gzungs sngags bton/ /sgam zhing des la byas shes drin du gzo/ /'jam mgon gzhon nur gyur la gsol ba 'debs/ /bgrang bya dgu dang bcu nas nyer bzung
ste/ /yi dam zhi khro'i dus grangs mtshan bsnyen dang / /'khor lo gsum ldan khrir phebs rab byung dang / /sngags 'chang dgos don bsgrubs la gsol ba 'debs/ /

yongs 'dzin bcu phrag bzhir nyer gsan mthar phyin/ /bsam byung rig pa'i rang rtsal thol byung grub/ /sgom sgrub nyin zhag phrug rer nyer bdun brtsams/ /gsan pa'i bya bar gzhol
la gsol ba 'debs/ /'chad la 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi spobs pa rdzogs/ /rtsod na phas rgol 'joms pa'i mthu stobs bdag /rtsom pa mkhas pa'i yid 'phrog thugs rje'i mgon/ /mkhas
pa'i bya bar gzhol la gsol ba 'debs/ /gang tshe gdul bya rjes su 'dzin pa'i dus/ /gzigs pa tsam gyis tshig don thugs chud de/ /gsung lam kho nas skal ldan nyin mtshan
kun/ /bar med chos 'khor bskor la gsol ba 'debs/ /gsar bskrun nyams gsos bstan la byi dor dang / /gan mdzod phyur dang dbul phongs sbyin gtong dang / /tshul khrims dri
zhim bzod bsran mgo me lta'i/ /brtson 'grus mtha' ru phyin la gsol ba 'debs/ /bskyed rdzogs mnyam gzhag nyin mtshan dus 'da' zhing / /ma 'dres so sor dpyod pa'i shes rab
bkra/ /rnam bzhi'i sbyin pa snyan smras 'khor bsdus nas/ /don spyod don mthun 'gro rnams skyong la 'dud/ /dngos nyams 'od gsal gzigs snang dang 'grogs nas/ /'gro ba'i khams
dang bsam pa bag nyal gyi/ /rgyud tshod ji bzhin mkhyen pa'i mngon shes kyis/ /dus gsum shes bya gzigs la gsol ba 'debs/ /zhi dul thugs rje'i chab kyis 'gro blo sbyangs/
/chab srid mnga' thang bla chen 'phags ltar rgyas/ /snang srid lha 'dre mi gsum dbang med 'dus/ /dgra 'dre'i

drag rtsub rang zhir mdzad la 'dud/ /yongs rdzogs bstan pa'i nyams len slob bshad chos/ /skal ldan gdul byar 'doms tshe ka bzhi dang / /gdung brgyad zhal slob lung bstan bdag
med ma'i/ /dbang tshe bdud rtsi 'khol 'bar lud la 'dud/ /gzhan yang snod ldan slob mar nang gi ni/ /phag mo mig lam stsal dang bir bsrungs dus/ /nyi zla 'gro 'ong bkag
sogs rdzu 'phrul gyi/ /ngo mtshar mang du bstan la gsol ba 'debs/ /dbang lung man ngag rjes gnang khrid kun kyang / /bka' babs phyag bzhes ngo sprod la sogs pa/ /ma 'dres
brda don 'phrod pa'i gsung snyan pos/ /gdul bya'i blo gros spel la gsol ba 'debs/ /sngags 'chang chos rje a mes zhabs sogs kyi/ /mdzad bzang rjes su slob pa'i thugs bskyed
ltar/ /tshogs phebs gdung rigs spel dang debs bsgrigs sogs/ /ngo mtshar phyag rjes srid mthar gsal la 'dud/ /bstan 'gro'i don du sku srog phongs med btang / /gdug rtsub
dgra 'dre byams dang snying rjes sbyangs/ /'khrul snang a 'thas rdzun gtibs kun 'dag dang / /kun bzang rang dbang thob la gsol ba 'debs/ /zhes sa gsum 'gro ba'i bla ma
yab rje rdo rje 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' blo gros sangs rgyas bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i rnam thar gsol 'debs mdor bsdus pa 'di'ang / gang gis skye ba du
mar rjes su bzung ba'i bka' slob kyi tha shal wa kun bkras kyis yud tsam zhig la sbyar ba'i dge bas bdag sogs skye 'gro kun gyi rgyud la byin rlabs myur du 'jug pa'i rgyur
gyur cig /de ltar rnam thar gsol 'debs mdor bsdus kyis/ /ngag snyan

zlos gar bsgyur 'dir tshig tshogs kyi/ /rjes 'brangs mkhas rnams re zhig bzod mdzod la/ /zhib mo'i gzur gnas go myong mdzad 'tshal lo/ /'di na skyes stobs blo gros rab phra
yang / /sbyangs stobs rang bzhin brjod kyi ngag tshig gi /phreng ba spel la longs 'khor 'khrol nas gda'/ /rlom sems dor nas bag yod ci bder bzhugs/ /zhes kyang smras so//
